012103 If any one says anything to you, you shall say, 'The Lord has need of them,' and he will send them immediately."
012104 This took place to fulfil what was spoken by the prophet, saying,
012105 "Tell the daughter of Zion, Behold, your king is coming to you, humble, and mounted on an ass, and on a colt, the foal of an ass."
012106 The disciples went and did as Jesus had directed them;
012107 they brought the ass and the colt, and put their garments on them, and he sat thereon.
012108 Most of the crowd spread their garments on the road, and others cut branches from the trees and spread them on the road.
012109 And the crowds that went before him and that followed him shouted, "Hosanna to the Son of David! Blessed is he who comes in the name of the Lord! Hosanna in the highest!"
012110 And when he entered Jerusalem, all the city was stirred, saying, "Who is this?"
012111 And the crowds said, "This is the prophet Jesus from Nazareth of Galilee."
012112 And Jesus entered the temple of God and drove out all who sold and bought in the temple, and he overturned the tables of the money-changers and the seats of those who sold pigeons.
012113 He said to them, "It is written, 'My house shall be called a house of prayer'; but you make it a den of robbers."
012114 And the blind and the lame came to him in the temple, and he healed them.
012115 But when the chief priests and the scribes saw the wonderful things that he did, and the children crying out in the temple, "Hosanna to the Son of David!" they were indignant;
012116 and they said to him, "Do you hear what these are saying?" And Jesus said to them, "Yes; have you never read, 'Out of the mouth of babes and sucklings thou hast brought perfect praise'?"
012117 And leaving them, he went out of the city to Bethany and lodged there.
012118 In the morning, as he was returning to the city, he was hungry.
012119 And seeing a fig tree by the wayside he went to it, and found nothing on it but leaves only. And he said to it, "May no fruit ever come from you again!" And the fig tree withered at once.
012120 When the disciples saw it they marveled, saying, "How did the fig tree wither at once?"
012121 And Jesus answered them, "Truly, I say to you, if you have faith and never doubt, you will not only do what has been done to the fig tree, but even if you say to this mountain, 'Be taken up and cast into the sea,' it will be done.
012122 And whatever you ask in prayer, you will receive, if you have faith."
012123 And when he entered the temple, the chief priests and the elders of the people came up to him as he was teaching, and said, "By what authority are you doing these things, and who gave you this authority?"
012124 Jesus answered them, "I also will ask you a question; and if you tell me the answer, then I also will tell you by what authority I do these things.
012125 The baptism of John, whence was it? From heaven or from men?" And they argued with one another, "If we say, 'From heaven,' he will say to us, 'Why then did you not believe him?'
012126 But if we say, 'From men,' we are afraid of the multitude; for all hold that John was a prophet."
012127 So they answered Jesus, "We do not know." And he said to them, "Neither will I tell you by what authority I do these things.
012128 "What do you think? A man had two sons; and he went to the first and said, 'Son, go and work in the vineyard today.'
012129 And he answered, 'I will not'; but afterward he repented and went.
012130 And he went to the second and said the same; and he answered, 'I go, sir,' but did not go.
012131 Which of the two did the will of his father?" They said, "The first." Jesus said to them, "Truly, I say to you, the tax collectors and the harlots go into the kingdom of God before you.
012132 For John came to you in the way of righteousness, and you did not believe him, but the tax collectors and the harlots believed him; and even when you saw it, you did not afterward repent and believe him.
012133 "Hear another parable. There was a householder who planted a vineyard, and set a hedge around it, and dug a wine press in it, and built a tower, and let it out to tenants, and went into another country.
012134 When the season of fruit drew near, he sent his servants to the tenants, to get his fruit;
012135 and the tenants took his servants and beat one, killed another, and stoned another.
012136 Again he sent other servants, more than the first; and they did the same to them.
012137 Afterward he sent his son to them, saying, 'They will respect my son.'
012138 But when the tenants saw the son, they said to themselves, 'This is the heir; come, let us kill him and have his inheritance.'
012139 And they took him and cast him out of the vineyard, and killed him.
012140 When therefore the owner of the vineyard comes, what will he do to those tenants?"
012141 They said to him, "He will put those wretches to a miserable death, and let out the vineyard to other tenants who will give him the fruits in their seasons."
012142 Jesus said to them, "Have you never read in the scriptures: 'The very stone which the builders rejected has become the head of the corner; this was the Lord's doing, and it is marvelous in our eyes'?
012143 Therefore I tell you, the kingdom of God will be taken away from you and given to a nation producing the fruits of it."
012144
012145 When the chief priests and the Pharisees heard his parables, they perceived that he was speaking about them.
012146 But when they tried to arrest him, they feared the multitudes, because they held him to be a prophet.
012201 And again Jesus spoke to them in parables, saying,
012202 "The kingdom of heaven may be compared to a king who gave a marriage feast for his son,
012203 and sent his servants to call those who were invited to the marriage feast; but they would not come.
012204 Again he sent other servants, saying, 'Tell those who are invited, Behold, I have made ready my dinner, my oxen and my fat calves are killed, and everything is ready; come to the marriage feast.'
012205 But they made light of it and went off, one to his farm, another to his business,
012206 while the rest seized his servants, treated them shamefully, and killed them.
012207 The king was angry, and he sent his troops and destroyed those murderers and burned their city.
012208 Then he said to his servants, 'The wedding is ready, but those invited were not worthy.
012209 Go therefore to the thoroughfares, and invite to the marriage feast as many as you find.'
012210 And those servants went out into the streets and gathered all whom they found, both bad and good; so the wedding hall was filled with guests.
012211 "But when the king came in to look at the guests, he saw there a man who had no wedding garment;
012212 and he said to him, 'Friend, how did you get in here without a wedding garment?' And he was speechless.
012213 Then the king said to the attendants, 'Bind him hand and foot, and cast him into the outer darkness; there men will weep and gnash their teeth.'
012214 For many are called, but few are chosen."
012215 Then the Pharisees went and took counsel how to entangle him in his talk.
012216 And they sent their disciples to him, along with the Hero'di-ans, saying, "Teacher, we know that you are true, and teach the way of God truthfully, and care for no man; for you do not regard the position of men.
012217 Tell us, then, what you think. Is it lawful to pay taxes to Caesar, or not?"
012218 But Jesus, aware of their malice, said, "Why put me to the test, you hypocrites?
012219 Show me the money for the tax." And they brought him a coin.
012220 And Jesus said to them, "Whose likeness and inscription is this?"
012221 They said, "Caesar's." Then he said to them, "Render therefore to Caesar the things that are Caesar's, and to God the things that are God's."
012222 When they heard it, they marveled; and they left him and went away.
012223 The same day Sad'ducees came to him, who say that there is no resurrection; and they asked him a question,
012224 saying, "Teacher, Moses said, 'If a man dies, having no children, his brother must marry the widow, and raise up children for his brother.'
012225 Now there were seven brothers among us; the first married, and died, and having no children left his wife to his brother.
012226 So too the second and third, down to the seventh.
012227 After them all, the woman died.
012228 In the resurrection, therefore, to which of the seven will she be wife? For they all had her."
012229 But Jesus answered them, "You are wrong, because you know neither the scriptures nor the power of God.
012230 For in the resurrection they neither marry nor are given in marriage, but are like angels in heaven.
012231 And as for the resurrection of the dead, have you not read what was said to you by God,
012232 'I am the God of Abraham, and the God of Isaac, and the God of Jacob'? He is not God of the dead, but of the living."
012233 And when the crowd heard it, they were astonished at his teaching.
012234 But when the Pharisees heard that he had silenced the Sad'ducees, they came together.
012235 And one of them, a lawyer, asked him a question, to test him.
012236 "Teacher, which is the great commandment in the law?"
012237 And he said to him, "You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart, and with all your soul, and with all your mind.
012238 This is the great and first commandment.
012239 And a second is like it, You shall love your neighbor as yourself.
012240 On these two commandments depend all the law and the prophets."
012241 Now while the Pharisees were gathered together, Jesus asked them a question,
012242 saying, "What do you think of the Christ? Whose son is he?" They said to him, "The son of David."
012243 He said to them, "How is it then that David, inspired by the Spirit, calls him Lord, saying,
012244 'The Lord said to my Lord, Sit at my right hand, till I put thy enemies under thy feet'?
012245 If David thus calls him Lord, how is he his son?"
012246 And no one was able to answer him a word, nor from that day did any one dare to ask him any more questions.
012301 Then said Jesus to the crowds and to his disciples,
012302 "The scribes and the Pharisees sit on Moses' seat;
012303 so practice and observe whatever they tell you, but not what they do; for they preach, but do not practice.
012304 They bind heavy burdens, hard to bear, and lay them on men's shoulders; but they themselves will not move them with their finger.
012305 They do all their deeds to be seen by men; for they make their phylacteries broad and their fringes long,
012306 and they love the place of honor at feasts and the best seats in the synagogues,
012307 and salutations in the market places, and being called rabbi by men.
012308 But you are not to be called rabbi, for you have one teacher, and you are all brethren.
012309 And call no man your father on earth, for you have one Father, who is in heaven.
012310 Neither be called masters, for you have one master, the Christ.
012311 He who is greatest among you shall be your servant;
012312 whoever exalts himself will be humbled, and whoever humbles himself will be exalted.
012313 "But woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! because you shut the kingdom of heaven against men; for you neither enter yourselves, nor allow those who would enter to go in.
012314
012315 Woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! for you traverse sea and land to make a single proselyte, and when he becomes a proselyte, you make him twice as much a child of hell as yourselves.
012316 "Woe to you, blind guides, who say, 'If any one swears by the temple, it is nothing; but if any one swears by the gold of the temple, he is bound by his oath.'
012317 You blind fools! For which is greater, the gold or the temple that has made the gold sacred?
012318 And you say, 'If any one swears by the altar, it is nothing; but if any one swears by the gift that is on the altar, he is bound by his oath.'
012319 You blind men! For which is greater, the gift or the altar that makes the gift sacred?
012320 So he who swears by the altar, swears by it and by everything on it;
012321 and he who swears by the temple, swears by it and by him who dwells in it;
012322 and he who swears by heaven, swears by the throne of God and by him who sits upon it.
012323 "Woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! for you tithe mint and dill and cummin, and have neglected the weightier matters of the law, justice and mercy and faith; these you ought to have done, without neglecting the others.
012324 You blind guides, straining out a gnat and swallowing a camel!
012325 "Woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! for you cleanse the outside of the cup and of the plate, but inside they are full of extortion and rapacity.
012326 You blind Pharisee! first cleanse the inside of the cup and of the plate, that the outside also may be clean.
012327 "Woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! for you are like whitewashed tombs, which outwardly appear beautiful, but within they are full of dead men's bones and all uncleanness.
012328 So you also outwardly appear righteous to men, but within you are full of hypocrisy and iniquity.
012329 "Woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! for you build the tombs of the prophets and adorn the monuments of the righteous,
012330 saying, 'If we had lived in the days of our fathers, we would not have taken part with them in shedding the blood of the prophets.'
012331 Thus you witness against yourselves, that you are sons of those who murdered the prophets.
012332 Fill up, then, the measure of your fathers.
012333 You serpents, you brood of vipers, how are you to escape being sentenced to hell?
012334 Therefore I send you prophets and wise men and scribes, some of whom you will kill and crucify, and some you will scourge in your synagogues and persecute from town to town,
012335 that upon you may come all the righteous blood shed on earth, from the blood of innocent Abel to the blood of Zechari'ah the son of Barachi'ah, whom you murdered between the sanctuary and the altar.
012336 Truly, I say to you, all this will come upon this generation.
012337 "O Jerusalem, Jerusalem, killing the prophets and stoning those who are sent to you! How often would I have gathered your children together as a hen gathers her brood under her wings, and you would not!
012338 Behold, your house is forsaken and desolate.
012339 For I tell you, you will not see me again, until you say, 'Blessed is he who comes in the name of the Lord.'"
012401 Jesus left the temple and was going away, when his disciples came to point out to him the buildings of the temple.
012402 But he answered them, "You see all these, do you not? Truly, I say to you, there will not be left here one stone upon another, that will not be thrown down."
012403 As he sat on the Mount of Olives, the disciples came to him privately, saying, "Tell us, when will this be, and what will be the sign of your coming and of the close of the age?"
012404 And Jesus answered them, "Take heed that no one leads you astray.
012405 For many will come in my name, saying, 'I am the Christ,' and they will lead many astray.
012406 And you will hear of wars and rumors of wars; see that you are not alarmed; for this must take place, but the end is not yet.
012407 For nation will rise against nation, and kingdom against kingdom, and there will be famines and earthquakes in various places:
012408 all this is but the beginning of the birth-pangs.
012409 "Then they will deliver you up to tribulation, and put you to death; and you will be hated by all nations for my name's sake.
012410 And then many will fall away, and betray one another, and hate one another.
012411 And many false prophets will arise and lead many astray.
012412 And because wickedness is multiplied, most men's love will grow cold.
012413 But he who endures to the end will be saved.
012414 And this gospel of the kingdom will be preached throughout the whole world, as a testimony to all nations; and then the end will come.
012415 "So when you see the desolating sacrilege spoken of by the prophet Daniel, standing in the holy place (let the reader understand),
012416 then let those who are in Judea flee to the mountains;
012417 let him who is on the housetop not go down to take what is in his house;
012418 and let him who is in the field not turn back to take his mantle.
012419 And alas for those who are with child and for those who give suck in those days!
012420 Pray that your flight may not be in winter or on a sabbath.
012421 For then there will be great tribulation, such as has not been from the beginning of the world until now, no, and never will be.
012422 And if those days had not been shortened, no human being would be saved; but for the sake of the elect those days will be shortened.
012423 Then if any one says to you, 'Lo, here is the Christ!' or 'There he is!' do not believe it.
012424 For false Christs and false prophets will arise and show great signs and wonders, so as to lead astray, if possible, even the elect.
012425 Lo, I have told you beforehand.
012426 So, if they say to you, 'Lo, he is in the wilderness,' do not go out; if they say, 'Lo, he is in the inner rooms,' do not believe it.
012427 For as the lightning comes from the east and shines as far as the west, so will be the coming of the Son of man.
012428 Wherever the body is, there the eagles will be gathered together.
012429 "Immediately after the tribulation of those days the sun will be darkened, and the moon will not give its light, and the stars will fall from heaven, and the powers of the heavens will be shaken;
012430 then will appear the sign of the Son of man in heaven, and then all the tribes of the earth will mourn, and they will see the Son of man coming on the clouds of heaven with power and great glory;
012431 and he will send out his angels with a loud trumpet call, and they will gather his elect from the four winds, from one end of heaven to the other.
012432 "From the fig tree learn its lesson: as soon as its branch becomes tender and puts forth its leaves, you know that summer is near.
012433 So also, when you see all these things, you know that he is near, at the very gates.
012434 Truly, I say to you, this generation will not pass away till all these things take place.
012435 Heaven and earth will pass away, but my words will not pass away.
012436 "But of that day and hour no one knows, not even the angels of heaven, nor the Son, but the Father only.
012437 As were the days of Noah, so will be the coming of the Son of man.
012438 For as in those days before the flood they were eating and drinking, marrying and giving in marriage, until the day when Noah entered the ark,
012439 and they did not know until the flood came and swept them all away, so will be the coming of the Son of man.
012440 Then two men will be in the field; one is taken and one is left.
012441 Two women will be grinding at the mill; one is taken and one is left.
012442 Watch therefore, for you do not know on what day your Lord is coming.
012443 But know this, that if the householder had known in what part of the night the thief was coming, he would have watched and would not have let his house be broken into.
012444 Therefore you also must be ready; for the Son of man is coming at an hour you do not expect.
012445 "Who then is the faithful and wise servant, whom his master has set over his household, to give them their food at the proper time?
012446 Blessed is that servant whom his master when he comes will find so doing.
012447 Truly, I say to you, he will set him over all his possessions.
012448 But if that wicked servant says to himself, 'My master is delayed,'
012449 and begins to beat his fellow servants, and eats and drinks with the drunken,
012450 the master of that servant will come on a day when he does not expect him and at an hour he does not know,
012451 and will punish him, and put him with the hypocrites; there men will weep and gnash their teeth.
012501 "Then the kingdom of heaven shall be compared to ten maidens who took their lamps and went to meet the bridegroom.
012502 Five of them were foolish, and five were wise.
012503 For when the foolish took their lamps, they took no oil with them;
012504 but the wise took flasks of oil with their lamps.
012505 As the bridegroom was delayed, they all slumbered and slept.
012506 But at midnight there was a cry, 'Behold, the bridegroom! Come out to meet him.'
012507 Then all those maidens rose and trimmed their lamps.
012508 And the foolish said to the wise, 'Give us some of your oil, for our lamps are going out.'
012509 But the wise replied, 'Perhaps there will not be enough for us and for you; go rather to the dealers and buy for yourselves.'
012510 And while they went to buy, the bridegroom came, and those who were ready went in with him to the marriage feast; and the door was shut.
012511 Afterward the other maidens came also, saying, 'Lord, lord, open to us.'
012512 But he replied, 'Truly, I say to you, I do not know you.'
012513 Watch therefore, for you know neither the day nor the hour.
012514 "For it will be as when a man going on a journey called his servants and entrusted to them his property;
012515 to one he gave five talents, to another two, to another one, to each according to his ability. Then he went away.
012516 He who had received the five talents went at once and traded with them; and he made five talents more.
012517 So also, he who had the two talents made two talents more.
012518 But he who had received the one talent went and dug in the ground and hid his master's money.
012519 Now after a long time the master of those servants came and settled accounts with them.
012520 And he who had received the five talents came forward, bringing five talents more, saying, 'Master, you delivered to me five talents; here I have made five talents more.'
012521 His master said to him, 'Well done, good and faithful servant; you have been faithful over a little, I will set you over much; enter into the joy of your master.'
012522 And he also who had the two talents came forward, saying, 'Master, you delivered to me two talents; here I have made two talents more.'
012523 His master said to him, 'Well done, good and faithful servant; you have been faithful over a little, I will set you over much; enter into the joy of your master.'
012524 He also who had received the one talent came forward, saying, 'Master, I knew you to be a hard man, reaping where you did not sow, and gathering where you did not winnow;
012525 so I was afraid, and I went and hid your talent in the ground. Here you have what is yours.'
012526 But his master answered him, 'You wicked and slothful servant! You knew that I reap where I have not sowed, and gather where I have not winnowed?
012527 Then you ought to have invested my money with the bankers, and at my coming I should have received what was my own with interest.
012528 So take the talent from him, and give it to him who has the ten talents.
012529 For to every one who has will more be given, and he will have abundance; but from him who has not, even what he has will be taken away.
012530 And cast the worthless servant into the outer darkness; there men will weep and gnash their teeth.'
012531 "When the Son of man comes in his glory, and all the angels with him, then he will sit on his glorious throne.
012532 Before him will be gathered all the nations, and he will separate them one from another as a shepherd separates the sheep from the goats,
012533 and he will place the sheep at his right hand, but the goats at the left.
012534 Then the King will say to those at his right hand, 'Come, O blessed of my Father, inherit the kingdom prepared for you from the foundation of the world;
012535 for I was hungry and you gave me food, I was thirsty and you gave me drink, I was a stranger and you welcomed me,
012536 I was naked and you clothed me, I was sick and you visited me, I was in prison and you came to me.'
012537 Then the righteous will answer him, 'Lord, when did we see thee hungry and feed thee, or thirsty and give thee drink?
012538 And when did we see thee a stranger and welcome thee, or naked and clothe thee?
012539 And when did we see thee sick or in prison and visit thee?'
012540 And the King will answer them, 'Truly, I say to you, as you did it to one of the least of these my brethren, you did it to me.'
012541 Then he will say to those at his left hand, 'Depart from me, you cursed, into the eternal fire prepared for the devil and his angels;
012542 for I was hungry and you gave me no food, I was thirsty and you gave me no drink,
012543 I was a stranger and you did not welcome me, naked and you did not clothe me, sick and in prison and you did not visit me.'
012544 Then they also will answer, 'Lord, when did we see thee hungry or thirsty or a stranger or naked or sick or in prison, and did not minister to thee?'
012545 Then he will answer them, 'Truly, I say to you, as you did it not to one of the least of these, you did it not to me.'
012546 And they will go away into eternal punishment, but the righteous into eternal life."
012601 When Jesus had finished all these sayings, he said to his disciples,
012602 "You know that after two days the Passover is coming, and the Son of man will be delivered up to be crucified."
012603 Then the chief priests and the elders of the people gathered in the palace of the high priest, who was called Ca'iaphas,
012604 and took counsel together in order to arrest Jesus by stealth and kill him.
012605 But they said, "Not during the feast, lest there be a tumult among the people."
012606 Now when Jesus was at Bethany in the house of Simon the leper,
012607 a woman came up to him with an alabaster flask of very expensive ointment, and she poured it on his head, as he sat at table.
012608 But when the disciples saw it, they were indignant, saying, "Why this waste?
012609 For this ointment might have been sold for a large sum, and given to the poor."
012610 But Jesus, aware of this, said to them, "Why do you trouble the woman? For she has done a beautiful thing to me.
012611 For you always have the poor with you, but you will not always have me.
012612 In pouring this ointment on my body she has done it to prepare me for burial.
012613 Truly, I say to you, wherever this gospel is preached in the whole world, what she has done will be told in memory of her."
012614 Then one of the twelve, who was called Judas Iscariot, went to the chief priests
012615 and said, "What will you give me if I deliver him to you?" And they paid him thirty pieces of silver.
012616 And from that moment he sought an opportunity to betray him.
012617 Now on the first day of Unleavened Bread the disciples came to Jesus, saying, "Where will you have us prepare for you to eat the passover?"
012618 He said, "Go into the city to a certain one, and say to him, 'The Teacher says, My time is at hand; I will keep the passover at your house with my disciples.'"
012619 And the disciples did as Jesus had directed them, and they prepared the passover.
012620 When it was evening, he sat at table with the twelve disciples;
012621 and as they were eating, he said, "Truly, I say to you, one of you will betray me."
012622 And they were very sorrowful, and began to say to him one after another, "Is it I, Lord?"
012623 He answered, "He who has dipped his hand in the dish with me, will betray me.
012624 The Son of man goes as it is written of him, but woe to that man by whom the Son of man is betrayed! It would have been better for that man if he had not been born."
012625 Judas, who betrayed him, said, "Is it I, Master?" He said to him, "You have said so."
012626 Now as they were eating, Jesus took bread, and blessed, and broke it, and gave it to the disciples and said, "Take, eat; this is my body."
012627 And he took a cup, and when he had given thanks he gave it to them, saying, "Drink of it, all of you;
012628 for this is my blood of the covenant, which is poured out for many for the forgiveness of sins.
012629 I tell you I shall not drink again of this fruit of the vine until that day when I drink it new with you in my Father's kingdom."
012630 And when they had sung a hymn, they went out to the Mount of Olives.
012631 Then Jesus said to them, "You will all fall away because of me this night; for it is written, 'I will strike the shepherd, and the sheep of the flock will be scattered.'
012632 But after I am raised up, I will go before you to Galilee."
012633 Peter declared to him, "Though they all fall away because of you, I will never fall away."
012634 Jesus said to him, "Truly, I say to you, this very night, before the cock crows, you will deny me three times."
012635 Peter said to him, "Even if I must die with you, I will not deny you." And so said all the disciples.
012636 Then Jesus went with them to a place called Gethsem'ane, and he said to his disciples, "Sit here, while I go yonder and pray."
012637 And taking with him Peter and the two sons of Zeb'edee, he began to be sorrowful and troubled.
012638 Then he said to them, "My soul is very sorrowful, even to death; remain here, and watch with me."
012639 And going a little farther he fell on his face and prayed, "My Father, if it be possible, let this cup pass from me; nevertheless, not as I will, but as thou wilt."
012640 And he came to the disciples and found them sleeping; and he said to Peter, "So, could you not watch with me one hour?
012641 Watch and pray that you may not enter into temptation; the spirit indeed is willing, but the flesh is weak."
012642 Again, for the second time, he went away and prayed, "My Father, if this cannot pass unless I drink it, thy will be done."
012643 And again he came and found them sleeping, for their eyes were heavy.
012644 So, leaving them again, he went away and prayed for the third time, saying the same words.
012645 Then he came to the disciples and said to them, "Are you still sleeping and taking your rest? Behold, the hour is at hand, and the Son of man is betrayed into the hands of sinners.
012646 Rise, let us be going; see, my betrayer is at hand."
012647 While he was still speaking, Judas came, one of the twelve, and with him a great crowd with swords and clubs, from the chief priests and the elders of the people.
012648 Now the betrayer had given them a sign, saying, "The one I shall kiss is the man; seize him."
012649 And he came up to Jesus at once and said, "Hail, Master!" And he kissed him.
012650 Jesus said to him, "Friend, why are you here?" Then they came up and laid hands on Jesus and seized him.
012651 And behold, one of those who were with Jesus stretched out his hand and drew his sword, and struck the slave of the high priest, and cut off his ear.
012652 Then Jesus said to him, "Put your sword back into its place; for all who take the sword will perish by the sword.
012653 Do you think that I cannot appeal to my Father, and he will at once send me more than twelve legions of angels?
012654 But how then should the scriptures be fulfilled, that it must be so?"
012655 At that hour Jesus said to the crowds, "Have you come out as against a robber, with swords and clubs to capture me? Day after day I sat in the temple teaching, and you did not seize me.
012656 But all this has taken place, that the scriptures of the prophets might be fulfilled." Then all the disciples forsook him and fled.
012657 Then those who had seized Jesus led him to Ca'iaphas the high priest, where the scribes and the elders had gathered.
012658 But Peter followed him at a distance, as far as the courtyard of the high priest, and going inside he sat with the guards to see the end.
012659 Now the chief priests and the whole council sought false testimony against Jesus that they might put him to death,
012660 but they found none, though many false witnesses came forward. At last two came forward
012661 and said, "This fellow said, 'I am able to destroy the temple of God, and to build it in three days.'"
012662 And the high priest stood up and said, "Have you no answer to make? What is it that these men testify against you?"
012663 But Jesus was silent. And the high priest said to him, "I adjure you by the living God, tell us if you are the Christ, the Son of God."
012664 Jesus said to him, "You have said so. But I tell you, hereafter you will see the Son of man seated at the right hand of Power, and coming on the clouds of heaven."
012665 Then the high priest tore his robes, and said, "He has uttered blasphemy. Why do we still need witnesses? You have now heard his blasphemy.
012666 What is your judgment?" They answered, "He deserves death."
012667 Then they spat in his face, and struck him; and some slapped him,
012668 saying, "Prophesy to us, you Christ! Who is it that struck you?"
012669 Now Peter was sitting outside in the courtyard. And a maid came up to him, and said, "You also were with Jesus the Galilean."
012670 But he denied it before them all, saying, "I do not know what you mean."
012671 And when he went out to the porch, another maid saw him, and she said to the bystanders, "This man was with Jesus of Nazareth."
012672 And again he denied it with an oath, "I do not know the man."
012673 After a little while the bystanders came up and said to Peter, "Certainly you are also one of them, for your accent betrays you."
012674 Then he began to invoke a curse on himself and to swear, "I do not know the man." And immediately the cock crowed.
012675 And Peter remembered the saying of Jesus, "Before the cock crows, you will deny me three times." And he went out and wept bitterly.
012701 When morning came, all the chief priests and the elders of the people took counsel against Jesus to put him to death;
012702 and they bound him and led him away and delivered him to Pilate the governor.
012703 When Judas, his betrayer, saw that he was condemned, he repented and brought back the thirty pieces of silver to the chief priests and the elders,
012704 saying, "I have sinned in betraying innocent blood." They said, "What is that to us? See to it yourself."
012705 And throwing down the pieces of silver in the temple, he departed; and he went and hanged himself.
012706 But the chief priests, taking the pieces of silver, said, "It is not lawful to put them into the treasury, since they are blood money."
012707 So they took counsel, and bought with them the potter's field, to bury strangers in.
012708 Therefore that field has been called the Field of Blood to this day.
012709 Then was fulfilled what had been spoken by the prophet Jeremiah, saying, "And they took the thirty pieces of silver, the price of him on whom a price had been set by some of the sons of Israel,
012710 and they gave them for the potter's field, as the Lord directed me."
012711 Now Jesus stood before the governor; and the governor asked him, "Are you the King of the Jews?" Jesus said, "You have said so."
012712 But when he was accused by the chief priests and elders, he made no answer.
012713 Then Pilate said to him, "Do you not hear how many things they testify against you?"
012714 But he gave him no answer, not even to a single charge; so that the governor wondered greatly.
012715 Now at the feast the governor was accustomed to release for the crowd any one prisoner whom they wanted.
012716 And they had then a notorious prisoner, called Barab'bas.
012717 So when they had gathered, Pilate said to them, "Whom do you want me to release for you, Barab'bas or Jesus who is called Christ?"
012718 For he knew that it was out of envy that they had delivered him up.
012719 Besides, while he was sitting on the judgment seat, his wife sent word to him, "Have nothing to do with that righteous man, for I have suffered much over him today in a dream."
012720 Now the chief priests and the elders persuaded the people to ask for Barab'bas and destroy Jesus.
012721 The governor again said to them, "Which of the two do you want me to release for you?" And they said, "Barab'bas."
012722 Pilate said to them, "Then what shall I do with Jesus who is called Christ?" They all said, "Let him be crucified."
012723 And he said, "Why, what evil has he done?" But they shouted all the more, "Let him be crucified."
012724 So when Pilate saw that he was gaining nothing, but rather that a riot was beginning, he took water and washed his hands before the crowd, saying, "I am innocent of this man's blood; see to it yourselves."
012725 And all the people answered, "His blood be on us and on our children!"
012726 Then he released for them Barab'bas, and having scourged Jesus, delivered him to be crucified.
012727 Then the soldiers of the governor took Jesus into the praetorium, and they gathered the whole battalion before him.
012728 And they stripped him and put a scarlet robe upon him,
012729 and plaiting a crown of thorns they put it on his head, and put a reed in his right hand. And kneeling before him they mocked him, saying, "Hail, King of the Jews!"
012730 And they spat upon him, and took the reed and struck him on the head.
012731 And when they had mocked him, they stripped him of the robe, and put his own clothes on him, and led him away to crucify him.
012732 As they went out, they came upon a man of Cyre'ne, Simon by name; this man they compelled to carry his cross.
012733 And when they came to a place called Gol'gotha (which means the place of a skull),
012734 they offered him wine to drink, mingled with gall; but when he tasted it, he would not drink it.
012735 And when they had crucified him, they divided his garments among them by casting lots;
012736 then they sat down and kept watch over him there.
012737 And over his head they put the charge against him, which read, "This is Jesus the King of the Jews."
012738 Then two robbers were crucified with him, one on the right and one on the left.
012739 And those who passed by derided him, wagging their heads
012740 and saying, "You who would destroy the temple and build it in three days, save yourself! If you are the Son of God, come down from the cross."
012741 So also the chief priests, with the scribes and elders, mocked him, saying,
012742 "He saved others; he cannot save himself. He is the King of Israel; let him come down now from the cross, and we will believe in him.
012743 He trusts in God; let God deliver him now, if he desires him; for he said, 'I am the Son of God.'"
012744 And the robbers who were crucified with him also reviled him in the same way.
012745 Now from the sixth hour there was darkness over all the land until the ninth hour.
012746 And about the ninth hour Jesus cried with a loud voice, "Eli, Eli, la'ma sabach-tha'ni?" that is, "My God, my God, why hast thou forsaken me?"
012747 And some of the bystanders hearing it said, "This man is calling Eli'jah."
012748 And one of them at once ran and took a sponge, filled it with vinegar, and put it on a reed, and gave it to him to drink.
012749 But the others said, "Wait, let us see whether Eli'jah will come to save him."
012750 And Jesus cried again with a loud voice and yielded up his spirit.
012751 And behold, the curtain of the temple was torn in two, from top to bottom; and the earth shook, and the rocks were split;
012752 the tombs also were opened, and many bodies of the saints who had fallen asleep were raised,
012753 and coming out of the tombs after his resurrection they went into the holy city and appeared to many.
012754 When the centurion and those who were with him, keeping watch over Jesus, saw the earthquake and what took place, they were filled with awe, and said, "Truly this was the Son of God!"
012755 There were also many women there, looking on from afar, who had followed Jesus from Galilee, ministering to him;
012756 among whom were Mary Mag'dalene, and Mary the mother of James and Joseph, and the mother of the sons of Zeb'edee.
012757 When it was evening, there came a rich man from Arimathe'a, named Joseph, who also was a disciple of Jesus.
012758 He went to Pilate and asked for the body of Jesus. Then Pilate ordered it to be given to him.
012759 And Joseph took the body, and wrapped it in a clean linen shroud,
012760 and laid it in his own new tomb, which he had hewn in the rock; and he rolled a great stone to the door of the tomb, and departed.
012761 Mary Mag'dalene and the other Mary were there, sitting opposite the sepulchre.
012762 Next day, that is, after the day of Preparation, the chief priests and the Pharisees gathered before Pilate
012763 and said, "Sir, we remember how that impostor said, while he was still alive, 'After three days I will rise again.'
012764 Therefore order the sepulchre to be made secure until the third day, lest his disciples go and steal him away, and tell the people, 'He has risen from the dead,' and the last fraud will be worse than the first."
012765 Pilate said to them, "You have a guard of soldiers; go, make it as secure as you can."
012766 So they went and made the sepulchre secure by sealing the stone and setting a guard.
012801 Now after the sabbath, toward the dawn of the first day of the week, Mary Mag'dalene and the other Mary went to see the sepulchre.
012802 And behold, there was a great earthquake; for an angel of the Lord descended from heaven and came and rolled back the stone, and sat upon it.
012803 His appearance was like lightning, and his raiment white as snow.
012804 And for fear of him the guards trembled and became like dead men.
012805 But the angel said to the women, "Do not be afraid; for I know that you seek Jesus who was crucified.
012806 He is not here; for he has risen, as he said. Come, see the place where he lay.
012807 Then go quickly and tell his disciples that he has risen from the dead, and behold, he is going before you to Galilee; there you will see him. Lo, I have told you."
012808 So they departed quickly from the tomb with fear and great joy, and ran to tell his disciples.
012809 And behold, Jesus met them and said, "Hail!" And they came up and took hold of his feet and worshiped him.
012810 Then Jesus said to them, "Do not be afraid; go and tell my brethren to go to Galilee, and there they will see me."
012811 While they were going, behold, some of the guard went into the city and told the chief priests all that had taken place.
012812 And when they had assembled with the elders and taken counsel, they gave a sum of money to the soldiers
012813 and said, "Tell people, 'His disciples came by night and stole him away while we were asleep.'
012814 And if this comes to the governor's ears, we will satisfy him and keep you out of trouble."
012815 So they took the money and did as they were directed; and this story has been spread among the Jews to this day.
012816 Now the eleven disciples went to Galilee, to the mountain to which Jesus had directed them.
012817 And when they saw him they worshiped him; but some doubted.
012818 And Jesus came and said to them, "All authority in heaven and on earth has been given to me.
012819 Go therefore and make disciples of all nations, baptizing them in the name of the Father and of the Son and of the Holy Spirit,
012820 teaching them to observe all that I have commanded you; and lo, I am with you always, to the close of the age."
020101 The beginning of the gospel of Jesus Christ, the Son of God.
020102 As it is written in Isaiah the prophet, "Behold, I send my messenger before thy face, who shall prepare thy way;
020103 the voice of one crying in the wilderness: Prepare the way of the Lord, make his paths straight -- "
020104 John the baptizer appeared in the wilderness, preaching a baptism of repentance for the forgiveness of sins.
020105 And there went out to him all the country of Judea, and all the people of Jerusalem; and they were baptized by him in the river Jordan, confessing their sins.
020106 Now John was clothed with camel's hair, and had a leather girdle around his waist, and ate locusts and wild honey.
020107 And he preached, saying, "After me comes he who is mightier than I, the thong of whose sandals I am not worthy to stoop down and untie.
020108 I have baptized you with water; but he will baptize you with the Holy Spirit."
020109 In those days Jesus came from Nazareth of Galilee and was baptized by John in the Jordan.
020110 And when he came up out of the water, immediately he saw the heavens opened and the Spirit descending upon him like a dove;
020111 and a voice came from heaven, "Thou art my beloved Son; with thee I am well pleased."
020112 The Spirit immediately drove him out into the wilderness.
020113 And he was in the wilderness forty days, tempted by Satan; and he was with the wild beasts; and the angels ministered to him.
020114 Now after John was arrested, Jesus came into Galilee, preaching the gospel of God,
020115 and saying, "The time is fulfilled, and the kingdom of God is at hand; repent, and believe in the gospel."
020116 And passing along by the Sea of Galilee, he saw Simon and Andrew the brother of Simon casting a net in the sea; for they were fishermen.
020117 And Jesus said to them, "Follow me and I will make you become fishers of men."
020118 And immediately they left their nets and followed him.
020119 And going on a little farther, he saw James the son of Zeb'edee and John his brother, who were in their boat mending the nets.
020120 And immediately he called them; and they left their father Zeb'edee in the boat with the hired servants, and followed him.
020121 And they went into Caper'na-um; and immediately on the sabbath he entered the synagogue and taught.
020122 And they were astonished at his teaching, for he taught them as one who had authority, and not as the scribes.
020123 And immediately there was in their synagogue a man with an unclean spirit;
020124 and he cried out, "What have you to do with us, Jesus of Nazareth? Have you come to destroy us? I know who you are, the Holy One of God."
020125 But Jesus rebuked him, saying, "Be silent, and come out of him!"
020126 And the unclean spirit, convulsing him and crying with a loud voice, came out of him.
020127 And they were all amazed, so that they questioned among themselves, saying, "What is this? A new teaching! With authority he commands even the unclean spirits, and they obey him."
020128 And at once his fame spread everywhere throughout all the surrounding region of Galilee.
020129 And immediately he left the synagogue, and entered the house of Simon and Andrew, with James and John.
020130 Now Simon's mother-in-law lay sick with a fever, and immediately they told him of her.
020131 And he came and took her by the hand and lifted her up, and the fever left her; and she served them.
020132 That evening, at sundown, they brought to him all who were sick or possessed with demons.
020133 And the whole city was gathered together about the door.
020134 And he healed many who were sick with various diseases, and cast out many demons; and he would not permit the demons to speak, because they knew him.
020135 And in the morning, a great while before day, he rose and went out to a lonely place, and there he prayed.
020136 And Simon and those who were with him pursued him,
020137 and they found him and said to him, "Every one is searching for you."
020138 And he said to them, "Let us go on to the next towns, that I may preach there also; for that is why I came out."
020139 And he went throughout all Galilee, preaching in their synagogues and casting out demons.
020140 And a leper came to him beseeching him, and kneeling said to him, "If you will, you can make me clean."
020141 Moved with pity, he stretched out his hand and touched him, and said to him, "I will; be clean."
020142 And immediately the leprosy left him, and he was made clean.
020143 And he sternly charged him, and sent him away at once,
020144 and said to him, "See that you say nothing to any one; but go, show yourself to the priest, and offer for your cleansing what Moses commanded, for a proof to the people."
020145 But he went out and began to talk freely about it, and to spread the news, so that Jesus could no longer openly enter a town, but was out in the country; and people came to him from every quarter.
020201 And when he returned to Caper'na-um after some days, it was reported that he was at home.
020202 And many were gathered together, so that there was no longer room for them, not even about the door; and he was preaching the word to them.
020203 And they came, bringing to him a paralytic carried by four men.
020204 And when they could not get near him because of the crowd, they removed the roof above him; and when they had made an opening, they let down the pallet on which the paralytic lay.
020205 And when Jesus saw their faith, he said to the paralytic, "My son, your sins are forgiven."
020206 Now some of the scribes were sitting there, questioning in their hearts,
020207 "Why does this man speak thus? It is blasphemy! Who can forgive sins but God alone?"
020208 And immediately Jesus, perceiving in his spirit that they thus questioned within themselves, said to them, "Why do you question thus in your hearts?
020209 Which is easier, to say to the paralytic, 'Your sins are forgiven,' or to say, 'Rise, take up your pallet and walk'?
020210 But that you may know that the Son of man has authority on earth to forgive sins" -- he said to the paralytic --
020211 "I say to you, rise, take up your pallet and go home."
020212 And he rose, and immediately took up the pallet and went out before them all; so that they were all amazed and glorified God, saying, "We never saw anything like this!"
020213 He went out again beside the sea; and all the crowd gathered about him, and he taught them.
020214 And as he passed on, he saw Levi the son of Alphaeus sitting at the tax office, and he said to him, "Follow me." And he rose and followed him.
020215 And as he sat at table in his house, many tax collectors and sinners were sitting with Jesus and his disciples; for there were many who followed him.
020216 And the scribes of the Pharisees, when they saw that he was eating with sinners and tax collectors, said to his disciples, "Why does he eat with tax collectors and sinners?"
020217 And when Jesus heard it, he said to them, "Those who are well have no need of a physician, but those who are sick; I came not to call the righteous, but sinners."
020218 Now John's disciples and the Pharisees were fasting; and people came and said to him, "Why do John's disciples and the disciples of the Pharisees fast, but your disciples do not fast?"
020219 And Jesus said to them, "Can the wedding guests fast while the bridegroom is with them? As long as they have the bridegroom with them, they cannot fast.
020220 The days will come, when the bridegroom is taken away from them, and then they will fast in that day.
020221 No one sews a piece of unshrunk cloth on an old garment; if he does, the patch tears away from it, the new from the old, and a worse tear is made.
020222 And no one puts new wine into old wineskins; if he does, the wine will burst the skins, and the wine is lost, and so are the skins; but new wine is for fresh skins."
020223 One sabbath he was going through the grainfields; and as they made their way his disciples began to pluck heads of grain.
020224 And the Pharisees said to him, "Look, why are they doing what is not lawful on the sabbath?"
020225 And he said to them, "Have you never read what David did, when he was in need and was hungry, he and those who were with him:
020226 how he entered the house of God, when Abi'athar was high priest, and ate the bread of the Presence, which it is not lawful for any but the priests to eat, and also gave it to those who were with him?"
020227 And he said to them, "The sabbath was made for man, not man for the sabbath;
020228 so the Son of man is lord even of the sabbath."
020301 Again he entered the synagogue, and a man was there who had a withered hand.
020302 And they watched him, to see whether he would heal him on the sabbath, so that they might accuse him.
020303 And he said to the man who had the withered hand, "Come here."
020304 And he said to them, "Is it lawful on the sabbath to do good or to do harm, to save life or to kill?" But they were silent.
020305 And he looked around at them with anger, grieved at their hardness of heart, and said to the man, "Stretch out your hand." He stretched it out, and his hand was restored.
020306 The Pharisees went out, and immediately held counsel with the Hero'di-ans against him, how to destroy him.
020307 Jesus withdrew with his disciples to the sea, and a great multitude from Galilee followed; also from Judea
020308 and Jerusalem and Idume'a and from beyond the Jordan and from about Tyre and Sidon a great multitude, hearing all that he did, came to him.
020309 And he told his disciples to have a boat ready for him because of the crowd, lest they should crush him;
020310 for he had healed many, so that all who had diseases pressed upon him to touch him.
020311 And whenever the unclean spirits beheld him, they fell down before him and cried out, "You are the Son of God."
020312 And he strictly ordered them not to make him known.
020313 And he went up on the mountain, and called to him those whom he desired; and they came to him.
020314 And he appointed twelve, to be with him, and to be sent out to preach
020315 and have authority to cast out demons:
020316 Simon whom he surnamed Peter;
020317 James the son of Zeb'edee and John the brother of James, whom he surnamed Bo-aner'ges, that is, sons of thunder;
020318 Andrew, and Philip, and Bartholomew, and Matthew, and Thomas, and James the son of Alphaeus, and Thaddaeus, and Simon the Cananaean,
020319 and Judas Iscariot, who betrayed him. Then he went home;
020320 and the crowd came together again, so that they could not even eat.
020321 And when his family heard it, they went out to seize him, for people were saying, "He is beside himself."
020322 And the scribes who came down from Jerusalem said, "He is possessed by Be-el'zebul, and by the prince of demons he casts out the demons."
020323 And he called them to him, and said to them in parables, "How can Satan cast out Satan?
020324 If a kingdom is divided against itself, that kingdom cannot stand.
020325 And if a house is divided against itself, that house will not be able to stand.
020326 And if Satan has risen up against himself and is divided, he cannot stand, but is coming to an end.
020327 But no one can enter a strong man's house and plunder his goods, unless he first binds the strong man; then indeed he may plunder his house.
020328 "Truly, I say to you, all sins will be forgiven the sons of men, and whatever blasphemies they utter;
020329 but whoever blasphemes against the Holy Spirit never has forgiveness, but is guilty of an eternal sin" --
020330 for they had said, "He has an unclean spirit."
020331 And his mother and his brothers came; and standing outside they sent to him and called him.
020332 And a crowd was sitting about him; and they said to him, "Your mother and your brothers are outside, asking for you."
020333 And he replied, "Who are my mother and my brothers?"
020334 And looking around on those who sat about him, he said, "Here are my mother and my brothers!
020335 Whoever does the will of God is my brother, and sister, and mother."
020401 Again he began to teach beside the sea. And a very large crowd gathered about him, so that he got into a boat and sat in it on the sea; and the whole crowd was beside the sea on the land.
020402 And he taught them many things in parables, and in his teaching he said to them:
020403 "Listen! A sower went out to sow.
020404 And as he sowed, some seed fell along the path, and the birds came and devoured it.
020405 Other seed fell on rocky ground, where it had not much soil, and immediately it sprang up, since it had no depth of soil;
020406 and when the sun rose it was scorched, and since it had no root it withered away.
020407 Other seed fell among thorns and the thorns grew up and choked it, and it yielded no grain.
020408 And other seeds fell into good soil and brought forth grain, growing up and increasing and yielding thirtyfold and sixtyfold and a hundredfold."
020409 And he said, "He who has ears to hear, let him hear."
020410 And when he was alone, those who were about him with the twelve asked him concerning the parables.
020411 And he said to them, "To you has been given the secret of the kingdom of God, but for those outside everything is in parables;
020412 so that they may indeed see but not perceive, and may indeed hear but not understand; lest they should turn again, and be forgiven."
020413 And he said to them, "Do you not understand this parable? How then will you understand all the parables?
020414 The sower sows the word.
020415 And these are the ones along the path, where the word is sown; when they hear, Satan immediately comes and takes away the word which is sown in them.
020416 And these in like manner are the ones sown upon rocky ground, who, when they hear the word, immediately receive it with joy;
020417 and they have no root in themselves, but endure for a while; then, when tribulation or persecution arises on account of the word, immediately they fall away.
020418 And others are the ones sown among thorns; they are those who hear the word,
020419 but the cares of the world, and the delight in riches, and the desire for other things, enter in and choke the word, and it proves unfruitful.
020420 But those that were sown upon the good soil are the ones who hear the word and accept it and bear fruit, thirtyfold and sixtyfold and a hundredfold."
020421 And he said to them, "Is a lamp brought in to be put under a bushel, or under a bed, and not on a stand?
020422 For there is nothing hid, except to be made manifest; nor is anything secret, except to come to light.
020423 If any man has ears to hear, let him hear."
020424 And he said to them, "Take heed what you hear; the measure you give will be the measure you get, and still more will be given you.
020425 For to him who has will more be given; and from him who has not, even what he has will be taken away."
020426 And he said, "The kingdom of God is as if a man should scatter seed upon the ground,
020427 and should sleep and rise night and day, and the seed should sprout and grow, he knows not how.
020428 The earth produces of itself, first the blade, then the ear, then the full grain in the ear.
020429 But when the grain is ripe, at once he puts in the sickle, because the harvest has come."
020430 And he said, "With what can we compare the kingdom of God, or what parable shall we use for it?
020431 It is like a grain of mustard seed, which, when sown upon the ground, is the smallest of all the seeds on earth;
020432 yet when it is sown it grows up and becomes the greatest of all shrubs, and puts forth large branches, so that the birds of the air can make nests in its shade."
020433 With many such parables he spoke the word to them, as they were able to hear it;
020434 he did not speak to them without a parable, but privately to his own disciples he explained everything.
020435 On that day, when evening had come, he said to them, "Let us go across to the other side."
020436 And leaving the crowd, they took him with them in the boat, just as he was. And other boats were with him.
020437 And a great storm of wind arose, and the waves beat into the boat, so that the boat was already filling.
020438 But he was in the stern, asleep on the cushion; and they woke him and said to him, "Teacher, do you not care if we perish?"
020439 And he awoke and rebuked the wind, and said to the sea, "Peace! Be still!" And the wind ceased, and there was a great calm.
020440 He said to them, "Why are you afraid? Have you no faith?"
020441 And they were filled with awe, and said to one another, "Who then is this, that even wind and sea obey him?"
020501 They came to the other side of the sea, to the country of the Ger'asenes.
020502 And when he had come out of the boat, there met him out of the tombs a man with an unclean spirit,
020503 who lived among the tombs; and no one could bind him any more, even with a chain;
020504 for he had often been bound with fetters and chains, but the chains he wrenched apart, and the fetters he broke in pieces; and no one had the strength to subdue him.
020505 Night and day among the tombs and on the mountains he was always crying out, and bruising himself with stones.
020506 And when he saw Jesus from afar, he ran and worshiped him;
020507 and crying out with a loud voice, he said, "What have you to do with me, Jesus, Son of the Most High God? I adjure you by God, do not torment me."
020508 For he had said to him, "Come out of the man, you unclean spirit!"
020509 And Jesus asked him, "What is your name?" He replied, "My name is Legion; for we are many."
020510 And he begged him eagerly not to send them out of the country.
020511 Now a great herd of swine was feeding there on the hillside;
020512 and they begged him, "Send us to the swine, let us enter them."
020513 So he gave them leave. And the unclean spirits came out, and entered the swine; and the herd, numbering about two thousand, rushed down the steep bank into the sea, and were drowned in the sea.
020514 The herdsmen fled, and told it in the city and in the country. And people came to see what it was that had happened.
020515 And they came to Jesus, and saw the demoniac sitting there, clothed and in his right mind, the man who had had the legion; and they were afraid.
020516 And those who had seen it told what had happened to the demoniac and to the swine.
020517 And they began to beg Jesus to depart from their neighborhood.
020518 And as he was getting into the boat, the man who had been possessed with demons begged him that he might be with him.
020519 But he refused, and said to him, "Go home to your friends, and tell them how much the Lord has done for you, and how he has had mercy on you."
020520 And he went away and began to proclaim in the Decap'olis how much Jesus had done for him; and all men marveled.
020521 And when Jesus had crossed again in the boat to the other side, a great crowd gathered about him; and he was beside the sea.
020522 Then came one of the rulers of the synagogue, Ja'irus by name; and seeing him, he fell at his feet,
020523 and besought him, saying, "My little daughter is at the point of death. Come and lay your hands on her, so that she may be made well, and live."
020524 And he went with him. And a great crowd followed him and thronged about him.
020525 And there was a woman who had had a flow of blood for twelve years,
020526 and who had suffered much under many physicians, and had spent all that she had, and was no better but rather grew worse.
020527 She had heard the reports about Jesus, and came up behind him in the crowd and touched his garment.
020528 For she said, "If I touch even his garments, I shall be made well."
020529 And immediately the hemorrhage ceased; and she felt in her body that she was healed of her disease.
020530 And Jesus, perceiving in himself that power had gone forth from him, immediately turned about in the crowd, and said, "Who touched my garments?"
020531 And his disciples said to him, "You see the crowd pressing around you, and yet you say, 'Who touched me?'"
020532 And he looked around to see who had done it.
020533 But the woman, knowing what had been done to her, came in fear and trembling and fell down before him, and told him the whole truth.
020534 And he said to her, "Daughter, your faith has made you well; go in peace, and be healed of your disease."
020535 While he was still speaking, there came from the ruler's house some who said, "Your daughter is dead. Why trouble the Teacher any further?"
020536 But ignoring what they said, Jesus said to the ruler of the synagogue, "Do not fear, only believe."
020537 And he allowed no one to follow him except Peter and James and John the brother of James.
020538 When they came to the house of the ruler of the synagogue, he saw a tumult, and people weeping and wailing loudly.
020539 And when he had entered, he said to them, "Why do you make a tumult and weep? The child is not dead but sleeping."
020540 And they laughed at him. But he put them all outside, and took the child's father and mother and those who were with him, and went in where the child was.
020541 Taking her by the hand he said to her, "Tal'itha cu'mi"; which means, "Little girl, I say to you, arise."
020542 And immediately the girl got up and walked (she was twelve years of age), and they were immediately overcome with amazement.
020543 And he strictly charged them that no one should know this, and told them to give her something to eat.
020601 He went away from there and came to his own country; and his disciples followed him.
020602 And on the sabbath he began to teach in the synagogue; and many who heard him were astonished, saying, "Where did this man get all this? What is the wisdom given to him? What mighty works are wrought by his hands!
020603 Is not this the carpenter, the son of Mary and brother of James and Joses and Judas and Simon, and are not his sisters here with us?" And they took offense at him.
020604 And Jesus said to them, "A prophet is not without honor, except in his own country, and among his own kin, and in his own house."
020605 And he could do no mighty work there, except that he laid his hands upon a few sick people and healed them.
020606 And he marveled because of their unbelief. And he went about among the villages teaching.
020607 And he called to him the twelve, and began to send them out two by two, and gave them authority over the unclean spirits.
020608 He charged them to take nothing for their journey except a staff; no bread, no bag, no money in their belts;
020609 but to wear sandals and not put on two tunics.
020610 And he said to them, "Where you enter a house, stay there until you leave the place.
020611 And if any place will not receive you and they refuse to hear you, when you leave, shake off the dust that is on your feet for a testimony against them."
020612 So they went out and preached that men should repent.
020613 And they cast out many demons, and anointed with oil many that were sick and healed them.
020614 King Herod heard of it; for Jesus' name had become known. Some said, "John the baptizer has been raised from the dead; that is why these powers are at work in him."
020615 But others said, "It is Eli'jah." And others said, "It is a prophet, like one of the prophets of old."
020616 But when Herod heard of it he said, "John, whom I beheaded, has been raised."
020617 For Herod had sent and seized John, and bound him in prison for the sake of Hero'di-as, his brother Philip's wife; because he had married her.
020618 For John said to Herod, "It is not lawful for you to have your brother's wife."
020619 And Hero'di-as had a grudge against him, and wanted to kill him. But she could not,
020620 for Herod feared John, knowing that he was a righteous and holy man, and kept him safe. When he heard him, he was much perplexed; and yet he heard him gladly.
020621 But an opportunity came when Herod on his birthday gave a banquet for his courtiers and officers and the leading men of Galilee.
020622 For when Hero'di-as' daughter came in and danced, she pleased Herod and his guests; and the king said to the girl, "Ask me for whatever you wish, and I will grant it."
020623 And he vowed to her, "Whatever you ask me, I will give you, even half of my kingdom."
020624 And she went out, and said to her mother, "What shall I ask?" And she said, "The head of John the baptizer."
020625 And she came in immediately with haste to the king, and asked, saying, "I want you to give me at once the head of John the Baptist on a platter."
020626 And the king was exceedingly sorry; but because of his oaths and his guests he did not want to break his word to her.
020627 And immediately the king sent a soldier of the guard and gave orders to bring his head. He went and beheaded him in the prison,
020628 and brought his head on a platter, and gave it to the girl; and the girl gave it to her mother.
020629 When his disciples heard of it, they came and took his body, and laid it in a tomb.
020630 The apostles returned to Jesus, and told him all that they had done and taught.
020631 And he said to them, "Come away by yourselves to a lonely place, and rest a while." For many were coming and going, and they had no leisure even to eat.
020632 And they went away in the boat to a lonely place by themselves.
020633 Now many saw them going, and knew them, and they ran there on foot from all the towns, and got there ahead of them.
020634 As he went ashore he saw a great throng, and he had compassion on them, because they were like sheep without a shepherd; and he began to teach them many things.
020635 And when it grew late, his disciples came to him and said, "This is a lonely place, and the hour is now late;
020636 send them away, to go into the country and villages round about and buy themselves something to eat."
020637 But he answered them, "You give them something to eat." And they said to him, "Shall we go and buy two hundred denarii worth of bread, and give it to them to eat?"
020638 And he said to them, "How many loaves have you? Go and see." And when they had found out, they said, "Five, and two fish."
020639 Then he commanded them all to sit down by companies upon the green grass.
020640 So they sat down in groups, by hundreds and by fifties.
020641 And taking the five loaves and the two fish he looked up to heaven, and blessed, and broke the loaves, and gave them to the disciples to set before the people; and he divided the two fish among them all.
020642 And they all ate and were satisfied.
020643 And they took up twelve baskets full of broken pieces and of the fish.
020644 And those who ate the loaves were five thousand men.
020645 Immediately he made his disciples get into the boat and go before him to the other side, to Beth-sa'ida, while he dismissed the crowd.
020646 And after he had taken leave of them, he went up on the mountain to pray.
020647 And when evening came, the boat was out on the sea, and he was alone on the land.
020648 And he saw that they were making headway painfully, for the wind was against them. And about the fourth watch of the night he came to them, walking on the sea. He meant to pass by them,
020649 but when they saw him walking on the sea they thought it was a ghost, and cried out;
020650 for they all saw him, and were terrified. But immediately he spoke to them and said, "Take heart, it is I; have no fear."
020651 And he got into the boat with them and the wind ceased. And they were utterly astounded,
020652 for they did not understand about the loaves, but their hearts were hardened.
020653 And when they had crossed over, they came to land at Gennes'aret, and moored to the shore.
020654 And when they got out of the boat, immediately the people recognized him,
020655 and ran about the whole neighborhood and began to bring sick people on their pallets to any place where they heard he was.
020656 And wherever he came, in villages, cities, or country, they laid the sick in the market places, and besought him that they might touch even the fringe of his garment; and as many as touched it were made well.
020701 Now when the Pharisees gathered together to him, with some of the scribes, who had come from Jerusalem,
020702 they saw that some of his disciples ate with hands defiled, that is, unwashed.
020703 (For the Pharisees, and all the Jews, do not eat unless they wash their hands, observing the tradition of the elders;
020704 and when they come from the market place, they do not eat unless they purify themselves; and there are many other traditions which they observe, the washing of cups and pots and vessels of bronze.)
020705 And the Pharisees and the scribes asked him, "Why do your disciples not live according to the tradition of the elders, but eat with hands defiled?"
020706 And he said to them, "Well did Isaiah prophesy of you hypocrites, as it is written, 'This people honors me with their lips, but their heart is far from me;
020707 in vain do they worship me, teaching as doctrines the precepts of men.'
020708 You leave the commandment of God, and hold fast the tradition of men."
020709 And he said to them, "You have a fine way of rejecting the commandment of God, in order to keep your tradition!
020710 For Moses said, 'Honor your father and your mother'; and, 'He who speaks evil of father or mother, let him surely die';
020711 but you say, 'If a man tells his father or his mother, What you would have gained from me is Corban' (that is, given to God) --
020712 then you no longer permit him to do anything for his father or mother,
020713 thus making void the word of God through your tradition which you hand on. And many such things you do."
020714 And he called the people to him again, and said to them, "Hear me, all of you, and understand:
020715 there is nothing outside a man which by going into him can defile him; but the things which come out of a man are what defile him."
020716
020717 And when he had entered the house, and left the people, his disciples asked him about the parable.
020718 And he said to them, "Then are you also without understanding? Do you not see that whatever goes into a man from outside cannot defile him,
020719 since it enters, not his heart but his stomach, and so passes on?" (Thus he declared all foods clean.)
020720 And he said, "What comes out of a man is what defiles a man.
020721 For from within, out of the heart of man, come evil thoughts, fornication, theft, murder, adultery,
020722 coveting, wickedness, deceit, licentiousness, envy, slander, pride, foolishness.
020723 All these evil things come from within, and they defile a man."
020724 And from there he arose and went away to the region of Tyre and Sidon. And he entered a house, and would not have any one know it; yet he could not be hid.
020725 But immediately a woman, whose little daughter was possessed by an unclean spirit, heard of him, and came and fell down at his feet.
020726 Now the woman was a Greek, a Syrophoeni'cian by birth. And she begged him to cast the demon out of her daughter.
020727 And he said to her, "Let the children first be fed, for it is not right to take the children's bread and throw it to the dogs."
020728 But she answered him, "Yes, Lord; yet even the dogs under the table eat the children's crumbs."
020729 And he said to her, "For this saying you may go your way; the demon has left your daughter."
020730 And she went home, and found the child lying in bed, and the demon gone.
020731 Then he returned from the region of Tyre, and went through Sidon to the Sea of Galilee, through the region of the Decap'olis.
020732 And they brought to him a man who was deaf and had an impediment in his speech; and they besought him to lay his hand upon him.
020733 And taking him aside from the multitude privately, he put his fingers into his ears, and he spat and touched his tongue;
020734 and looking up to heaven, he sighed, and said to him, "Eph'phatha," that is, "Be opened."
020735 And his ears were opened, his tongue was released, and he spoke plainly.
020736 And he charged them to tell no one; but the more he charged them, the more zealously they proclaimed it.
020737 And they were astonished beyond measure, saying, "He has done all things well; he even makes the deaf hear and the dumb speak."
020801 In those days, when again a great crowd had gathered, and they had nothing to eat, he called his disciples to him, and said to them,
020802 "I have compassion on the crowd, because they have been with me now three days, and have nothing to eat;
020803 and if I send them away hungry to their homes, they will faint on the way; and some of them have come a long way."
020804 And his disciples answered him, "How can one feed these men with bread here in the desert?"
020805 And he asked them, "How many loaves have you?" They said, "Seven."
020806 And he commanded the crowd to sit down on the ground; and he took the seven loaves, and having given thanks he broke them and gave them to his disciples to set before the people; and they set them before the crowd.
020807 And they had a few small fish; and having blessed them, he commanded that these also should be set before them.
020808 And they ate, and were satisfied; and they took up the broken pieces left over, seven baskets full.
020809 And there were about four thousand people.
020810 And he sent them away; and immediately he got into the boat with his disciples, and went to the district of Dalmanu'tha.
020811 The Pharisees came and began to argue with him, seeking from him a sign from heaven, to test him.
020812 And he sighed deeply in his spirit, and said, "Why does this generation seek a sign? Truly, I say to you, no sign shall be given to this generation."
020813 And he left them, and getting into the boat again he departed to the other side.
020814 Now they had forgotten to bring bread; and they had only one loaf with them in the boat.
020815 And he cautioned them, saying, "Take heed, beware of the leaven of the Pharisees and the leaven of Herod."
020816 And they discussed it with one another, saying, "We have no bread."
020817 And being aware of it, Jesus said to them, "Why do you discuss the fact that you have no bread? Do you not yet perceive or understand? Are your hearts hardened?
020818 Having eyes do you not see, and having ears do you not hear? And do you not remember?
020819 When I broke the five loaves for the five thousand, how many baskets full of broken pieces did you take up?" They said to him, "Twelve."
020820 "And the seven for the four thousand, how many baskets full of broken pieces did you take up?" And they said to him, "Seven."
020821 And he said to them, "Do you not yet understand?"
020822 And they came to Beth-sa'ida. And some people brought to him a blind man, and begged him to touch him.
020823 And he took the blind man by the hand, and led him out of the village; and when he had spit on his eyes and laid his hands upon him, he asked him, "Do you see anything?"
020824 And he looked up and said, "I see men; but they look like trees, walking."
020825 Then again he laid his hands upon his eyes; and he looked intently and was restored, and saw everything clearly.
020826 And he sent him away to his home, saying, "Do not even enter the village."
020827 And Jesus went on with his disciples, to the villages of Caesare'a Philip'pi; and on the way he asked his disciples, "Who do men say that I am?"
020828 And they told him, "John the Baptist; and others say, Eli'jah; and others one of the prophets."
020829 And he asked them, "But who do you say that I am?" Peter answered him, "You are the Christ."
020830 And he charged them to tell no one about him.
020831 And he began to teach them that the Son of man must suffer many things, and be rejected by the elders and the chief priests and the scribes, and be killed, and after three days rise again.
020832 And he said this plainly. And Peter took him, and began to rebuke him.
020833 But turning and seeing his disciples, he rebuked Peter, and said, "Get behind me, Satan! For you are not on the side of God, but of men."
020834 And he called to him the multitude with his disciples, and said to them, "If any man would come after me, let him deny himself and take up his cross and follow me.
020835 For whoever would save his life will lose it; and whoever loses his life for my sake and the gospel's will save it.
020836 For what does it profit a man, to gain the whole world and forfeit his life?
020837 For what can a man give in return for his life?
