020838 For whoever is ashamed of me and of my words in this adulterous and sinful generation, of him will the Son of man also be ashamed, when he comes in the glory of his Father with the holy angels."
020901 And he said to them, "Truly, I say to you, there are some standing here who will not taste death before they see that the kingdom of God has come with power."
020902 And after six days Jesus took with him Peter and James and John, and led them up a high mountain apart by themselves; and he was transfigured before them,
020903 and his garments became glistening, intensely white, as no fuller on earth could bleach them.
020904 And there appeared to them Eli'jah with Moses; and they were talking to Jesus.
020905 And Peter said to Jesus, "Master, it is well that we are here; let us make three booths, one for you and one for Moses and one for Eli'jah."
020906 For he did not know what to say, for they were exceedingly afraid.
020907 And a cloud overshadowed them, and a voice came out of the cloud, "This is my beloved Son; listen to him."
020908 And suddenly looking around they no longer saw any one with them but Jesus only.
020909 And as they were coming down the mountain, he charged them to tell no one what they had seen, until the Son of man should have risen from the dead.
020910 So they kept the matter to themselves, questioning what the rising from the dead meant.
020911 And they asked him, "Why do the scribes say that first Eli'jah must come?"
020912 And he said to them, "Eli'jah does come first to restore all things; and how is it written of the Son of man, that he should suffer many things and be treated with contempt?
020913 But I tell you that Eli'jah has come, and they did to him whatever they pleased, as it is written of him."
020914 And when they came to the disciples, they saw a great crowd about them, and scribes arguing with them.
020915 And immediately all the crowd, when they saw him, were greatly amazed, and ran up to him and greeted him.
020916 And he asked them, "What are you discussing with them?"
020917 And one of the crowd answered him, "Teacher, I brought my son to you, for he has a dumb spirit;
020918 and wherever it seizes him, it dashes him down; and he foams and grinds his teeth and becomes rigid; and I asked your disciples to cast it out, and they were not able."
020919 And he answered them, "O faithless generation, how long am I to be with you? How long am I to bear with you? Bring him to me."
020920 And they brought the boy to him; and when the spirit saw him, immediately it convulsed the boy, and he fell on the ground and rolled about, foaming at the mouth.
020921 And Jesus asked his father, "How long has he had this?" And he said, "From childhood.
020922 And it has often cast him into the fire and into the water, to destroy him; but if you can do anything, have pity on us and help us."
020923 And Jesus said to him, "If you can! All things are possible to him who believes."
020924 Immediately the father of the child cried out and said, "I believe; help my unbelief!"
020925 And when Jesus saw that a crowd came running together, he rebuked the unclean spirit, saying to it, "You dumb and deaf spirit, I command you, come out of him, and never enter him again."
020926 And after crying out and convulsing him terribly, it came out, and the boy was like a corpse; so that most of them said, "He is dead."
020927 But Jesus took him by the hand and lifted him up, and he arose.
020928 And when he had entered the house, his disciples asked him privately, "Why could we not cast it out?"
020929 And he said to them, "This kind cannot be driven out by anything but prayer."
020930 They went on from there and passed through Galilee. And he would not have any one know it;
020931 for he was teaching his disciples, saying to them, "The Son of man will be delivered into the hands of men, and they will kill him; and when he is killed, after three days he will rise."
020932 But they did not understand the saying, and they were afraid to ask him.
020933 And they came to Caper'na-um; and when he was in the house he asked them, "What were you discussing on the way?"
020934 But they were silent; for on the way they had discussed with one another who was the greatest.
020935 And he sat down and called the twelve; and he said to them, "If any one would be first, he must be last of all and servant of all."
020936 And he took a child, and put him in the midst of them; and taking him in his arms, he said to them,
020937 "Whoever receives one such child in my name receives me; and whoever receives me, receives not me but him who sent me."
020938 John said to him, "Teacher, we saw a man casting out demons in your name, and we forbade him, because he was not following us."
020939 But Jesus said, "Do not forbid him; for no one who does a mighty work in my name will be able soon after to speak evil of me.
020940 For he that is not against us is for us.
020941 For truly, I say to you, whoever gives you a cup of water to drink because you bear the name of Christ, will by no means lose his reward.
020942 "Whoever causes one of these little ones who believe in me to sin, it would be better for him if a great millstone were hung round his neck and he were thrown into the sea.
020943 And if your hand causes you to sin, cut it off; it is better for you to enter life maimed than with two hands to go to hell, to the unquenchable fire.
020944
020945 And if your foot causes you to sin, cut it off; it is better for you to enter life lame than with two feet to be thrown into hell.
020946
020947 And if your eye causes you to sin, pluck it out; it is better for you to enter the kingdom of God with one eye than with two eyes to be thrown into hell,
020948 where their worm does not die, and the fire is not quenched.
020949 For every one will be salted with fire.
020950 Salt is good; but if the salt has lost its saltness, how will you season it? Have salt in yourselves, and be at peace with one another."
021001 And he left there and went to the region of Judea and beyond the Jordan, and crowds gathered to him again; and again, as his custom was, he taught them.
021002 And Pharisees came up and in order to test him asked, "Is it lawful for a man to divorce his wife?"
021003 He answered them, "What did Moses command you?"
021004 They said, "Moses allowed a man to write a certificate of divorce, and to put her away."
021005 But Jesus said to them, "For your hardness of heart he wrote you this commandment.
021006 But from the beginning of creation, 'God made them male and female.'
021007 'For this reason a man shall leave his father and mother and be joined to his wife,
021008 and the two shall become one flesh.' So they are no longer two but one flesh.
021009 What therefore God has joined together, let not man put asunder."
021010 And in the house the disciples asked him again about this matter.
021011 And he said to them, "Whoever divorces his wife and marries another, commits adultery against her;
021012 and if she divorces her husband and marries another, she commits adultery."
021013 And they were bringing children to him, that he might touch them; and the disciples rebuked them.
021014 But when Jesus saw it he was indignant, and said to them, "Let the children come to me, do not hinder them; for to such belongs the kingdom of God.
021015 Truly, I say to you, whoever does not receive the kingdom of God like a child shall not enter it."
021016 And he took them in his arms and blessed them, laying his hands upon them.
021017 And as he was setting out on his journey, a man ran up and knelt before him, and asked him, "Good Teacher, what must I do to inherit eternal life?"
021018 And Jesus said to him, "Why do you call me good? No one is good but God alone.
021019 You know the commandments: 'Do not kill, Do not commit adultery, Do not steal, Do not bear false witness, Do not defraud, Honor your father and mother.'"
021020 And he said to him, "Teacher, all these I have observed from my youth."
021021 And Jesus looking upon him loved him, and said to him, "You lack one thing; go, sell what you have, and give to the poor, and you will have treasure in heaven; and come, follow me."
021022 At that saying his countenance fell, and he went away sorrowful; for he had great possessions.
021023 And Jesus looked around and said to his disciples, "How hard it will be for those who have riches to enter the kingdom of God!"
021024 And the disciples were amazed at his words. But Jesus said to them again, "Children, how hard it is to enter the kingdom of God!
021025 It is easier for a camel to go through the eye of a needle than for a rich man to enter the kingdom of God."
021026 And they were exceedingly astonished, and said to him, "Then who can be saved?"
021027 Jesus looked at them and said, "With men it is impossible, but not with God; for all things are possible with God."
021028 Peter began to say to him, "Lo, we have left everything and followed you."
021029 Jesus said, "Truly, I say to you, there is no one who has left house or brothers or sisters or mother or father or children or lands, for my sake and for the gospel,
021030 who will not receive a hundredfold now in this time, houses and brothers and sisters and mothers and children and lands, with persecutions, and in the age to come eternal life.
021031 But many that are first will be last, and the last first."
021032 And they were on the road, going up to Jerusalem, and Jesus was walking ahead of them; and they were amazed, and those who followed were afraid. And taking the twelve again, he began to tell them what was to happen to him,
021033 saying, "Behold, we are going up to Jerusalem; and the Son of man will be delivered to the chief priests and the scribes, and they will condemn him to death, and deliver him to the Gentiles;
021034 and they will mock him, and spit upon him, and scourge him, and kill him; and after three days he will rise."
021035 And James and John, the sons of Zeb'edee, came forward to him, and said to him, "Teacher, we want you to do for us whatever we ask of you."
021036 And he said to them, "What do you want me to do for you?"
021037 And they said to him, "Grant us to sit, one at your right hand and one at your left, in your glory."
021038 But Jesus said to them, "You do not know what you are asking. Are you able to drink the cup that I drink, or to be baptized with the baptism with which I am baptized?"
021039 And they said to him, "We are able." And Jesus said to them, "The cup that I drink you will drink; and with the baptism with which I am baptized, you will be baptized;
021040 but to sit at my right hand or at my left is not mine to grant, but it is for those for whom it has been prepared."
021041 And when the ten heard it, they began to be indignant at James and John.
021042 And Jesus called them to him and said to them, "You know that those who are supposed to rule over the Gentiles lord it over them, and their great men exercise authority over them.
021043 But it shall not be so among you; but whoever would be great among you must be your servant,
021044 and whoever would be first among you must be slave of all.
021045 For the Son of man also came not to be served but to serve, and to give his life as a ransom for many."
021046 And they came to Jericho; and as he was leaving Jericho with his disciples and a great multitude, Bartimae'us, a blind beggar, the son of Timae'us, was sitting by the roadside.
021047 And when he heard that it was Jesus of Nazareth, he began to cry out and say, "Jesus, Son of David, have mercy on me!"
021048 And many rebuked him, telling him to be silent; but he cried out all the more, "Son of David, have mercy on me!"
021049 And Jesus stopped and said, "Call him." And they called the blind man, saying to him, "Take heart; rise, he is calling you."
021050 And throwing off his mantle he sprang up and came to Jesus.
021051 And Jesus said to him, "What do you want me to do for you?" And the blind man said to him, "Master, let me receive my sight."
021052 And Jesus said to him, "Go your way; your faith has made you well." And immediately he received his sight and followed him on the way.
021101 And when they drew near to Jerusalem, to Beth'phage and Bethany, at the Mount of Olives, he sent two of his disciples,
021102 and said to them, "Go into the village opposite you, and immediately as you enter it you will find a colt tied, on which no one has ever sat; untie it and bring it.
021103 If any one says to you, 'Why are you doing this?' say, 'The Lord has need of it and will send it back here immediately.'"
021104 And they went away, and found a colt tied at the door out in the open street; and they untied it.
021105 And those who stood there said to them, "What are you doing, untying the colt?"
021106 And they told them what Jesus had said; and they let them go.
021107 And they brought the colt to Jesus, and threw their garments on it; and he sat upon it.
021108 And many spread their garments on the road, and others spread leafy branches which they had cut from the fields.
021109 And those who went before and those who followed cried out, "Hosanna! Blessed is he who comes in the name of the Lord!
021110 Blessed is the kingdom of our father David that is coming! Hosanna in the highest!"
021111 And he entered Jerusalem, and went into the temple; and when he had looked round at everything, as it was already late, he went out to Bethany with the twelve.
021112 On the following day, when they came from Bethany, he was hungry.
021113 And seeing in the distance a fig tree in leaf, he went to see if he could find anything on it. When he came to it, he found nothing but leaves, for it was not the season for figs.
021114 And he said to it, "May no one ever eat fruit from you again." And his disciples heard it.
021115 And they came to Jerusalem. And he entered the temple and began to drive out those who sold and those who bought in the temple, and he overturned the tables of the money-changers and the seats of those who sold pigeons;
021116 and he would not allow any one to carry anything through the temple.
021117 And he taught, and said to them, "Is it not written, 'My house shall be called a house of prayer for all the nations'? But you have made it a den of robbers."
021118 And the chief priests and the scribes heard it and sought a way to destroy him; for they feared him, because all the multitude was astonished at his teaching.
021119 And when evening came they went out of the city.
021120 As they passed by in the morning, they saw the fig tree withered away to its roots.
021121 And Peter remembered and said to him, "Master, look! The fig tree which you cursed has withered."
021122 And Jesus answered them, "Have faith in God.
021123 Truly, I say to you, whoever says to this mountain, 'Be taken up and cast into the sea,' and does not doubt in his heart, but believes that what he says will come to pass, it will be done for him.
021124 Therefore I tell you, whatever you ask in prayer, believe that you have received it, and it will be yours.
021125 And whenever you stand praying, forgive, if you have anything against any one; so that your Father also who is in heaven may forgive you your trespasses."
021126
021127 And they came again to Jerusalem. And as he was walking in the temple, the chief priests and the scribes and the elders came to him,
021128 and they said to him, "By what authority are you doing these things, or who gave you this authority to do them?"
021129 Jesus said to them, "I will ask you a question; answer me, and I will tell you by what authority I do these things.
021130 Was the baptism of John from heaven or from men? Answer me."
021131 And they argued with one another, "If we say, 'From heaven,' he will say, 'Why then did you not believe him?'
021132 But shall we say, 'From men'?" -- they were afraid of the people, for all held that John was a real prophet.
021133 So they answered Jesus, "We do not know." And Jesus said to them, "Neither will I tell you by what authority I do these things."
021201 And he began to speak to them in parables. "A man planted a vineyard, and set a hedge around it, and dug a pit for the wine press, and built a tower, and let it out to tenants, and went into another country.
021202 When the time came, he sent a servant to the tenants, to get from them some of the fruit of the vineyard.
021203 And they took him and beat him, and sent him away empty-handed.
021204 Again he sent to them another servant, and they wounded him in the head, and treated him shamefully.
021205 And he sent another, and him they killed; and so with many others, some they beat and some they killed.
021206 He had still one other, a beloved son; finally he sent him to them, saying, 'They will respect my son.'
021207 But those tenants said to one another, 'This is the heir; come, let us kill him, and the inheritance will be ours.'
021208 And they took him and killed him, and cast him out of the vineyard.
021209 What will the owner of the vineyard do? He will come and destroy the tenants, and give the vineyard to others.
021210 Have you not read this scripture: 'The very stone which the builders rejected has become the head of the corner;
021211 this was the Lord's doing, and it is marvelous in our eyes'?"
021212 And they tried to arrest him, but feared the multitude, for they perceived that he had told the parable against them; so they left him and went away.
021213 And they sent to him some of the Pharisees and some of the Hero'di-ans, to entrap him in his talk.
021214 And they came and said to him, "Teacher, we know that you are true, and care for no man; for you do not regard the position of men, but truly teach the way of God. Is it lawful to pay taxes to Caesar, or not?
021215 Should we pay them, or should we not?" But knowing their hypocrisy, he said to them, "Why put me to the test? Bring me a coin, and let me look at it."
021216 And they brought one. And he said to them, "Whose likeness and inscription is this?" They said to him, "Caesar's."
021217 Jesus said to them, "Render to Caesar the things that are Caesar's, and to God the things that are God's." And they were amazed at him.
021218 And Sad'ducees came to him, who say that there is no resurrection; and they asked him a question, saying,
021219 "Teacher, Moses wrote for us that if a man's brother dies and leaves a wife, but leaves no child, the man must take the wife, and raise up children for his brother.
021220 There were seven brothers; the first took a wife, and when he died left no children;
021221 and the second took her, and died, leaving no children; and the third likewise;
021222 and the seven left no children. Last of all the woman also died.
021223 In the resurrection whose wife will she be? For the seven had her as wife."
021224 Jesus said to them, "Is not this why you are wrong, that you know neither the scriptures nor the power of God?
021225 For when they rise from the dead, they neither marry nor are given in marriage, but are like angels in heaven.
021226 And as for the dead being raised, have you not read in the book of Moses, in the passage about the bush, how God said to him, 'I am the God of Abraham, and the God of Isaac, and the God of Jacob'?
021227 He is not God of the dead, but of the living; you are quite wrong."
021228 And one of the scribes came up and heard them disputing with one another, and seeing that he answered them well, asked him, "Which commandment is the first of all?"
021229 Jesus answered, "The first is, 'Hear, O Israel: The Lord our God, the Lord is one;
021230 and you shall love the Lord your God with all your heart, and with all your soul, and with all your mind, and with all your strength.'
021231 The second is this, 'You shall love your neighbor as yourself.' There is no other commandment greater than these."
021232 And the scribe said to him, "You are right, Teacher; you have truly said that he is one, and there is no other but he;
021233 and to love him with all the heart, and with all the understanding, and with all the strength, and to love one's neighbor as oneself, is much more than all whole burnt offerings and sacrifices."
021234 And when Jesus saw that he answered wisely, he said to him, "You are not far from the kingdom of God." And after that no one dared to ask him any question.
021235 And as Jesus taught in the temple, he said, "How can the scribes say that the Christ is the son of David?
021236 David himself, inspired by the Holy Spirit, declared, 'The Lord said to my Lord, Sit at my right hand, till I put thy enemies under thy feet.'
021237 David himself calls him Lord; so how is he his son?" And the great throng heard him gladly.
021238 And in his teaching he said, "Beware of the scribes, who like to go about in long robes, and to have salutations in the market places
021239 and the best seats in the synagogues and the places of honor at feasts,
021240 who devour widows' houses and for a pretense make long prayers. They will receive the greater condemnation."
021241 And he sat down opposite the treasury, and watched the multitude putting money into the treasury. Many rich people put in large sums.
021242 And a poor widow came, and put in two copper coins, which make a penny.
021243 And he called his disciples to him, and said to them, "Truly, I say to you, this poor widow has put in more than all those who are contributing to the treasury.
021244 For they all contributed out of their abundance; but she out of her poverty has put in everything she had, her whole living."
021301 And as he came out of the temple, one of his disciples said to him, "Look, Teacher, what wonderful stones and what wonderful buildings!"
021302 And Jesus said to him, "Do you see these great buildings? There will not be left here one stone upon another, that will not be thrown down."
021303 And as he sat on the Mount of Olives opposite the temple, Peter and James and John and Andrew asked him privately,
021304 "Tell us, when will this be, and what will be the sign when these things are all to be accomplished?"
021305 And Jesus began to say to them, "Take heed that no one leads you astray.
021306 Many will come in my name, saying, 'I am he!' and they will lead many astray.
021307 And when you hear of wars and rumors of wars, do not be alarmed; this must take place, but the end is not yet.
021308 For nation will rise against nation, and kingdom against kingdom; there will be earthquakes in various places, there will be famines; this is but the beginning of the birth-pangs.
021309 "But take heed to yourselves; for they will deliver you up to councils; and you will be beaten in synagogues; and you will stand before governors and kings for my sake, to bear testimony before them.
021310 And the gospel must first be preached to all nations.
021311 And when they bring you to trial and deliver you up, do not be anxious beforehand what you are to say; but say whatever is given you in that hour, for it is not you who speak, but the Holy Spirit.
021312 And brother will deliver up brother to death, and the father his child, and children will rise against parents and have them put to death;
021313 and you will be hated by all for my name's sake. But he who endures to the end will be saved.
021314 "But when you see the desolating sacrilege set up where it ought not to be (let the reader understand), then let those who are in Judea flee to the mountains;
021315 let him who is on the housetop not go down, nor enter his house, to take anything away;
021316 and let him who is in the field not turn back to take his mantle.
021317 And alas for those who are with child and for those who give suck in those days!
021318 Pray that it may not happen in winter.
021319 For in those days there will be such tribulation as has not been from the beginning of the creation which God created until now, and never will be.
021320 And if the Lord had not shortened the days, no human being would be saved; but for the sake of the elect, whom he chose, he shortened the days.
021321 And then if any one says to you, 'Look, here is the Christ!' or 'Look, there he is!' do not believe it.
021322 False Christs and false prophets will arise and show signs and wonders, to lead astray, if possible, the elect.
021323 But take heed; I have told you all things beforehand.
021324 "But in those days, after that tribulation, the sun will be darkened, and the moon will not give its light,
021325 and the stars will be falling from heaven, and the powers in the heavens will be shaken.
021326 And then they will see the Son of man coming in clouds with great power and glory.
021327 And then he will send out the angels, and gather his elect from the four winds, from the ends of the earth to the ends of heaven.
021328 "From the fig tree learn its lesson: as soon as its branch becomes tender and puts forth its leaves, you know that summer is near.
021329 So also, when you see these things taking place, you know that he is near, at the very gates.
021330 Truly, I say to you, this generation will not pass away before all these things take place.
021331 Heaven and earth will pass away, but my words will not pass away.
021332 "But of that day or that hour no one knows, not even the angels in heaven, nor the Son, but only the Father.
021333 Take heed, watch; for you do not know when the time will come.
021334 It is like a man going on a journey, when he leaves home and puts his servants in charge, each with his work, and commands the doorkeeper to be on the watch.
021335 Watch therefore -- for you do not know when the master of the house will come, in the evening, or at midnight, or at cockcrow, or in the morning --
021336 lest he come suddenly and find you asleep.
021337 And what I say to you I say to all: Watch."
021401 It was now two days before the Passover and the feast of Unleavened Bread. And the chief priests and the scribes were seeking how to arrest him by stealth, and kill him;
021402 for they said, "Not during the feast, lest there be a tumult of the people."
021403 And while he was at Bethany in the house of Simon the leper, as he sat at table, a woman came with an alabaster flask of ointment of pure nard, very costly, and she broke the flask and poured it over his head.
021404 But there were some who said to themselves indignantly, "Why was the ointment thus wasted?
021405 For this ointment might have been sold for more than three hundred denarii, and given to the poor." And they reproached her.
021406 But Jesus said, "Let her alone; why do you trouble her? She has done a beautiful thing to me.
021407 For you always have the poor with you, and whenever you will, you can do good to them; but you will not always have me.
021408 She has done what she could; she has anointed my body beforehand for burying.
021409 And truly, I say to you, wherever the gospel is preached in the whole world, what she has done will be told in memory of her."
021410 Then Judas Iscariot, who was one of the twelve, went to the chief priests in order to betray him to them.
021411 And when they heard it they were glad, and promised to give him money. And he sought an opportunity to betray him.
021412 And on the first day of Unleavened Bread, when they sacrificed the passover lamb, his disciples said to him, "Where will you have us go and prepare for you to eat the passover?"
021413 And he sent two of his disciples, and said to them, "Go into the city, and a man carrying a jar of water will meet you; follow him,
021414 and wherever he enters, say to the householder, 'The Teacher says, Where is my guest room, where I am to eat the passover with my disciples?'
021415 And he will show you a large upper room furnished and ready; there prepare for us."
021416 And the disciples set out and went to the city, and found it as he had told them; and they prepared the passover.
021417 And when it was evening he came with the twelve.
021418 And as they were at table eating, Jesus said, "Truly, I say to you, one of you will betray me, one who is eating with me."
021419 They began to be sorrowful, and to say to him one after another, "Is it I?"
021420 He said to them, "It is one of the twelve, one who is dipping bread into the dish with me.
021421 For the Son of man goes as it is written of him, but woe to that man by whom the Son of man is betrayed! It would have been better for that man if he had not been born."
021422 And as they were eating, he took bread, and blessed, and broke it, and gave it to them, and said, "Take; this is my body."
021423 And he took a cup, and when he had given thanks he gave it to them, and they all drank of it.
021424 And he said to them, "This is my blood of the covenant, which is poured out for many.
021425 Truly, I say to you, I shall not drink again of the fruit of the vine until that day when I drink it new in the kingdom of God."
021426 And when they had sung a hymn, they went out to the Mount of Olives.
021427 And Jesus said to them, "You will all fall away; for it is written, 'I will strike the shepherd, and the sheep will be scattered.'
021428 But after I am raised up, I will go before you to Galilee."
021429 Peter said to him, "Even though they all fall away, I will not."
021430 And Jesus said to him, "Truly, I say to you, this very night, before the cock crows twice, you will deny me three times."
021431 But he said vehemently, "If I must die with you, I will not deny you." And they all said the same.
021432 And they went to a place which was called Gethsem'ane; and he said to his disciples, "Sit here, while I pray."
021433 And he took with him Peter and James and John, and began to be greatly distressed and troubled.
021434 And he said to them, "My soul is very sorrowful, even to death; remain here, and watch."
021435 And going a little farther, he fell on the ground and prayed that, if it were possible, the hour might pass from him.
021436 And he said, "Abba, Father, all things are possible to thee; remove this cup from me; yet not what I will, but what thou wilt."
021437 And he came and found them sleeping, and he said to Peter, "Simon, are you asleep? Could you not watch one hour?
021438 Watch and pray that you may not enter into temptation; the spirit indeed is willing, but the flesh is weak."
021439 And again he went away and prayed, saying the same words.
021440 And again he came and found them sleeping, for their eyes were very heavy; and they did not know what to answer him.
021441 And he came the third time, and said to them, "Are you still sleeping and taking your rest? It is enough; the hour has come; the Son of man is betrayed into the hands of sinners.
021442 Rise, let us be going; see, my betrayer is at hand."
021443 And immediately, while he was still speaking, Judas came, one of the twelve, and with him a crowd with swords and clubs, from the chief priests and the scribes and the elders.
021444 Now the betrayer had given them a sign, saying, "The one I shall kiss is the man; seize him and lead him away under guard."
021445 And when he came, he went up to him at once, and said, "Master!" And he kissed him.
021446 And they laid hands on him and seized him.
021447 But one of those who stood by drew his sword, and struck the slave of the high priest and cut off his ear.
021448 And Jesus said to them, "Have you come out as against a robber, with swords and clubs to capture me?
021449 Day after day I was with you in the temple teaching, and you did not seize me. But let the scriptures be fulfilled."
021450 And they all forsook him, and fled.
021451 And a young man followed him, with nothing but a linen cloth about his body; and they seized him,
021452 but he left the linen cloth and ran away naked.
021453 And they led Jesus to the high priest; and all the chief priests and the elders and the scribes were assembled.
021454 And Peter had followed him at a distance, right into the courtyard of the high priest; and he was sitting with the guards, and warming himself at the fire.
021455 Now the chief priests and the whole council sought testimony against Jesus to put him to death; but they found none.
021456 For many bore false witness against him, and their witness did not agree.
021457 And some stood up and bore false witness against him, saying,
021458 "We heard him say, 'I will destroy this temple that is made with hands, and in three days I will build another, not made with hands.'"
021459 Yet not even so did their testimony agree.
021460 And the high priest stood up in the midst, and asked Jesus, "Have you no answer to make? What is it that these men testify against you?"
021461 But he was silent and made no answer. Again the high priest asked him, "Are you the Christ, the Son of the Blessed?"
021462 And Jesus said, "I am; and you will see the Son of man seated at the right hand of Power, and coming with the clouds of heaven."
021463 And the high priest tore his garments, and said, "Why do we still need witnesses?
021464 You have heard his blasphemy. What is your decision?" And they all condemned him as deserving death.
021465 And some began to spit on him, and to cover his face, and to strike him, saying to him, "Prophesy!" And the guards received him with blows.
021466 And as Peter was below in the courtyard, one of the maids of the high priest came;
021467 and seeing Peter warming himself, she looked at him, and said, "You also were with the Nazarene, Jesus."
021468 But he denied it, saying, "I neither know nor understand what you mean." And he went out into the gateway.
021469 And the maid saw him, and began again to say to the bystanders, "This man is one of them."
021470 But again he denied it. And after a little while again the bystanders said to Peter, "Certainly you are one of them; for you are a Galilean."
021471 But he began to invoke a curse on himself and to swear, "I do not know this man of whom you speak."
021472 And immediately the cock crowed a second time. And Peter remembered how Jesus had said to him, "Before the cock crows twice, you will deny me three times." And he broke down and wept.
021501 And as soon as it was morning the chief priests, with the elders and scribes, and the whole council held a consultation; and they bound Jesus and led him away and delivered him to Pilate.
021502 And Pilate asked him, "Are you the King of the Jews?" And he answered him, "You have said so."
021503 And the chief priests accused him of many things.
021504 And Pilate again asked him, "Have you no answer to make? See how many charges they bring against you."
021505 But Jesus made no further answer, so that Pilate wondered.
021506 Now at the feast he used to release for them one prisoner for whom they asked.
021507 And among the rebels in prison, who had committed murder in the insurrection, there was a man called Barab'bas.
021508 And the crowd came up and began to ask Pilate to do as he was wont to do for them.
021509 And he answered them, "Do you want me to release for you the King of the Jews?"
021510 For he perceived that it was out of envy that the chief priests had delivered him up.
021511 But the chief priests stirred up the crowd to have him release for them Barab'bas instead.
021512 And Pilate again said to them, "Then what shall I do with the man whom you call the King of the Jews?"
021513 And they cried out again, "Crucify him."
021514 And Pilate said to them, "Why, what evil has he done?" But they shouted all the more, "Crucify him."
021515 So Pilate, wishing to satisfy the crowd, released for them Barab'bas; and having scourged Jesus, he delivered him to be crucified.
021516 And the soldiers led him away inside the palace (that is, the praetorium); and they called together the whole battalion.
021517 And they clothed him in a purple cloak, and plaiting a crown of thorns they put it on him.
021518 And they began to salute him, "Hail, King of the Jews!"
021519 And they struck his head with a reed, and spat upon him, and they knelt down in homage to him.
021520 And when they had mocked him, they stripped him of the purple cloak, and put his own clothes on him. And they led him out to crucify him.
021521 And they compelled a passer-by, Simon of Cyre'ne, who was coming in from the country, the father of Alexander and Rufus, to carry his cross.
021522 And they brought him to the place called Gol'gotha (which means the place of a skull).
021523 And they offered him wine mingled with myrrh; but he did not take it.
021524 And they crucified him, and divided his garments among them, casting lots for them, to decide what each should take.
021525 And it was the third hour, when they crucified him.
021526 And the inscription of the charge against him read, "The King of the Jews."
021527 And with him they crucified two robbers, one on his right and one on his left.
021528
021529 And those who passed by derided him, wagging their heads, and saying, "Aha! You who would destroy the temple and build it in three days,
021530 save yourself, and come down from the cross!"
021531 So also the chief priests mocked him to one another with the scribes, saying, "He saved others; he cannot save himself.
021532 Let the Christ, the King of Israel, come down now from the cross, that we may see and believe." Those who were crucified with him also reviled him.
021533 And when the sixth hour had come, there was darkness over the whole land until the ninth hour.
021534 And at the ninth hour Jesus cried with a loud voice, "E'lo-i, E'lo-i, la'ma sabach-tha'ni?" which means, "My God, my God, why hast thou forsaken me?"
021535 And some of the bystanders hearing it said, "Behold, he is calling Eli'jah."
021536 And one ran and, filling a sponge full of vinegar, put it on a reed and gave it to him to drink, saying, "Wait, let us see whether Eli'jah will come to take him down."
021537 And Jesus uttered a loud cry, and breathed his last.
021538 And the curtain of the temple was torn in two, from top to bottom.
021539 And when the centurion, who stood facing him, saw that he thus breathed his last, he said, "Truly this man was the Son of God!"
021540 There were also women looking on from afar, among whom were Mary Mag'dalene, and Mary the mother of James the younger and of Joses, and Salo'me,
021541 who, when he was in Galilee, followed him, and ministered to him; and also many other women who came up with him to Jerusalem.
021542 And when evening had come, since it was the day of Preparation, that is, the day before the sabbath,
021543 Joseph of Arimathe'a, a respected member of the council, who was also himself looking for the kingdom of God, took courage and went to Pilate, and asked for the body of Jesus.
021544 And Pilate wondered if he were already dead; and summoning the centurion, he asked him whether he was already dead.
021545 And when he learned from the centurion that he was dead, he granted the body to Joseph.
021546 And he bought a linen shroud, and taking him down, wrapped him in the linen shroud, and laid him in a tomb which had been hewn out of the rock; and he rolled a stone against the door of the tomb.
021547 Mary Mag'dalene and Mary the mother of Joses saw where he was laid.
021601 And when the sabbath was past, Mary Mag'dalene, and Mary the mother of James, and Salo'me, bought spices, so that they might go and anoint him.
021602 And very early on the first day of the week they went to the tomb when the sun had risen.
021603 And they were saying to one another, "Who will roll away the stone for us from the door of the tomb?"
021604 And looking up, they saw that the stone was rolled back; -- it was very large.
021605 And entering the tomb, they saw a young man sitting on the right side, dressed in a white robe; and they were amazed.
021606 And he said to them, "Do not be amazed; you seek Jesus of Nazareth, who was crucified. He has risen, he is not here; see the place where they laid him.
021607 But go, tell his disciples and Peter that he is going before you to Galilee; there you will see him, as he told you."
021608 And they went out and fled from the tomb; for trembling and astonishment had come upon them; and they said nothing to any one, for they were afraid.
021609 Now when he rose early on the first day of the week, he appeared first to Mary Magdalene, from whom he had cast out seven demons.
021610 She went and told those who had been with him, as they mourned and wept.
021611 But when they heard that he was alive and had been seen by her, they would not believe it.
021612 After this he appeared in another form to two of them, as they were walking into the country.
021613 And they went back and told the rest, but they did not believe them.
021614 Afterward he appeared to the eleven themselves as they sat at table; and he upbraided them for their unbelief and hardness of heart, because they had not believed those who saw him after he had risen.
021615 And he said to them, "Go into all the world and preach the gospel to the whole creation.
021616 He who believes and is baptized will be saved; but he who does not believe will be condemned.
021617 And these signs will accompany those who believe: in my name they will cast out demons; they will speak in new tongues;
021618 they will pick up serpents, and if they drink any deadly thing, it will not hurt them; they will lay their hands on the sick, and they will recover."
021619 So then the Lord Jesus, after he had spoken to them, was taken up into heaven, and sat down at the right hand of God.
021620 And they went forth and preached everywhere, while the Lord worked with them and confirmed the message by the signs that attended it. Amen.
030101 Inasmuch as many have undertaken to compile a narrative of the things which have been accomplished among us,
030102 just as they were delivered to us by those who from the beginning were eyewitnesses and ministers of the word,
030103 it seemed good to me also, having followed all things closely for some time past, to write an orderly account for you, most excellent The-oph'ilus,
030104 that you may know the truth concerning the things of which you have been informed.
030105 In the days of Herod, king of Judea, there was a priest named Zechari'ah, of the division of Abi'jah; and he had a wife of the daughters of Aaron, and her name was Elizabeth.
030106 And they were both righteous before God, walking in all the commandments and ordinances of the Lord blameless.
030107 But they had no child, because Elizabeth was barren, and both were advanced in years.
030108 Now while he was serving as priest before God when his division was on duty,
030109 according to the custom of the priesthood, it fell to him by lot to enter the temple of the Lord and burn incense.
030110 And the whole multitude of the people were praying outside at the hour of incense.
030111 And there appeared to him an angel of the Lord standing on the right side of the altar of incense.
030112 And Zechari'ah was troubled when he saw him, and fear fell upon him.
030113 But the angel said to him, "Do not be afraid, Zechari'ah, for your prayer is heard, and your wife Elizabeth will bear you a son, and you shall call his name John.
030114 And you will have joy and gladness, and many will rejoice at his birth;
030115 for he will be great before the Lord, and he shall drink no wine nor strong drink, and he will be filled with the Holy Spirit, even from his mother's womb.
030116 And he will turn many of the sons of Israel to the Lord their God,
030117 and he will go before him in the spirit and power of Eli'jah, to turn the hearts of the fathers to the children, and the disobedient to the wisdom of the just, to make ready for the Lord a people prepared."
030118 And Zechari'ah said to the angel, "How shall I know this? For I am an old man, and my wife is advanced in years."
030119 And the angel answered him, "I am Gabriel, who stand in the presence of God; and I was sent to speak to you, and to bring you this good news.
030120 And behold, you will be silent and unable to speak until the day that these things come to pass, because you did not believe my words, which will be fulfilled in their time."
030121 And the people were waiting for Zechari'ah, and they wondered at his delay in the temple.
030122 And when he came out, he could not speak to them, and they perceived that he had seen a vision in the temple; and he made signs to them and remained dumb.
030123 And when his time of service was ended, he went to his home.
030124 After these days his wife Elizabeth conceived, and for five months she hid herself, saying,
030125 "Thus the Lord has done to me in the days when he looked on me, to take away my reproach among men."
030126 In the sixth month the angel Gabriel was sent from God to a city of Galilee named Nazareth,
030127 to a virgin betrothed to a man whose name was Joseph, of the house of David; and the virgin's name was Mary.
030128 And he came to her and said, "Hail, O favored one, the Lord is with you!"
030129 But she was greatly troubled at the saying, and considered in her mind what sort of greeting this might be.
030130 And the angel said to her, "Do not be afraid, Mary, for you have found favor with God.
030131 And behold, you will conceive in your womb and bear a son, and you shall call his name Jesus.
030132 He will be great, and will be called the Son of the Most High; and the Lord God will give to him the throne of his father David,
030133 and he will reign over the house of Jacob for ever; and of his kingdom there will be no end."
030134 And Mary said to the angel, "How shall this be, since I have no husband?"
030135 And the angel said to her, "The Holy Spirit will come upon you, and the power of the Most High will overshadow you; therefore the child to be born will be called holy, the Son of God.
030136 And behold, your kinswoman Elizabeth in her old age has also conceived a son; and this is the sixth month with her who was called barren.
030137 For with God nothing will be impossible."
030138 And Mary said, "Behold, I am the handmaid of the Lord; let it be to me according to your word." And the angel departed from her.
030139 In those days Mary arose and went with haste into the hill country, to a city of Judah,
030140 and she entered the house of Zechari'ah and greeted Elizabeth.
030141 And when Elizabeth heard the greeting of Mary, the babe leaped in her womb; and Elizabeth was filled with the Holy Spirit
030142 and she exclaimed with a loud cry, "Blessed are you among women, and blessed is the fruit of your womb!
030143 And why is this granted me, that the mother of my Lord should come to me?
030144 For behold, when the voice of your greeting came to my ears, the babe in my womb leaped for joy.
030145 And blessed is she who believed that there would be a fulfilment of what was spoken to her from the Lord."
030146 And Mary said, "My soul magnifies the Lord,
030147 and my spirit rejoices in God my Savior,
030148 for he has regarded the low estate of his handmaiden. For behold, henceforth all generations will call me blessed;
030149 for he who is mighty has done great things for me, and holy is his name.
030150 And his mercy is on those who fear him from generation to generation.
030151 He has shown strength with his arm, he has scattered the proud in the imagination of their hearts,
030152 he has put down the mighty from their thrones, and exalted those of low degree;
030153 he has filled the hungry with good things, and the rich he has sent empty away.
030154 He has helped his servant Israel, in remembrance of his mercy,
030155 as he spoke to our fathers, to Abraham and to his posterity for ever."
030156 And Mary remained with her about three months, and returned to her home.
030157 Now the time came for Elizabeth to be delivered, and she gave birth to a son.
030158 And her neighbors and kinsfolk heard that the Lord had shown great mercy to her, and they rejoiced with her.
030159 And on the eighth day they came to circumcise the child; and they would have named him Zechari'ah after his father,
030160 but his mother said, "Not so; he shall be called John."
030161 And they said to her, "None of your kindred is called by this name."
030162 And they made signs to his father, inquiring what he would have him called.
030163 And he asked for a writing tablet, and wrote, "His name is John." And they all marveled.
030164 And immediately his mouth was opened and his tongue loosed, and he spoke, blessing God.
030165 And fear came on all their neighbors. And all these things were talked about through all the hill country of Judea;
030166 and all who heard them laid them up in their hearts, saying, "What then will this child be?" For the hand of the Lord was with him.
030167 And his father Zechari'ah was filled with the Holy Spirit, and prophesied, saying,
030168 "Blessed be the Lord God of Israel, for he has visited and redeemed his people,
030169 and has raised up a horn of salvation for us in the house of his servant David,
030170 as he spoke by the mouth of his holy prophets from of old,
030171 that we should be saved from our enemies, and from the hand of all who hate us;
030172 to perform the mercy promised to our fathers, and to remember his holy covenant,
030173 the oath which he swore to our father Abraham,
030174 to grant us that we, being delivered from the hand of our enemies, might serve him without fear,
030175 in holiness and righteousness before him all the days of our life.
030176 And you, child, will be called the prophet of the Most High; for you will go before the Lord to prepare his ways,
030177 to give knowledge of salvation to his people in the forgiveness of their sins,
030178 through the tender mercy of our God, when the day shall dawn upon us from on high
030179 to give light to those who sit in darkness and in the shadow of death, to guide our feet into the way of peace."
030180 And the child grew and became strong in spirit, and he was in the wilderness till the day of his manifestation to Israel.
030201 In those days a decree went out from Caesar Augustus that all the world should be enrolled.
030202 This was the first enrollment, when Quirin'i-us was governor of Syria.
030203 And all went to be enrolled, each to his own city.
030204 And Joseph also went up from Galilee, from the city of Nazareth, to Judea, to the city of David, which is called Bethlehem, because he was of the house and lineage of David,
030205 to be enrolled with Mary, his betrothed, who was with child.
030206 And while they were there, the time came for her to be delivered.
030207 And she gave birth to her first-born son and wrapped him in swaddling cloths, and laid him in a manger, because there was no place for them in the inn.
030208 And in that region there were shepherds out in the field, keeping watch over their flock by night.
030209 And an angel of the Lord appeared to them, and the glory of the Lord shone around them, and they were filled with fear.
030210 And the angel said to them, "Be not afraid; for behold, I bring you good news of a great joy which will come to all the people;
030211 for to you is born this day in the city of David a Savior, who is Christ the Lord.
030212 And this will be a sign for you: you will find a babe wrapped in swaddling cloths and lying in a manger."
030213 And suddenly there was with the angel a multitude of the heavenly host praising God and saying,
030214 "Glory to God in the highest, and on earth peace among men with whom he is pleased!"
030215 When the angels went away from them into heaven, the shepherds said to one another, "Let us go over to Bethlehem and see this thing that has happened, which the Lord has made known to us."
030216 And they went with haste, and found Mary and Joseph, and the babe lying in a manger.
030217 And when they saw it they made known the saying which had been told them concerning this child;
030218 and all who heard it wondered at what the shepherds told them.
030219 But Mary kept all these things, pondering them in her heart.
030220 And the shepherds returned, glorifying and praising God for all they had heard and seen, as it had been told them.
030221 And at the end of eight days, when he was circumcised, he was called Jesus, the name given by the angel before he was conceived in the womb.
030222 And when the time came for their purification according to the law of Moses, they brought him up to Jerusalem to present him to the Lord
030223 (as it is written in the law of the Lord, "Every male that opens the womb shall be called holy to the Lord")
030224 and to offer a sacrifice according to what is said in the law of the Lord, "a pair of turtledoves, or two young pigeons."
030225 Now there was a man in Jerusalem, whose name was Simeon, and this man was righteous and devout, looking for the consolation of Israel, and the Holy Spirit was upon him.
030226 And it had been revealed to him by the Holy Spirit that he should not see death before he had seen the Lord's Christ.
030227 And inspired by the Spirit he came into the temple; and when the parents brought in the child Jesus, to do for him according to the custom of the law,
030228 he took him up in his arms and blessed God and said,
030229 "Lord, now lettest thou thy servant depart in peace, according to thy word;
030230 for mine eyes have seen thy salvation
030231 which thou hast prepared in the presence of all peoples,
030232 a light for revelation to the Gentiles, and for glory to thy people Israel."
030233 And his father and his mother marveled at what was said about him;
030234 and Simeon blessed them and said to Mary his mother, "Behold, this child is set for the fall and rising of many in Israel, and for a sign that is spoken against
030235 (and a sword will pierce through your own soul also), that thoughts out of many hearts may be revealed."
030236 And there was a prophetess, Anna, the daughter of Phan'u-el, of the tribe of Asher; she was of a great age, having lived with her husband seven years from her virginity,
030237 and as a widow till she was eighty-four. She did not depart from the temple, worshiping with fasting and prayer night and day.
030238 And coming up at that very hour she gave thanks to God, and spoke of him to all who were looking for the redemption of Jerusalem.
030239 And when they had performed everything according to the law of the Lord, they returned into Galilee, to their own city, Nazareth.
030240 And the child grew and became strong, filled with wisdom; and the favor of God was upon him.
030241 Now his parents went to Jerusalem every year at the feast of the Passover.
030242 And when he was twelve years old, they went up according to custom;
030243 and when the feast was ended, as they were returning, the boy Jesus stayed behind in Jerusalem. His parents did not know it,
030244 but supposing him to be in the company they went a day's journey, and they sought him among their kinsfolk and acquaintances;
030245 and when they did not find him, they returned to Jerusalem, seeking him.
030246 After three days they found him in the temple, sitting among the teachers, listening to them and asking them questions;
030247 and all who heard him were amazed at his understanding and his answers.
030248 And when they saw him they were astonished; and his mother said to him, "Son, why have you treated us so? Behold, your father and I have been looking for you anxiously."
030249 And he said to them, "How is it that you sought me? Did you not know that I must be in my Father's house?"
030250 And they did not understand the saying which he spoke to them.
030251 And he went down with them and came to Nazareth, and was obedient to them; and his mother kept all these things in her heart.
030252 And Jesus increased in wisdom and in stature, and in favor with God and man.
030301 In the fifteenth year of the reign of Tiber'i-us Caesar, Pontius Pilate being governor of Judea, and Herod being tetrarch of Galilee, and his brother Philip tetrarch of the region of Iturae'a and Trachoni'tis, and Lysa'ni-as tetrarch of Abile'ne,
030302 in the high-priesthood of Annas and Ca'iaphas, the word of God came to John the son of Zechari'ah in the wilderness;
030303 and he went into all the region about the Jordan, preaching a baptism of repentance for the forgiveness of sins.
030304 As it is written in the book of the words of Isaiah the prophet, "The voice of one crying in the wilderness: Prepare the way of the Lord, make his paths straight.
030305 Every valley shall be filled, and every mountain and hill shall be brought low, and the crooked shall be made straight, and the rough ways shall be made smooth;
030306 and all flesh shall see the salvation of God."
030307 He said therefore to the multitudes that came out to be baptized by him, "You brood of vipers! Who warned you to flee from the wrath to come?
030308 Bear fruits that befit repentance, and do not begin to say to yourselves, 'We have Abraham as our father'; for I tell you, God is able from these stones to raise up children to Abraham.
030309 Even now the axe is laid to the root of the trees; every tree therefore that does not bear good fruit is cut down and thrown into the fire."
030310 And the multitudes asked him, "What then shall we do?"
030311 And he answered them, "He who has two coats, let him share with him who has none; and he who has food, let him do likewise."
030312 Tax collectors also came to be baptized, and said to him, "Teacher, what shall we do?"
030313 And he said to them, "Collect no more than is appointed you."
030314 Soldiers also asked him, "And we, what shall we do?" And he said to them, "Rob no one by violence or by false accusation, and be content with your wages."
030315 As the people were in expectation, and all men questioned in their hearts concerning John, whether perhaps he were the Christ,
030316 John answered them all, "I baptize you with water; but he who is mightier than I is coming, the thong of whose sandals I am not worthy to untie; he will baptize you with the Holy Spirit and with fire.
030317 His winnowing fork is in his hand, to clear his threshing floor, and to gather the wheat into his granary, but the chaff he will burn with unquenchable fire."
030318 So, with many other exhortations, he preached good news to the people.
030319 But Herod the tetrarch, who had been reproved by him for Hero'di-as, his brother's wife, and for all the evil things that Herod had done,
030320 added this to them all, that he shut up John in prison.
030321 Now when all the people were baptized, and when Jesus also had been baptized and was praying, the heaven was opened,
030322 and the Holy Spirit descended upon him in bodily form, as a dove, and a voice came from heaven, "Thou art my beloved Son; with thee I am well pleased."
030323 Jesus, when he began his ministry, was about thirty years of age, being the son (as was supposed) of Joseph, the son of Heli,
030324 the son of Matthat, the son of Levi, the son of Melchi, the son of Jan'na-i, the son of Joseph,
030325 the son of Mattathi'as, the son of Amos, the son of Nahum, the son of Esli, the son of Nag'ga-i,
030326 the son of Ma'ath, the son of Mattathi'as, the son of Sem'e-in, the son of Josech, the son of Joda,
030327 the son of Jo-an'an, the son of Rhesa, the son of Zerub'babel, the son of She-al'ti-el, the son of Neri,
030328 the son of Melchi, the son of Addi, the son of Cosam, the son of Elma'dam, the son of Er,
030329 the son of Joshua, the son of Elie'zer, the son of Jorim, the son of Matthat, the son of Levi,
030330 the son of Simeon, the son of Judah, the son of Joseph, the son of Jonam, the son of Eli'akim,
030331 the son of Me'le-a, the son of Menna, the son of Mat'tatha, the son of Nathan, the son of David,
030332 the son of Jesse, the son of Obed, the son of Bo'az, the son of Sala, the son of Nahshon,
030333 the son of Ammin'adab, the son of Admin, the son of Arni, the son of Hezron, the son of Perez, the son of Judah,
030334 the son of Jacob, the son of Isaac, the son of Abraham, the son of Terah, the son of Nahor,
030335 the son of Serug, the son of Re'u, the son of Peleg, the son of Eber, the son of Shelah,
030336 the son of Ca-i'nan, the son of Arphax'ad, the son of Shem, the son of Noah, the son of Lamech,
030337 the son of Methuselah, the son of Enoch, the son of Jared, the son of Maha'lale-el, the son of Ca-i'nan,
030338 the son of Enos, the son of Seth, the son of Adam, the son of God.
030401 And Jesus, full of the Holy Spirit, returned from the Jordan, and was led by the Spirit
030402 for forty days in the wilderness, tempted by the devil. And he ate nothing in those days; and when they were ended, he was hungry.
030403 The devil said to him, "If you are the Son of God, command this stone to become bread."
030404 And Jesus answered him, "It is written, 'Man shall not live by bread alone.'"
030405 And the devil took him up, and showed him all the kingdoms of the world in a moment of time,
030406 and said to him, "To you I will give all this authority and their glory; for it has been delivered to me, and I give it to whom I will.
030407 If you, then, will worship me, it shall all be yours."
030408 And Jesus answered him, "It is written, 'You shall worship the Lord your God, and him only shall you serve.'"
030409 And he took him to Jerusalem, and set him on the pinnacle of the temple, and said to him, "If you are the Son of God, throw yourself down from here;
030410 for it is written, 'He will give his angels charge of you, to guard you,'
030411 and 'On their hands they will bear you up, lest you strike your foot against a stone.'"
030412 And Jesus answered him, "It is said, 'You shall not tempt the Lord your God.'"
030413 And when the devil had ended every temptation, he departed from him until an opportune time.
030414 And Jesus returned in the power of the Spirit into Galilee, and a report concerning him went out through all the surrounding country.
030415 And he taught in their synagogues, being glorified by all.
030416 And he came to Nazareth, where he had been brought up; and he went to the synagogue, as his custom was, on the sabbath day. And he stood up to read;
030417 and there was given to him the book of the prophet Isaiah. He opened the book and found the place where it was written,
030418 "The Spirit of the Lord is upon me, because he has anointed me to preach good news to the poor. He has sent me to proclaim release to the captives and recovering of sight to the blind, to set at liberty those who are oppressed,
030419 to proclaim the acceptable year of the Lord."
030420 And he closed the book, and gave it back to the attendant, and sat down; and the eyes of all in the synagogue were fixed on him.
030421 And he began to say to them, "Today this scripture has been fulfilled in your hearing."
030422 And all spoke well of him, and wondered at the gracious words which proceeded out of his mouth; and they said, "Is not this Joseph's son?"
030423 And he said to them, "Doubtless you will quote to me this proverb, 'Physician, heal yourself; what we have heard you did at Caper'na-um, do here also in your own country.'"
030424 And he said, "Truly, I say to you, no prophet is acceptable in his own country.
030425 But in truth, I tell you, there were many widows in Israel in the days of Eli'jah, when the heaven was shut up three years and six months, when there came a great famine over all the land;
030426 and Eli'jah was sent to none of them but only to Zar'ephath, in the land of Sidon, to a woman who was a widow.
030427 And there were many lepers in Israel in the time of the prophet Eli'sha; and none of them was cleansed, but only Na'aman the Syrian."
030428 When they heard this, all in the synagogue were filled with wrath.
030429 And they rose up and put him out of the city, and led him to the brow of the hill on which their city was built, that they might throw him down headlong.
030430 But passing through the midst of them he went away.
030431 And he went down to Caper'na-um, a city of Galilee. And he was teaching them on the sabbath;
030432 and they were astonished at his teaching, for his word was with authority.
030433 And in the synagogue there was a man who had the spirit of an unclean demon; and he cried out with a loud voice,
030434 "Ah! What have you to do with us, Jesus of Nazareth? Have you come to destroy us? I know who you are, the Holy One of God."
030435 But Jesus rebuked him, saying, "Be silent, and come out of him!" And when the demon had thrown him down in the midst, he came out of him, having done him no harm.
030436 And they were all amazed and said to one another, "What is this word? For with authority and power he commands the unclean spirits, and they come out."
030437 And reports of him went out into every place in the surrounding region.
030438 And he arose and left the synagogue, and entered Simon's house. Now Simon's mother-in-law was ill with a high fever, and they besought him for her.
030439 And he stood over her and rebuked the fever, and it left her; and immediately she rose and served them.
030440 Now when the sun was setting, all those who had any that were sick with various diseases brought them to him; and he laid his hands on every one of them and healed them.
030441 And demons also came out of many, crying, "You are the Son of God!" But he rebuked them, and would not allow them to speak, because they knew that he was the Christ.
030442 And when it was day he departed and went into a lonely place. And the people sought him and came to him, and would have kept him from leaving them;
030443 but he said to them, "I must preach the good news of the kingdom of God to the other cities also; for I was sent for this purpose."
030444 And he was preaching in the synagogues of Judea.
030501 While the people pressed upon him to hear the word of God, he was standing by the lake of Gennes'aret.
030502 And he saw two boats by the lake; but the fishermen had gone out of them and were washing their nets.
030503 Getting into one of the boats, which was Simon's, he asked him to put out a little from the land. And he sat down and taught the people from the boat.
030504 And when he had ceased speaking, he said to Simon, "Put out into the deep and let down your nets for a catch."
030505 And Simon answered, "Master, we toiled all night and took nothing! But at your word I will let down the nets."
030506 And when they had done this, they enclosed a great shoal of fish; and as their nets were breaking,
030507 they beckoned to their partners in the other boat to come and help them. And they came and filled both the boats, so that they began to sink.
030508 But when Simon Peter saw it, he fell down at Jesus' knees, saying, "Depart from me, for I am a sinful man, O Lord."
030509 For he was astonished, and all that were with him, at the catch of fish which they had taken;
030510 and so also were James and John, sons of Zeb'edee, who were partners with Simon. And Jesus said to Simon, "Do not be afraid; henceforth you will be catching men."
030511 And when they had brought their boats to land, they left everything and followed him.
030512 While he was in one of the cities, there came a man full of leprosy; and when he saw Jesus, he fell on his face and besought him, "Lord, if you will, you can make me clean."
030513 And he stretched out his hand, and touched him, saying, "I will; be clean." And immediately the leprosy left him.
030514 And he charged him to tell no one; but "go and show yourself to the priest, and make an offering for your cleansing, as Moses commanded, for a proof to the people."
030515 But so much the more the report went abroad concerning him; and great multitudes gathered to hear and to be healed of their infirmities.
030516 But he withdrew to the wilderness and prayed.
030517 On one of those days, as he was teaching, there were Pharisees and teachers of the law sitting by, who had come from every village of Galilee and Judea and from Jerusalem; and the power of the Lord was with him to heal.
030518 And behold, men were bringing on a bed a man who was paralyzed, and they sought to bring him in and lay him before Jesus;
030519 but finding no way to bring him in, because of the crowd, they went up on the roof and let him down with his bed through the tiles into the midst before Jesus.
030520 And when he saw their faith he said, "Man, your sins are forgiven you."
030521 And the scribes and the Pharisees began to question, saying, "Who is this that speaks blasphemies? Who can forgive sins but God only?"
030522 When Jesus perceived their questionings, he answered them, "Why do you question in your hearts?
030523 Which is easier, to say, 'Your sins are forgiven you,' or to say, 'Rise and walk'?
030524 But that you may know that the Son of man has authority on earth to forgive sins" -- he said to the man who was paralyzed -- "I say to you, rise, take up your bed and go home."
030525 And immediately he rose before them, and took up that on which he lay, and went home, glorifying God.
030526 And amazement seized them all, and they glorified God and were filled with awe, saying, "We have seen strange things today."
030527 After this he went out, and saw a tax collector, named Levi, sitting at the tax office; and he said to him, "Follow me."
030528 And he left everything, and rose and followed him.
030529 And Levi made him a great feast in his house; and there was a large company of tax collectors and others sitting at table with them.
030530 And the Pharisees and their scribes murmured against his disciples, saying, "Why do you eat and drink with tax collectors and sinners?"
030531 And Jesus answered them, "Those who are well have no need of a physician, but those who are sick;
030532 I have not come to call the righteous, but sinners to repentance."
030533 And they said to him, "The disciples of John fast often and offer prayers, and so do the disciples of the Pharisees, but yours eat and drink."
030534 And Jesus said to them, "Can you make wedding guests fast while the bridegroom is with them?
030535 The days will come, when the bridegroom is taken away from them, and then they will fast in those days."
030536 He told them a parable also: "No one tears a piece from a new garment and puts it upon an old garment; if he does, he will tear the new, and the piece from the new will not match the old.
030537 And no one puts new wine into old wineskins; if he does, the new wine will burst the skins and it will be spilled, and the skins will be destroyed.
030538 But new wine must be put into fresh wineskins.
030539 And no one after drinking old wine desires new; for he says, 'The old is good.'"
030601 On a sabbath, while he was going through the grainfields, his disciples plucked and ate some heads of grain, rubbing them in their hands.
030602 But some of the Pharisees said, "Why are you doing what is not lawful to do on the sabbath?"
030603 And Jesus answered, "Have you not read what David did when he was hungry, he and those who were with him:
030604 how he entered the house of God, and took and ate the bread of the Presence, which it is not lawful for any but the priests to eat, and also gave it to those with him?"
030605 And he said to them, "The Son of man is lord of the sabbath."
030606 On another sabbath, when he entered the synagogue and taught, a man was there whose right hand was withered.
030607 And the scribes and the Pharisees watched him, to see whether he would heal on the sabbath, so that they might find an accusation against him.
030608 But he knew their thoughts, and he said to the man who had the withered hand, "Come and stand here." And he rose and stood there.
030609 And Jesus said to them, "I ask you, is it lawful on the sabbath to do good or to do harm, to save life or to destroy it?"
030610 And he looked around on them all, and said to him, "Stretch out your hand." And he did so, and his hand was restored.
030611 But they were filled with fury and discussed with one another what they might do to Jesus.
030612 In these days he went out to the mountain to pray; and all night he continued in prayer to God.
030613 And when it was day, he called his disciples, and chose from them twelve, whom he named apostles;
030614 Simon, whom he named Peter, and Andrew his brother, and James and John, and Philip, and Bartholomew,
030615 and Matthew, and Thomas, and James the son of Alphaeus, and Simon who was called the Zealot,
030616 and Judas the son of James, and Judas Iscariot, who became a traitor.
030617 And he came down with them and stood on a level place, with a great crowd of his disciples and a great multitude of people from all Judea and Jerusalem and the seacoast of Tyre and Sidon, who came to hear him and to be healed of their diseases;
030618 and those who were troubled with unclean spirits were cured.
030619 And all the crowd sought to touch him, for power came forth from him and healed them all.
030620 And he lifted up his eyes on his disciples, and said: "Blessed are you poor, for yours is the kingdom of God.
030621 "Blessed are you that hunger now, for you shall be satisfied. "Blessed are you that weep now, for you shall laugh.
030622 "Blessed are you when men hate you, and when they exclude you and revile you, and cast out your name as evil, on account of the Son of man!
030623 Rejoice in that day, and leap for joy, for behold, your reward is great in heaven; for so their fathers did to the prophets.
030624 "But woe to you that are rich, for you have received your consolation.
030625 "Woe to you that are full now, for you shall hunger. "Woe to you that laugh now, for you shall mourn and weep.
030626 "Woe to you, when all men speak well of you, for so their fathers did to the false prophets.
030627 "But I say to you that hear, Love your enemies, do good to those who hate you,
030628 bless those who curse you, pray for those who abuse you.
030629 To him who strikes you on the cheek, offer the other also; and from him who takes away your coat do not withhold even your shirt.
030630 Give to every one who begs from you; and of him who takes away your goods do not ask them again.
030631 And as you wish that men would do to you, do so to them.
030632 "If you love those who love you, what credit is that to you? For even sinners love those who love them.
030633 And if you do good to those who do good to you, what credit is that to you? For even sinners do the same.
030634 And if you lend to those from whom you hope to receive, what credit is that to you? Even sinners lend to sinners, to receive as much again.
030635 But love your enemies, and do good, and lend, expecting nothing in return; and your reward will be great, and you will be sons of the Most High; for he is kind to the ungrateful and the selfish.
030636 Be merciful, even as your Father is merciful.
030637 "Judge not, and you will not be judged; condemn not, and you will not be condemned; forgive, and you will be forgiven;
030638 give, and it will be given to you; good measure, pressed down, shaken together, running over, will be put into your lap. For the measure you give will be the measure you get back."
030639 He also told them a parable: "Can a blind man lead a blind man? Will they not both fall into a pit?
030640 A disciple is not above his teacher, but every one when he is fully taught will be like his teacher.
030641 Why do you see the speck that is in your brother's eye, but do not notice the log that is in your own eye?
030642 Or how can you say to your brother, 'Brother, let me take out the speck that is in your eye,' when you yourself do not see the log that is in your own eye? You hypocrite, first take the log out of your own eye, and then you will see clearly to take out the speck that is in your brother's eye.
030643 "For no good tree bears bad fruit, nor again does a bad tree bear good fruit;
030644 for each tree is known by its own fruit. For figs are not gathered from thorns, nor are grapes picked from a bramble bush.
030645 The good man out of the good treasure of his heart produces good, and the evil man out of his evil treasure produces evil; for out of the abundance of the heart his mouth speaks.
030646 "Why do you call me 'Lord, Lord,' and not do what I tell you?
030647 Every one who comes to me and hears my words and does them, I will show you what he is like:
030648 he is like a man building a house, who dug deep, and laid the foundation upon rock; and when a flood arose, the stream broke against that house, and could not shake it, because it had been well built.
030649 But he who hears and does not do them is like a man who built a house on the ground without a foundation; against which the stream broke, and immediately it fell, and the ruin of that house was great."
030701 After he had ended all his sayings in the hearing of the people he entered Caper'na-um.
030702 Now a centurion had a slave who was dear to him, who was sick and at the point of death.
030703 When he heard of Jesus, he sent to him elders of the Jews, asking him to come and heal his slave.
030704 And when they came to Jesus, they besought him earnestly, saying, "He is worthy to have you do this for him,
030705 for he loves our nation, and he built us our synagogue."
030706 And Jesus went with them. When he was not far from the house, the centurion sent friends to him, saying to him, "Lord, do not trouble yourself, for I am not worthy to have you come under my roof;
030707 therefore I did not presume to come to you. But say the word, and let my servant be healed.
030708 For I am a man set under authority, with soldiers under me: and I say to one, 'Go,' and he goes; and to another, 'Come,' and he comes; and to my slave, 'Do this,' and he does it."
030709 When Jesus heard this he marveled at him, and turned and said to the multitude that followed him, "I tell you, not even in Israel have I found such faith."
030710 And when those who had been sent returned to the house, they found the slave well.
030711 Soon afterward he went to a city called Na'in, and his disciples and a great crowd went with him.
030712 As he drew near to the gate of the city, behold, a man who had died was being carried out, the only son of his mother, and she was a widow; and a large crowd from the city was with her.
030713 And when the Lord saw her, he had compassion on her and said to her, "Do not weep."
030714 And he came and touched the bier, and the bearers stood still. And he said, "Young man, I say to you, arise."
030715 And the dead man sat up, and began to speak. And he gave him to his mother.
030716 Fear seized them all; and they glorified God, saying, "A great prophet has arisen among us!" and "God has visited his people!"
030717 And this report concerning him spread through the whole of Judea and all the surrounding country.
030718 The disciples of John told him of all these things.
030719 And John, calling to him two of his disciples, sent them to the Lord, saying, "Are you he who is to come, or shall we look for another?"
030720 And when the men had come to him, they said, "John the Baptist has sent us to you, saying, 'Are you he who is to come, or shall we look for another?'"
030721 In that hour he cured many of diseases and plagues and evil spirits, and on many that were blind he bestowed sight.
030722 And he answered them, "Go and tell John what you have seen and heard: the blind receive their sight, the lame walk, lepers are cleansed, and the deaf hear, the dead are raised up, the poor have good news preached to them.
030723 And blessed is he who takes no offense at me."
030724 When the messengers of John had gone, he began to speak to the crowds concerning John: "What did you go out into the wilderness to behold? A reed shaken by the wind?
030725 What then did you go out to see? A man clothed in soft clothing? Behold, those who are gorgeously appareled and live in luxury are in kings' courts.
030726 What then did you go out to see? A prophet? Yes, I tell you, and more than a prophet.
