030727 This is he of whom it is written, 'Behold, I send my messenger before thy face, who shall prepare thy way before thee.'
030728 I tell you, among those born of women none is greater than John; yet he who is least in the kingdom of God is greater than he."
030729 (When they heard this all the people and the tax collectors justified God, having been baptized with the baptism of John;
030730 but the Pharisees and the lawyers rejected the purpose of God for themselves, not having been baptized by him.)
030731 "To what then shall I compare the men of this generation, and what are they like?
030732 They are like children sitting in the market place and calling to one another, 'We piped to you, and you did not dance; we wailed, and you did not weep.'
030733 For John the Baptist has come eating no bread and drinking no wine; and you say, 'He has a demon.'
030734 The Son of man has come eating and drinking; and you say, 'Behold, a glutton and a drunkard, a friend of tax collectors and sinners!'
030735 Yet wisdom is justified by all her children."
030736 One of the Pharisees asked him to eat with him, and he went into the Pharisee's house, and took his place at table.
030737 And behold, a woman of the city, who was a sinner, when she learned that he was at table in the Pharisee's house, brought an alabaster flask of ointment,
030738 and standing behind him at his feet, weeping, she began to wet his feet with her tears, and wiped them with the hair of her head, and kissed his feet, and anointed them with the ointment.
030739 Now when the Pharisee who had invited him saw it, he said to himself, "If this man were a prophet, he would have known who and what sort of woman this is who is touching him, for she is a sinner."
030740 And Jesus answering said to him, "Simon, I have something to say to you." And he answered, "What is it, Teacher?"
030741 "A certain creditor had two debtors; one owed five hundred denarii, and the other fifty.
030742 When they could not pay, he forgave them both. Now which of them will love him more?"
030743 Simon answered, "The one, I suppose, to whom he forgave more." And he said to him, "You have judged rightly."
030744 Then turning toward the woman he said to Simon, "Do you see this woman? I entered your house, you gave me no water for my feet, but she has wet my feet with her tears and wiped them with her hair.
030745 You gave me no kiss, but from the time I came in she has not ceased to kiss my feet.
030746 You did not anoint my head with oil, but she has anointed my feet with ointment.
030747 Therefore I tell you, her sins, which are many, are forgiven, for she loved much; but he who is forgiven little, loves little."
030748 And he said to her, "Your sins are forgiven."
030749 Then those who were at table with him began to say among themselves, "Who is this, who even forgives sins?"
030750 And he said to the woman, "Your faith has saved you; go in peace."
030801 Soon afterward he went on through cities and villages, preaching and bringing the good news of the kingdom of God. And the twelve were with him,
030802 and also some women who had been healed of evil spirits and infirmities: Mary, called Mag'dalene, from whom seven demons had gone out,
030803 and Joan'na, the wife of Chuza, Herod's steward, and Susanna, and many others, who provided for them out of their means.
030804 And when a great crowd came together and people from town after town came to him, he said in a parable:
030805 "A sower went out to sow his seed; and as he sowed, some fell along the path, and was trodden under foot, and the birds of the air devoured it.
030806 And some fell on the rock; and as it grew up, it withered away, because it had no moisture.
030807 And some fell among thorns; and the thorns grew with it and choked it.
030808 And some fell into good soil and grew, and yielded a hundredfold." As he said this, he called out, "He who has ears to hear, let him hear."
030809 And when his disciples asked him what this parable meant,
030810 he said, "To you it has been given to know the secrets of the kingdom of God; but for others they are in parables, so that seeing they may not see, and hearing they may not understand.
030811 Now the parable is this: The seed is the word of God.
030812 The ones along the path are those who have heard; then the devil comes and takes away the word from their hearts, that they may not believe and be saved.
030813 And the ones on the rock are those who, when they hear the word, receive it with joy; but these have no root, they believe for a while and in time of temptation fall away.
030814 And as for what fell among the thorns, they are those who hear, but as they go on their way they are choked by the cares and riches and pleasures of life, and their fruit does not mature.
030815 And as for that in the good soil, they are those who, hearing the word, hold it fast in an honest and good heart, and bring forth fruit with patience.
030816 "No one after lighting a lamp covers it with a vessel, or puts it under a bed, but puts it on a stand, that those who enter may see the light.
030817 For nothing is hid that shall not be made manifest, nor anything secret that shall not be known and come to light.
030818 Take heed then how you hear; for to him who has will more be given, and from him who has not, even what he thinks that he has will be taken away."
030819 Then his mother and his brothers came to him, but they could not reach him for the crowd.
030820 And he was told, "Your mother and your brothers are standing outside, desiring to see you."
030821 But he said to them, "My mother and my brothers are those who hear the word of God and do it."
030822 One day he got into a boat with his disciples, and he said to them, "Let us go across to the other side of the lake." So they set out,
030823 and as they sailed he fell asleep. And a storm of wind came down on the lake, and they were filling with water, and were in danger.
030824 And they went and woke him, saying, "Master, Master, we are perishing!" And he awoke and rebuked the wind and the raging waves; and they ceased, and there was a calm.
030825 He said to them, "Where is your faith?" And they were afraid, and they marveled, saying to one another, "Who then is this, that he commands even wind and water, and they obey him?"
030826 Then they arrived at the country of the Ger'asenes, which is opposite Galilee.
030827 And as he stepped out on land, there met him a man from the city who had demons; for a long time he had worn no clothes, and he lived not in a house but among the tombs.
030828 When he saw Jesus, he cried out and fell down before him, and said with a loud voice, "What have you to do with me, Jesus, Son of the Most High God? I beseech you, do not torment me."
030829 For he had commanded the unclean spirit to come out of the man. (For many a time it had seized him; he was kept under guard, and bound with chains and fetters, but he broke the bonds and was driven by the demon into the desert.)
030830 Jesus then asked him, "What is your name?" And he said, "Legion"; for many demons had entered him.
030831 And they begged him not to command them to depart into the abyss.
030832 Now a large herd of swine was feeding there on the hillside; and they begged him to let them enter these. So he gave them leave.
030833 Then the demons came out of the man and entered the swine, and the herd rushed down the steep bank into the lake and were drowned.
030834 When the herdsmen saw what had happened, they fled, and told it in the city and in the country.
030835 Then people went out to see what had happened, and they came to Jesus, and found the man from whom the demons had gone, sitting at the feet of Jesus, clothed and in his right mind; and they were afraid.
030836 And those who had seen it told them how he who had been possessed with demons was healed.
030837 Then all the people of the surrounding country of the Ger'asenes asked him to depart from them; for they were seized with great fear; so he got into the boat and returned.
030838 The man from whom the demons had gone begged that he might be with him; but he sent him away, saying,
030839 "Return to your home, and declare how much God has done for you." And he went away, proclaiming throughout the whole city how much Jesus had done for him.
030840 Now when Jesus returned, the crowd welcomed him, for they were all waiting for him.
030841 And there came a man named Ja'irus, who was a ruler of the synagogue; and falling at Jesus' feet he besought him to come to his house,
030842 for he had an only daughter, about twelve years of age, and she was dying. As he went, the people pressed round him.
030843 And a woman who had had a flow of blood for twelve years and could not be healed by any one,
030844 came up behind him, and touched the fringe of his garment; and immediately her flow of blood ceased.
030845 And Jesus said, "Who was it that touched me?" When all denied it, Peter said, "Master, the multitudes surround you and press upon you!"
030846 But Jesus said, "Some one touched me; for I perceive that power has gone forth from me."
030847 And when the woman saw that she was not hidden, she came trembling, and falling down before him declared in the presence of all the people why she had touched him, and how she had been immediately healed.
030848 And he said to her, "Daughter, your faith has made you well; go in peace."
030849 While he was still speaking, a man from the ruler's house came and said, "Your daughter is dead; do not trouble the Teacher any more."
030850 But Jesus on hearing this answered him, "Do not fear; only believe, and she shall be well."
030851 And when he came to the house, he permitted no one to enter with him, except Peter and John and James, and the father and mother of the child.
030852 And all were weeping and bewailing her; but he said, "Do not weep; for she is not dead but sleeping."
030853 And they laughed at him, knowing that she was dead.
030854 But taking her by the hand he called, saying, "Child, arise."
030855 And her spirit returned, and she got up at once; and he directed that something should be given her to eat.
030856 And her parents were amazed; but he charged them to tell no one what had happened.
030901 And he called the twelve together and gave them power and authority over all demons and to cure diseases,
030902 and he sent them out to preach the kingdom of God and to heal.
030903 And he said to them, "Take nothing for your journey, no staff, nor bag, nor bread, nor money; and do not have two tunics.
030904 And whatever house you enter, stay there, and from there depart.
030905 And wherever they do not receive you, when you leave that town shake off the dust from your feet as a testimony against them."
030906 And they departed and went through the villages, preaching the gospel and healing everywhere.
030907 Now Herod the tetrarch heard of all that was done, and he was perplexed, because it was said by some that John had been raised from the dead,
030908 by some that Eli'jah had appeared, and by others that one of the old prophets had risen.
030909 Herod said, "John I beheaded; but who is this about whom I hear such things?" And he sought to see him.
030910 On their return the apostles told him what they had done. And he took them and withdrew apart to a city called Beth-sa'ida.
030911 When the crowds learned it, they followed him; and he welcomed them and spoke to them of the kingdom of God, and cured those who had need of healing.
030912 Now the day began to wear away; and the twelve came and said to him, "Send the crowd away, to go into the villages and country round about, to lodge and get provisions; for we are here in a lonely place."
030913 But he said to them, "You give them something to eat." They said, "We have no more than five loaves and two fish -- unless we are to go and buy food for all these people."
030914 For there were about five thousand men. And he said to his disciples, "Make them sit down in companies, about fifty each."
030915 And they did so, and made them all sit down.
030916 And taking the five loaves and the two fish he looked up to heaven, and blessed and broke them, and gave them to the disciples to set before the crowd.
030917 And all ate and were satisfied. And they took up what was left over, twelve baskets of broken pieces.
030918 Now it happened that as he was praying alone the disciples were with him; and he asked them, "Who do the people say that I am?"
030919 And they answered, "John the Baptist; but others say, Eli'jah; and others, that one of the old prophets has risen."
030920 And he said to them, "But who do you say that I am?" And Peter answered, "The Christ of God."
030921 But he charged and commanded them to tell this to no one,
030922 saying, "The Son of man must suffer many things, and be rejected by the elders and chief priests and scribes, and be killed, and on the third day be raised."
030923 And he said to all, "If any man would come after me, let him deny himself and take up his cross daily and follow me.
030924 For whoever would save his life will lose it; and whoever loses his life for my sake, he will save it.
030925 For what does it profit a man if he gains the whole world and loses or forfeits himself?
030926 For whoever is ashamed of me and of my words, of him will the Son of man be ashamed when he comes in his glory and the glory of the Father and of the holy angels.
030927 But I tell you truly, there are some standing here who will not taste death before they see the kingdom of God."
030928 Now about eight days after these sayings he took with him Peter and John and James, and went up on the mountain to pray.
030929 And as he was praying, the appearance of his countenance was altered, and his raiment became dazzling white.
030930 And behold, two men talked with him, Moses and Eli'jah,
030931 who appeared in glory and spoke of his departure, which he was to accomplish at Jerusalem.
030932 Now Peter and those who were with him were heavy with sleep, and when they wakened they saw his glory and the two men who stood with him.
030933 And as the men were parting from him, Peter said to Jesus, "Master, it is well that we are here; let us make three booths, one for you and one for Moses and one for Eli'jah" -- not knowing what he said.
030934 As he said this, a cloud came and overshadowed them; and they were afraid as they entered the cloud.
030935 And a voice came out of the cloud, saying, "This is my Son, my Chosen; listen to him!"
030936 And when the voice had spoken, Jesus was found alone. And they kept silence and told no one in those days anything of what they had seen.
030937 On the next day, when they had come down from the mountain, a great crowd met him.
030938 And behold, a man from the crowd cried, "Teacher, I beg you to look upon my son, for he is my only child;
030939 and behold, a spirit seizes him, and he suddenly cries out; it convulses him till he foams, and shatters him, and will hardly leave him.
030940 And I begged your disciples to cast it out, but they could not."
030941 Jesus answered, "O faithless and perverse generation, how long am I to be with you and bear with you? Bring your son here."
030942 While he was coming, the demon tore him and convulsed him. But Jesus rebuked the unclean spirit, and healed the boy, and gave him back to his father.
030943 And all were astonished at the majesty of God. But while they were all marveling at everything he did, he said to his disciples,
030944 "Let these words sink into your ears; for the Son of man is to be delivered into the hands of men."
030945 But they did not understand this saying, and it was concealed from them, that they should not perceive it; and they were afraid to ask him about this saying.
030946 And an argument arose among them as to which of them was the greatest.
030947 But when Jesus perceived the thought of their hearts, he took a child and put him by his side,
030948 and said to them, "Whoever receives this child in my name receives me, and whoever receives me receives him who sent me; for he who is least among you all is the one who is great."
030949 John answered, "Master, we saw a man casting out demons in your name, and we forbade him, because he does not follow with us."
030950 But Jesus said to him, "Do not forbid him; for he that is not against you is for you."
030951 When the days drew near for him to be received up, he set his face to go to Jerusalem.
030952 And he sent messengers ahead of him, who went and entered a village of the Samaritans, to make ready for him;
030953 but the people would not receive him, because his face was set toward Jerusalem.
030954 And when his disciples James and John saw it, they said, "Lord, do you want us to bid fire come down from heaven and consume them?"
030955 But he turned and rebuked them.
030956 And they went on to another village.
030957 As they were going along the road, a man said to him, "I will follow you wherever you go."
030958 And Jesus said to him, "Foxes have holes, and birds of the air have nests; but the Son of man has nowhere to lay his head."
030959 To another he said, "Follow me." But he said, "Lord, let me first go and bury my father."
030960 But he said to him, "Leave the dead to bury their own dead; but as for you, go and proclaim the kingdom of God."
030961 Another said, "I will follow you, Lord; but let me first say farewell to those at my home."
030962 Jesus said to him, "No one who puts his hand to the plow and looks back is fit for the kingdom of God."
031001 After this the Lord appointed seventy others, and sent them on ahead of him, two by two, into every town and place where he himself was about to come.
031002 And he said to them, "The harvest is plentiful, but the laborers are few; pray therefore the Lord of the harvest to send out laborers into his harvest.
031003 Go your way; behold, I send you out as lambs in the midst of wolves.
031004 Carry no purse, no bag, no sandals; and salute no one on the road.
031005 Whatever house you enter, first say, 'Peace be to this house!'
031006 And if a son of peace is there, your peace shall rest upon him; but if not, it shall return to you.
031007 And remain in the same house, eating and drinking what they provide, for the laborer deserves his wages; do not go from house to house.
031008 Whenever you enter a town and they receive you, eat what is set before you;
031009 heal the sick in it and say to them, 'The kingdom of God has come near to you.'
031010 But whenever you enter a town and they do not receive you, go into its streets and say,
031011 'Even the dust of your town that clings to our feet, we wipe off against you; nevertheless know this, that the kingdom of God has come near.'
031012 I tell you, it shall be more tolerable on that day for Sodom than for that town.
031013 "Woe to you, Chora'zin! woe to you, Beth-sa'ida! for if the mighty works done in you had been done in Tyre and Sidon, they would have repented long ago, sitting in sackcloth and ashes.
031014 But it shall be more tolerable in the judgment for Tyre and Sidon than for you.
031015 And you, Caper'na-um, will you be exalted to heaven? You shall be brought down to Hades.
031016 "He who hears you hears me, and he who rejects you rejects me, and he who rejects me rejects him who sent me."
031017 The seventy returned with joy, saying, "Lord, even the demons are subject to us in your name!"
031018 And he said to them, "I saw Satan fall like lightning from heaven.
031019 Behold, I have given you authority to tread upon serpents and scorpions, and over all the power of the enemy; and nothing shall hurt you.
031020 Nevertheless do not rejoice in this, that the spirits are subject to you; but rejoice that your names are written in heaven."
031021 In that same hour he rejoiced in the Holy Spirit and said, "I thank thee, Father, Lord of heaven and earth, that thou hast hidden these things from the wise and understanding and revealed them to babes; yea, Father, for such was thy gracious will.
031022 All things have been delivered to me by my Father; and no one knows who the Son is except the Father, or who the Father is except the Son and any one to whom the Son chooses to reveal him."
031023 Then turning to the disciples he said privately, "Blessed are the eyes which see what you see!
031024 For I tell you that many prophets and kings desired to see what you see, and did not see it, and to hear what you hear, and did not hear it."
031025 And behold, a lawyer stood up to put him to the test, saying, "Teacher, what shall I do to inherit eternal life?"
031026 He said to him, "What is written in the law? How do you read?"
031027 And he answered, "You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart, and with all your soul, and with all your strength, and with all your mind; and your neighbor as yourself."
031028 And he said to him, "You have answered right; do this, and you will live."
031029 But he, desiring to justify himself, said to Jesus, "And who is my neighbor?"
031030 Jesus replied, "A man was going down from Jerusalem to Jericho, and he fell among robbers, who stripped him and beat him, and departed, leaving him half dead.
031031 Now by chance a priest was going down that road; and when he saw him he passed by on the other side.
031032 So likewise a Levite, when he came to the place and saw him, passed by on the other side.
031033 But a Samaritan, as he journeyed, came to where he was; and when he saw him, he had compassion,
031034 and went to him and bound up his wounds, pouring on oil and wine; then he set him on his own beast and brought him to an inn, and took care of him.
031035 And the next day he took out two denarii and gave them to the innkeeper, saying, 'Take care of him; and whatever more you spend, I will repay you when I come back.'
031036 Which of these three, do you think, proved neighbor to the man who fell among the robbers?"
031037 He said, "The one who showed mercy on him." And Jesus said to him, "Go and do likewise."
031038 Now as they went on their way, he entered a village; and a woman named Martha received him into her house.
031039 And she had a sister called Mary, who sat at the Lord's feet and listened to his teaching.
031040 But Martha was distracted with much serving; and she went to him and said, "Lord, do you not care that my sister has left me to serve alone? Tell her then to help me."
031041 But the Lord answered her, "Martha, Martha, you are anxious and troubled about many things;
031042 one thing is needful. Mary has chosen the good portion, which shall not be taken away from her."
031101 He was praying in a certain place, and when he ceased, one of his disciples said to him, "Lord, teach us to pray, as John taught his disciples."
031102 And he said to them, "When you pray, say: "Father, hallowed be thy name. Thy kingdom come.
031103 Give us each day our daily bread;
031104 and forgive us our sins, for we ourselves forgive every one who is indebted to us; and lead us not into temptation."
031105 And he said to them, "Which of you who has a friend will go to him at midnight and say to him, 'Friend, lend me three loaves;
031106 for a friend of mine has arrived on a journey, and I have nothing to set before him';
031107 and he will answer from within, 'Do not bother me; the door is now shut, and my children are with me in bed; I cannot get up and give you anything'?
031108 I tell you, though he will not get up and give him anything because he is his friend, yet because of his importunity he will rise and give him whatever he needs.
031109 And I tell you, Ask, and it will be given you; seek, and you will find; knock, and it will be opened to you.
031110 For every one who asks receives, and he who seeks finds, and to him who knocks it will be opened.
031111 What father among you, if his son asks for a fish, will instead of a fish give him a serpent;
031112 or if he asks for an egg, will give him a scorpion?
031113 If you then, who are evil, know how to give good gifts to your children, how much more will the heavenly Father give the Holy Spirit to those who ask him!"
031114 Now he was casting out a demon that was dumb; when the demon had gone out, the dumb man spoke, and the people marveled.
031115 But some of them said, "He casts out demons by Be-el'zebul, the prince of demons";
031116 while others, to test him, sought from him a sign from heaven.
031117 But he, knowing their thoughts, said to them, "Every kingdom divided against itself is laid waste, and a divided household falls.
031118 And if Satan also is divided against himself, how will his kingdom stand? For you say that I cast out demons by Be-el'zebul.
031119 And if I cast out demons by Be-el'zebul, by whom do your sons cast them out? Therefore they shall be your judges.
031120 But if it is by the finger of God that I cast out demons, then the kingdom of God has come upon you.
031121 When a strong man, fully armed, guards his own palace, his goods are in peace;
031122 but when one stronger than he assails him and overcomes him, he takes away his armor in which he trusted, and divides his spoil.
031123 He who is not with me is against me, and he who does not gather with me scatters.
031124 "When the unclean spirit has gone out of a man, he passes through waterless places seeking rest; and finding none he says, 'I will return to my house from which I came.'
031125 And when he comes he finds it swept and put in order.
031126 Then he goes and brings seven other spirits more evil than himself, and they enter and dwell there; and the last state of that man becomes worse than the first."
031127 As he said this, a woman in the crowd raised her voice and said to him, "Blessed is the womb that bore you, and the breasts that you sucked!"
031128 But he said, "Blessed rather are those who hear the word of God and keep it!"
031129 When the crowds were increasing, he began to say, "This generation is an evil generation; it seeks a sign, but no sign shall be given to it except the sign of Jonah.
031130 For as Jonah became a sign to the men of Nin'eveh, so will the Son of man be to this generation.
031131 The queen of the South will arise at the judgment with the men of this generation and condemn them; for she came from the ends of the earth to hear the wisdom of Solomon, and behold, something greater than Solomon is here.
031132 The men of Nin'eveh will arise at the judgment with this generation and condemn it; for they repented at the preaching of Jonah, and behold, something greater than Jonah is here.
031133 "No one after lighting a lamp puts it in a cellar or under a bushel, but on a stand, that those who enter may see the light.
031134 Your eye is the lamp of your body; when your eye is sound, your whole body is full of light; but when it is not sound, your body is full of darkness.
031135 Therefore be careful lest the light in you be darkness.
031136 If then your whole body is full of light, having no part dark, it will be wholly bright, as when a lamp with its rays gives you light."
031137 While he was speaking, a Pharisee asked him to dine with him; so he went in and sat at table.
031138 The Pharisee was astonished to see that he did not first wash before dinner.
031139 And the Lord said to him, "Now you Pharisees cleanse the outside of the cup and of the dish, but inside you are full of extortion and wickedness.
031140 You fools! Did not he who made the outside make the inside also?
031141 But give for alms those things which are within; and behold, everything is clean for you.
031142 "But woe to you Pharisees! for you tithe mint and rue and every herb, and neglect justice and the love of God; these you ought to have done, without neglecting the others.
031143 Woe to you Pharisees! for you love the best seat in the synagogues and salutations in the market places.
031144 Woe to you! for you are like graves which are not seen, and men walk over them without knowing it."
031145 One of the lawyers answered him, "Teacher, in saying this you reproach us also."
031146 And he said, "Woe to you lawyers also! for you load men with burdens hard to bear, and you yourselves do not touch the burdens with one of your fingers.
031147 Woe to you! for you build the tombs of the prophets whom your fathers killed.
031148 So you are witnesses and consent to the deeds of your fathers; for they killed them, and you build their tombs.
031149 Therefore also the Wisdom of God said, 'I will send them prophets and apostles, some of whom they will kill and persecute,'
031150 that the blood of all the prophets, shed from the foundation of the world, may be required of this generation,
031151 from the blood of Abel to the blood of Zechari'ah, who perished between the altar and the sanctuary. Yes, I tell you, it shall be required of this generation.
031152 Woe to you lawyers! for you have taken away the key of knowledge; you did not enter yourselves, and you hindered those who were entering."
031153 As he went away from there, the scribes and the Pharisees began to press him hard, and to provoke him to speak of many things,
031154 lying in wait for him, to catch at something he might say.
031201 In the meantime, when so many thousands of the multitude had gathered together that they trod upon one another, he began to say to his disciples first, "Beware of the leaven of the Pharisees, which is hypocrisy.
031202 Nothing is covered up that will not be revealed, or hidden that will not be known.
031203 Therefore whatever you have said in the dark shall be heard in the light, and what you have whispered in private rooms shall be proclaimed upon the housetops.
031204 "I tell you, my friends, do not fear those who kill the body, and after that have no more that they can do.
031205 But I will warn you whom to fear: fear him who, after he has killed, has power to cast into hell; yes, I tell you, fear him!
031206 Are not five sparrows sold for two pennies? And not one of them is forgotten before God.
031207 Why, even the hairs of your head are all numbered. Fear not; you are of more value than many sparrows.
031208 "And I tell you, every one who acknowledges me before men, the Son of man also will acknowledge before the angels of God;
031209 but he who denies me before men will be denied before the angels of God.
031210 And every one who speaks a word against the Son of man will be forgiven; but he who blasphemes against the Holy Spirit will not be forgiven.
031211 And when they bring you before the synagogues and the rulers and the authorities, do not be anxious how or what you are to answer or what you are to say;
031212 for the Holy Spirit will teach you in that very hour what you ought to say."
031213 One of the multitude said to him, "Teacher, bid my brother divide the inheritance with me."
031214 But he said to him, "Man, who made me a judge or divider over you?"
031215 And he said to them, "Take heed, and beware of all covetousness; for a man's life does not consist in the abundance of his possessions."
031216 And he told them a parable, saying, "The land of a rich man brought forth plentifully;
031217 and he thought to himself, 'What shall I do, for I have nowhere to store my crops?'
031218 And he said, 'I will do this: I will pull down my barns, and build larger ones; and there I will store all my grain and my goods.
031219 And I will say to my soul, Soul, you have ample goods laid up for many years; take your ease, eat, drink, be merry.'
031220 But God said to him, 'Fool! This night your soul is required of you; and the things you have prepared, whose will they be?'
031221 So is he who lays up treasure for himself, and is not rich toward God."
031222 And he said to his disciples, "Therefore I tell you, do not be anxious about your life, what you shall eat, nor about your body, what you shall put on.
031223 For life is more than food, and the body more than clothing.
031224 Consider the ravens: they neither sow nor reap, they have neither storehouse nor barn, and yet God feeds them. Of how much more value are you than the birds!
031225 And which of you by being anxious can add a cubit to his span of life?
031226 If then you are not able to do as small a thing as that, why are you anxious about the rest?
031227 Consider the lilies, how they grow; they neither toil nor spin; yet I tell you, even Solomon in all his glory was not arrayed like one of these.
031228 But if God so clothes the grass which is alive in the field today and tomorrow is thrown into the oven, how much more will he clothe you, O men of little faith!
031229 And do not seek what you are to eat and what you are to drink, nor be of anxious mind.
031230 For all the nations of the world seek these things; and your Father knows that you need them.
031231 Instead, seek his kingdom, and these things shall be yours as well.
031232 "Fear not, little flock, for it is your Father's good pleasure to give you the kingdom.
031233 Sell your possessions, and give alms; provide yourselves with purses that do not grow old, with a treasure in the heavens that does not fail, where no thief approaches and no moth destroys.
031234 For where your treasure is, there will your heart be also.
031235 "Let your loins be girded and your lamps burning,
031236 and be like men who are waiting for their master to come home from the marriage feast, so that they may open to him at once when he comes and knocks.
031237 Blessed are those servants whom the master finds awake when he comes; truly, I say to you, he will gird himself and have them sit at table, and he will come and serve them.
031238 If he comes in the second watch, or in the third, and finds them so, blessed are those servants!
031239 But know this, that if the householder had known at what hour the thief was coming, he would not have left his house to be broken into.
031240 You also must be ready; for the Son of man is coming at an unexpected hour."
031241 Peter said, "Lord, are you telling this parable for us or for all?"
031242 And the Lord said, "Who then is the faithful and wise steward, whom his master will set over his household, to give them their portion of food at the proper time?
031243 Blessed is that servant whom his master when he comes will find so doing.
031244 Truly, I say to you, he will set him over all his possessions.
031245 But if that servant says to himself, 'My master is delayed in coming,' and begins to beat the menservants and the maidservants, and to eat and drink and get drunk,
031246 the master of that servant will come on a day when he does not expect him and at an hour he does not know, and will punish him, and put him with the unfaithful.
031247 And that servant who knew his master's will, but did not make ready or act according to his will, shall receive a severe beating.
031248 But he who did not know, and did what deserved a beating, shall receive a light beating. Every one to whom much is given, of him will much be required; and of him to whom men commit much they will demand the more.
031249 "I came to cast fire upon the earth; and would that it were already kindled!
031250 I have a baptism to be baptized with; and how I am constrained until it is accomplished!
031251 Do you think that I have come to give peace on earth? No, I tell you, but rather division;
031252 for henceforth in one house there will be five divided, three against two and two against three;
031253 they will be divided, father against son and son against father, mother against daughter and daughter against her mother, mother-in-law against her daughter-in-law and daughter-in-law against her mother-in-law."
031254 He also said to the multitudes, "When you see a cloud rising in the west, you say at once, 'A shower is coming'; and so it happens.
031255 And when you see the south wind blowing, you say, 'There will be scorching heat'; and it happens.
031256 You hypocrites! You know how to interpret the appearance of earth and sky; but why do you not know how to interpret the present time?
031257 "And why do you not judge for yourselves what is right?
031258 As you go with your accuser before the magistrate, make an effort to settle with him on the way, lest he drag you to the judge, and the judge hand you over to the officer, and the officer put you in prison.
031259 I tell you, you will never get out till you have paid the very last copper."
031301 There were some present at that very time who told him of the Galileans whose blood Pilate had mingled with their sacrifices.
031302 And he answered them, "Do you think that these Galileans were worse sinners than all the other Galileans, because they suffered thus?
031303 I tell you, No; but unless you repent you will all likewise perish.
031304 Or those eighteen upon whom the tower in Silo'am fell and killed them, do you think that they were worse offenders than all the others who dwelt in Jerusalem?
031305 I tell you, No; but unless you repent you will all likewise perish."
031306 And he told this parable: "A man had a fig tree planted in his vineyard; and he came seeking fruit on it and found none.
031307 And he said to the vinedresser, 'Lo, these three years I have come seeking fruit on this fig tree, and I find none. Cut it down; why should it use up the ground?'
031308 And he answered him, 'Let it alone, sir, this year also, till I dig about it and put on manure.
031309 And if it bears fruit next year, well and good; but if not, you can cut it down.'"
031310 Now he was teaching in one of the synagogues on the sabbath.
031311 And there was a woman who had had a spirit of infirmity for eighteen years; she was bent over and could not fully straighten herself.
031312 And when Jesus saw her, he called her and said to her, "Woman, you are freed from your infirmity."
031313 And he laid his hands upon her, and immediately she was made straight, and she praised God.
031314 But the ruler of the synagogue, indignant because Jesus had healed on the sabbath, said to the people, "There are six days on which work ought to be done; come on those days and be healed, and not on the sabbath day."
031315 Then the Lord answered him, "You hypocrites! Does not each of you on the sabbath untie his ox or his ass from the manger, and lead it away to water it?
031316 And ought not this woman, a daughter of Abraham whom Satan bound for eighteen years, be loosed from this bond on the sabbath day?"
031317 As he said this, all his adversaries were put to shame; and all the people rejoiced at all the glorious things that were done by him.
031318 He said therefore, "What is the kingdom of God like? And to what shall I compare it?
031319 It is like a grain of mustard seed which a man took and sowed in his garden; and it grew and became a tree, and the birds of the air made nests in its branches."
031320 And again he said, "To what shall I compare the kingdom of God?
031321 It is like leaven which a woman took and hid in three measures of flour, till it was all leavened."
031322 He went on his way through towns and villages, teaching, and journeying toward Jerusalem.
031323 And some one said to him, "Lord, will those who are saved be few?" And he said to them,
031324 "Strive to enter by the narrow door; for many, I tell you, will seek to enter and will not be able.
031325 When once the householder has risen up and shut the door, you will begin to stand outside and to knock at the door, saying, 'Lord, open to us.' He will answer you, 'I do not know where you come from.'
031326 Then you will begin to say, 'We ate and drank in your presence, and you taught in our streets.'
031327 But he will say, 'I tell you, I do not know where you come from; depart from me, all you workers of iniquity!'
031328 There you will weep and gnash your teeth, when you see Abraham and Isaac and Jacob and all the prophets in the kingdom of God and you yourselves thrust out.
031329 And men will come from east and west, and from north and south, and sit at table in the kingdom of God.
031330 And behold, some are last who will be first, and some are first who will be last."
031331 At that very hour some Pharisees came, and said to him, "Get away from here, for Herod wants to kill you."
031332 And he said to them, "Go and tell that fox, 'Behold, I cast out demons and perform cures today and tomorrow, and the third day I finish my course.
031333 Nevertheless I must go on my way today and tomorrow and the day following; for it cannot be that a prophet should perish away from Jerusalem.'
031334 O Jerusalem, Jerusalem, killing the prophets and stoning those who are sent to you! How often would I have gathered your children together as a hen gathers her brood under her wings, and you would not!
031335 Behold, your house is forsaken. And I tell you, you will not see me until you say, 'Blessed is he who comes in the name of the Lord!'"
031401 One sabbath when he went to dine at the house of a ruler who belonged to the Pharisees, they were watching him.
031402 And behold, there was a man before him who had dropsy.
031403 And Jesus spoke to the lawyers and Pharisees, saying, "Is it lawful to heal on the sabbath, or not?"
031404 But they were silent. Then he took him and healed him, and let him go.
031405 And he said to them, "Which of you, having a son or an ox that has fallen into a well, will not immediately pull him out on a sabbath day?"
031406 And they could not reply to this.
031407 Now he told a parable to those who were invited, when he marked how they chose the places of honor, saying to them,
031408 "When you are invited by any one to a marriage feast, do not sit down in a place of honor, lest a more eminent man than you be invited by him;
031409 and he who invited you both will come and say to you, 'Give place to this man,' and then you will begin with shame to take the lowest place.
031410 But when you are invited, go and sit in the lowest place, so that when your host comes he may say to you, 'Friend, go up higher'; then you will be honored in the presence of all who sit at table with you.
031411 For every one who exalts himself will be humbled, and he who humbles himself will be exalted."
031412 He said also to the man who had invited him, "When you give a dinner or a banquet, do not invite your friends or your brothers or your kinsmen or rich neighbors, lest they also invite you in return, and you be repaid.
031413 But when you give a feast, invite the poor, the maimed, the lame, the blind,
031414 and you will be blessed, because they cannot repay you. You will be repaid at the resurrection of the just."
031415 When one of those who sat at table with him heard this, he said to him, "Blessed is he who shall eat bread in the kingdom of God!"
031416 But he said to him, "A man once gave a great banquet, and invited many;
031417 and at the time for the banquet he sent his servant to say to those who had been invited, 'Come; for all is now ready.'
031418 But they all alike began to make excuses. The first said to him, 'I have bought a field, and I must go out and see it; I pray you, have me excused.'
031419 And another said, 'I have bought five yoke of oxen, and I go to examine them; I pray you, have me excused.'
031420 And another said, 'I have married a wife, and therefore I cannot come.'
031421 So the servant came and reported this to his master. Then the householder in anger said to his servant, 'Go out quickly to the streets and lanes of the city, and bring in the poor and maimed and blind and lame.'
031422 And the servant said, 'Sir, what you commanded has been done, and still there is room.'
031423 And the master said to the servant, 'Go out to the highways and hedges, and compel people to come in, that my house may be filled.
031424 For I tell you, none of those men who were invited shall taste my banquet.'"
031425 Now great multitudes accompanied him; and he turned and said to them,
031426 "If any one comes to me and does not hate his own father and mother and wife and children and brothers and sisters, yes, and even his own life, he cannot be my disciple.
031427 Whoever does not bear his own cross and come after me, cannot be my disciple.
031428 For which of you, desiring to build a tower, does not first sit down and count the cost, whether he has enough to complete it?
031429 Otherwise, when he has laid a foundation, and is not able to finish, all who see it begin to mock him,
031430 saying, 'This man began to build, and was not able to finish.'
031431 Or what king, going to encounter another king in war, will not sit down first and take counsel whether he is able with ten thousand to meet him who comes against him with twenty thousand?
031432 And if not, while the other is yet a great way off, he sends an embassy and asks terms of peace.
031433 So therefore, whoever of you does not renounce all that he has cannot be my disciple.
031434 "Salt is good; but if salt has lost its taste, how shall its saltness be restored?
031435 It is fit neither for the land nor for the dunghill; men throw it away. He who has ears to hear, let him hear."
031501 Now the tax collectors and sinners were all drawing near to hear him.
031502 And the Pharisees and the scribes murmured, saying, "This man receives sinners and eats with them."
031503 So he told them this parable:
031504 "What man of you, having a hundred sheep, if he has lost one of them, does not leave the ninety-nine in the wilderness, and go after the one which is lost, until he finds it?
031505 And when he has found it, he lays it on his shoulders, rejoicing.
031506 And when he comes home, he calls together his friends and his neighbors, saying to them, 'Rejoice with me, for I have found my sheep which was lost.'
031507 Just so, I tell you, there will be more joy in heaven over one sinner who repents than over ninety-nine righteous persons who need no repentance.
031508 "Or what woman, having ten silver coins, if she loses one coin, does not light a lamp and sweep the house and seek diligently until she finds it?
031509 And when she has found it, she calls together her friends and neighbors, saying, 'Rejoice with me, for I have found the coin which I had lost.'
031510 Just so, I tell you, there is joy before the angels of God over one sinner who repents."
031511 And he said, "There was a man who had two sons;
031512 and the younger of them said to his father, 'Father, give me the share of property that falls to me.' And he divided his living between them.
031513 Not many days later, the younger son gathered all he had and took his journey into a far country, and there he squandered his property in loose living.
031514 And when he had spent everything, a great famine arose in that country, and he began to be in want.
031515 So he went and joined himself to one of the citizens of that country, who sent him into his fields to feed swine.
031516 And he would gladly have fed on the pods that the swine ate; and no one gave him anything.
031517 But when he came to himself he said, 'How many of my father's hired servants have bread enough and to spare, but I perish here with hunger!
031518 I will arise and go to my father, and I will say to him, "Father, I have sinned against heaven and before you;
031519 I am no longer worthy to be called your son; treat me as one of your hired servants."'
031520 And he arose and came to his father. But while he was yet at a distance, his father saw him and had compassion, and ran and embraced him and kissed him.
031521 And the son said to him, 'Father, I have sinned against heaven and before you; I am no longer worthy to be called your son.'
031522 But the father said to his servants, 'Bring quickly the best robe, and put it on him; and put a ring on his hand, and shoes on his feet;
031523 and bring the fatted calf and kill it, and let us eat and make merry;
031524 for this my son was dead, and is alive again; he was lost, and is found.' And they began to make merry.
031525 "Now his elder son was in the field; and as he came and drew near to the house, he heard music and dancing.
031526 And he called one of the servants and asked what this meant.
031527 And he said to him, 'Your brother has come, and your father has killed the fatted calf, because he has received him safe and sound.'
031528 But he was angry and refused to go in. His father came out and entreated him,
031529 but he answered his father, 'Lo, these many years I have served you, and I never disobeyed your command; yet you never gave me a kid, that I might make merry with my friends.
031530 But when this son of yours came, who has devoured your living with harlots, you killed for him the fatted calf!'
031531 And he said to him, 'Son, you are always with me, and all that is mine is yours.
031532 It was fitting to make merry and be glad, for this your brother was dead, and is alive; he was lost, and is found.'"
031601 He also said to the disciples, "There was a rich man who had a steward, and charges were brought to him that this man was wasting his goods.
031602 And he called him and said to him, 'What is this that I hear about you? Turn in the account of your stewardship, for you can no longer be steward.'
031603 And the steward said to himself, 'What shall I do, since my master is taking the stewardship away from me? I am not strong enough to dig, and I am ashamed to beg.
031604 I have decided what to do, so that people may receive me into their houses when I am put out of the stewardship.'
031605 So, summoning his master's debtors one by one, he said to the first, 'How much do you owe my master?'
031606 He said, 'A hundred measures of oil.' And he said to him, 'Take your bill, and sit down quickly and write fifty.'
031607 Then he said to another, 'And how much do you owe?' He said, 'A hundred measures of wheat.' He said to him, 'Take your bill, and write eighty.'
031608 The master commended the dishonest steward for his shrewdness; for the sons of this world are more shrewd in dealing with their own generation than the sons of light.
031609 And I tell you, make friends for yourselves by means of unrighteous mammon, so that when it fails they may receive you into the eternal habitations.
031610 "He who is faithful in a very little is faithful also in much; and he who is dishonest in a very little is dishonest also in much.
031611 If then you have not been faithful in the unrighteous mammon, who will entrust to you the true riches?
031612 And if you have not been faithful in that which is another's, who will give you that which is your own?
031613 No servant can serve two masters; for either he will hate the one and love the other, or he will be devoted to the one and despise the other. You cannot serve God and mammon."
031614 The Pharisees, who were lovers of money, heard all this, and they scoffed at him.
031615 But he said to them, "You are those who justify yourselves before men, but God knows your hearts; for what is exalted among men is an abomination in the sight of God.
031616 "The law and the prophets were until John; since then the good news of the kingdom of God is preached, and every one enters it violently.
031617 But it is easier for heaven and earth to pass away, than for one dot of the law to become void.
031618 "Every one who divorces his wife and marries another commits adultery, and he who marries a woman divorced from her husband commits adultery.
031619 "There was a rich man, who was clothed in purple and fine linen and who feasted sumptuously every day.
031620 And at his gate lay a poor man named Laz'arus, full of sores,
031621 who desired to be fed with what fell from the rich man's table; moreover the dogs came and licked his sores.
031622 The poor man died and was carried by the angels to Abraham's bosom. The rich man also died and was buried;
031623 and in Hades, being in torment, he lifted up his eyes, and saw Abraham far off and Laz'arus in his bosom.
031624 And he called out, 'Father Abraham, have mercy upon me, and send Laz'arus to dip the end of his finger in water and cool my tongue; for I am in anguish in this flame.'
031625 But Abraham said, 'Son, remember that you in your lifetime received your good things, and Laz'arus in like manner evil things; but now he is comforted here, and you are in anguish.
031626 And besides all this, between us and you a great chasm has been fixed, in order that those who would pass from here to you may not be able, and none may cross from there to us.'
031627 And he said, 'Then I beg you, father, to send him to my father's house,
031628 for I have five brothers, so that he may warn them, lest they also come into this place of torment.'
031629 But Abraham said, 'They have Moses and the prophets; let them hear them.'
031630 And he said, 'No, father Abraham; but if some one goes to them from the dead, they will repent.'
031631 He said to him, 'If they do not hear Moses and the prophets, neither will they be convinced if some one should rise from the dead.'"
031701 And he said to his disciples, "Temptations to sin are sure to come; but woe to him by whom they come!
031702 It would be better for him if a millstone were hung round his neck and he were cast into the sea, than that he should cause one of these little ones to sin.
031703 Take heed to yourselves; if your brother sins, rebuke him, and if he repents, forgive him;
031704 and if he sins against you seven times in the day, and turns to you seven times, and says, 'I repent,' you must forgive him."
031705 The apostles said to the Lord, "Increase our faith!"
031706 And the Lord said, "If you had faith as a grain of mustard seed, you could say to this sycamine tree, 'Be rooted up, and be planted in the sea,' and it would obey you.
031707 "Will any one of you, who has a servant plowing or keeping sheep, say to him when he has come in from the field, 'Come at once and sit down at table'?
031708 Will he not rather say to him, 'Prepare supper for me, and gird yourself and serve me, till I eat and drink; and afterward you shall eat and drink'?
031709 Does he thank the servant because he did what was commanded?
031710 So you also, when you have done all that is commanded you, say, 'We are unworthy servants; we have only done what was our duty.'"
031711 On the way to Jerusalem he was passing along between Sama'ria and Galilee.
031712 And as he entered a village, he was met by ten lepers, who stood at a distance
031713 and lifted up their voices and said, "Jesus, Master, have mercy on us."
031714 When he saw them he said to them, "Go and show yourselves to the priests." And as they went they were cleansed.
031715 Then one of them, when he saw that he was healed, turned back, praising God with a loud voice;
031716 and he fell on his face at Jesus' feet, giving him thanks. Now he was a Samaritan.
031717 Then said Jesus, "Were not ten cleansed? Where are the nine?
031718 Was no one found to return and give praise to God except this foreigner?"
031719 And he said to him, "Rise and go your way; your faith has made you well."
031720 Being asked by the Pharisees when the kingdom of God was coming, he answered them, "The kingdom of God is not coming with signs to be observed;
031721 nor will they say, 'Lo, here it is!' or 'There!' for behold, the kingdom of God is in the midst of you."
031722 And he said to the disciples, "The days are coming when you will desire to see one of the days of the Son of man, and you will not see it.
031723 And they will say to you, 'Lo, there!' or 'Lo, here!' Do not go, do not follow them.
031724 For as the lightning flashes and lights up the sky from one side to the other, so will the Son of man be in his day.
031725 But first he must suffer many things and be rejected by this generation.
031726 As it was in the days of Noah, so will it be in the days of the Son of man.
031727 They ate, they drank, they married, they were given in marriage, until the day when Noah entered the ark, and the flood came and destroyed them all.
031728 Likewise as it was in the days of Lot -- they ate, they drank, they bought, they sold, they planted, they built,
031729 but on the day when Lot went out from Sodom fire and sulphur rained from heaven and destroyed them all --
031730 so will it be on the day when the Son of man is revealed.
031731 On that day, let him who is on the housetop, with his goods in the house, not come down to take them away; and likewise let him who is in the field not turn back.
031732 Remember Lot's wife.
031733 Whoever seeks to gain his life will lose it, but whoever loses his life will preserve it.
031734 I tell you, in that night there will be two in one bed; one will be taken and the other left.
031735 There will be two women grinding together; one will be taken and the other left."
031736
031737 And they said to him, "Where, Lord?" He said to them, "Where the body is, there the eagles will be gathered together."
031801 And he told them a parable, to the effect that they ought always to pray and not lose heart.
031802 He said, "In a certain city there was a judge who neither feared God nor regarded man;
031803 and there was a widow in that city who kept coming to him and saying, 'Vindicate me against my adversary.'
031804 For a while he refused; but afterward he said to himself, 'Though I neither fear God nor regard man,
031805 yet because this widow bothers me, I will vindicate her, or she will wear me out by her continual coming.'"
031806 And the Lord said, "Hear what the unrighteous judge says.
031807 And will not God vindicate his elect, who cry to him day and night? Will he delay long over them?
031808 I tell you, he will vindicate them speedily. Nevertheless, when the Son of man comes, will he find faith on earth?"
031809 He also told this parable to some who trusted in themselves that they were righteous and despised others:
031810 "Two men went up into the temple to pray, one a Pharisee and the other a tax collector.
031811 The Pharisee stood and prayed thus with himself, 'God, I thank thee that I am not like other men, extortioners, unjust, adulterers, or even like this tax collector.
031812 I fast twice a week, I give tithes of all that I get.'
031813 But the tax collector, standing far off, would not even lift up his eyes to heaven, but beat his breast, saying, 'God, be merciful to me a sinner!'
031814 I tell you, this man went down to his house justified rather than the other; for every one who exalts himself will be humbled, but he who humbles himself will be exalted."
031815 Now they were bringing even infants to him that he might touch them; and when the disciples saw it, they rebuked them.
031816 But Jesus called them to him, saying, "Let the children come to me, and do not hinder them; for to such belongs the kingdom of God.
031817 Truly, I say to you, whoever does not receive the kingdom of God like a child shall not enter it."
031818 And a ruler asked him, "Good Teacher, what shall I do to inherit eternal life?"
031819 And Jesus said to him, "Why do you call me good? No one is good but God alone.
031820 You know the commandments: 'Do not commit adultery, Do not kill, Do not steal, Do not bear false witness, Honor your father and mother.'"
031821 And he said, "All these I have observed from my youth."
031822 And when Jesus heard it, he said to him, "One thing you still lack. Sell all that you have and distribute to the poor, and you will have treasure in heaven; and come, follow me."
031823 But when he heard this he became sad, for he was very rich.
031824 Jesus looking at him said, "How hard it is for those who have riches to enter the kingdom of God!
031825 For it is easier for a camel to go through the eye of a needle than for a rich man to enter the kingdom of God."
031826 Those who heard it said, "Then who can be saved?"
031827 But he said, "What is impossible with men is possible with God."
031828 And Peter said, "Lo, we have left our homes and followed you."
031829 And he said to them, "Truly, I say to you, there is no man who has left house or wife or brothers or parents or children, for the sake of the kingdom of God,
031830 who will not receive manifold more in this time, and in the age to come eternal life."
031831 And taking the twelve, he said to them, "Behold, we are going up to Jerusalem, and everything that is written of the Son of man by the prophets will be accomplished.
031832 For he will be delivered to the Gentiles, and will be mocked and shamefully treated and spit upon;
031833 they will scourge him and kill him, and on the third day he will rise."
031834 But they understood none of these things; this saying was hid from them, and they did not grasp what was said.
031835 As he drew near to Jericho, a blind man was sitting by the roadside begging;
031836 and hearing a multitude going by, he inquired what this meant.
031837 They told him, "Jesus of Nazareth is passing by."
031838 And he cried, "Jesus, Son of David, have mercy on me!"
031839 And those who were in front rebuked him, telling him to be silent; but he cried out all the more, "Son of David, have mercy on me!"
031840 And Jesus stopped, and commanded him to be brought to him; and when he came near, he asked him,
031841 "What do you want me to do for you?" He said, "Lord, let me receive my sight."
031842 And Jesus said to him, "Receive your sight; your faith has made you well."
031843 And immediately he received his sight and followed him, glorifying God; and all the people, when they saw it, gave praise to God.
031901 He entered Jericho and was passing through.
031902 And there was a man named Zacchae'us; he was a chief tax collector, and rich.
031903 And he sought to see who Jesus was, but could not, on account of the crowd, because he was small of stature.
031904 So he ran on ahead and climbed up into a sycamore tree to see him, for he was to pass that way.
031905 And when Jesus came to the place, he looked up and said to him, "Zacchae'us, make haste and come down; for I must stay at your house today."
031906 So he made haste and came down, and received him joyfully.
031907 And when they saw it they all murmured, "He has gone in to be the guest of a man who is a sinner."
031908 And Zacchae'us stood and said to the Lord, "Behold, Lord, the half of my goods I give to the poor; and if I have defrauded any one of anything, I restore it fourfold."
031909 And Jesus said to him, "Today salvation has come to this house, since he also is a son of Abraham.
031910 For the Son of man came to seek and to save the lost."
031911 As they heard these things, he proceeded to tell a parable, because he was near to Jerusalem, and because they supposed that the kingdom of God was to appear immediately.
031912 He said therefore, "A nobleman went into a far country to receive a kingdom and then return.
031913 Calling ten of his servants, he gave them ten pounds, and said to them, 'Trade with these till I come.'
031914 But his citizens hated him and sent an embassy after him, saying, 'We do not want this man to reign over us.'
031915 When he returned, having received the kingdom, he commanded these servants, to whom he had given the money, to be called to him, that he might know what they had gained by trading.
031916 The first came before him, saying, 'Lord, your pound has made ten pounds more.'
031917 And he said to him, 'Well done, good servant! Because you have been faithful in a very little, you shall have authority over ten cities.'
031918 And the second came, saying, 'Lord, your pound has made five pounds.'
031919 And he said to him, 'And you are to be over five cities.'
031920 Then another came, saying, 'Lord, here is your pound, which I kept laid away in a napkin;
031921 for I was afraid of you, because you are a severe man; you take up what you did not lay down, and reap what you did not sow.'
031922 He said to him, 'I will condemn you out of your own mouth, you wicked servant! You knew that I was a severe man, taking up what I did not lay down and reaping what I did not sow?
031923 Why then did you not put my money into the bank, and at my coming I should have collected it with interest?'
031924 And he said to those who stood by, 'Take the pound from him, and give it to him who has the ten pounds.'
031925 (And they said to him, 'Lord, he has ten pounds!')
031926 'I tell you, that to every one who has will more be given; but from him who has not, even what he has will be taken away.
031927 But as for these enemies of mine, who did not want me to reign over them, bring them here and slay them before me.'"
031928 And when he had said this, he went on ahead, going up to Jerusalem.
031929 When he drew near to Beth'phage and Bethany, at the mount that is called Olivet, he sent two of the disciples,
031930 saying, "Go into the village opposite, where on entering you will find a colt tied, on which no one has ever yet sat; untie it and bring it here.
031931 If any one asks you, 'Why are you untying it?' you shall say this, 'The Lord has need of it.'"
031932 So those who were sent went away and found it as he had told them.
031933 And as they were untying the colt, its owners said to them, "Why are you untying the colt?"
031934 And they said, "The Lord has need of it."
031935 And they brought it to Jesus, and throwing their garments on the colt they set Jesus upon it.
031936 And as he rode along, they spread their garments on the road.
031937 As he was now drawing near, at the descent of the Mount of Olives, the whole multitude of the disciples began to rejoice and praise God with a loud voice for all the mighty works that they had seen,
031938 saying, "Blessed is the King who comes in the name of the Lord! Peace in heaven and glory in the highest!"
031939 And some of the Pharisees in the multitude said to him, "Teacher, rebuke your disciples."
031940 He answered, "I tell you, if these were silent, the very stones would cry out."
031941 And when he drew near and saw the city he wept over it,
031942 saying, "Would that even today you knew the things that make for peace! But now they are hid from your eyes.
031943 For the days shall come upon you, when your enemies will cast up a bank about you and surround you, and hem you in on every side,
031944 and dash you to the ground, you and your children within you, and they will not leave one stone upon another in you; because you did not know the time of your visitation."
031945 And he entered the temple and began to drive out those who sold,
031946 saying to them, "It is written, 'My house shall be a house of prayer'; but you have made it a den of robbers."
031947 And he was teaching daily in the temple. The chief priests and the scribes and the principal men of the people sought to destroy him;
031948 but they did not find anything they could do, for all the people hung upon his words.
032001 One day, as he was teaching the people in the temple and preaching the gospel, the chief priests and the scribes with the elders came up
032002 and said to him, "Tell us by what authority you do these things, or who it is that gave you this authority."
032003 He answered them, "I also will ask you a question; now tell me,
032004 Was the baptism of John from heaven or from men?"
032005 And they discussed it with one another, saying, "If we say, 'From heaven,' he will say, 'Why did you not believe him?'
032006 But if we say, 'From men,' all the people will stone us; for they are convinced that John was a prophet."
032007 So they answered that they did not know whence it was.
032008 And Jesus said to them, "Neither will I tell you by what authority I do these things."
032009 And he began to tell the people this parable: "A man planted a vineyard, and let it out to tenants, and went into another country for a long while.
032010 When the time came, he sent a servant to the tenants, that they should give him some of the fruit of the vineyard; but the tenants beat him, and sent him away empty-handed.
032011 And he sent another servant; him also they beat and treated shamefully, and sent him away empty-handed.
032012 And he sent yet a third; this one they wounded and cast out.
032013 Then the owner of the vineyard said, 'What shall I do? I will send my beloved son; it may be they will respect him.'
032014 But when the tenants saw him, they said to themselves, 'This is the heir; let us kill him, that the inheritance may be ours.'
032015 And they cast him out of the vineyard and killed him. What then will the owner of the vineyard do to them?
032016 He will come and destroy those tenants, and give the vineyard to others." When they heard this, they said, "God forbid!"
032017 But he looked at them and said, "What then is this that is written: 'The very stone which the builders rejected has become the head of the corner'?
032018 Every one who falls on that stone will be broken to pieces; but when it falls on any one it will crush him."
032019 The scribes and the chief priests tried to lay hands on him at that very hour, but they feared the people; for they perceived that he had told this parable against them.
032020 So they watched him, and sent spies, who pretended to be sincere, that they might take hold of what he said, so as to deliver him up to the authority and jurisdiction of the governor.
032021 They asked him, "Teacher, we know that you speak and teach rightly, and show no partiality, but truly teach the way of God.
032022 Is it lawful for us to give tribute to Caesar, or not?"
032023 But he perceived their craftiness, and said to them,
032024 "Show me a coin. Whose likeness and inscription has it?" They said, "Caesar's."
032025 He said to them, "Then render to Caesar the things that are Caesar's, and to God the things that are God's."
032026 And they were not able in the presence of the people to catch him by what he said; but marveling at his answer they were silent.
032027 There came to him some Sadducees, those who say that there is no resurrection,
032028 and they asked him a question, saying, "Teacher, Moses wrote for us that if a man's brother dies, having a wife but no children, the man must take the wife and raise up children for his brother.
032029 Now there were seven brothers; the first took a wife, and died without children;
032030 and the second
032031 and the third took her, and likewise all seven left no children and died.
032032 Afterward the woman also died.
032033 In the resurrection, therefore, whose wife will the woman be? For the seven had her as wife."
032034 And Jesus said to them, "The sons of this age marry and are given in marriage;
032035 but those who are accounted worthy to attain to that age and to the resurrection from the dead neither marry nor are given in marriage,
032036 for they cannot die any more, because they are equal to angels and are sons of God, being sons of the resurrection.
032037 But that the dead are raised, even Moses showed, in the passage about the bush, where he calls the Lord the God of Abraham and the God of Isaac and the God of Jacob.
032038 Now he is not God of the dead, but of the living; for all live to him."
032039 And some of the scribes answered, "Teacher, you have spoken well."
032040 For they no longer dared to ask him any question.
032041 But he said to them, "How can they say that the Christ is David's son?
032042 For David himself says in the Book of Psalms, 'The Lord said to my Lord, Sit at my right hand,
032043 till I make thy enemies a stool for thy feet.'
032044 David thus calls him Lord; so how is he his son?"
032045 And in the hearing of all the people he said to his disciples,
032046 "Beware of the scribes, who like to go about in long robes, and love salutations in the market places and the best seats in the synagogues and the places of honor at feasts,
032047 who devour widows' houses and for a pretense make long prayers. They will receive the greater condemnation."
032101 He looked up and saw the rich putting their gifts into the treasury;
032102 and he saw a poor widow put in two copper coins.
032103 And he said, "Truly I tell you, this poor widow has put in more than all of them;
032104 for they all contributed out of their abundance, but she out of her poverty put in all the living that she had."
032105 And as some spoke of the temple, how it was adorned with noble stones and offerings, he said,
032106 "As for these things which you see, the days will come when there shall not be left here one stone upon another that will not be thrown down."
032107 And they asked him, "Teacher, when will this be, and what will be the sign when this is about to take place?"
032108 And he said, "Take heed that you are not led astray; for many will come in my name, saying, 'I am he!' and, 'The time is at hand!' Do not go after them.
032109 And when you hear of wars and tumults, do not be terrified; for this must first take place, but the end will not be at once."
032110 Then he said to them, "Nation will rise against nation, and kingdom against kingdom;
032111 there will be great earthquakes, and in various places famines and pestilences; and there will be terrors and great signs from heaven.
032112 But before all this they will lay their hands on you and persecute you, delivering you up to the synagogues and prisons, and you will be brought before kings and governors for my name's sake.
032113 This will be a time for you to bear testimony.
032114 Settle it therefore in your minds, not to meditate beforehand how to answer;
032115 for I will give you a mouth and wisdom, which none of your adversaries will be able to withstand or contradict.
032116 You will be delivered up even by parents and brothers and kinsmen and friends, and some of you they will put to death;
032117 you will be hated by all for my name's sake.
032118 But not a hair of your head will perish.
032119 By your endurance you will gain your lives.
032120 "But when you see Jerusalem surrounded by armies, then know that its desolation has come near.
032121 Then let those who are in Judea flee to the mountains, and let those who are inside the city depart, and let not those who are out in the country enter it;
032122 for these are days of vengeance, to fulfil all that is written.
032123 Alas for those who are with child and for those who give suck in those days! For great distress shall be upon the earth and wrath upon this people;
032124 they will fall by the edge of the sword, and be led captive among all nations; and Jerusalem will be trodden down by the Gentiles, until the times of the Gentiles are fulfilled.
032125 "And there will be signs in sun and moon and stars, and upon the earth distress of nations in perplexity at the roaring of the sea and the waves,
032126 men fainting with fear and with foreboding of what is coming on the world; for the powers of the heavens will be shaken.
032127 And then they will see the Son of man coming in a cloud with power and great glory.
032128 Now when these things begin to take place, look up and raise your heads, because your redemption is drawing near."
032129 And he told them a parable: "Look at the fig tree, and all the trees;
032130 as soon as they come out in leaf, you see for yourselves and know that the summer is already near.
032131 So also, when you see these things taking place, you know that the kingdom of God is near.
032132 Truly, I say to you, this generation will not pass away till all has taken place.
032133 Heaven and earth will pass away, but my words will not pass away.
032134 "But take heed to yourselves lest your hearts be weighed down with dissipation and drunkenness and cares of this life, and that day come upon you suddenly like a snare;
032135 for it will come upon all who dwell upon the face of the whole earth.
032136 But watch at all times, praying that you may have strength to escape all these things that will take place, and to stand before the Son of man."
032137 And every day he was teaching in the temple, but at night he went out and lodged on the mount called Olivet.
032138 And early in the morning all the people came to him in the temple to hear him.
032201 Now the feast of Unleavened Bread drew near, which is called the Passover.
032202 And the chief priests and the scribes were seeking how to put him to death; for they feared the people.
032203 Then Satan entered into Judas called Iscariot, who was of the number of the twelve;
032204 he went away and conferred with the chief priests and officers how he might betray him to them.
032205 And they were glad, and engaged to give him money.
032206 So he agreed, and sought an opportunity to betray him to them in the absence of the multitude.
032207 Then came the day of Unleavened Bread, on which the passover lamb had to be sacrificed.
032208 So Jesus sent Peter and John, saying, "Go and prepare the passover for us, that we may eat it."
032209 They said to him, "Where will you have us prepare it?"
032210 He said to them, "Behold, when you have entered the city, a man carrying a jar of water will meet you; follow him into the house which he enters,
032211 and tell the householder, 'The Teacher says to you, Where is the guest room, where I am to eat the passover with my disciples?'
032212 And he will show you a large upper room furnished; there make ready."
032213 And they went, and found it as he had told them; and they prepared the passover.
032214 And when the hour came, he sat at table, and the apostles with him.
032215 And he said to them, "I have earnestly desired to eat this passover with you before I suffer;
032216 for I tell you I shall not eat it until it is fulfilled in the kingdom of God."
032217 And he took a cup, and when he had given thanks he said, "Take this, and divide it among yourselves;
032218 for I tell you that from now on I shall not drink of the fruit of the vine until the kingdom of God comes."
032219 And he took bread, and when he had given thanks he broke it and gave it to them, saying, "This is my body which is given for you. Do this in remembrance of me."
032220 And likewise the cup after supper, saying, "This cup which is poured out for you is the new covenant in my blood.
032221 But behold the hand of him who betrays me is with me on the table.
032222 For the Son of man goes as it has been determined; but woe to that man by whom he is betrayed!"
032223 And they began to question one another, which of them it was that would do this.
032224 A dispute also arose among them, which of them was to be regarded as the greatest.
032225 And he said to them, "The kings of the Gentiles exercise lordship over them; and those in authority over them are called benefactors.
032226 But not so with you; rather let the greatest among you become as the youngest, and the leader as one who serves.
032227 For which is the greater, one who sits at table, or one who serves? Is it not the one who sits at table? But I am among you as one who serves.
032228 "You are those who have continued with me in my trials;
032229 and I assign to you, as my Father assigned to me, a kingdom,
032230 that you may eat and drink at my table in my kingdom, and sit on thrones judging the twelve tribes of Israel.
032231 "Simon, Simon, behold, Satan demanded to have you, that he might sift you like wheat,
032232 but I have prayed for you that your faith may not fail; and when you have turned again, strengthen your brethren."
032233 And he said to him, "Lord, I am ready to go with you to prison and to death."
032234 He said, "I tell you, Peter, the cock will not crow this day, until you three times deny that you know me."
032235 And he said to them, "When I sent you out with no purse or bag or sandals, did you lack anything?" They said, "Nothing."
032236 He said to them, "But now, let him who has a purse take it, and likewise a bag. And let him who has no sword sell his mantle and buy one.
032237 For I tell you that this scripture must be fulfilled in me, 'And he was reckoned with transgressors'; for what is written about me has its fulfilment."
032238 And they said, "Look, Lord, here are two swords." And he said to them, "It is enough."
