032239 And he came out, and went, as was his custom, to the Mount of Olives; and the disciples followed him.
032240 And when he came to the place he said to them, "Pray that you may not enter into temptation."
032241 And he withdrew from them about a stone's throw, and knelt down and prayed,
032242 "Father, if thou art willing, remove this cup from me; nevertheless not my will, but thine, be done."
032243
032244
032245 And when he rose from prayer, he came to the disciples and found them sleeping for sorrow,
032246 and he said to them, "Why do you sleep? Rise and pray that you may not enter into temptation."
032247 While he was still speaking, there came a crowd, and the man called Judas, one of the twelve, was leading them. He drew near to Jesus to kiss him;
032248 but Jesus said to him, "Judas, would you betray the Son of man with a kiss?"
032249 And when those who were about him saw what would follow, they said, "Lord, shall we strike with the sword?"
032250 And one of them struck the slave of the high priest and cut off his right ear.
032251 But Jesus said, "No more of this!" And he touched his ear and healed him.
032252 Then Jesus said to the chief priests and officers of the temple and elders, who had come out against him, "Have you come out as against a robber, with swords and clubs?
032253 When I was with you day after day in the temple, you did not lay hands on me. But this is your hour, and the power of darkness."
032254 Then they seized him and led him away, bringing him into the high priest's house. Peter followed at a distance;
032255 and when they had kindled a fire in the middle of the courtyard and sat down together, Peter sat among them.
032256 Then a maid, seeing him as he sat in the light and gazing at him, said, "This man also was with him."
032257 But he denied it, saying, "Woman, I do not know him."
032258 And a little later some one else saw him and said, "You also are one of them." But Peter said, "Man, I am not."
032259 And after an interval of about an hour still another insisted, saying, "Certainly this man also was with him; for he is a Galilean."
032260 But Peter said, "Man, I do not know what you are saying." And immediately, while he was still speaking, the cock crowed.
032261 And the Lord turned and looked at Peter. And Peter remembered the word of the Lord, how he had said to him, "Before the cock crows today, you will deny me three times."
032262 And he went out and wept bitterly.
032263 Now the men who were holding Jesus mocked him and beat him;
032264 they also blindfolded him and asked him, "Prophesy! Who is it that struck you?"
032265 And they spoke many other words against him, reviling him.
032266 When day came, the assembly of the elders of the people gathered together, both chief priests and scribes; and they led him away to their council, and they said,
032267 "If you are the Christ, tell us." But he said to them, "If I tell you, you will not believe;
032268 and if I ask you, you will not answer.
032269 But from now on the Son of man shall be seated at the right hand of the power of God."
032270 And they all said, "Are you the Son of God, then?" And he said to them, "You say that I am."
032271 And they said, "What further testimony do we need? We have heard it ourselves from his own lips."
032301 Then the whole company of them arose, and brought him before Pilate.
032302 And they began to accuse him, saying, "We found this man perverting our nation, and forbidding us to give tribute to Caesar, and saying that he himself is Christ a king."
032303 And Pilate asked him, "Are you the King of the Jews?" And he answered him, "You have said so."
032304 And Pilate said to the chief priests and the multitudes, "I find no crime in this man."
032305 But they were urgent, saying, "He stirs up the people, teaching throughout all Judea, from Galilee even to this place."
032306 When Pilate heard this, he asked whether the man was a Galilean.
032307 And when he learned that he belonged to Herod's jurisdiction, he sent him over to Herod, who was himself in Jerusalem at that time.
032308 When Herod saw Jesus, he was very glad, for he had long desired to see him, because he had heard about him, and he was hoping to see some sign done by him.
032309 So he questioned him at some length; but he made no answer.
032310 The chief priests and the scribes stood by, vehemently accusing him.
032311 And Herod with his soldiers treated him with contempt and mocked him; then, arraying him in gorgeous apparel, he sent him back to Pilate.
032312 And Herod and Pilate became friends with each other that very day, for before this they had been at enmity with each other.
032313 Pilate then called together the chief priests and the rulers and the people,
032314 and said to them, "You brought me this man as one who was perverting the people; and after examining him before you, behold, I did not find this man guilty of any of your charges against him;
032315 neither did Herod, for he sent him back to us. Behold, nothing deserving death has been done by him;
032316 I will therefore chastise him and release him."
032317
032318 But they all cried out together, "Away with this man, and release to us Barab'bas" --
032319 a man who had been thrown into prison for an insurrection started in the city, and for murder.
032320 Pilate addressed them once more, desiring to release Jesus;
032321 but they shouted out, "Crucify, crucify him!"
032322 A third time he said to them, "Why, what evil has he done? I have found in him no crime deserving death; I will therefore chastise him and release him."
032323 But they were urgent, demanding with loud cries that he should be crucified. And their voices prevailed.
032324 So Pilate gave sentence that their demand should be granted.
032325 He released the man who had been thrown into prison for insurrection and murder, whom they asked for; but Jesus he delivered up to their will.
032326 And as they led him away, they seized one Simon of Cyre'ne, who was coming in from the country, and laid on him the cross, to carry it behind Jesus.
032327 And there followed him a great multitude of the people, and of women who bewailed and lamented him.
032328 But Jesus turning to them said, "Daughters of Jerusalem, do not weep for me, but weep for yourselves and for your children.
032329 For behold, the days are coming when they will say, 'Blessed are the barren, and the wombs that never bore, and the breasts that never gave suck!'
032330 Then they will begin to say to the mountains, 'Fall on us'; and to the hills, 'Cover us.'
032331 For if they do this when the wood is green, what will happen when it is dry?"
032332 Two others also, who were criminals, were led away to be put to death with him.
032333 And when they came to the place which is called The Skull, there they crucified him, and the criminals, one on the right and one on the left.
032334 And Jesus said, "Father, forgive them; for they know not what they do." And they cast lots to divide his garments.
032335 And the people stood by, watching; but the rulers scoffed at him, saying, "He saved others; let him save himself, if he is the Christ of God, his Chosen One!"
032336 The soldiers also mocked him, coming up and offering him vinegar,
032337 and saying, "If you are the King of the Jews, save yourself!"
032338 There was also an inscription over him, "This is the King of the Jews."
032339 One of the criminals who were hanged railed at him, saying, "Are you not the Christ? Save yourself and us!"
032340 But the other rebuked him, saying, "Do you not fear God, since you are under the same sentence of condemnation?
032341 And we indeed justly; for we are receiving the due reward of our deeds; but this man has done nothing wrong."
032342 And he said, "Jesus, remember me when you come into your kingdom."
032343 And he said to him, "Truly, I say to you, today you will be with me in Paradise."
032344 It was now about the sixth hour, and there was darkness over the whole land until the ninth hour,
032345 while the sun's light failed; and the curtain of the temple was torn in two.
032346 Then Jesus, crying with a loud voice, said, "Father, into thy hands I commit my spirit!" And having said this he breathed his last.
032347 Now when the centurion saw what had taken place, he praised God, and said, "Certainly this man was innocent!"
032348 And all the multitudes who assembled to see the sight, when they saw what had taken place, returned home beating their breasts.
032349 And all his acquaintances and the women who had followed him from Galilee stood at a distance and saw these things.
032350 Now there was a man named Joseph from the Jewish town of Arimathe'a. He was a member of the council, a good and righteous man,
032351 who had not consented to their purpose and deed, and he was looking for the kingdom of God.
032352 This man went to Pilate and asked for the body of Jesus.
032353 Then he took it down and wrapped it in a linen shroud, and laid him in a rock-hewn tomb, where no one had ever yet been laid.
032354 It was the day of Preparation, and the sabbath was beginning.
032355 The women who had come with him from Galilee followed, and saw the tomb, and how his body was laid;
032356 then they returned, and prepared spices and ointments. On the sabbath they rested according to the commandment.
032401 But on the first day of the week, at early dawn, they went to the tomb, taking the spices which they had prepared.
032402 And they found the stone rolled away from the tomb,
032403 but when they went in they did not find the body.
032404 While they were perplexed about this, behold, two men stood by them in dazzling apparel;
032405 and as they were frightened and bowed their faces to the ground, the men said to them, "Why do you seek the living among the dead?
032406 Remember how he told you, while he was still in Galilee,
032407 that the Son of man must be delivered into the hands of sinful men, and be crucified, and on the third day rise."
032408 And they remembered his words,
032409 and returning from the tomb they told all this to the eleven and to all the rest.
032410 Now it was Mary Mag'dalene and Jo-an'na and Mary the mother of James and the other women with them who told this to the apostles;
032411 but these words seemed to them an idle tale, and they did not believe them.
032412
032413 That very day two of them were going to a village named Emma'us, about seven miles from Jerusalem,
032414 and talking with each other about all these things that had happened.
032415 While they were talking and discussing together, Jesus himself drew near and went with them.
032416 But their eyes were kept from recognizing him.
032417 And he said to them, "What is this conversation which you are holding with each other as you walk?" And they stood still, looking sad.
032418 Then one of them, named Cle'opas, answered him, "Are you the only visitor to Jerusalem who does not know the things that have happened there in these days?"
032419 And he said to them, "What things?" And they said to him, "Concerning Jesus of Nazareth, who was a prophet mighty in deed and word before God and all the people,
032420 and how our chief priests and rulers delivered him up to be condemned to death, and crucified him.
032421 But we had hoped that he was the one to redeem Israel. Yes, and besides all this, it is now the third day since this happened.
032422 Moreover, some women of our company amazed us. They were at the tomb early in the morning
032423 and did not find his body; and they came back saying that they had even seen a vision of angels, who said that he was alive.
032424 Some of those who were with us went to the tomb, and found it just as the women had said; but him they did not see."
032425 And he said to them, "O foolish men, and slow of heart to believe all that the prophets have spoken!
032426 Was it not necessary that the Christ should suffer these things and enter into his glory?"
032427 And beginning with Moses and all the prophets, he interpreted to them in all the scriptures the things concerning himself.
032428 So they drew near to the village to which they were going. He appeared to be going further,
032429 but they constrained him, saying, "Stay with us, for it is toward evening and the day is now far spent." So he went in to stay with them.
032430 When he was at table with them, he took the bread and blessed, and broke it, and gave it to them.
032431 And their eyes were opened and they recognized him; and he vanished out of their sight.
032432 They said to each other, "Did not our hearts burn within us while he talked to us on the road, while he opened to us the scriptures?"
032433 And they rose that same hour and returned to Jerusalem; and they found the eleven gathered together and those who were with them,
032434 who said, "The Lord has risen indeed, and has appeared to Simon!"
032435 Then they told what had happened on the road, and how he was known to them in the breaking of the bread.
032436 As they were saying this, Jesus himself stood among them.
032437 But they were startled and frightened, and supposed that they saw a spirit.
032438 And he said to them, "Why are you troubled, and why do questionings rise in your hearts?
032439 See my hands and my feet, that it is I myself; handle me, and see; for a spirit has not flesh and bones as you see that I have."
032440
032441 And while they still disbelieved for joy, and wondered, he said to them, "Have you anything here to eat?"
032442 They gave him a piece of broiled fish,
032443 and he took it and ate before them.
032444 Then he said to them, "These are my words which I spoke to you, while I was still with you, that everything written about me in the law of Moses and the prophets and the psalms must be fulfilled."
032445 Then he opened their minds to understand the scriptures,
032446 and said to them, "Thus it is written, that the Christ should suffer and on the third day rise from the dead,
032447 and that repentance and forgiveness of sins should be preached in his name to all nations, beginning from Jerusalem.
032448 You are witnesses of these things.
032449 And behold, I send the promise of my Father upon you; but stay in the city, until you are clothed with power from on high."
032450 Then he led them out as far as Bethany, and lifting up his hands he blessed them.
032451 While he blessed them, he parted from them, and was carried up into heaven.
032452 And they returned to Jerusalem with great joy,
032453 and were continually in the temple blessing God.
040101 In the beginning was the Word, and the Word was with God, and the Word was God.
040102 He was in the beginning with God;
040103 all things were made through him, and without him was not anything made that was made.
040104 In him was life, and the life was the light of men.
040105 The light shines in the darkness, and the darkness has not overcome it.
040106 There was a man sent from God, whose name was John.
040107 He came for testimony, to bear witness to the light, that all might believe through him.
040108 He was not the light, but came to bear witness to the light.
040109 The true light that enlightens every man was coming into the world.
040110 He was in the world, and the world was made through him, yet the world knew him not.
040111 He came to his own home, and his own people received him not.
040112 But to all who received him, who believed in his name, he gave power to become children of God;
040113 who were born, not of blood nor of the will of the flesh nor of the will of man, but of God.
040114 And the Word became flesh and dwelt among us, full of grace and truth; we have beheld his glory, glory as of the only Son from the Father.
040115 (John bore witness to him, and cried, "This was he of whom I said, 'He who comes after me ranks before me, for he was before me.'")
040116 And from his fulness have we all received, grace upon grace.
040117 For the law was given through Moses; grace and truth came through Jesus Christ.
040118 No one has ever seen God; the only Son, who is in the bosom of the Father, he has made him known.
040119 And this is the testimony of John, when the Jews sent priests and Levites from Jerusalem to ask him, "Who are you?"
040120 He confessed, he did not deny, but confessed, "I am not the Christ."
040121 And they asked him, "What then? Are you Elijah?" He said, "I am not." "Are you the prophet?" And he answered, "No."
040122 They said to him then, "Who are you? Let us have an answer for those who sent us. What do you say about yourself?"
040123 He said, "I am the voice of one crying in the wilderness, 'Make straight the way of the Lord,' as the prophet Isaiah said."
040124 Now they had been sent from the Pharisees.
040125 They asked him, "Then why are you baptizing, if you are neither the Christ, nor Elijah, nor the prophet?"
040126 John answered them, "I baptize with water; but among you stands one whom you do not know,
040127 even he who comes after me, the thong of whose sandal I am not worthy to untie."
040128 This took place in Bethany beyond the Jordan, where John was baptizing.
040129 The next day he saw Jesus coming toward him, and said, "Behold, the Lamb of God, who takes away the sin of the world!
040130 This is he of whom I said, 'After me comes a man who ranks before me, for he was before me.'
040131 I myself did not know him; but for this I came baptizing with water, that he might be revealed to Israel."
040132 And John bore witness, "I saw the Spirit descend as a dove from heaven, and it remained on him.
040133 I myself did not know him; but he who sent me to baptize with water said to me, 'He on whom you see the Spirit descend and remain, this is he who baptizes with the Holy Spirit.'
040134 And I have seen and have borne witness that this is the Son of God."
040135 The next day again John was standing with two of his disciples;
040136 and he looked at Jesus as he walked, and said, "Behold, the Lamb of God!"
040137 The two disciples heard him say this, and they followed Jesus.
040138 Jesus turned, and saw them following, and said to them, "What do you seek?" And they said to him, "Rabbi" (which means Teacher), "where are you staying?"
040139 He said to them, "Come and see." They came and saw where he was staying; and they stayed with him that day, for it was about the tenth hour.
040140 One of the two who heard John speak, and followed him, was Andrew, Simon Peter's brother.
040141 He first found his brother Simon, and said to him, "We have found the Messiah" (which means Christ).
040142 He brought him to Jesus. Jesus looked at him, and said, "So you are Simon the son of John? You shall be called Cephas" (which means Peter).
040143 The next day Jesus decided to go to Galilee. And he found Philip and said to him, "Follow me."
040144 Now Philip was from Beth-sa'ida, the city of Andrew and Peter.
040145 Philip found Nathan'a-el, and said to him, "We have found him of whom Moses in the law and also the prophets wrote, Jesus of Nazareth, the son of Joseph."
040146 Nathan'a-el said to him, "Can anything good come out of Nazareth?" Philip said to him, "Come and see."
040147 Jesus saw Nathan'a-el coming to him, and said of him, "Behold, an Israelite indeed, in whom is no guile!"
040148 Nathan'a-el said to him, "How do you know me?" Jesus answered him, "Before Philip called you, when you were under the fig tree, I saw you."
040149 Nathan'a-el answered him, "Rabbi, you are the Son of God! You are the King of Israel!"
040150 Jesus answered him, "Because I said to you, I saw you under the fig tree, do you believe? You shall see greater things than these."
040151 And he said to him, "Truly, truly, I say to you, you will see heaven opened, and the angels of God ascending and descending upon the Son of man."
040201 On the third day there was a marriage at Cana in Galilee, and the mother of Jesus was there;
040202 Jesus also was invited to the marriage, with his disciples.
040203 When the wine failed, the mother of Jesus said to him, "They have no wine."
040204 And Jesus said to her, "O woman, what have you to do with me? My hour has not yet come."
040205 His mother said to the servants, "Do whatever he tells you."
040206 Now six stone jars were standing there, for the Jewish rites of purification, each holding twenty or thirty gallons.
040207 Jesus said to them, "Fill the jars with water." And they filled them up to the brim.
040208 He said to them, "Now draw some out, and take it to the steward of the feast." So they took it.
040209 When the steward of the feast tasted the water now become wine, and did not know where it came from (though the servants who had drawn the water knew), the steward of the feast called the bridegroom
040210 and said to him, "Every man serves the good wine first; and when men have drunk freely, then the poor wine; but you have kept the good wine until now."
040211 This, the first of his signs, Jesus did at Cana in Galilee, and manifested his glory; and his disciples believed in him.
040212 After this he went down to Caper'na-um, with his mother and his brothers and his disciples; and there they stayed for a few days.
040213 The Passover of the Jews was at hand, and Jesus went up to Jerusalem.
040214 In the temple he found those who were selling oxen and sheep and pigeons, and the money-changers at their business.
040215 And making a whip of cords, he drove them all, with the sheep and oxen, out of the temple; and he poured out the coins of the money-changers and overturned their tables.
040216 And he told those who sold the pigeons, "Take these things away; you shall not make my Father's house a house of trade."
040217 His disciples remembered that it was written, "Zeal for thy house will consume me."
040218 The Jews then said to him, "What sign have you to show us for doing this?"
040219 Jesus answered them, "Destroy this temple, and in three days I will raise it up."
040220 The Jews then said, "It has taken forty-six years to build this temple, and will you raise it up in three days?"
040221 But he spoke of the temple of his body.
040222 When therefore he was raised from the dead, his disciples remembered that he had said this; and they believed the scripture and the word which Jesus had spoken.
040223 Now when he was in Jerusalem at the Passover feast, many believed in his name when they saw the signs which he did;
040224 but Jesus did not trust himself to them,
040225 because he knew all men and needed no one to bear witness of man; for he himself knew what was in man.
040301 Now there was a man of the Pharisees, named Nicode'mus, a ruler of the Jews.
040302 This man came to Jesus by night and said to him, "Rabbi, we know that you are a teacher come from God; for no one can do these signs that you do, unless God is with him."
040303 Jesus answered him, "Truly, truly, I say to you, unless one is born anew, he cannot see the kingdom of God."
040304 Nicode'mus said to him, "How can a man be born when he is old? Can he enter a second time into his mother's womb and be born?"
040305 Jesus answered, "Truly, truly, I say to you, unless one is born of water and the Spirit, he cannot enter the kingdom of God.
040306 That which is born of the flesh is flesh, and that which is born of the Spirit is spirit.
040307 Do not marvel that I said to you, 'You must be born anew.'
040308 The wind blows where it wills, and you hear the sound of it, but you do not know whence it comes or whither it goes; so it is with every one who is born of the Spirit."
040309 Nicode'mus said to him, "How can this be?"
040310 Jesus answered him, "Are you a teacher of Israel, and yet you do not understand this?
040311 Truly, truly, I say to you, we speak of what we know, and bear witness to what we have seen; but you do not receive our testimony.
040312 If I have told you earthly things and you do not believe, how can you believe if I tell you heavenly things?
040313 No one has ascended into heaven but he who descended from heaven, the Son of man.
040314 And as Moses lifted up the serpent in the wilderness, so must the Son of man be lifted up,
040315 that whoever believes in him may have eternal life."
040316 For God so loved the world that he gave his only Son, that whoever believes in him should not perish but have eternal life.
040317 For God sent the Son into the world, not to condemn the world, but that the world might be saved through him.
040318 He who believes in him is not condemned; he who does not believe is condemned already, because he has not believed in the name of the only Son of God.
040319 And this is the judgment, that the light has come into the world, and men loved darkness rather than light, because their deeds were evil.
040320 For every one who does evil hates the light, and does not come to the light, lest his deeds should be exposed.
040321 But he who does what is true comes to the light, that it may be clearly seen that his deeds have been wrought in God.
040322 After this Jesus and his disciples went into the land of Judea; there he remained with them and baptized.
040323 John also was baptizing at Ae'non near Salim, because there was much water there; and people came and were baptized.
040324 For John had not yet been put in prison.
040325 Now a discussion arose between John's disciples and a Jew over purifying.
040326 And they came to John, and said to him, "Rabbi, he who was with you beyond the Jordan, to whom you bore witness, here he is, baptizing, and all are going to him."
040327 John answered, "No one can receive anything except what is given him from heaven.
040328 You yourselves bear me witness, that I said, I am not the Christ, but I have been sent before him.
040329 He who has the bride is the bridegroom; the friend of the bridegroom, who stands and hears him, rejoices greatly at the bridegroom's voice; therefore this joy of mine is now full.
040330 He must increase, but I must decrease."
040331 He who comes from above is above all; he who is of the earth belongs to the earth, and of the earth he speaks; he who comes from heaven is above all.
040332 He bears witness to what he has seen and heard, yet no one receives his testimony;
040333 he who receives his testimony sets his seal to this, that God is true.
040334 For he whom God has sent utters the words of God, for it is not by measure that he gives the Spirit;
040335 the Father loves the Son, and has given all things into his hand.
040336 He who believes in the Son has eternal life; he who does not obey the Son shall not see life, but the wrath of God rests upon him.
040401 Now when the Lord knew that the Pharisees had heard that Jesus was making and baptizing more disciples than John
040402 (although Jesus himself did not baptize, but only his disciples),
040403 he left Judea and departed again to Galilee.
040404 He had to pass through Samar'ia.
040405 So he came to a city of Samar'ia, called Sy'char, near the field that Jacob gave to his son Joseph.
040406 Jacob's well was there, and so Jesus, wearied as he was with his journey, sat down beside the well. It was about the sixth hour.
040407 There came a woman of Samar'ia to draw water. Jesus said to her, "Give me a drink."
040408 For his disciples had gone away into the city to buy food.
040409 The Samaritan woman said to him, "How is it that you, a Jew, ask a drink of me, a woman of Samar'ia?" For Jews have no dealings with Samaritans.
040410 Jesus answered her, "If you knew the gift of God, and who it is that is saying to you, 'Give me a drink,' you would have asked him, and he would have given you living water."
040411 The woman said to him, "Sir, you have nothing to draw with, and the well is deep; where do you get that living water?
040412 Are you greater than our father Jacob, who gave us the well, and drank from it himself, and his sons, and his cattle?"
040413 Jesus said to her, "Every one who drinks of this water will thirst again,
040414 but whoever drinks of the water that I shall give him will never thirst; the water that I shall give him will become in him a spring of water welling up to eternal life."
040415 The woman said to him, "Sir, give me this water, that I may not thirst, nor come here to draw."
040416 Jesus said to her, "Go, call your husband, and come here."
040417 The woman answered him, "I have no husband." Jesus said to her, "You are right in saying, 'I have no husband';
040418 for you have had five husbands, and he whom you now have is not your husband; this you said truly."
040419 The woman said to him, "Sir, I perceive that you are a prophet.
040420 Our fathers worshiped on this mountain; and you say that in Jerusalem is the place where men ought to worship."
040421 Jesus said to her, "Woman, believe me, the hour is coming when neither on this mountain nor in Jerusalem will you worship the Father.
040422 You worship what you do not know; we worship what we know, for salvation is from the Jews.
040423 But the hour is coming, and now is, when the true worshipers will worship the Father in spirit and truth, for such the Father seeks to worship him.
040424 God is spirit, and those who worship him must worship in spirit and truth."
040425 The woman said to him, "I know that Messiah is coming (he who is called Christ); when he comes, he will show us all things."
040426 Jesus said to her, "I who speak to you am he."
040427 Just then his disciples came. They marveled that he was talking with a woman, but none said, "What do you wish?" or, "Why are you talking with her?"
040428 So the woman left her water jar, and went away into the city, and said to the people,
040429 "Come, see a man who told me all that I ever did. Can this be the Christ?"
040430 They went out of the city and were coming to him.
040431 Meanwhile the disciples besought him, saying, "Rabbi, eat."
040432 But he said to them, "I have food to eat of which you do not know."
040433 So the disciples said to one another, "Has any one brought him food?"
040434 Jesus said to them, "My food is to do the will of him who sent me, and to accomplish his work.
040435 Do you not say, 'There are yet four months, then comes the harvest'? I tell you, lift up your eyes, and see how the fields are already white for harvest.
040436 He who reaps receives wages, and gathers fruit for eternal life, so that sower and reaper may rejoice together.
040437 For here the saying holds true, 'One sows and another reaps.'
040438 I sent you to reap that for which you did not labor; others have labored, and you have entered into their labor."
040439 Many Samaritans from that city believed in him because of the woman's testimony, "He told me all that I ever did."
040440 So when the Samaritans came to him, they asked him to stay with them; and he stayed there two days.
040441 And many more believed because of his word.
040442 They said to the woman, "It is no longer because of your words that we believe, for we have heard for ourselves, and we know that this is indeed the Savior of the world."
040443 After the two days he departed to Galilee.
040444 For Jesus himself testified that a prophet has no honor in his own country.
040445 So when he came to Galilee, the Galileans welcomed him, having seen all that he had done in Jerusalem at the feast, for they too had gone to the feast.
040446 So he came again to Cana in Galilee, where he had made the water wine. And at Caper'na-um there was an official whose son was ill.
040447 When he heard that Jesus had come from Judea to Galilee, he went and begged him to come down and heal his son, for he was at the point of death.
040448 Jesus therefore said to him, "Unless you see signs and wonders you will not believe."
040449 The official said to him, "Sir, come down before my child dies."
040450 Jesus said to him, "Go; your son will live." The man believed the word that Jesus spoke to him and went his way.
040451 As he was going down, his servants met him and told him that his son was living.
040452 So he asked them the hour when he began to mend, and they said to him, "Yesterday at the seventh hour the fever left him."
040453 The father knew that was the hour when Jesus had said to him, "Your son will live"; and he himself believed, and all his household.
040454 This was now the second sign that Jesus did when he had come from Judea to Galilee.
040501 After this there was a feast of the Jews, and Jesus went up to Jerusalem.
040502 Now there is in Jerusalem by the Sheep Gate a pool, in Hebrew called Beth-za'tha, which has five porticoes.
040503 In these lay a multitude of invalids, blind, lame, paralyzed, waiting for the stirring of the water;
040504 for an angel of the Lord went down at certain seasons into the pool, and stirred up the water; whoever stepped in first after the stirring of the water was made well from whatever disease that person had.
040505 One man was there, who had been ill for thirty-eight years.
040506 When Jesus saw him and knew that he had been lying there a long time, he said to him, "Do you want to be healed?"
040507 The sick man answered him, "Sir, I have no man to put me into the pool when the water is troubled, and while I am going another steps down before me."
040508 Jesus said to him, "Rise, take up your pallet, and walk."
040509 And at once the man was healed, and he took up his pallet and walked. Now that day was the sabbath.
040510 So the Jews said to the man who was cured, "It is the sabbath, it is not lawful for you to carry your pallet."
040511 But he answered them, "The man who healed me said to me, 'Take up your pallet, and walk.'"
040512 They asked him, "Who is the man who said to you, 'Take up your pallet, and walk'?"
040513 Now the man who had been healed did not know who it was, for Jesus had withdrawn, as there was a crowd in the place.
040514 Afterward, Jesus found him in the temple, and said to him, "See, you are well! Sin no more, that nothing worse befall you."
040515 The man went away and told the Jews that it was Jesus who had healed him.
040516 And this was why the Jews persecuted Jesus, because he did this on the sabbath.
040517 But Jesus answered them, "My Father is working still, and I am working."
040518 This was why the Jews sought all the more to kill him, because he not only broke the sabbath but also called God his Father, making himself equal with God.
040519 Jesus said to them, "Truly, truly, I say to you, the Son can do nothing of his own accord, but only what he sees the Father doing; for whatever he does, that the Son does likewise.
040520 For the Father loves the Son, and shows him all that he himself is doing; and greater works than these will he show him, that you may marvel.
040521 For as the Father raises the dead and gives them life, so also the Son gives life to whom he will.
040522 The Father judges no one, but has given all judgment to the Son,
040523 that all may honor the Son, even as they honor the Father. He who does not honor the Son does not honor the Father who sent him.
040524 Truly, truly, I say to you, he who hears my word and believes him who sent me, has eternal life; he does not come into judgment, but has passed from death to life.
040525 "Truly, truly, I say to you, the hour is coming, and now is, when the dead will hear the voice of the Son of God, and those who hear will live.
040526 For as the Father has life in himself, so he has granted the Son also to have life in himself,
040527 and has given him authority to execute judgment, because he is the Son of man.
040528 Do not marvel at this; for the hour is coming when all who are in the tombs will hear his voice
040529 and come forth, those who have done good, to the resurrection of life, and those who have done evil, to the resurrection of judgment.
040530 "I can do nothing on my own authority; as I hear, I judge; and my judgment is just, because I seek not my own will but the will of him who sent me.
040531 If I bear witness to myself, my testimony is not true;
040532 there is another who bears witness to me, and I know that the testimony which he bears to me is true.
040533 You sent to John, and he has borne witness to the truth.
040534 Not that the testimony which I receive is from man; but I say this that you may be saved.
040535 He was a burning and shining lamp, and you were willing to rejoice for a while in his light.
040536 But the testimony which I have is greater than that of John; for the works which the Father has granted me to accomplish, these very works which I am doing, bear me witness that the Father has sent me.
040537 And the Father who sent me has himself borne witness to me. His voice you have never heard, his form you have never seen;
040538 and you do not have his word abiding in you, for you do not believe him whom he has sent.
040539 You search the scriptures, because you think that in them you have eternal life; and it is they that bear witness to me;
040540 yet you refuse to come to me that you may have life.
040541 I do not receive glory from men.
040542 But I know that you have not the love of God within you.
040543 I have come in my Father's name, and you do not receive me; if another comes in his own name, him you will receive.
040544 How can you believe, who receive glory from one another and do not seek the glory that comes from the only God?
040545 Do not think that I shall accuse you to the Father; it is Moses who accuses you, on whom you set your hope.
040546 If you believed Moses, you would believe me, for he wrote of me.
040547 But if you do not believe his writings, how will you believe my words?"
040601 After this Jesus went to the other side of the Sea of Galilee, which is the Sea of Tiber'i-as.
040602 And a multitude followed him, because they saw the signs which he did on those who were diseased.
040603 Jesus went up on the mountain, and there sat down with his disciples.
040604 Now the Passover, the feast of the Jews, was at hand.
040605 Lifting up his eyes, then, and seeing that a multitude was coming to him, Jesus said to Philip, "How are we to buy bread, so that these people may eat?"
040606 This he said to test him, for he himself knew what he would do.
040607 Philip answered him, "Two hundred denarii would not buy enough bread for each of them to get a little."
040608 One of his disciples, Andrew, Simon Peter's brother, said to him,
040609 "There is a lad here who has five barley loaves and two fish; but what are they among so many?"
040610 Jesus said, "Make the people sit down." Now there was much grass in the place; so the men sat down, in number about five thousand.
040611 Jesus then took the loaves, and when he had given thanks, he distributed them to those who were seated; so also the fish, as much as they wanted.
040612 And when they had eaten their fill, he told his disciples, "Gather up the fragments left over, that nothing may be lost."
040613 So they gathered them up and filled twelve baskets with fragments from the five barley loaves, left by those who had eaten.
040614 When the people saw the sign which he had done, they said, "This is indeed the prophet who is to come into the world!"
040615 Perceiving then that they were about to come and take him by force to make him king, Jesus withdrew again to the mountain by himself.
040616 When evening came, his disciples went down to the sea,
040617 got into a boat, and started across the sea to Caper'na-um. It was now dark, and Jesus had not yet come to them.
040618 The sea rose because a strong wind was blowing.
040619 When they had rowed about three or four miles, they saw Jesus walking on the sea and drawing near to the boat. They were frightened,
040620 but he said to them, "It is I; do not be afraid."
040621 Then they were glad to take him into the boat, and immediately the boat was at the land to which they were going.
040622 On the next day the people who remained on the other side of the sea saw that there had been only one boat there, and that Jesus had not entered the boat with his disciples, but that his disciples had gone away alone.
040623 However, boats from Tiber'i-as came near the place where they ate the bread after the Lord had given thanks.
040624 So when the people saw that Jesus was not there, nor his disciples, they themselves got into the boats and went to Caper'na-um, seeking Jesus.
040625 When they found him on the other side of the sea, they said to him, "Rabbi, when did you come here?"
040626 Jesus answered them, "Truly, truly, I say to you, you seek me, not because you saw signs, but because you ate your fill of the loaves.
040627 Do not labor for the food which perishes, but for the food which endures to eternal life, which the Son of man will give to you; for on him has God the Father set his seal."
040628 Then they said to him, "What must we do, to be doing the works of God?"
040629 Jesus answered them, "This is the work of God, that you believe in him whom he has sent."
040630 So they said to him, "Then what sign do you do, that we may see, and believe you? What work do you perform?
040631 Our fathers ate the manna in the wilderness; as it is written, 'He gave them bread from heaven to eat.'"
040632 Jesus then said to them, "Truly, truly, I say to you, it was not Moses who gave you the bread from heaven; my Father gives you the true bread from heaven.
040633 For the bread of God is that which comes down from heaven, and gives life to the world."
040634 They said to him, "Lord, give us this bread always."
040635 Jesus said to them, "I am the bread of life; he who comes to me shall not hunger, and he who believes in me shall never thirst.
040636 But I said to you that you have seen me and yet do not believe.
040637 All that the Father gives me will come to me; and him who comes to me I will not cast out.
040638 For I have come down from heaven, not to do my own will, but the will of him who sent me;
040639 and this is the will of him who sent me, that I should lose nothing of all that he has given me, but raise it up at the last day.
040640 For this is the will of my Father, that every one who sees the Son and believes in him should have eternal life; and I will raise him up at the last day."
040641 The Jews then murmured at him, because he said, "I am the bread which came down from heaven."
040642 They said, "Is not this Jesus, the son of Joseph, whose father and mother we know? How does he now say, 'I have come down from heaven'?"
040643 Jesus answered them, "Do not murmur among yourselves.
040644 No one can come to me unless the Father who sent me draws him; and I will raise him up at the last day.
040645 It is written in the prophets, 'And they shall all be taught by God.' Every one who has heard and learned from the Father comes to me.
040646 Not that any one has seen the Father except him who is from God; he has seen the Father.
040647 Truly, truly, I say to you, he who believes has eternal life.
040648 I am the bread of life.
040649 Your fathers ate the manna in the wilderness, and they died.
040650 This is the bread which comes down from heaven, that a man may eat of it and not die.
040651 I am the living bread which came down from heaven; if any one eats of this bread, he will live for ever; and the bread which I shall give for the life of the world is my flesh."
040652 The Jews then disputed among themselves, saying, "How can this man give us his flesh to eat?"
040653 So Jesus said to them, "Truly, truly, I say to you, unless you eat the flesh of the Son of man and drink his blood, you have no life in you;
040654 he who eats my flesh and drinks my blood has eternal life, and I will raise him up at the last day.
040655 For my flesh is food indeed, and my blood is drink indeed.
040656 He who eats my flesh and drinks my blood abides in me, and I in him.
040657 As the living Father sent me, and I live because of the Father, so he who eats me will live because of me.
040658 This is the bread which came down from heaven, not such as the fathers ate and died; he who eats this bread will live for ever."
040659 This he said in the synagogue, as he taught at Caper'na-um.
040660 Many of his disciples, when they heard it, said, "This is a hard saying; who can listen to it?"
040661 But Jesus, knowing in himself that his disciples murmured at it, said to them, "Do you take offense at this?
040662 Then what if you were to see the Son of man ascending where he was before?
040663 It is the spirit that gives life, the flesh is of no avail; the words that I have spoken to you are spirit and life.
040664 But there are some of you that do not believe." For Jesus knew from the first who those were that did not believe, and who it was that would betray him.
040665 And he said, "This is why I told you that no one can come to me unless it is granted him by the Father."
040666 After this many of his disciples drew back and no longer went about with him.
040667 Jesus said to the twelve, "Do you also wish to go away?"
040668 Simon Peter answered him, "Lord, to whom shall we go? You have the words of eternal life;
040669 and we have believed, and have come to know, that you are the Holy One of God."
040670 Jesus answered them, "Did I not choose you, the twelve, and one of you is a devil?"
040671 He spoke of Judas the son of Simon Iscariot, for he, one of the twelve, was to betray him.
040701 After this Jesus went about in Galilee; he would not go about in Judea, because the Jews sought to kill him.
040702 Now the Jews' feast of Tabernacles was at hand.
040703 So his brothers said to him, "Leave here and go to Judea, that your disciples may see the works you are doing.
040704 For no man works in secret if he seeks to be known openly. If you do these things, show yourself to the world."
040705 For even his brothers did not believe in him.
040706 Jesus said to them, "My time has not yet come, but your time is always here.
040707 The world cannot hate you, but it hates me because I testify of it that its works are evil.
040708 Go to the feast yourselves; I am not going up to this feast, for my time has not yet fully come."
040709 So saying, he remained in Galilee.
040710 But after his brothers had gone up to the feast, then he also went up, not publicly but in private.
040711 The Jews were looking for him at the feast, and saying, "Where is he?"
040712 And there was much muttering about him among the people. While some said, "He is a good man," others said, "No, he is leading the people astray."
040713 Yet for fear of the Jews no one spoke openly of him.
040714 About the middle of the feast Jesus went up into the temple and taught.
040715 The Jews marveled at it, saying, "How is it that this man has learning, when he has never studied?"
040716 So Jesus answered them, "My teaching is not mine, but his who sent me;
040717 if any man's will is to do his will, he shall know whether the teaching is from God or whether I am speaking on my own authority.
040718 He who speaks on his own authority seeks his own glory; but he who seeks the glory of him who sent him is true, and in him there is no falsehood.
040719 Did not Moses give you the law? Yet none of you keeps the law. Why do you seek to kill me?"
040720 The people answered, "You have a demon! Who is seeking to kill you?"
040721 Jesus answered them, "I did one deed, and you all marvel at it.
040722 Moses gave you circumcision (not that it is from Moses, but from the fathers), and you circumcise a man upon the sabbath.
040723 If on the sabbath a man receives circumcision, so that the law of Moses may not be broken, are you angry with me because on the sabbath I made a man's whole body well?
040724 Do not judge by appearances, but judge with right judgment."
040725 Some of the people of Jerusalem therefore said, "Is not this the man whom they seek to kill?
040726 And here he is, speaking openly, and they say nothing to him! Can it be that the authorities really know that this is the Christ?
040727 Yet we know where this man comes from; and when the Christ appears, no one will know where he comes from."
040728 So Jesus proclaimed, as he taught in the temple, "You know me, and you know where I come from? But I have not come of my own accord; he who sent me is true, and him you do not know.
040729 I know him, for I come from him, and he sent me."
040730 So they sought to arrest him; but no one laid hands on him, because his hour had not yet come.
040731 Yet many of the people believed in him; they said, "When the Christ appears, will he do more signs than this man has done?"
040732 The Pharisees heard the crowd thus muttering about him, and the chief priests and Pharisees sent officers to arrest him.
040733 Jesus then said, "I shall be with you a little longer, and then I go to him who sent me;
040734 you will seek me and you will not find me; where I am you cannot come."
040735 The Jews said to one another, "Where does this man intend to go that we shall not find him? Does he intend to go to the Dispersion among the Greeks and teach the Greeks?
040736 What does he mean by saying, 'You will seek me and you will not find me,' and, 'Where I am you cannot come'?"
040737 On the last day of the feast, the great day, Jesus stood up and proclaimed, "If any one thirst, let him come to me and drink.
040738 He who believes in me, as the scripture has said, 'Out of his heart shall flow rivers of living water.'"
040739 Now this he said about the Spirit, which those who believed in him were to receive; for as yet the Spirit had not been given, because Jesus was not yet glorified.
040740 When they heard these words, some of the people said, "This is really the prophet."
040741 Others said, "This is the Christ." But some said, "Is the Christ to come from Galilee?
040742 Has not the scripture said that the Christ is descended from David, and comes from Bethlehem, the village where David was?"
040743 So there was a division among the people over him.
040744 Some of them wanted to arrest him, but no one laid hands on him.
040745 The officers then went back to the chief priests and Pharisees, who said to them, "Why did you not bring him?"
040746 The officers answered, "No man ever spoke like this man!"
040747 The Pharisees answered them, "Are you led astray, you also?
040748 Have any of the authorities or of the Pharisees believed in him?
040749 But this crowd, who do not know the law, are accursed."
040750 Nicode'mus, who had gone to him before, and who was one of them, said to them,
040751 "Does our law judge a man without first giving him a hearing and learning what he does?"
040752 They replied, "Are you from Galilee too? Search and you will see that no prophet is to rise from Galilee."
040753 They went each to his own house,
040801 but Jesus went to the Mount of Olives.
040802 Early in the morning he came again to the temple; all the people came to him, and he sat down and taught them.
040803 The scribes and the Pharisees brought a woman who had been caught in adultery, and placing her in the midst
040804 they said to him, "Teacher, this woman has been caught in the act of adultery.
040805 Now in the law Moses commanded us to stone such. What do you say about her?"
040806 This they said to test him, that they might have some charge to bring against him. Jesus bent down and wrote with his finger on the ground.
040807 And as they continued to ask him, he stood up and said to them, "Let him who is without sin among you be the first to throw a stone at her."
040808 And once more he bent down and wrote with his finger on the ground.
040809 But when they heard it, they went away, one by one, beginning with the eldest, and Jesus was left alone with the woman standing before him.
040810 Jesus looked up and said to her, "Woman, where are they? Has no one condemned you?"
040811 She said, "No one, Lord." And Jesus said, "Neither do I condemn you; go, and do not sin again."
040812 Again Jesus spoke to them, saying, "I am the light of the world; he who follows me will not walk in darkness, but will have the light of life."
040813 The Pharisees then said to him, "You are bearing witness to yourself; your testimony is not true."
040814 Jesus answered, "Even if I do bear witness to myself, my testimony is true, for I know whence I have come and whither I am going, but you do not know whence I come or whither I am going.
040815 You judge according to the flesh, I judge no one.
040816 Yet even if I do judge, my judgment is true, for it is not I alone that judge, but I and he who sent me.
040817 In your law it is written that the testimony of two men is true;
040818 I bear witness to myself, and the Father who sent me bears witness to me."
040819 They said to him therefore, "Where is your Father?" Jesus answered, "You know neither me nor my Father; if you knew me, you would know my Father also."
040820 These words he spoke in the treasury, as he taught in the temple; but no one arrested him, because his hour had not yet come.
040821 Again he said to them, "I go away, and you will seek me and die in your sin; where I am going, you cannot come."
040822 Then said the Jews, "Will he kill himself, since he says, 'Where I am going, you cannot come'?"
040823 He said to them, "You are from below, I am from above; you are of this world, I am not of this world.
040824 I told you that you would die in your sins, for you will die in your sins unless you believe that I am he."
040825 They said to him, "Who are you?" Jesus said to them, "Even what I have told you from the beginning.
040826 I have much to say about you and much to judge; but he who sent me is true, and I declare to the world what I have heard from him."
040827 They did not understand that he spoke to them of the Father.
040828 So Jesus said, "When you have lifted up the Son of man, then you will know that I am he, and that I do nothing on my own authority but speak thus as the Father taught me.
040829 And he who sent me is with me; he has not left me alone, for I always do what is pleasing to him."
040830 As he spoke thus, many believed in him.
040831 Jesus then said to the Jews who had believed in him, "If you continue in my word, you are truly my disciples,
040832 and you will know the truth, and the truth will make you free."
040833 They answered him, "We are descendants of Abraham, and have never been in bondage to any one. How is it that you say, 'You will be made free'?"
040834 Jesus answered them, "Truly, truly, I say to you, every one who commits sin is a slave to sin.
040835 The slave does not continue in the house for ever; the son continues for ever.
040836 So if the Son makes you free, you will be free indeed.
040837 I know that you are descendants of Abraham; yet you seek to kill me, because my word finds no place in you.
040838 I speak of what I have seen with my Father, and you do what you have heard from your father."
040839 They answered him, "Abraham is our father." Jesus said to them, "If you were Abraham's children, you would do what Abraham did,
040840 but now you seek to kill me, a man who has told you the truth which I heard from God; this is not what Abraham did.
040841 You do what your father did." They said to him, "We were not born of fornication; we have one Father, even God."
040842 Jesus said to them, "If God were your Father, you would love me, for I proceeded and came forth from God; I came not of my own accord, but he sent me.
040843 Why do you not understand what I say? It is because you cannot bear to hear my word.
040844 You are of your father the devil, and your will is to do your father's desires. He was a murderer from the beginning, and has nothing to do with the truth, because there is no truth in him. When he lies, he speaks according to his own nature, for he is a liar and the father of lies.
040845 But, because I tell the truth, you do not believe me.
040846 Which of you convicts me of sin? If I tell the truth, why do you not believe me?
040847 He who is of God hears the words of God; the reason why you do not hear them is that you are not of God."
040848 The Jews answered him, "Are we not right in saying that you are a Samaritan and have a demon?"
040849 Jesus answered, "I have not a demon; but I honor my Father, and you dishonor me.
040850 Yet I do not seek my own glory; there is One who seeks it and he will be the judge.
040851 Truly, truly, I say to you, if any one keeps my word, he will never see death."
040852 The Jews said to him, "Now we know that you have a demon. Abraham died, as did the prophets; and you say, 'If any one keeps my word, he will never taste death.'
040853 Are you greater than our father Abraham, who died? And the prophets died! Who do you claim to be?"
040854 Jesus answered, "If I glorify myself, my glory is nothing; it is my Father who glorifies me, of whom you say that he is your God.
040855 But you have not known him; I know him. If I said, I do not know him, I should be a liar like you; but I do know him and I keep his word.
040856 Your father Abraham rejoiced that he was to see my day; he saw it and was glad."
040857 The Jews then said to him, "You are not yet fifty years old, and have you seen Abraham?"
040858 Jesus said to them, "Truly, truly, I say to you, before Abraham was, I am."
040859 So they took up stones to throw at him; but Jesus hid himself, and went out of the temple.
040901 As he passed by, he saw a man blind from his birth.
040902 And his disciples asked him, "Rabbi, who sinned, this man or his parents, that he was born blind?"
040903 Jesus answered, "It was not that this man sinned, or his parents, but that the works of God might be made manifest in him.
040904 We must work the works of him who sent me, while it is day; night comes, when no one can work.
040905 As long as I am in the world, I am the light of the world."
040906 As he said this, he spat on the ground and made clay of the spittle and anointed the man's eyes with the clay,
040907 saying to him, "Go, wash in the pool of Silo'am" (which means Sent). So he went and washed and came back seeing.
040908 The neighbors and those who had seen him before as a beggar, said, "Is not this the man who used to sit and beg?"
040909 Some said, "It is he"; others said, "No, but he is like him." He said, "I am the man."
040910 They said to him, "Then how were your eyes opened?"
040911 He answered, "The man called Jesus made clay and anointed my eyes and said to me, 'Go to Silo'am and wash'; so I went and washed and received my sight."
040912 They said to him, "Where is he?" He said, "I do not know."
040913 They brought to the Pharisees the man who had formerly been blind.
040914 Now it was a sabbath day when Jesus made the clay and opened his eyes.
040915 The Pharisees again asked him how he had received his sight. And he said to them, "He put clay on my eyes, and I washed, and I see."
040916 Some of the Pharisees said, "This man is not from God, for he does not keep the sabbath." But others said, "How can a man who is a sinner do such signs?" There was a division among them.
040917 So they again said to the blind man, "What do you say about him, since he has opened your eyes?" He said, "He is a prophet."
040918 The Jews did not believe that he had been blind and had received his sight, until they called the parents of the man who had received his sight,
040919 and asked them, "Is this your son, who you say was born blind? How then does he now see?"
040920 His parents answered, "We know that this is our son, and that he was born blind;
040921 but how he now sees we do not know, nor do we know who opened his eyes. Ask him; he is of age, he will speak for himself."
040922 His parents said this because they feared the Jews, for the Jews had already agreed that if any one should confess him to be Christ, he was to be put out of the synagogue.
040923 Therefore his parents said, "He is of age, ask him."
040924 So for the second time they called the man who had been blind, and said to him, "Give God the praise; we know that this man is a sinner."
040925 He answered, "Whether he is a sinner, I do not know; one thing I know, that though I was blind, now I see."
040926 They said to him, "What did he do to you? How did he open your eyes?"
040927 He answered them, "I have told you already, and you would not listen. Why do you want to hear it again? Do you too want to become his disciples?"
040928 And they reviled him, saying, "You are his disciple, but we are disciples of Moses.
040929 We know that God has spoken to Moses, but as for this man, we do not know where he comes from."
040930 The man answered, "Why, this is a marvel! You do not know where he comes from, and yet he opened my eyes.
040931 We know that God does not listen to sinners, but if any one is a worshiper of God and does his will, God listens to him.
040932 Never since the world began has it been heard that any one opened the eyes of a man born blind.
040933 If this man were not from God, he could do nothing."
040934 They answered him, "You were born in utter sin, and would you teach us?" And they cast him out.
040935 Jesus heard that they had cast him out, and having found him he said, "Do you believe in the Son of man?"
040936 He answered, "And who is he, sir, that I may believe in him?"
040937 Jesus said to him, "You have seen him, and it is he who speaks to you."
040938 He said, "Lord, I believe"; and he worshiped him.
040939 Jesus said, "For judgment I came into this world, that those who do not see may see, and that those who see may become blind."
040940 Some of the Pharisees near him heard this, and they said to him, "Are we also blind?"
040941 Jesus said to them, "If you were blind, you would have no guilt; but now that you say, 'We see,' your guilt remains.
041001 "Truly, truly, I say to you, he who does not enter the sheepfold by the door but climbs in by another way, that man is a thief and a robber;
041002 but he who enters by the door is the shepherd of the sheep.
041003 To him the gatekeeper opens; the sheep hear his voice, and he calls his own sheep by name and leads them out.
041004 When he has brought out all his own, he goes before them, and the sheep follow him, for they know his voice.
041005 A stranger they will not follow, but they will flee from him, for they do not know the voice of strangers."
041006 This figure Jesus used with them, but they did not understand what he was saying to them.
041007 So Jesus again said to them, "Truly, truly, I say to you, I am the door of the sheep.
041008 All who came before me are thieves and robbers; but the sheep did not heed them.
041009 I am the door; if any one enters by me, he will be saved, and will go in and out and find pasture.
041010 The thief comes only to steal and kill and destroy; I came that they may have life, and have it abundantly.
041011 I am the good shepherd. The good shepherd lays down his life for the sheep.
041012 He who is a hireling and not a shepherd, whose own the sheep are not, sees the wolf coming and leaves the sheep and flees; and the wolf snatches them and scatters them.
041013 He flees because he is a hireling and cares nothing for the sheep.
041014 I am the good shepherd; I know my own and my own know me,
041015 as the Father knows me and I know the Father; and I lay down my life for the sheep.
041016 And I have other sheep, that are not of this fold; I must bring them also, and they will heed my voice. So there shall be one flock, one shepherd.
041017 For this reason the Father loves me, because I lay down my life, that I may take it again.
041018 No one takes it from me, but I lay it down of my own accord. I have power to lay it down, and I have power to take it again; this charge I have received from my Father."
041019 There was again a division among the Jews because of these words.
041020 Many of them said, "He has a demon, and he is mad; why listen to him?"
041021 Others said, "These are not the sayings of one who has a demon. Can a demon open the eyes of the blind?"
041022 It was the feast of the Dedication at Jerusalem;
041023 it was winter, and Jesus was walking in the temple, in the portico of Solomon.
041024 So the Jews gathered round him and said to him, "How long will you keep us in suspense? If you are the Christ, tell us plainly."
041025 Jesus answered them, "I told you, and you do not believe. The works that I do in my Father's name, they bear witness to me;
041026 but you do not believe, because you do not belong to my sheep.
041027 My sheep hear my voice, and I know them, and they follow me;
041028 and I give them eternal life, and they shall never perish, and no one shall snatch them out of my hand.
041029 My Father, who has given them to me, is greater than all, and no one is able to snatch them out of the Father's hand.
041030 I and the Father are one."
041031 The Jews took up stones again to stone him.
041032 Jesus answered them, "I have shown you many good works from the Father; for which of these do you stone me?"
041033 The Jews answered him, "It is not for a good work that we stone you but for blasphemy; because you, being a man, make yourself God."
041034 Jesus answered them, "Is it not written in your law, 'I said, you are gods'?
041035 If he called them gods to whom the word of God came (and scripture cannot be broken),
041036 do you say of him whom the Father consecrated and sent into the world, 'You are blaspheming,' because I said, 'I am the Son of God'?
041037 If I am not doing the works of my Father, then do not believe me;
041038 but if I do them, even though you do not believe me, believe the works, that you may know and understand that the Father is in me and I am in the Father."
041039 Again they tried to arrest him, but he escaped from their hands.
041040 He went away again across the Jordan to the place where John at first baptized, and there he remained.
041041 And many came to him; and they said, "John did no sign, but everything that John said about this man was true."
041042 And many believed in him there.
041101 Now a certain man was ill, Laz'arus of Bethany, the village of Mary and her sister Martha.
041102 It was Mary who anointed the Lord with ointment and wiped his feet with her hair, whose brother Laz'arus was ill.
041103 So the sisters sent to him, saying, "Lord, he whom you love is ill."
041104 But when Jesus heard it he said, "This illness is not unto death; it is for the glory of God, so that the Son of God may be glorified by means of it."
041105 Now Jesus loved Martha and her sister and Laz'arus.
041106 So when he heard that he was ill, he stayed two days longer in the place where he was.
041107 Then after this he said to the disciples, "Let us go into Judea again."
041108 The disciples said to him, "Rabbi, the Jews were but now seeking to stone you, and are you going there again?"
041109 Jesus answered, "Are there not twelve hours in the day? If any one walks in the day, he does not stumble, because he sees the light of this world.
041110 But if any one walks in the night, he stumbles, because the light is not in him."
041111 Thus he spoke, and then he said to them, "Our friend Laz'arus has fallen asleep, but I go to awake him out of sleep."
041112 The disciples said to him, "Lord, if he has fallen asleep, he will recover."
041113 Now Jesus had spoken of his death, but they thought that he meant taking rest in sleep.
041114 Then Jesus told them plainly, "Laz'arus is dead;
041115 and for your sake I am glad that I was not there, so that you may believe. But let us go to him."
041116 Thomas, called the Twin, said to his fellow disciples, "Let us also go, that we may die with him."
041117 Now when Jesus came, he found that Laz'arus had already been in the tomb four days.
041118 Bethany was near Jerusalem, about two miles off,
041119 and many of the Jews had come to Martha and Mary to console them concerning their brother.
041120 When Martha heard that Jesus was coming, she went and met him, while Mary sat in the house.
041121 Martha said to Jesus, "Lord, if you had been here, my brother would not have died.
041122 And even now I know that whatever you ask from God, God will give you."
041123 Jesus said to her, "Your brother will rise again."
041124 Martha said to him, "I know that he will rise again in the resurrection at the last day."
041125 Jesus said to her, "I am the resurrection and the life; he who believes in me, though he die, yet shall he live,
041126 and whoever lives and believes in me shall never die. Do you believe this?"
041127 She said to him, "Yes, Lord; I believe that you are the Christ, the Son of God, he who is coming into the world."
041128 When she had said this, she went and called her sister Mary, saying quietly, "The Teacher is here and is calling for you."
041129 And when she heard it, she rose quickly and went to him.
041130 Now Jesus had not yet come to the village, but was still in the place where Martha had met him.
041131 When the Jews who were with her in the house, consoling her, saw Mary rise quickly and go out, they followed her, supposing that she was going to the tomb to weep there.
041132 Then Mary, when she came where Jesus was and saw him, fell at his feet, saying to him, "Lord, if you had been here, my brother would not have died."
041133 When Jesus saw her weeping, and the Jews who came with her also weeping, he was deeply moved in spirit and troubled;
041134 and he said, "Where have you laid him?" They said to him, "Lord, come and see."
041135 Jesus wept.
041136 So the Jews said, "See how he loved him!"
041137 But some of them said, "Could not he who opened the eyes of the blind man have kept this man from dying?"
041138 Then Jesus, deeply moved again, came to the tomb; it was a cave, and a stone lay upon it.
041139 Jesus said, "Take away the stone." Martha, the sister of the dead man, said to him, "Lord, by this time there will be an odor, for he has been dead four days."
041140 Jesus said to her, "Did I not tell you that if you would believe you would see the glory of God?"
041141 So they took away the stone. And Jesus lifted up his eyes and said, "Father, I thank thee that thou hast heard me.
041142 I knew that thou hearest me always, but I have said this on account of the people standing by, that they may believe that thou didst send me."
041143 When he had said this, he cried with a loud voice, "Laz'arus, come out."
041144 The dead man came out, his hands and feet bound with bandages, and his face wrapped with a cloth. Jesus said to them, "Unbind him, and let him go."
041145 Many of the Jews therefore, who had come with Mary and had seen what he did, believed in him;
041146 but some of them went to the Pharisees and told them what Jesus had done.
041147 So the chief priests and the Pharisees gathered the council, and said, "What are we to do? For this man performs many signs.
041148 If we let him go on thus, every one will believe in him, and the Romans will come and destroy both our holy place and our nation."
041149 But one of them, Ca'iaphas, who was high priest that year, said to them, "You know nothing at all;
041150 you do not understand that it is expedient for you that one man should die for the people, and that the whole nation should not perish."
041151 He did not say this of his own accord, but being high priest that year he prophesied that Jesus should die for the nation,
041152 and not for the nation only, but to gather into one the children of God who are scattered abroad.
041153 So from that day on they took counsel how to put him to death.
041154 Jesus therefore no longer went about openly among the Jews, but went from there to the country near the wilderness, to a town called E'phraim; and there he stayed with the disciples.
041155 Now the Passover of the Jews was at hand, and many went up from the country to Jerusalem before the Passover, to purify themselves.
041156 They were looking for Jesus and saying to one another as they stood in the temple, "What do you think? That he will not come to the feast?"
041157 Now the chief priests and the Pharisees had given orders that if any one knew where he was, he should let them know, so that they might arrest him.
041201 Six days before the Passover, Jesus came to Bethany, where Laz'arus was, whom Jesus had raised from the dead.
041202 There they made him a supper; Martha served, and Laz'arus was one of those at table with him.
041203 Mary took a pound of costly ointment of pure nard and anointed the feet of Jesus and wiped his feet with her hair; and the house was filled with the fragrance of the ointment.
041204 But Judas Iscariot, one of his disciples (he who was to betray him), said,
041205 "Why was this ointment not sold for three hundred denarii and given to the poor?"
041206 This he said, not that he cared for the poor but because he was a thief, and as he had the money box he used to take what was put into it.
041207 Jesus said, "Let her alone, let her keep it for the day of my burial.
041208 The poor you always have with you, but you do not always have me."
041209 When the great crowd of the Jews learned that he was there, they came, not only on account of Jesus but also to see Laz'arus, whom he had raised from the dead.
041210 So the chief priests planned to put Laz'arus also to death,
041211 because on account of him many of the Jews were going away and believing in Jesus.
041212 The next day a great crowd who had come to the feast heard that Jesus was coming to Jerusalem.
041213 So they took branches of palm trees and went out to meet him, crying, "Hosanna! Blessed is he who comes in the name of the Lord, even the King of Israel!"
041214 And Jesus found a young ass and sat upon it; as it is written,
041215 "Fear not, daughter of Zion; behold, your king is coming, sitting on an ass's colt!"
041216 His disciples did not understand this at first; but when Jesus was glorified, then they remembered that this had been written of him and had been done to him.
041217 The crowd that had been with him when he called Laz'arus out of the tomb and raised him from the dead bore witness.
041218 The reason why the crowd went to meet him was that they heard he had done this sign.
041219 The Pharisees then said to one another, "You see that you can do nothing; look, the world has gone after him."
041220 Now among those who went up to worship at the feast were some Greeks.
041221 So these came to Philip, who was from Beth-sa'ida in Galilee, and said to him, "Sir, we wish to see Jesus."
041222 Philip went and told Andrew; Andrew went with Philip and they told Jesus.
041223 And Jesus answered them, "The hour has come for the Son of man to be glorified.
041224 Truly, truly, I say to you, unless a grain of wheat falls into the earth and dies, it remains alone; but if it dies, it bears much fruit.
041225 He who loves his life loses it, and he who hates his life in this world will keep it for eternal life.
041226 If any one serves me, he must follow me; and where I am, there shall my servant be also; if any one serves me, the Father will honor him.
041227 "Now is my soul troubled. And what shall I say? 'Father, save me from this hour'? No, for this purpose I have come to this hour.
041228 Father, glorify thy name." Then a voice came from heaven, "I have glorified it, and I will glorify it again."
041229 The crowd standing by heard it and said that it had thundered. Others said, "An angel has spoken to him."
041230 Jesus answered, "This voice has come for your sake, not for mine.
041231 Now is the judgment of this world, now shall the ruler of this world be cast out;
041232 and I, when I am lifted up from the earth, will draw all men to myself."
041233 He said this to show by what death he was to die.
041234 The crowd answered him, "We have heard from the law that the Christ remains for ever. How can you say that the Son of man must be lifted up? Who is this Son of man?"
041235 Jesus said to them, "The light is with you for a little longer. Walk while you have the light, lest the darkness overtake you; he who walks in the darkness does not know where he goes.
041236 While you have the light, believe in the light, that you may become sons of light." When Jesus had said this, he departed and hid himself from them.
041237 Though he had done so many signs before them, yet they did not believe in him;
041238 it was that the word spoken by the prophet Isaiah might be fulfilled: "Lord, who has believed our report, and to whom has the arm of the Lord been revealed?"
041239 Therefore they could not believe. For Isaiah again said,
041240 "He has blinded their eyes and hardened their heart, lest they should see with their eyes and perceive with their heart, and turn for me to heal them."
041241 Isaiah said this because he saw his glory and spoke of him.
041242 Nevertheless many even of the authorities believed in him, but for fear of the Pharisees they did not confess it, lest they should be put out of the synagogue:
041243 for they loved the praise of men more than the praise of God.
041244 And Jesus cried out and said, "He who believes in me, believes not in me but in him who sent me.
041245 And he who sees me sees him who sent me.
041246 I have come as light into the world, that whoever believes in me may not remain in darkness.
041247 If any one hears my sayings and does not keep them, I do not judge him; for I did not come to judge the world but to save the world.
041248 He who rejects me and does not receive my sayings has a judge; the word that I have spoken will be his judge on the last day.
041249 For I have not spoken on my own authority; the Father who sent me has himself given me commandment what to say and what to speak.
041250 And I know that his commandment is eternal life. What I say, therefore, I say as the Father has bidden me."
041301 Now before the feast of the Passover, when Jesus knew that his hour had come to depart out of this world to the Father, having loved his own who were in the world, he loved them to the end.
041302 And during supper, when the devil had already put it into the heart of Judas Iscariot, Simon's son, to betray him,
041303 Jesus, knowing that the Father had given all things into his hands, and that he had come from God and was going to God,
041304 rose from supper, laid aside his garments, and girded himself with a towel.
041305 Then he poured water into a basin, and began to wash the disciples' feet, and to wipe them with the towel with which he was girded.
041306 He came to Simon Peter; and Peter said to him, "Lord, do you wash my feet?"
041307 Jesus answered him, "What I am doing you do not know now, but afterward you will understand."
041308 Peter said to him, "You shall never wash my feet." Jesus answered him, "If I do not wash you, you have no part in me."
041309 Simon Peter said to him, "Lord, not my feet only but also my hands and my head!"
041310 Jesus said to him, "He who has bathed does not need to wash, except for his feet, but he is clean all over; and you are clean, but not every one of you."
041311 For he knew who was to betray him; that was why he said, "You are not all clean."
041312 When he had washed their feet, and taken his garments, and resumed his place, he said to them, "Do you know what I have done to you?
041313 You call me Teacher and Lord; and you are right, for so I am.
041314 If I then, your Lord and Teacher, have washed your feet, you also ought to wash one another's feet.
041315 For I have given you an example, that you also should do as I have done to you.
041316 Truly, truly, I say to you, a servant is not greater than his master; nor is he who is sent greater than he who sent him.
041317 If you know these things, blessed are you if you do them.
041318 I am not speaking of you all; I know whom I have chosen; it is that the scripture may be fulfilled, 'He who ate my bread has lifted his heel against me.'
041319 I tell you this now, before it takes place, that when it does take place you may believe that I am he.
041320 Truly, truly, I say to you, he who receives any one whom I send receives me; and he who receives me receives him who sent me."
