041321 When Jesus had thus spoken, he was troubled in spirit, and testified, "Truly, truly, I say to you, one of you will betray me."
041322 The disciples looked at one another, uncertain of whom he spoke.
041323 One of his disciples, whom Jesus loved, was lying close to the breast of Jesus;
041324 so Simon Peter beckoned to him and said, "Tell us who it is of whom he speaks."
041325 So lying thus, close to the breast of Jesus, he said to him, "Lord, who is it?"
041326 Jesus answered, "It is he to whom I shall give this morsel when I have dipped it." So when he had dipped the morsel, he gave it to Judas, the son of Simon Iscariot.
041327 Then after the morsel, Satan entered into him. Jesus said to him, "What you are going to do, do quickly."
041328 Now no one at the table knew why he said this to him.
041329 Some thought that, because Judas had the money box, Jesus was telling him, "Buy what we need for the feast"; or, that he should give something to the poor.
041330 So, after receiving the morsel, he immediately went out; and it was night.
041331 When he had gone out, Jesus said, "Now is the Son of man glorified, and in him God is glorified;
041332 if God is glorified in him, God will also glorify him in himself, and glorify him at once.
041333 Little children, yet a little while I am with you. You will seek me; and as I said to the Jews so now I say to you, 'Where I am going you cannot come.'
041334 A new commandment I give to you, that you love one another; even as I have loved you, that you also love one another.
041335 By this all men will know that you are my disciples, if you have love for one another."
041336 Simon Peter said to him, "Lord, where are you going?" Jesus answered, "Where I am going you cannot follow me now; but you shall follow afterward."
041337 Peter said to him, "Lord, why cannot I follow you now? I will lay down my life for you."
041338 Jesus answered, "Will you lay down your life for me? Truly, truly, I say to you, the cock will not crow, till you have denied me three times.
041401 "Let not your hearts be troubled; believe in God, believe also in me.
041402 In my Father's house are many rooms; if it were not so, would I have told you that I go to prepare a place for you?
041403 And when I go and prepare a place for you, I will come again and will take you to myself, that where I am you may be also.
041404 And you know the way where I am going."
041405 Thomas said to him, "Lord, we do not know where you are going; how can we know the way?"
041406 Jesus said to him, "I am the way, and the truth, and the life; no one comes to the Father, but by me.
041407 If you had known me, you would have known my Father also; henceforth you know him and have seen him."
041408 Philip said to him, "Lord, show us the Father, and we shall be satisfied."
041409 Jesus said to him, "Have I been with you so long, and yet you do not know me, Philip? He who has seen me has seen the Father; how can you say, 'Show us the Father'?
041410 Do you not believe that I am in the Father and the Father in me? The words that I say to you I do not speak on my own authority; but the Father who dwells in me does his works.
041411 Believe me that I am in the Father and the Father in me; or else believe me for the sake of the works themselves.
041412 "Truly, truly, I say to you, he who believes in me will also do the works that I do; and greater works than these will he do, because I go to the Father.
041413 Whatever you ask in my name, I will do it, that the Father may be glorified in the Son;
041414 if you ask anything in my name, I will do it.
041415 "If you love me, you will keep my commandments.
041416 And I will pray the Father, and he will give you another Counselor, to be with you for ever,
041417 even the Spirit of truth, whom the world cannot receive, because it neither sees him nor knows him; you know him, for he dwells with you, and will be in you.
041418 "I will not leave you desolate; I will come to you.
041419 Yet a little while, and the world will see me no more, but you will see me; because I live, you will live also.
041420 In that day you will know that I am in my Father, and you in me, and I in you.
041421 He who has my commandments and keeps them, he it is who loves me; and he who loves me will be loved by my Father, and I will love him and manifest myself to him."
041422 Judas (not Iscariot) said to him, "Lord, how is it that you will manifest yourself to us, and not to the world?"
041423 Jesus answered him, "If a man loves me, he will keep my word, and my Father will love him, and we will come to him and make our home with him.
041424 He who does not love me does not keep my words; and the word which you hear is not mine but the Father's who sent me.
041425 "These things I have spoken to you, while I am still with you.
041426 But the Counselor, the Holy Spirit, whom the Father will send in my name, he will teach you all things, and bring to your remembrance all that I have said to you.
041427 Peace I leave with you; my peace I give to you; not as the world gives do I give to you. Let not your hearts be troubled, neither let them be afraid.
041428 You heard me say to you, 'I go away, and I will come to you.' If you loved me, you would have rejoiced, because I go to the Father; for the Father is greater than I.
041429 And now I have told you before it takes place, so that when it does take place, you may believe.
041430 I will no longer talk much with you, for the ruler of this world is coming. He has no power over me;
041431 but I do as the Father has commanded me, so that the world may know that I love the Father. Rise, let us go hence.
041501 "I am the true vine, and my Father is the vinedresser.
041502 Every branch of mine that bears no fruit, he takes away, and every branch that does bear fruit he prunes, that it may bear more fruit.
041503 You are already made clean by the word which I have spoken to you.
041504 Abide in me, and I in you. As the branch cannot bear fruit by itself, unless it abides in the vine, neither can you, unless you abide in me.
041505 I am the vine, you are the branches. He who abides in me, and I in him, he it is that bears much fruit, for apart from me you can do nothing.
041506 If a man does not abide in me, he is cast forth as a branch and withers; and the branches are gathered, thrown into the fire and burned.
041507 If you abide in me, and my words abide in you, ask whatever you will, and it shall be done for you.
041508 By this my Father is glorified, that you bear much fruit, and so prove to be my disciples.
041509 As the Father has loved me, so have I loved you; abide in my love.
041510 If you keep my commandments, you will abide in my love, just as I have kept my Father's commandments and abide in his love.
041511 These things I have spoken to you, that my joy may be in you, and that your joy may be full.
041512 "This is my commandment, that you love one another as I have loved you.
041513 Greater love has no man than this, that a man lay down his life for his friends.
041514 You are my friends if you do what I command you.
041515 No longer do I call you servants, for the servant does not know what his master is doing; but I have called you friends, for all that I have heard from my Father I have made known to you.
041516 You did not choose me, but I chose you and appointed you that you should go and bear fruit and that your fruit should abide; so that whatever you ask the Father in my name, he may give it to you.
041517 This I command you, to love one another.
041518 "If the world hates you, know that it has hated me before it hated you.
041519 If you were of the world, the world would love its own; but because you are not of the world, but I chose you out of the world, therefore the world hates you.
041520 Remember the word that I said to you, 'A servant is not greater than his master.' If they persecuted me, they will persecute you; if they kept my word, they will keep yours also.
041521 But all this they will do to you on my account, because they do not know him who sent me.
041522 If I had not come and spoken to them, they would not have sin; but now they have no excuse for their sin.
041523 He who hates me hates my Father also.
041524 If I had not done among them the works which no one else did, they would not have sin; but now they have seen and hated both me and my Father.
041525 It is to fulfil the word that is written in their law, 'They hated me without a cause.'
041526 But when the Counselor comes, whom I shall send to you from the Father, even the Spirit of truth, who proceeds from the Father, he will bear witness to me;
041527 and you also are witnesses, because you have been with me from the beginning.
041601 "I have said all this to you to keep you from falling away.
041602 They will put you out of the synagogues; indeed, the hour is coming when whoever kills you will think he is offering service to God.
041603 And they will do this because they have not known the Father, nor me.
041604 But I have said these things to you, that when their hour comes you may remember that I told you of them. "I did not say these things to you from the beginning, because I was with you.
041605 But now I am going to him who sent me; yet none of you asks me, 'Where are you going?'
041606 But because I have said these things to you, sorrow has filled your hearts.
041607 Nevertheless I tell you the truth: it is to your advantage that I go away, for if I do not go away, the Counselor will not come to you; but if I go, I will send him to you.
041608 And when he comes, he will convince the world concerning sin and righteousness and judgment:
041609 concerning sin, because they do not believe in me;
041610 concerning righteousness, because I go to the Father, and you will see me no more;
041611 concerning judgment, because the ruler of this world is judged.
041612 "I have yet many things to say to you, but you cannot bear them now.
041613 When the Spirit of truth comes, he will guide you into all the truth; for he will not speak on his own authority, but whatever he hears he will speak, and he will declare to you the things that are to come.
041614 He will glorify me, for he will take what is mine and declare it to you.
041615 All that the Father has is mine; therefore I said that he will take what is mine and declare it to you.
041616 "A little while, and you will see me no more; again a little while, and you will see me."
041617 Some of his disciples said to one another, "What is this that he says to us, 'A little while, and you will not see me, and again a little while, and you will see me'; and, 'because I go to the Father'?"
041618 They said, "What does he mean by 'a little while'? We do not know what he means."
041619 Jesus knew that they wanted to ask him; so he said to them, "Is this what you are asking yourselves, what I meant by saying, 'A little while, and you will not see me, and again a little while, and you will see me'?
041620 Truly, truly, I say to you, you will weep and lament, but the world will rejoice; you will be sorrowful, but your sorrow will turn into joy.
041621 When a woman is in travail she has sorrow, because her hour has come; but when she is delivered of the child, she no longer remembers the anguish, for joy that a child is born into the world.
041622 So you have sorrow now, but I will see you again and your hearts will rejoice, and no one will take your joy from you.
041623 In that day you will ask nothing of me. Truly, truly, I say to you, if you ask anything of the Father, he will give it to you in my name.
041624 Hitherto you have asked nothing in my name; ask, and you will receive, that your joy may be full.
041625 "I have said this to you in figures; the hour is coming when I shall no longer speak to you in figures but tell you plainly of the Father.
041626 In that day you will ask in my name; and I do not say to you that I shall pray the Father for you;
041627 for the Father himself loves you, because you have loved me and have believed that I came from the Father.
041628 I came from the Father and have come into the world; again, I am leaving the world and going to the Father."
041629 His disciples said, "Ah, now you are speaking plainly, not in any figure!
041630 Now we know that you know all things, and need none to question you; by this we believe that you came from God."
041631 Jesus answered them, "Do you now believe?
041632 The hour is coming, indeed it has come, when you will be scattered, every man to his home, and will leave me alone; yet I am not alone, for the Father is with me.
041633 I have said this to you, that in me you may have peace. In the world you have tribulation; but be of good cheer, I have overcome the world."
041701 When Jesus had spoken these words, he lifted up his eyes to heaven and said, "Father, the hour has come; glorify thy Son that the Son may glorify thee,
041702 since thou hast given him power over all flesh, to give eternal life to all whom thou hast given him.
041703 And this is eternal life, that they know thee the only true God, and Jesus Christ whom thou hast sent.
041704 I glorified thee on earth, having accomplished the work which thou gavest me to do;
041705 and now, Father, glorify thou me in thy own presence with the glory which I had with thee before the world was made.
041706 "I have manifested thy name to the men whom thou gavest me out of the world; thine they were, and thou gavest them to me, and they have kept thy word.
041707 Now they know that everything that thou hast given me is from thee;
041708 for I have given them the words which thou gavest me, and they have received them and know in truth that I came from thee; and they have believed that thou didst send me.
041709 I am praying for them; I am not praying for the world but for those whom thou hast given me, for they are thine;
041710 all mine are thine, and thine are mine, and I am glorified in them.
041711 And now I am no more in the world, but they are in the world, and I am coming to thee. Holy Father, keep them in thy name, which thou hast given me, that they may be one, even as we are one.
041712 While I was with them, I kept them in thy name, which thou hast given me; I have guarded them, and none of them is lost but the son of perdition, that the scripture might be fulfilled.
041713 But now I am coming to thee; and these things I speak in the world, that they may have my joy fulfilled in themselves.
041714 I have given them thy word; and the world has hated them because they are not of the world, even as I am not of the world.
041715 I do not pray that thou shouldst take them out of the world, but that thou shouldst keep them from the evil one.
041716 They are not of the world, even as I am not of the world.
041717 Sanctify them in the truth; thy word is truth.
041718 As thou didst send me into the world, so I have sent them into the world.
041719 And for their sake I consecrate myself, that they also may be consecrated in truth.
041720 "I do not pray for these only, but also for those who believe in me through their word,
041721 that they may all be one; even as thou, Father, art in me, and I in thee, that they also may be in us, so that the world may believe that thou hast sent me.
041722 The glory which thou hast given me I have given to them, that they may be one even as we are one,
041723 I in them and thou in me, that they may become perfectly one, so that the world may know that thou hast sent me and hast loved them even as thou hast loved me.
041724 Father, I desire that they also, whom thou hast given me, may be with me where I am, to behold my glory which thou hast given me in thy love for me before the foundation of the world.
041725 O righteous Father, the world has not known thee, but I have known thee; and these know that thou hast sent me.
041726 I made known to them thy name, and I will make it known, that the love with which thou hast loved me may be in them, and I in them."
041801 When Jesus had spoken these words, he went forth with his disciples across the Kidron valley, where there was a garden, which he and his disciples entered.
041802 Now Judas, who betrayed him, also knew the place; for Jesus often met there with his disciples.
041803 So Judas, procuring a band of soldiers and some officers from the chief priests and the Pharisees, went there with lanterns and torches and weapons.
041804 Then Jesus, knowing all that was to befall him, came forward and said to them, "Whom do you seek?"
041805 They answered him, "Jesus of Nazareth." Jesus said to them, "I am he." Judas, who betrayed him, was standing with them.
041806 When he said to them, "I am he," they drew back and fell to the ground.
041807 Again he asked them, "Whom do you seek?" And they said, "Jesus of Nazareth."
041808 Jesus answered, "I told you that I am he; so, if you seek me, let these men go."
041809 This was to fulfil the word which he had spoken, "Of those whom thou gavest me I lost not one."
041810 Then Simon Peter, having a sword, drew it and struck the high priest's slave and cut off his right ear. The slave's name was Malchus.
041811 Jesus said to Peter, "Put your sword into its sheath; shall I not drink the cup which the Father has given me?"
041812 So the band of soldiers and their captain and the officers of the Jews seized Jesus and bound him.
041813 First they led him to Annas; for he was the father-in-law of Ca'iaphas, who was high priest that year.
041814 It was Ca'iaphas who had given counsel to the Jews that it was expedient that one man should die for the people.
041815 Simon Peter followed Jesus, and so did another disciple. As this disciple was known to the high priest, he entered the court of the high priest along with Jesus,
041816 while Peter stood outside at the door. So the other disciple, who was known to the high priest, went out and spoke to the maid who kept the door, and brought Peter in.
041817 The maid who kept the door said to Peter, "Are not you also one of this man's disciples?" He said, "I am not."
041818 Now the servants and officers had made a charcoal fire, because it was cold, and they were standing and warming themselves; Peter also was with them, standing and warming himself.
041819 The high priest then questioned Jesus about his disciples and his teaching.
041820 Jesus answered him, "I have spoken openly to the world; I have always taught in synagogues and in the temple, where all Jews come together; I have said nothing secretly.
041821 Why do you ask me? Ask those who have heard me, what I said to them; they know what I said."
041822 When he had said this, one of the officers standing by struck Jesus with his hand, saying, "Is that how you answer the high priest?"
041823 Jesus answered him, "If I have spoken wrongly, bear witness to the wrong; but if I have spoken rightly, why do you strike me?"
041824 Annas then sent him bound to Ca'iaphas the high priest.
041825 Now Simon Peter was standing and warming himself. They said to him, "Are not you also one of his disciples?" He denied it and said, "I am not."
041826 One of the servants of the high priest, a kinsman of the man whose ear Peter had cut off, asked, "Did I not see you in the garden with him?"
041827 Peter again denied it; and at once the cock crowed.
041828 Then they led Jesus from the house of Ca'iaphas to the praetorium. It was early. They themselves did not enter the praetorium, so that they might not be defiled, but might eat the passover.
041829 So Pilate went out to them and said, "What accusation do you bring against this man?"
041830 They answered him, "If this man were not an evildoer, we would not have handed him over."
041831 Pilate said to them, "Take him yourselves and judge him by your own law." The Jews said to him, "It is not lawful for us to put any man to death."
041832 This was to fulfil the word which Jesus had spoken to show by what death he was to die.
041833 Pilate entered the praetorium again and called Jesus, and said to him, "Are you the King of the Jews?"
041834 Jesus answered, "Do you say this of your own accord, or did others say it to you about me?"
041835 Pilate answered, "Am I a Jew? Your own nation and the chief priests have handed you over to me; what have you done?"
041836 Jesus answered, "My kingship is not of this world; if my kingship were of this world, my servants would fight, that I might not be handed over to the Jews; but my kingship is not from the world."
041837 Pilate said to him, "So you are a king?" Jesus answered, "You say that I am a king. For this I was born, and for this I have come into the world, to bear witness to the truth. Every one who is of the truth hears my voice."
041838 Pilate said to him, "What is truth?" After he had said this, he went out to the Jews again, and told them, "I find no crime in him.
041839 But you have a custom that I should release one man for you at the Passover; will you have me release for you the King of the Jews?"
041840 They cried out again, "Not this man, but Barab'bas!" Now Barab'bas was a robber.
041901 Then Pilate took Jesus and scourged him.
041902 And the soldiers plaited a crown of thorns, and put it on his head, and arrayed him in a purple robe;
041903 they came up to him, saying, "Hail, King of the Jews!" and struck him with their hands.
041904 Pilate went out again, and said to them, "See, I am bringing him out to you, that you may know that I find no crime in him."
041905 So Jesus came out, wearing the crown of thorns and the purple robe. Pilate said to them, "Behold the man!"
041906 When the chief priests and the officers saw him, they cried out, "Crucify him, crucify him!" Pilate said to them, "Take him yourselves and crucify him, for I find no crime in him."
041907 The Jews answered him, "We have a law, and by that law he ought to die, because he has made himself the Son of God."
041908 When Pilate heard these words, he was the more afraid;
041909 he entered the praetorium again and said to Jesus, "Where are you from?" But Jesus gave no answer.
041910 Pilate therefore said to him, "You will not speak to me? Do you not know that I have power to release you, and power to crucify you?"
041911 Jesus answered him, "You would have no power over me unless it had been given you from above; therefore he who delivered me to you has the greater sin."
041912 Upon this Pilate sought to release him, but the Jews cried out, "If you release this man, you are not Caesar's friend; every one who makes himself a king sets himself against Caesar."
041913 When Pilate heard these words, he brought Jesus out and sat down on the judgment seat at a place called The Pavement, and in Hebrew, Gab'batha.
041914 Now it was the day of Preparation of the Passover; it was about the sixth hour. He said to the Jews, "Behold your King!"
041915 They cried out, "Away with him, away with him, crucify him!" Pilate said to them, "Shall I crucify your King?" The chief priests answered, "We have no king but Caesar."
041916 Then he handed him over to them to be crucified.
041917 So they took Jesus, and he went out, bearing his own cross, to the place called the place of a skull, which is called in Hebrew Gol'gotha.
041918 There they crucified him, and with him two others, one on either side, and Jesus between them.
041919 Pilate also wrote a title and put it on the cross; it read, "Jesus of Nazareth, the King of the Jews."
041920 Many of the Jews read this title, for the place where Jesus was crucified was near the city; and it was written in Hebrew, in Latin, and in Greek.
041921 The chief priests of the Jews then said to Pilate, "Do not write, 'The King of the Jews,' but, 'This man said, I am King of the Jews.'"
041922 Pilate answered, "What I have written I have written."
041923 When the soldiers had crucified Jesus they took his garments and made four parts, one for each soldier; also his tunic. But the tunic was without seam, woven from top to bottom;
041924 so they said to one another, "Let us not tear it, but cast lots for it to see whose it shall be." This was to fulfil the scripture, "They parted my garments among them, and for my clothing they cast lots."
041925 So the soldiers did this. But standing by the cross of Jesus were his mother, and his mother's sister, Mary the wife of Clopas, and Mary Mag'dalene.
041926 When Jesus saw his mother, and the disciple whom he loved standing near, he said to his mother, "Woman, behold, your son!"
041927 Then he said to the disciple, "Behold, your mother!" And from that hour the disciple took her to his own home.
041928 After this Jesus, knowing that all was now finished, said (to fulfil the scripture), "I thirst."
041929 A bowl full of vinegar stood there; so they put a sponge full of the vinegar on hyssop and held it to his mouth.
041930 When Jesus had received the vinegar, he said, "It is finished"; and he bowed his head and gave up his spirit.
041931 Since it was the day of Preparation, in order to prevent the bodies from remaining on the cross on the sabbath (for that sabbath was a high day), the Jews asked Pilate that their legs might be broken, and that they might be taken away.
041932 So the soldiers came and broke the legs of the first, and of the other who had been crucified with him;
041933 but when they came to Jesus and saw that he was already dead, they did not break his legs.
041934 But one of the soldiers pierced his side with a spear, and at once there came out blood and water.
041935 He who saw it has borne witness -- his testimony is true, and he knows that he tells the truth -- that you also may believe.
041936 For these things took place that the scripture might be fulfilled, "Not a bone of him shall be broken."
041937 And again another scripture says, "They shall look on him whom they have pierced."
041938 After this Joseph of Arimathe'a, who was a disciple of Jesus, but secretly, for fear of the Jews, asked Pilate that he might take away the body of Jesus, and Pilate gave him leave. So he came and took away his body.
041939 Nicode'mus also, who had at first come to him by night, came bringing a mixture of myrrh and aloes, about a hundred pounds' weight.
041940 They took the body of Jesus, and bound it in linen cloths with the spices, as is the burial custom of the Jews.
041941 Now in the place where he was crucified there was a garden, and in the garden a new tomb where no one had ever been laid.
041942 So because of the Jewish day of Preparation, as the tomb was close at hand, they laid Jesus there.
042001 Now on the first day of the week Mary Mag'dalene came to the tomb early, while it was still dark, and saw that the stone had been taken away from the tomb.
042002 So she ran, and went to Simon Peter and the other disciple, the one whom Jesus loved, and said to them, "They have taken the Lord out of the tomb, and we do not know where they have laid him."
042003 Peter then came out with the other disciple, and they went toward the tomb.
042004 They both ran, but the other disciple outran Peter and reached the tomb first;
042005 and stooping to look in, he saw the linen cloths lying there, but he did not go in.
042006 Then Simon Peter came, following him, and went into the tomb; he saw the linen cloths lying,
042007 and the napkin, which had been on his head, not lying with the linen cloths but rolled up in a place by itself.
042008 Then the other disciple, who reached the tomb first, also went in, and he saw and believed;
042009 for as yet they did not know the scripture, that he must rise from the dead.
042010 Then the disciples went back to their homes.
042011 But Mary stood weeping outside the tomb, and as she wept she stooped to look into the tomb;
042012 and she saw two angels in white, sitting where the body of Jesus had lain, one at the head and one at the feet.
042013 They said to her, "Woman, why are you weeping?" She said to them, "Because they have taken away my Lord, and I do not know where they have laid him."
042014 Saying this, she turned round and saw Jesus standing, but she did not know that it was Jesus.
042015 Jesus said to her, "Woman, why are you weeping? Whom do you seek?" Supposing him to be the gardener, she said to him, "Sir, if you have carried him away, tell me where you have laid him, and I will take him away."
042016 Jesus said to her, "Mary." She turned and said to him in Hebrew, "Rab-bo'ni!" (which means Teacher).
042017 Jesus said to her, "Do not hold me, for I have not yet ascended to the Father; but go to my brethren and say to them, I am ascending to my Father and your Father, to my God and your God."
042018 Mary Mag'dalene went and said to the disciples, "I have seen the Lord"; and she told them that he had said these things to her.
042019 On the evening of that day, the first day of the week, the doors being shut where the disciples were, for fear of the Jews, Jesus came and stood among them and said to them, "Peace be with you."
042020 When he had said this, he showed them his hands and his side. Then the disciples were glad when they saw the Lord.
042021 Jesus said to them again, "Peace be with you. As the Father has sent me, even so I send you."
042022 And when he had said this, he breathed on them, and said to them, "Receive the Holy Spirit.
042023 If you forgive the sins of any, they are forgiven; if you retain the sins of any, they are retained."
042024 Now Thomas, one of the twelve, called the Twin, was not with them when Jesus came.
042025 So the other disciples told him, "We have seen the Lord." But he said to them, "Unless I see in his hands the print of the nails, and place my finger in the mark of the nails, and place my hand in his side, I will not believe."
042026 Eight days later, his disciples were again in the house, and Thomas was with them. The doors were shut, but Jesus came and stood among them, and said, "Peace be with you."
042027 Then he said to Thomas, "Put your finger here, and see my hands; and put out your hand, and place it in my side; do not be faithless, but believing."
042028 Thomas answered him, "My Lord and my God!"
042029 Jesus said to him, "Have you believed because you have seen me? Blessed are those who have not seen and yet believe."
042030 Now Jesus did many other signs in the presence of the disciples, which are not written in this book;
042031 but these are written that you may believe that Jesus is the Christ, the Son of God, and that believing you may have life in his name.
042101 After this Jesus revealed himself again to the disciples by the Sea of Tibe'ri-as; and he revealed himself in this way.
042102 Simon Peter, Thomas called the Twin, Nathan'a-el of Cana in Galilee, the sons of Zeb'edee, and two others of his disciples were together.
042103 Simon Peter said to them, "I am going fishing." They said to him, "We will go with you." They went out and got into the boat; but that night they caught nothing.
042104 Just as day was breaking, Jesus stood on the beach; yet the disciples did not know that it was Jesus.
042105 Jesus said to them, "Children, have you any fish?" They answered him, "No."
042106 He said to them, "Cast the net on the right side of the boat, and you will find some." So they cast it, and now they were not able to haul it in, for the quantity of fish.
042107 That disciple whom Jesus loved said to Peter, "It is the Lord!" When Simon Peter heard that it was the Lord, he put on his clothes, for he was stripped for work, and sprang into the sea.
042108 But the other disciples came in the boat, dragging the net full of fish, for they were not far from the land, but about a hundred yards off.
042109 When they got out on land, they saw a charcoal fire there, with fish lying on it, and bread.
042110 Jesus said to them, "Bring some of the fish that you have just caught."
042111 So Simon Peter went aboard and hauled the net ashore, full of large fish, a hundred and fifty-three of them; and although there were so many, the net was not torn.
042112 Jesus said to them, "Come and have breakfast." Now none of the disciples dared ask him, "Who are you?" They knew it was the Lord.
042113 Jesus came and took the bread and gave it to them, and so with the fish.
042114 This was now the third time that Jesus was revealed to the disciples after he was raised from the dead.
042115 When they had finished breakfast, Jesus said to Simon Peter, "Simon, son of John, do you love me more than these?" He said to him, "Yes, Lord; you know that I love you." He said to him, "Feed my lambs."
042116 A second time he said to him, "Simon, son of John, do you love me?" He said to him, "Yes, Lord; you know that I love you." He said to him, "Tend my sheep."
042117 He said to him the third time, "Simon, son of John, do you love me?" Peter was grieved because he said to him the third time, "Do you love me?" And he said to him, "Lord, you know everything; you know that I love you." Jesus said to him, "Feed my sheep.
042118 Truly, truly, I say to you, when you were young, you girded yourself and walked where you would; but when you are old, you will stretch out your hands, and another will gird you and carry you where you do not wish to go."
042119 (This he said to show by what death he was to glorify God.) And after this he said to him, "Follow me."
042120 Peter turned and saw following them the disciple whom Jesus loved, who had lain close to his breast at the supper and had said, "Lord, who is it that is going to betray you?"
042121 When Peter saw him, he said to Jesus, "Lord, what about this man?"
042122 Jesus said to him, "If it is my will that he remain until I come, what is that to you? Follow me!"
042123 The saying spread abroad among the brethren that this disciple was not to die; yet Jesus did not say to him that he was not to die, but, "If it is my will that he remain until I come, what is that to you?"
042124 This is the disciple who is bearing witness to these things, and who has written these things; and we know that his testimony is true.
042125 But there are also many other things which Jesus did; were every one of them to be written, I suppose that the world itself could not contain the books that would be written.
050101 In the first book, O The-oph'ilus, I have dealt with all that Jesus began to do and teach,
050102 until the day when he was taken up, after he had given commandment through the Holy Spirit to the apostles whom he had chosen.
050103 To them he presented himself alive after his passion by many proofs, appearing to them during forty days, and speaking of the kingdom of God.
050104 And while staying with them he charged them not to depart from Jerusalem, but to wait for the promise of the Father, which, he said, "you heard from me,
050105 for John baptized with water, but before many days you shall be baptized with the Holy Spirit."
050106 So when they had come together, they asked him, "Lord, will you at this time restore the kingdom to Israel?"
050107 He said to them, "It is not for you to know times or seasons which the Father has fixed by his own authority.
050108 But you shall receive power when the Holy Spirit has come upon you; and you shall be my witnesses in Jerusalem and in all Judea and Sama'ria and to the end of the earth."
050109 And when he had said this, as they were looking on, he was lifted up, and a cloud took him out of their sight.
050110 And while they were gazing into heaven as he went, behold, two men stood by them in white robes,
050111 and said, "Men of Galilee, why do you stand looking into heaven? This Jesus, who was taken up from you into heaven, will come in the same way as you saw him go into heaven."
050112 Then they returned to Jerusalem from the mount called Olivet, which is near Jerusalem, a sabbath day's journey away;
050113 and when they had entered, they went up to the upper room, where they were staying, Peter and John and James and Andrew, Philip and Thomas, Bartholomew and Matthew, James the son of Alphaeus and Simon the Zealot and Judas the son of James.
050114 All these with one accord devoted themselves to prayer, together with the women and Mary the mother of Jesus, and with his brothers.
050115 In those days Peter stood up among the brethren (the company of persons was in all about a hundred and twenty), and said,
050116 "Brethren, the scripture had to be fulfilled, which the Holy Spirit spoke beforehand by the mouth of David, concerning Judas who was guide to those who arrested Jesus.
050117 For he was numbered among us, and was allotted his share in this ministry.
050118 (Now this man bought a field with the reward of his wickedness; and falling headlong he burst open in the middle and all his bowels gushed out.
050119 And it became known to all the inhabitants of Jerusalem, so that the field was called in their language Akel'dama, that is, Field of Blood.)
050120 For it is written in the book of Psalms, 'Let his habitation become desolate, and let there be no one to live in it'; and 'His office let another take.'
050121 So one of the men who have accompanied us during all the time that the Lord Jesus went in and out among us,
050122 beginning from the baptism of John until the day when he was taken up from us -- one of these men must become with us a witness to his resurrection."
050123 And they put forward two, Joseph called Barsab'bas, who was surnamed Justus, and Matthi'as.
050124 And they prayed and said, "Lord, who knowest the hearts of all men, show which one of these two thou hast chosen
050125 to take the place in this ministry and apostleship from which Judas turned aside, to go to his own place."
050126 And they cast lots for them, and the lot fell on Matthi'as; and he was enrolled with the eleven apostles.
050201 When the day of Pentecost had come, they were all together in one place.
050202 And suddenly a sound came from heaven like the rush of a mighty wind, and it filled all the house where they were sitting.
050203 And there appeared to them tongues as of fire, distributed and resting on each one of them.
050204 And they were all filled with the Holy Spirit and began to speak in other tongues, as the Spirit gave them utterance.
050205 Now there were dwelling in Jerusalem Jews, devout men from every nation under heaven.
050206 And at this sound the multitude came together, and they were bewildered, because each one heard them speaking in his own language.
050207 And they were amazed and wondered, saying, "Are not all these who are speaking Galileans?
050208 And how is it that we hear, each of us in his own native language?
050209 Par'thians and Medes and E'lamites and residents of Mesopota'mia, Judea and Cappado'cia, Pontus and Asia,
050210 Phryg'ia and Pamphyl'ia, Egypt and the parts of Libya belonging to Cyre'ne, and visitors from Rome, both Jews and proselytes,
050211 Cretans and Arabians, we hear them telling in our own tongues the mighty works of God."
050212 And all were amazed and perplexed, saying to one another, "What does this mean?"
050213 But others mocking said, "They are filled with new wine."
050214 But Peter, standing with the eleven, lifted up his voice and addressed them, "Men of Judea and all who dwell in Jerusalem, let this be known to you, and give ear to my words.
050215 For these men are not drunk, as you suppose, since it is only the third hour of the day;
050216 but this is what was spoken by the prophet Joel:
050217 'And in the last days it shall be, God declares, that I will pour out my Spirit upon all flesh, and your sons and your daughters shall prophesy, and your young men shall see visions, and your old men shall dream dreams;
050218 yea, and on my menservants and my maidservants in those days I will pour out my Spirit; and they shall prophesy.
050219 And I will show wonders in the heaven above and signs on the earth beneath, blood, and fire, and vapor of smoke;
050220 the sun shall be turned into darkness and the moon into blood, before the day of the Lord comes, the great and manifest day.
050221 And it shall be that whoever calls on the name of the Lord shall be saved.'
050222 "Men of Israel, hear these words: Jesus of Nazareth, a man attested to you by God with mighty works and wonders and signs which God did through him in your midst, as you yourselves know --
050223 this Jesus, delivered up according to the definite plan and foreknowledge of God, you crucified and killed by the hands of lawless men.
050224 But God raised him up, having loosed the pangs of death, because it was not possible for him to be held by it.
050225 For David says concerning him, 'I saw the Lord always before me, for he is at my right hand that I may not be shaken;
050226 therefore my heart was glad, and my tongue rejoiced; moreover my flesh will dwell in hope.
050227 For thou wilt not abandon my soul to Hades, nor let thy Holy One see corruption.
050228 Thou hast made known to me the ways of life; thou wilt make me full of gladness with thy presence.'
050229 "Brethren, I may say to you confidently of the patriarch David that he both died and was buried, and his tomb is with us to this day.
050230 Being therefore a prophet, and knowing that God had sworn with an oath to him that he would set one of his descendants upon his throne,
050231 he foresaw and spoke of the resurrection of the Christ, that he was not abandoned to Hades, nor did his flesh see corruption.
050232 This Jesus God raised up, and of that we all are witnesses.
050233 Being therefore exalted at the right hand of God, and having received from the Father the promise of the Holy Spirit, he has poured out this which you see and hear.
050234 For David did not ascend into the heavens; but he himself says, 'The Lord said to my Lord, Sit at my right hand,
050235 till I make thy enemies a stool for thy feet.'
050236 Let all the house of Israel therefore know assuredly that God has made him both Lord and Christ, this Jesus whom you crucified."
050237 Now when they heard this they were cut to the heart, and said to Peter and the rest of the apostles, "Brethren, what shall we do?"
050238 And Peter said to them, "Repent, and be baptized every one of you in the name of Jesus Christ for the forgiveness of your sins; and you shall receive the gift of the Holy Spirit.
050239 For the promise is to you and to your children and to all that are far off, every one whom the Lord our God calls to him."
050240 And he testified with many other words and exhorted them, saying, "Save yourselves from this crooked generation."
050241 So those who received his word were baptized, and there were added that day about three thousand souls.
050242 And they devoted themselves to the apostles' teaching and fellowship, to the breaking of bread and the prayers.
050243 And fear came upon every soul; and many wonders and signs were done through the apostles.
050244 And all who believed were together and had all things in common;
050245 and they sold their possessions and goods and distributed them to all, as any had need.
050246 And day by day, attending the temple together and breaking bread in their homes, they partook of food with glad and generous hearts,
050247 praising God and having favor with all the people. And the Lord added to their number day by day those who were being saved.
050301 Now Peter and John were going up to the temple at the hour of prayer, the ninth hour.
050302 And a man lame from birth was being carried, whom they laid daily at that gate of the temple which is called Beautiful to ask alms of those who entered the temple.
050303 Seeing Peter and John about to go into the temple, he asked for alms.
050304 And Peter directed his gaze at him, with John, and said, "Look at us."
050305 And he fixed his attention upon them, expecting to receive something from them.
050306 But Peter said, "I have no silver and gold, but I give you what I have; in the name of Jesus Christ of Nazareth, walk."
050307 And he took him by the right hand and raised him up; and immediately his feet and ankles were made strong.
050308 And leaping up he stood and walked and entered the temple with them, walking and leaping and praising God.
050309 And all the people saw him walking and praising God,
050310 and recognized him as the one who sat for alms at the Beautiful Gate of the temple; and they were filled with wonder and amazement at what had happened to him.
050311 While he clung to Peter and John, all the people ran together to them in the portico called Solomon's, astounded.
050312 And when Peter saw it he addressed the people, "Men of Israel, why do you wonder at this, or why do you stare at us, as though by our own power or piety we had made him walk?
050313 The God of Abraham and of Isaac and of Jacob, the God of our fathers, glorified his servant Jesus, whom you delivered up and denied in the presence of Pilate, when he had decided to release him.
050314 But you denied the Holy and Righteous One, and asked for a murderer to be granted to you,
050315 and killed the Author of life, whom God raised from the dead. To this we are witnesses.
050316 And his name, by faith in his name, has made this man strong whom you see and know; and the faith which is through Jesus has given the man this perfect health in the presence of you all.
050317 "And now, brethren, I know that you acted in ignorance, as did also your rulers.
050318 But what God foretold by the mouth of all the prophets, that his Christ should suffer, he thus fulfilled.
050319 Repent therefore, and turn again, that your sins may be blotted out, that times of refreshing may come from the presence of the Lord,
050320 and that he may send the Christ appointed for you, Jesus,
050321 whom heaven must receive until the time for establishing all that God spoke by the mouth of his holy prophets from of old.
050322 Moses said, 'The Lord God will raise up for you a prophet from your brethren as he raised me up. You shall listen to him in whatever he tells you.
050323 And it shall be that every soul that does not listen to that prophet shall be destroyed from the people.'
050324 And all the prophets who have spoken, from Samuel and those who came afterwards, also proclaimed these days.
050325 You are the sons of the prophets and of the covenant which God gave to your fathers, saying to Abraham, 'And in your posterity shall all the families of the earth be blessed.'
050326 God, having raised up his servant, sent him to you first, to bless you in turning every one of you from your wickedness."
050401 And as they were speaking to the people, the priests and the captain of the temple and the Sad'ducees came upon them,
050402 annoyed because they were teaching the people and proclaiming in Jesus the resurrection from the dead.
050403 And they arrested them and put them in custody until the morrow, for it was already evening.
050404 But many of those who heard the word believed; and the number of the men came to about five thousand.
050405 On the morrow their rulers and elders and scribes were gathered together in Jerusalem,
050406 with Annas the high priest and Ca'iaphas and John and Alexander, and all who were of the high-priestly family.
050407 And when they had set them in the midst, they inquired, "By what power or by what name did you do this?"
050408 Then Peter, filled with the Holy Spirit, said to them, "Rulers of the people and elders,
050409 if we are being examined today concerning a good deed done to a cripple, by what means this man has been healed,
050410 be it known to you all, and to all the people of Israel, that by the name of Jesus Christ of Nazareth, whom you crucified, whom God raised from the dead, by him this man is standing before you well.
050411 This is the stone which was rejected by you builders, but which has become the head of the corner.
050412 And there is salvation in no one else, for there is no other name under heaven given among men by which we must be saved."
050413 Now when they saw the boldness of Peter and John, and perceived that they were uneducated, common men, they wondered; and they recognized that they had been with Jesus.
050414 But seeing the man that had been healed standing beside them, they had nothing to say in opposition.
050415 But when they had commanded them to go aside out of the council, they conferred with one another,
050416 saying, "What shall we do with these men? For that a notable sign has been performed through them is manifest to all the inhabitants of Jerusalem, and we cannot deny it.
050417 But in order that it may spread no further among the people, let us warn them to speak no more to any one in this name."
050418 So they called them and charged them not to speak or teach at all in the name of Jesus.
050419 But Peter and John answered them, "Whether it is right in the sight of God to listen to you rather than to God, you must judge;
050420 for we cannot but speak of what we have seen and heard."
050421 And when they had further threatened them, they let them go, finding no way to punish them, because of the people; for all men praised God for what had happened.
050422 For the man on whom this sign of healing was performed was more than forty years old.
050423 When they were released they went to their friends and reported what the chief priests and the elders had said to them.
050424 And when they heard it, they lifted their voices together to God and said, "Sovereign Lord, who didst make the heaven and the earth and the sea and everything in them,
050425 who by the mouth of our father David, thy servant, didst say by the Holy Spirit, 'Why did the Gentiles rage, and the peoples imagine vain things?
050426 The kings of the earth set themselves in array, and the rulers were gathered together, against the Lord and against his Anointed' --
050427 for truly in this city there were gathered together against thy holy servant Jesus, whom thou didst anoint, both Herod and Pontius Pilate, with the Gentiles and the peoples of Israel,
050428 to do whatever thy hand and thy plan had predestined to take place.
050429 And now, Lord, look upon their threats, and grant to thy servants to speak thy word with all boldness,
050430 while thou stretchest out thy hand to heal, and signs and wonders are performed through the name of thy holy servant Jesus."
050431 And when they had prayed, the place in which they were gathered together was shaken; and they were all filled with the Holy Spirit and spoke the word of God with boldness.
050432 Now the company of those who believed were of one heart and soul, and no one said that any of the things which he possessed was his own, but they had everything in common.
050433 And with great power the apostles gave their testimony to the resurrection of the Lord Jesus, and great grace was upon them all.
050434 There was not a needy person among them, for as many as were possessors of lands or houses sold them, and brought the proceeds of what was sold
050435 and laid it at the apostles' feet; and distribution was made to each as any had need.
050436 Thus Joseph who was surnamed by the apostles Barnabas (which means, Son of encouragement), a Levite, a native of Cyprus,
050437 sold a field which belonged to him, and brought the money and laid it at the apostles' feet.
050501 But a man named Anani'as with his wife Sapphi'ra sold a piece of property,
050502 and with his wife's knowledge he kept back some of the proceeds, and brought only a part and laid it at the apostles' feet.
050503 But Peter said, "Anani'as, why has Satan filled your heart to lie to the Holy Spirit and to keep back part of the proceeds of the land?
050504 While it remained unsold, did it not remain your own? And after it was sold, was it not at your disposal? How is it that you have contrived this deed in your heart? You have not lied to men but to God."
050505 When Anani'as heard these words, he fell down and died. And great fear came upon all who heard of it.
050506 The young men rose and wrapped him up and carried him out and buried him.
050507 After an interval of about three hours his wife came in, not knowing what had happened.
050508 And Peter said to her, "Tell me whether you sold the land for so much." And she said, "Yes, for so much."
050509 But Peter said to her, "How is it that you have agreed together to tempt the Spirit of the Lord? Hark, the feet of those that have buried your husband are at the door, and they will carry you out."
050510 Immediately she fell down at his feet and died. When the young men came in they found her dead, and they carried her out and buried her beside her husband.
050511 And great fear came upon the whole church, and upon all who heard of these things.
050512 Now many signs and wonders were done among the people by the hands of the apostles. And they were all together in Solomon's Portico.
050513 None of the rest dared join them, but the people held them in high honor.
050514 And more than ever believers were added to the Lord, multitudes both of men and women,
050515 so that they even carried out the sick into the streets, and laid them on beds and pallets, that as Peter came by at least his shadow might fall on some of them.
050516 The people also gathered from the towns around Jerusalem, bringing the sick and those afflicted with unclean spirits, and they were all healed.
050517 But the high priest rose up and all who were with him, that is, the party of the Sad'ducees, and filled with jealousy
050518 they arrested the apostles and put them in the common prison.
050519 But at night an angel of the Lord opened the prison doors and brought them out and said,
050520 "Go and stand in the temple and speak to the people all the words of this Life."
050521 And when they heard this, they entered the temple at daybreak and taught. Now the high priest came and those who were with him and called together the council and all the senate of Israel, and sent to the prison to have them brought.
050522 But when the officers came, they did not find them in the prison, and they returned and reported,
050523 "We found the prison securely locked and the sentries standing at the doors, but when we opened it we found no one inside."
050524 Now when the captain of the temple and the chief priests heard these words, they were much perplexed about them, wondering what this would come to.
050525 And some one came and told them, "The men whom you put in prison are standing in the temple and teaching the people."
050526 Then the captain with the officers went and brought them, but without violence, for they were afraid of being stoned by the people.
050527 And when they had brought them, they set them before the council. And the high priest questioned them,
050528 saying, "We strictly charged you not to teach in this name, yet here you have filled Jerusalem with your teaching and you intend to bring this man's blood upon us."
050529 But Peter and the apostles answered, "We must obey God rather than men.
050530 The God of our fathers raised Jesus whom you killed by hanging him on a tree.
050531 God exalted him at his right hand as Leader and Savior, to give repentance to Israel and forgiveness of sins.
050532 And we are witnesses to these things, and so is the Holy Spirit whom God has given to those who obey him."
050533 When they heard this they were enraged and wanted to kill them.
050534 But a Pharisee in the council named Gama'li-el, a teacher of the law, held in honor by all the people, stood up and ordered the men to be put outside for a while.
050535 And he said to them, "Men of Israel, take care what you do with these men.
050536 For before these days Theu'das arose, giving himself out to be somebody, and a number of men, about four hundred, joined him; but he was slain and all who followed him were dispersed and came to nothing.
050537 After him Judas the Galilean arose in the days of the census and drew away some of the people after him; he also perished, and all who followed him were scattered.
050538 So in the present case I tell you, keep away from these men and let them alone; for if this plan or this undertaking is of men, it will fail;
050539 but if it is of God, you will not be able to overthrow them. You might even be found opposing God!"
050540 So they took his advice, and when they had called in the apostles, they beat them and charged them not to speak in the name of Jesus, and let them go.
050541 Then they left the presence of the council, rejoicing that they were counted worthy to suffer dishonor for the name.
050542 And every day in the temple and at home they did not cease teaching and preaching Jesus as the Christ.
050601 Now in these days when the disciples were increasing in number, the Hellenists murmured against the Hebrews because their widows were neglected in the daily distribution.
050602 And the twelve summoned the body of the disciples and said, "It is not right that we should give up preaching the word of God to serve tables.
050603 Therefore, brethren, pick out from among you seven men of good repute, full of the Spirit and of wisdom, whom we may appoint to this duty.
050604 But we will devote ourselves to prayer and to the ministry of the word."
050605 And what they said pleased the whole multitude, and they chose Stephen, a man full of faith and of the Holy Spirit, and Philip, and Proch'orus, and Nica'nor, and Ti'mon, and Par'menas, and Nicola'us, a proselyte of Antioch.
050606 These they set before the apostles, and they prayed and laid their hands upon them.
050607 And the word of God increased; and the number of the disciples multiplied greatly in Jerusalem, and a great many of the priests were obedient to the faith.
050608 And Stephen, full of grace and power, did great wonders and signs among the people.
050609 Then some of those who belonged to the synagogue of the Freedmen (as it was called), and of the Cyre'nians, and of the Alexandrians, and of those from Cili'cia and Asia, arose and disputed with Stephen.
050610 But they could not withstand the wisdom and the Spirit with which he spoke.
050611 Then they secretly instigated men, who said, "We have heard him speak blasphemous words against Moses and God."
050612 And they stirred up the people and the elders and the scribes, and they came upon him and seized him and brought him before the council,
050613 and set up false witnesses who said, "This man never ceases to speak words against this holy place and the law;
050614 for we have heard him say that this Jesus of Nazareth will destroy this place, and will change the customs which Moses delivered to us."
050615 And gazing at him, all who sat in the council saw that his face was like the face of an angel.
050701 And the high priest said, "Is this so?"
050702 And Stephen said: "Brethren and fathers, hear me. The God of glory appeared to our father Abraham, when he was in Mesopota'mia, before he lived in Haran,
050703 and said to him, 'Depart from your land and from your kindred and go into the land which I will show you.'
050704 Then he departed from the land of the Chalde'ans, and lived in Haran. And after his father died, God removed him from there into this land in which you are now living;
050705 yet he gave him no inheritance in it, not even a foot's length, but promised to give it to him in possession and to his posterity after him, though he had no child.
050706 And God spoke to this effect, that his posterity would be aliens in a land belonging to others, who would enslave them and ill-treat them four hundred years.
050707 'But I will judge the nation which they serve,' said God, 'and after that they shall come out and worship me in this place.'
050708 And he gave him the covenant of circumcision. And so Abraham became the father of Isaac, and circumcised him on the eighth day; and Isaac became the father of Jacob, and Jacob of the twelve patriarchs.
050709 "And the patriarchs, jealous of Joseph, sold him into Egypt; but God was with him,
050710 and rescued him out of all his afflictions, and gave him favor and wisdom before Pharaoh, king of Egypt, who made him governor over Egypt and over all his household.
050711 Now there came a famine throughout all Egypt and Canaan, and great affliction, and our fathers could find no food.
050712 But when Jacob heard that there was grain in Egypt, he sent forth our fathers the first time.
050713 And at the second visit Joseph made himself known to his brothers, and Joseph's family became known to Pharaoh.
050714 And Joseph sent and called to him Jacob his father and all his kindred, seventy-five souls;
050715 and Jacob went down into Egypt. And he died, himself and our fathers,
050716 and they were carried back to Shechem and laid in the tomb that Abraham had bought for a sum of silver from the sons of Hamor in Shechem.
050717 "But as the time of the promise drew near, which God had granted to Abraham, the people grew and multiplied in Egypt
050718 till there arose over Egypt another king who had not known Joseph.
050719 He dealt craftily with our race and forced our fathers to expose their infants, that they might not be kept alive.
050720 At this time Moses was born, and was beautiful before God. And he was brought up for three months in his father's house;
050721 and when he was exposed, Pharaoh's daughter adopted him and brought him up as her own son.
050722 And Moses was instructed in all the wisdom of the Egyptians, and he was mighty in his words and deeds.
050723 "When he was forty years old, it came into his heart to visit his brethren, the sons of Israel.
050724 And seeing one of them being wronged, he defended the oppressed man and avenged him by striking the Egyptian.
050725 He supposed that his brethren understood that God was giving them deliverance by his hand, but they did not understand.
050726 And on the following day he appeared to them as they were quarreling and would have reconciled them, saying, 'Men, you are brethren, why do you wrong each other?'
050727 But the man who was wronging his neighbor thrust him aside, saying, 'Who made you a ruler and a judge over us?
050728 Do you want to kill me as you killed the Egyptian yesterday?'
050729 At this retort Moses fled, and became an exile in the land of Mid'ian, where he became the father of two sons.
050730 "Now when forty years had passed, an angel appeared to him in the wilderness of Mount Sinai, in a flame of fire in a bush.
050731 When Moses saw it he wondered at the sight; and as he drew near to look, the voice of the Lord came,
050732 'I am the God of your fathers, the God of Abraham and of Isaac and of Jacob.' And Moses trembled and did not dare to look.
050733 And the Lord said to him, 'Take off the shoes from your feet, for the place where you are standing is holy ground.
050734 I have surely seen the ill-treatment of my people that are in Egypt and heard their groaning, and I have come down to deliver them. And now come, I will send you to Egypt.'
050735 "This Moses whom they refused, saying, 'Who made you a ruler and a judge?' God sent as both ruler and deliverer by the hand of the angel that appeared to him in the bush.
050736 He led them out, having performed wonders and signs in Egypt and at the Red Sea, and in the wilderness for forty years.
050737 This is the Moses who said to the Israelites, 'God will raise up for you a prophet from your brethren as he raised me up.'
050738 This is he who was in the congregation in the wilderness with the angel who spoke to him at Mount Sinai, and with our fathers; and he received living oracles to give to us.
050739 Our fathers refused to obey him, but thrust him aside, and in their hearts they turned to Egypt,
050740 saying to Aaron, 'Make for us gods to go before us; as for this Moses who led us out from the land of Egypt, we do not know what has become of him.'
050741 And they made a calf in those days, and offered a sacrifice to the idol and rejoiced in the works of their hands.
050742 But God turned and gave them over to worship the host of heaven, as it is written in the book of the prophets: 'Did you offer to me slain beasts and sacrifices, forty years in the wilderness, O house of Israel?
050743 And you took up the tent of Moloch, and the star of the god Rephan, the figures which you made to worship; and I will remove you beyond Babylon.'
050744 "Our fathers had the tent of witness in the wilderness, even as he who spoke to Moses directed him to make it, according to the pattern that he had seen.
050745 Our fathers in turn brought it in with Joshua when they dispossessed the nations which God thrust out before our fathers. So it was until the days of David,
050746 who found favor in the sight of God and asked leave to find a habitation for the God of Jacob.
050747 But it was Solomon who built a house for him.
050748 Yet the Most High does not dwell in houses made with hands; as the prophet says,
050749 'Heaven is my throne, and earth my footstool. What house will you build for me, says the Lord, or what is the place of my rest?
050750 Did not my hand make all these things?'
050751 "You stiff-necked people, uncircumcised in heart and ears, you always resist the Holy Spirit. As your fathers did, so do you.
050752 Which of the prophets did not your fathers persecute? And they killed those who announced beforehand the coming of the Righteous One, whom you have now betrayed and murdered,
050753 you who received the law as delivered by angels and did not keep it."
050754 Now when they heard these things they were enraged, and they ground their teeth against him.
050755 But he, full of the Holy Spirit, gazed into heaven and saw the glory of God, and Jesus standing at the right hand of God;
050756 and he said, "Behold, I see the heavens opened, and the Son of man standing at the right hand of God."
050757 But they cried out with a loud voice and stopped their ears and rushed together upon him.
050758 Then they cast him out of the city and stoned him; and the witnesses laid down their garments at the feet of a young man named Saul.
050759 And as they were stoning Stephen, he prayed, "Lord Jesus, receive my spirit."
050760 And he knelt down and cried with a loud voice, "Lord, do not hold this sin against them." And when he had said this, he fell asleep.
050801 And Saul was consenting to his death. And on that day a great persecution arose against the church in Jerusalem; and they were all scattered throughout the region of Judea and Sama'ria, except the apostles.
050802 Devout men buried Stephen, and made great lamentation over him.
050803 But Saul was ravaging the church, and entering house after house, he dragged off men and women and committed them to prison.
050804 Now those who were scattered went about preaching the word.
050805 Philip went down to a city of Sama'ria, and proclaimed to them the Christ.
050806 And the multitudes with one accord gave heed to what was said by Philip, when they heard him and saw the signs which he did.
050807 For unclean spirits came out of many who were possessed, crying with a loud voice; and many who were paralyzed or lame were healed.
050808 So there was much joy in that city.
050809 But there was a man named Simon who had previously practiced magic in the city and amazed the nation of Sama'ria, saying that he himself was somebody great.
050810 They all gave heed to him, from the least to the greatest, saying, "This man is that power of God which is called Great."
050811 And they gave heed to him, because for a long time he had amazed them with his magic.
050812 But when they believed Philip as he preached good news about the kingdom of God and the name of Jesus Christ, they were baptized, both men and women.
050813 Even Simon himself believed, and after being baptized he continued with Philip. And seeing signs and great miracles performed, he was amazed.
050814 Now when the apostles at Jerusalem heard that Sama'ria had received the word of God, they sent to them Peter and John,
050815 who came down and prayed for them that they might receive the Holy Spirit;
050816 for it had not yet fallen on any of them, but they had only been baptized in the name of the Lord Jesus.
050817 Then they laid their hands on them and they received the Holy Spirit.
050818 Now when Simon saw that the Spirit was given through the laying on of the apostles' hands, he offered them money,
050819 saying, "Give me also this power, that any one on whom I lay my hands may receive the Holy Spirit."
050820 But Peter said to him, "Your silver perish with you, because you thought you could obtain the gift of God with money!
050821 You have neither part nor lot in this matter, for your heart is not right before God.
050822 Repent therefore of this wickedness of yours, and pray to the Lord that, if possible, the intent of your heart may be forgiven you.
050823 For I see that you are in the gall of bitterness and in the bond of iniquity."
050824 And Simon answered, "Pray for me to the Lord, that nothing of what you have said may come upon me."
050825 Now when they had testified and spoken the word of the Lord, they returned to Jerusalem, preaching the gospel to many villages of the Samaritans.
050826 But an angel of the Lord said to Philip, "Rise and go toward the south to the road that goes down from Jerusalem to Gaza." This is a desert road.
050827 And he rose and went. And behold, an Ethiopian, a eunuch, a minister of the Can'dace, queen of the Ethiopians, in charge of all her treasure, had come to Jerusalem to worship
050828 and was returning; seated in his chariot, he was reading the prophet Isaiah.
050829 And the Spirit said to Philip, "Go up and join this chariot."
050830 So Philip ran to him, and heard him reading Isaiah the prophet, and asked, "Do you understand what you are reading?"
050831 And he said, "How can I, unless some one guides me?" And he invited Philip to come up and sit with him.
050832 Now the passage of the scripture which he was reading was this: "As a sheep led to the slaughter or a lamb before its shearer is dumb, so he opens not his mouth.
050833 In his humiliation justice was denied him. Who can describe his generation? For his life is taken up from the earth."
050834 And the eunuch said to Philip, "About whom, pray, does the prophet say this, about himself or about some one else?"
050835 Then Philip opened his mouth, and beginning with this scripture he told him the good news of Jesus.
050836 And as they went along the road they came to some water, and the eunuch said, "See, here is water! What is to prevent my being baptized?"
050837
050838 And he commanded the chariot to stop, and they both went down into the water, Philip and the eunuch, and he baptized him.
050839 And when they came up out of the water, the Spirit of the Lord caught up Philip; and the eunuch saw him no more, and went on his way rejoicing.
050840 But Philip was found at Azo'tus, and passing on he preached the gospel to all the towns till he came to Caesare'a.
050901 But Saul, still breathing threats and murder against the disciples of the Lord, went to the high priest
050902 and asked him for letters to the synagogues at Damascus, so that if he found any belonging to the Way, men or women, he might bring them bound to Jerusalem.
050903 Now as he journeyed he approached Damascus, and suddenly a light from heaven flashed about him.
050904 And he fell to the ground and heard a voice saying to him, "Saul, Saul, why do you persecute me?"
050905 And he said, "Who are you, Lord?" And he said, "I am Jesus, whom you are persecuting;
050906 but rise and enter the city, and you will be told what you are to do."
050907 The men who were traveling with him stood speechless, hearing the voice but seeing no one.
050908 Saul arose from the ground; and when his eyes were opened, he could see nothing; so they led him by the hand and brought him into Damascus.
050909 And for three days he was without sight, and neither ate nor drank.
050910 Now there was a disciple at Damascus named Anani'as. The Lord said to him in a vision, "Anani'as." And he said, "Here I am, Lord."
050911 And the Lord said to him, "Rise and go to the street called Straight, and inquire in the house of Judas for a man of Tarsus named Saul; for behold, he is praying,
050912 and he has seen a man named Anani'as come in and lay his hands on him so that he might regain his sight."
050913 But Anani'as answered, "Lord, I have heard from many about this man, how much evil he has done to thy saints at Jerusalem;
050914 and here he has authority from the chief priests to bind all who call upon thy name."
050915 But the Lord said to him, "Go, for he is a chosen instrument of mine to carry my name before the Gentiles and kings and the sons of Israel;
050916 for I will show him how much he must suffer for the sake of my name."
050917 So Anani'as departed and entered the house. And laying his hands on him he said, "Brother Saul, the Lord Jesus who appeared to you on the road by which you came, has sent me that you may regain your sight and be filled with the Holy Spirit."
050918 And immediately something like scales fell from his eyes and he regained his sight. Then he rose and was baptized,
050919 and took food and was strengthened. For several days he was with the disciples at Damascus.
050920 And in the synagogues immediately he proclaimed Jesus, saying, "He is the Son of God."
050921 And all who heard him were amazed, and said, "Is not this the man who made havoc in Jerusalem of those who called on this name? And he has come here for this purpose, to bring them bound before the chief priests."
050922 But Saul increased all the more in strength, and confounded the Jews who lived in Damascus by proving that Jesus was the Christ.
050923 When many days had passed, the Jews plotted to kill him,
050924 but their plot became known to Saul. They were watching the gates day and night, to kill him;
050925 but his disciples took him by night and let him down over the wall, lowering him in a basket.
050926 And when he had come to Jerusalem he attempted to join the disciples; and they were all afraid of him, for they did not believe that he was a disciple.
050927 But Barnabas took him, and brought him to the apostles, and declared to them how on the road he had seen the Lord, who spoke to him, and how at Damascus he had preached boldly in the name of Jesus.
050928 So he went in and out among them at Jerusalem,
050929 preaching boldly in the name of the Lord. And he spoke and disputed against the Hellenists; but they were seeking to kill him.
050930 And when the brethren knew it, they brought him down to Caesare'a, and sent him off to Tarsus.
050931 So the church throughout all Judea and Galilee and Sama'ria had peace and was built up; and walking in the fear of the Lord and in the comfort of the Holy Spirit it was multiplied.
050932 Now as Peter went here and there among them all, he came down also to the saints that lived at Lydda.
050933 There he found a man named Aene'as, who had been bedridden for eight years and was paralyzed.
050934 And Peter said to him, "Aene'as, Jesus Christ heals you; rise and make your bed." And immediately he rose.
050935 And all the residents of Lydda and Sharon saw him, and they turned to the Lord.
050936 Now there was at Joppa a disciple named Tabitha, which means Dorcas. She was full of good works and acts of charity.
050937 In those days she fell sick and died; and when they had washed her, they laid her in an upper room.
050938 Since Lydda was near Joppa, the disciples, hearing that Peter was there, sent two men to him entreating him, "Please come to us without delay."
050939 So Peter rose and went with them. And when he had come, they took him to the upper room. All the widows stood beside him weeping, and showing tunics and other garments which Dorcas made while she was with them.
050940 But Peter put them all outside and knelt down and prayed; then turning to the body he said, "Tabitha, rise." And she opened her eyes, and when she saw Peter she sat up.
050941 And he gave her his hand and lifted her up. Then calling the saints and widows he presented her alive.
050942 And it became known throughout all Joppa, and many believed in the Lord.
050943 And he stayed in Joppa for many days with one Simon, a tanner.
051001 At Caesare'a there was a man named Cornelius, a centurion of what was known as the Italian Cohort,
051002 a devout man who feared God with all his household, gave alms liberally to the people, and prayed constantly to God.
051003 About the ninth hour of the day he saw clearly in a vision an angel of God coming in and saying to him, "Cornelius."
051004 And he stared at him in terror, and said, "What is it, Lord?" And he said to him, "Your prayers and your alms have ascended as a memorial before God.
051005 And now send men to Joppa, and bring one Simon who is called Peter;
051006 he is lodging with Simon, a tanner, whose house is by the seaside."
051007 When the angel who spoke to him had departed, he called two of his servants and a devout soldier from among those that waited on him,
051008 and having related everything to them, he sent them to Joppa.
051009 The next day, as they were on their journey and coming near the city, Peter went up on the housetop to pray, about the sixth hour.
051010 And he became hungry and desired something to eat; but while they were preparing it, he fell into a trance
051011 and saw the heaven opened, and something descending, like a great sheet, let down by four corners upon the earth.
051012 In it were all kinds of animals and reptiles and birds of the air.
051013 And there came a voice to him, "Rise, Peter; kill and eat."
051014 But Peter said, "No, Lord; for I have never eaten anything that is common or unclean."
051015 And the voice came to him again a second time, "What God has cleansed, you must not call common."
051016 This happened three times, and the thing was taken up at once to heaven.
051017 Now while Peter was inwardly perplexed as to what the vision which he had seen might mean, behold, the men that were sent by Cornelius, having made inquiry for Simon's house, stood before the gate
051018 and called out to ask whether Simon who was called Peter was lodging there.
051019 And while Peter was pondering the vision, the Spirit said to him, "Behold, three men are looking for you.
051020 Rise and go down, and accompany them without hesitation; for I have sent them."
051021 And Peter went down to the men and said, "I am the one you are looking for; what is the reason for your coming?"
051022 And they said, "Cornelius, a centurion, an upright and God-fearing man, who is well spoken of by the whole Jewish nation, was directed by a holy angel to send for you to come to his house, and to hear what you have to say."
051023 So he called them in to be his guests. The next day he rose and went off with them, and some of the brethren from Joppa accompanied him.
051024 And on the following day they entered Caesare'a. Cornelius was expecting them and had called together his kinsmen and close friends.
051025 When Peter entered, Cornelius met him and fell down at his feet and worshiped him.
051026 But Peter lifted him up, saying, "Stand up; I too am a man."
051027 And as he talked with him, he went in and found many persons gathered;
051028 and he said to them, "You yourselves know how unlawful it is for a Jew to associate with or to visit any one of another nation; but God has shown me that I should not call any man common or unclean.
051029 So when I was sent for, I came without objection. I ask then why you sent for me."
051030 And Cornelius said, "Four days ago, about this hour, I was keeping the ninth hour of prayer in my house; and behold, a man stood before me in bright apparel,
051031 saying, 'Cornelius, your prayer has been heard and your alms have been remembered before God.
051032 Send therefore to Joppa and ask for Simon who is called Peter; he is lodging in the house of Simon, a tanner, by the seaside.'
