052804 When the natives saw the creature hanging from his hand, they said to one another, "No doubt this man is a murderer. Though he has escaped from the sea, justice has not allowed him to live."
052805 He, however, shook off the creature into the fire and suffered no harm.
052806 They waited, expecting him to swell up or suddenly fall down dead; but when they had waited a long time and saw no misfortune come to him, they changed their minds and said that he was a god.
052807 Now in the neighborhood of that place were lands belonging to the chief man of the island, named Publius, who received us and entertained us hospitably for three days.
052808 It happened that the father of Publius lay sick with fever and dysentery; and Paul visited him and prayed, and putting his hands on him healed him.
052809 And when this had taken place, the rest of the people on the island who had diseases also came and were cured.
052810 They presented many gifts to us; and when we sailed, they put on board whatever we needed.
052811 After three months we set sail in a ship which had wintered in the island, a ship of Alexandria, with the Twin Brothers as figurehead.
052812 Putting in at Syracuse, we stayed there for three days.
052813 And from there we made a circuit and arrived at Rhe'gium; and after one day a south wind sprang up, and on the second day we came to Pute'oli.
052814 There we found brethren, and were invited to stay with them for seven days. And so we came to Rome.
052815 And the brethren there, when they heard of us, came as far as the Forum of Ap'pius and Three Taverns to meet us. On seeing them Paul thanked God and took courage.
052816 And when we came into Rome, Paul was allowed to stay by himself, with the soldier that guarded him.
052817 After three days he called together the local leaders of the Jews; and when they had gathered, he said to them, "Brethren, though I had done nothing against the people or the customs of our fathers, yet I was delivered prisoner from Jerusalem into the hands of the Romans.
052818 When they had examined me, they wished to set me at liberty, because there was no reason for the death penalty in my case.
052819 But when the Jews objected, I was compelled to appeal to Caesar -- though I had no charge to bring against my nation.
052820 For this reason therefore I have asked to see you and speak with you, since it is because of the hope of Israel that I am bound with this chain."
052821 And they said to him, "We have received no letters from Judea about you, and none of the brethren coming here has reported or spoken any evil about you.
052822 But we desire to hear from you what your views are; for with regard to this sect we know that everywhere it is spoken against."
052823 When they had appointed a day for him, they came to him at his lodging in great numbers. And he expounded the matter to them from morning till evening, testifying to the kingdom of God and trying to convince them about Jesus both from the law of Moses and from the prophets.
052824 And some were convinced by what he said, while others disbelieved.
052825 So, as they disagreed among themselves, they departed, after Paul had made one statement: "The Holy Spirit was right in saying to your fathers through Isaiah the prophet:
052826 'Go to this people, and say, You shall indeed hear but never understand, and you shall indeed see but never perceive.
052827 For this people's heart has grown dull, and their ears are heavy of hearing, and their eyes they have closed; lest they should perceive with their eyes, and hear with their ears, and understand with their heart, and turn for me to heal them.'
052828 Let it be known to you then that this salvation of God has been sent to the Gentiles; they will listen."
052829
052830 And he lived there two whole years at his own expense, and welcomed all who came to him,
052831 preaching the kingdom of God and teaching about the Lord Jesus Christ quite openly and unhindered.
060101 Paul, a servant of Jesus Christ, called to be an apostle, set apart for the gospel of God
060102 which he promised beforehand through his prophets in the holy scriptures,
060103 the gospel concerning his Son, who was descended from David according to the flesh
060104 and designated Son of God in power according to the Spirit of holiness by his resurrection from the dead, Jesus Christ our Lord,
060105 through whom we have received grace and apostleship to bring about the obedience of faith for the sake of his name among all the nations,
060106 including yourselves who are called to belong to Jesus Christ;
060107 To all God's beloved in Rome, who are called to be saints: Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ.
060108 First, I thank my God through Jesus Christ for all of you, because your faith is proclaimed in all the world.
060109 For God is my witness, whom I serve with my spirit in the gospel of his Son, that without ceasing I mention you always in my prayers,
060110 asking that somehow by God's will I may now at last succeed in coming to you.
060111 For I long to see you, that I may impart to you some spiritual gift to strengthen you,
060112 that is, that we may be mutually encouraged by each other's faith, both yours and mine.
060113 I want you to know, brethren, that I have often intended to come to you (but thus far have been prevented), in order that I may reap some harvest among you as well as among the rest of the Gentiles.
060114 I am under obligation both to Greeks and to barbarians, both to the wise and to the foolish:
060115 so I am eager to preach the gospel to you also who are in Rome.
060116 For I am not ashamed of the gospel: it is the power of God for salvation to every one who has faith, to the Jew first and also to the Greek.
060117 For in it the righteousness of God is revealed through faith for faith; as it is written, "He who through faith is righteous shall live."
060118 For the wrath of God is revealed from heaven against all ungodliness and wickedness of men who by their wickedness suppress the truth.
060119 For what can be known about God is plain to them, because God has shown it to them.
060120 Ever since the creation of the world his invisible nature, namely, his eternal power and deity, has been clearly perceived in the things that have been made. So they are without excuse;
060121 for although they knew God they did not honor him as God or give thanks to him, but they became futile in their thinking and their senseless minds were darkened.
060122 Claiming to be wise, they became fools,
060123 and exchanged the glory of the immortal God for images resembling mortal man or birds or animals or reptiles.
060124 Therefore God gave them up in the lusts of their hearts to impurity, to the dishonoring of their bodies among themselves,
060125 because they exchanged the truth about God for a lie and worshiped and served the creature rather than the Creator, who is blessed for ever! Amen.
060126 For this reason God gave them up to dishonorable passions. Their women exchanged natural relations for unnatural,
060127 and the men likewise gave up natural relations with women and were consumed with passion for one another, men committing shameless acts with men and receiving in their own persons the due penalty for their error.
060128 And since they did not see fit to acknowledge God, God gave them up to a base mind and to improper conduct.
060129 They were filled with all manner of wickedness, evil, covetousness, malice. Full of envy, murder, strife, deceit, malignity, they are gossips,
060130 slanderers, haters of God, insolent, haughty, boastful, inventors of evil, disobedient to parents,
060131 foolish, faithless, heartless, ruthless.
060132 Though they know God's decree that those who do such things deserve to die, they not only do them but approve those who practice them.
060201 Therefore you have no excuse, O man, whoever you are, when you judge another; for in passing judgment upon him you condemn yourself, because you, the judge, are doing the very same things.
060202 We know that the judgment of God rightly falls upon those who do such things.
060203 Do you suppose, O man, that when you judge those who do such things and yet do them yourself, you will escape the judgment of God?
060204 Or do you presume upon the riches of his kindness and forbearance and patience? Do you not know that God's kindness is meant to lead you to repentance?
060205 But by your hard and impenitent heart you are storing up wrath for yourself on the day of wrath when God's righteous judgment will be revealed.
060206 For he will render to every man according to his works:
060207 to those who by patience in well-doing seek for glory and honor and immortality, he will give eternal life;
060208 but for those who are factious and do not obey the truth, but obey wickedness, there will be wrath and fury.
060209 There will be tribulation and distress for every human being who does evil, the Jew first and also the Greek,
060210 but glory and honor and peace for every one who does good, the Jew first and also the Greek.
060211 For God shows no partiality.
060212 All who have sinned without the law will also perish without the law, and all who have sinned under the law will be judged by the law.
060213 For it is not the hearers of the law who are righteous before God, but the doers of the law who will be justified.
060214 When Gentiles who have not the law do by nature what the law requires, they are a law to themselves, even though they do not have the law.
060215 They show that what the law requires is written on their hearts, while their conscience also bears witness and their conflicting thoughts accuse or perhaps excuse them
060216 on that day when, according to my gospel, God judges the secrets of men by Christ Jesus.
060217 But if you call yourself a Jew and rely upon the law and boast of your relation to God
060218 and know his will and approve what is excellent, because you are instructed in the law,
060219 and if you are sure that you are a guide to the blind, a light to those who are in darkness,
060220 a corrector of the foolish, a teacher of children, having in the law the embodiment of knowledge and truth --
060221 you then who teach others, will you not teach yourself? While you preach against stealing, do you steal?
060222 You who say that one must not commit adultery, do you commit adultery? You who abhor idols, do you rob temples?
060223 You who boast in the law, do you dishonor God by breaking the law?
060224 For, as it is written, "The name of God is blasphemed among the Gentiles because of you."
060225 Circumcision indeed is of value if you obey the law; but if you break the law, your circumcision becomes uncircumcision.
060226 So, if a man who is uncircumcised keeps the precepts of the law, will not his uncircumcision be regarded as circumcision?
060227 Then those who are physically uncircumcised but keep the law will condemn you who have the written code and circumcision but break the law.
060228 For he is not a real Jew who is one outwardly, nor is true circumcision something external and physical.
060229 He is a Jew who is one inwardly, and real circumcision is a matter of the heart, spiritual and not literal. His praise is not from men but from God.
060301 Then what advantage has the Jew? Or what is the value of circumcision?
060302 Much in every way. To begin with, the Jews are entrusted with the oracles of God.
060303 What if some were unfaithful? Does their faithlessness nullify the faithfulness of God?
060304 By no means! Let God be true though every man be false, as it is written, "That thou mayest be justified in thy words, and prevail when thou art judged."
060305 But if our wickedness serves to show the justice of God, what shall we say? That God is unjust to inflict wrath on us? (I speak in a human way.)
060306 By no means! For then how could God judge the world?
060307 But if through my falsehood God's truthfulness abounds to his glory, why am I still being condemned as a sinner?
060308 And why not do evil that good may come? -- as some people slanderously charge us with saying. Their condemnation is just.
060309 What then? Are we Jews any better off? No, not at all; for I have already charged that all men, both Jews and Greeks, are under the power of sin,
060310 as it is written: "None is righteous, no, not one;
060311 no one understands, no one seeks for God.
060312 All have turned aside, together they have gone wrong; no one does good, not even one."
060313 "Their throat is an open grave, they use their tongues to deceive." "The venom of asps is under their lips."
060314 "Their mouth is full of curses and bitterness."
060315 "Their feet are swift to shed blood,
060316 in their paths are ruin and misery,
060317 and the way of peace they do not know."
060318 "There is no fear of God before their eyes."
060319 Now we know that whatever the law says it speaks to those who are under the law, so that every mouth may be stopped, and the whole world may be held accountable to God.
060320 For no human being will be justified in his sight by works of the law, since through the law comes knowledge of sin.
060321 But now the righteousness of God has been manifested apart from law, although the law and the prophets bear witness to it,
060322 the righteousness of God through faith in Jesus Christ for all who believe. For there is no distinction;
060323 since all have sinned and fall short of the glory of God,
060324 they are justified by his grace as a gift, through the redemption which is in Christ Jesus,
060325 whom God put forward as an expiation by his blood, to be received by faith. This was to show God's righteousness, because in his divine forbearance he had passed over former sins;
060326 it was to prove at the present time that he himself is righteous and that he justifies him who has faith in Jesus.
060327 Then what becomes of our boasting? It is excluded. On what principle? On the principle of works? No, but on the principle of faith.
060328 For we hold that a man is justified by faith apart from works of law.
060329 Or is God the God of Jews only? Is he not the God of Gentiles also? Yes, of Gentiles also,
060330 since God is one; and he will justify the circumcised on the ground of their faith and the uncircumcised through their faith.
060331 Do we then overthrow the law by this faith? By no means! On the contrary, we uphold the law.
060401 What then shall we say about Abraham, our forefather according to the flesh?
060402 For if Abraham was justified by works, he has something to boast about, but not before God.
060403 For what does the scripture say? "Abraham believed God, and it was reckoned to him as righteousness."
060404 Now to one who works, his wages are not reckoned as a gift but as his due.
060405 And to one who does not work but trusts him who justifies the ungodly, his faith is reckoned as righteousness.
060406 So also David pronounces a blessing upon the man to whom God reckons righteousness apart from works:
060407 "Blessed are those whose iniquities are forgiven, and whose sins are covered;
060408 blessed is the man against whom the Lord will not reckon his sin."
060409 Is this blessing pronounced only upon the circumcised, or also upon the uncircumcised? We say that faith was reckoned to Abraham as righteousness.
060410 How then was it reckoned to him? Was it before or after he had been circumcised? It was not after, but before he was circumcised.
060411 He received circumcision as a sign or seal of the righteousness which he had by faith while he was still uncircumcised. The purpose was to make him the father of all who believe without being circumcised and who thus have righteousness reckoned to them,
060412 and likewise the father of the circumcised who are not merely circumcised but also follow the example of the faith which our father Abraham had before he was circumcised.
060413 The promise to Abraham and his descendants, that they should inherit the world, did not come through the law but through the righteousness of faith.
060414 If it is the adherents of the law who are to be the heirs, faith is null and the promise is void.
060415 For the law brings wrath, but where there is no law there is no transgression.
060416 That is why it depends on faith, in order that the promise may rest on grace and be guaranteed to all his descendants -- not only to the adherents of the law but also to those who share the faith of Abraham, for he is the father of us all,
060417 as it is written, "I have made you the father of many nations" -- in the presence of the God in whom he believed, who gives life to the dead and calls into existence the things that do not exist.
060418 In hope he believed against hope, that he should become the father of many nations; as he had been told, "So shall your descendants be."
060419 He did not weaken in faith when he considered his own body, which was as good as dead because he was about a hundred years old, or when he considered the barrenness of Sarah's womb.
060420 No distrust made him waver concerning the promise of God, but he grew strong in his faith as he gave glory to God,
060421 fully convinced that God was able to do what he had promised.
060422 That is why his faith was "reckoned to him as righteousness."
060423 But the words, "it was reckoned to him," were written not for his sake alone,
060424 but for ours also. It will be reckoned to us who believe in him that raised from the dead Jesus our Lord,
060425 who was put to death for our trespasses and raised for our justification.
060501 Therefore, since we are justified by faith, we have peace with God through our Lord Jesus Christ.
060502 Through him we have obtained access to this grace in which we stand, and we rejoice in our hope of sharing the glory of God.
060503 More than that, we rejoice in our sufferings, knowing that suffering produces endurance,
060504 and endurance produces character, and character produces hope,
060505 and hope does not disappoint us, because God's love has been poured into our hearts through the Holy Spirit which has been given to us.
060506 While we were still weak, at the right time Christ died for the ungodly.
060507 Why, one will hardly die for a righteous man -- though perhaps for a good man one will dare even to die.
060508 But God shows his love for us in that while we were yet sinners Christ died for us.
060509 Since, therefore, we are now justified by his blood, much more shall we be saved by him from the wrath of God.
060510 For if while we were enemies we were reconciled to God by the death of his Son, much more, now that we are reconciled, shall we be saved by his life.
060511 Not only so, but we also rejoice in God through our Lord Jesus Christ, through whom we have now received our reconciliation.
060512 Therefore as sin came into the world through one man and death through sin, and so death spread to all men because all men sinned --
060513 sin indeed was in the world before the law was given, but sin is not counted where there is no law.
060514 Yet death reigned from Adam to Moses, even over those whose sins were not like the transgression of Adam, who was a type of the one who was to come.
060515 But the free gift is not like the trespass. For if many died through one man's trespass, much more have the grace of God and the free gift in the grace of that one man Jesus Christ abounded for many.
060516 And the free gift is not like the effect of that one man's sin. For the judgment following one trespass brought condemnation, but the free gift following many trespasses brings justification.
060517 If, because of one man's trespass, death reigned through that one man, much more will those who receive the abundance of grace and the free gift of righteousness reign in life through the one man Jesus Christ.
060518 Then as one man's trespass led to condemnation for all men, so one man's act of righteousness leads to acquittal and life for all men.
060519 For as by one man's disobedience many were made sinners, so by one man's obedience many will be made righteous.
060520 Law came in, to increase the trespass; but where sin increased, grace abounded all the more,
060521 so that, as sin reigned in death, grace also might reign through righteousness to eternal life through Jesus Christ our Lord.
060601 What shall we say then? Are we to continue in sin that grace may abound?
060602 By no means! How can we who died to sin still live in it?
060603 Do you not know that all of us who have been baptized into Christ Jesus were baptized into his death?
060604 We were buried therefore with him by baptism into death, so that as Christ was raised from the dead by the glory of the Father, we too might walk in newness of life.
060605 For if we have been united with him in a death like his, we shall certainly be united with him in a resurrection like his.
060606 We know that our old self was crucified with him so that the sinful body might be destroyed, and we might no longer be enslaved to sin.
060607 For he who has died is freed from sin.
060608 But if we have died with Christ, we believe that we shall also live with him.
060609 For we know that Christ being raised from the dead will never die again; death no longer has dominion over him.
060610 The death he died he died to sin, once for all, but the life he lives he lives to God.
060611 So you also must consider yourselves dead to sin and alive to God in Christ Jesus.
060612 Let not sin therefore reign in your mortal bodies, to make you obey their passions.
060613 Do not yield your members to sin as instruments of wickedness, but yield yourselves to God as men who have been brought from death to life, and your members to God as instruments of righteousness.
060614 For sin will have no dominion over you, since you are not under law but under grace.
060615 What then? Are we to sin because we are not under law but under grace? By no means!
060616 Do you not know that if you yield yourselves to any one as obedient slaves, you are slaves of the one whom you obey, either of sin, which leads to death, or of obedience, which leads to righteousness?
060617 But thanks be to God, that you who were once slaves of sin have become obedient from the heart to the standard of teaching to which you were committed,
060618 and, having been set free from sin, have become slaves of righteousness.
060619 I am speaking in human terms, because of your natural limitations. For just as you once yielded your members to impurity and to greater and greater iniquity, so now yield your members to righteousness for sanctification.
060620 When you were slaves of sin, you were free in regard to righteousness.
060621 But then what return did you get from the things of which you are now ashamed? The end of those things is death.
060622 But now that you have been set free from sin and have become slaves of God, the return you get is sanctification and its end, eternal life.
060623 For the wages of sin is death, but the free gift of God is eternal life in Christ Jesus our Lord.
060701 Do you not know, brethren -- for I am speaking to those who know the law -- that the law is binding on a person only during his life?
060702 Thus a married woman is bound by law to her husband as long as he lives; but if her husband dies she is discharged from the law concerning the husband.
060703 Accordingly, she will be called an adulteress if she lives with another man while her husband is alive. But if her husband dies she is free from that law, and if she marries another man she is not an adulteress.
060704 Likewise, my brethren, you have died to the law through the body of Christ, so that you may belong to another, to him who has been raised from the dead in order that we may bear fruit for God.
060705 While we were living in the flesh, our sinful passions, aroused by the law, were at work in our members to bear fruit for death.
060706 But now we are discharged from the law, dead to that which held us captive, so that we serve not under the old written code but in the new life of the Spirit.
060707 What then shall we say? That the law is sin? By no means! Yet, if it had not been for the law, I should not have known sin. I should not have known what it is to covet if the law had not said, "You shall not covet."
060708 But sin, finding opportunity in the commandment, wrought in me all kinds of covetousness. Apart from the law sin lies dead.
060709 I was once alive apart from the law, but when the commandment came, sin revived and I died;
060710 the very commandment which promised life proved to be death to me.
060711 For sin, finding opportunity in the commandment, deceived me and by it killed me.
060712 So the law is holy, and the commandment is holy and just and good.
060713 Did that which is good, then, bring death to me? By no means! It was sin, working death in me through what is good, in order that sin might be shown to be sin, and through the commandment might become sinful beyond measure.
060714 We know that the law is spiritual; but I am carnal, sold under sin.
060715 I do not understand my own actions. For I do not do what I want, but I do the very thing I hate.
060716 Now if I do what I do not want, I agree that the law is good.
060717 So then it is no longer I that do it, but sin which dwells within me.
060718 For I know that nothing good dwells within me, that is, in my flesh. I can will what is right, but I cannot do it.
060719 For I do not do the good I want, but the evil I do not want is what I do.
060720 Now if I do what I do not want, it is no longer I that do it, but sin which dwells within me.
060721 So I find it to be a law that when I want to do right, evil lies close at hand.
060722 For I delight in the law of God, in my inmost self,
060723 but I see in my members another law at war with the law of my mind and making me captive to the law of sin which dwells in my members.
060724 Wretched man that I am! Who will deliver me from this body of death?
060725 Thanks be to God through Jesus Christ our Lord! So then, I of myself serve the law of God with my mind, but with my flesh I serve the law of sin.
060801 There is therefore now no condemnation for those who are in Christ Jesus.
060802 For the law of the Spirit of life in Christ Jesus has set me free from the law of sin and death.
060803 For God has done what the law, weakened by the flesh, could not do: sending his own Son in the likeness of sinful flesh and for sin, he condemned sin in the flesh,
060804 in order that the just requirement of the law might be fulfilled in us, who walk not according to the flesh but according to the Spirit.
060805 For those who live according to the flesh set their minds on the things of the flesh, but those who live according to the Spirit set their minds on the things of the Spirit.
060806 To set the mind on the flesh is death, but to set the mind on the Spirit is life and peace.
060807 For the mind that is set on the flesh is hostile to God; it does not submit to God's law, indeed it cannot;
060808 and those who are in the flesh cannot please God.
060809 But you are not in the flesh, you are in the Spirit, if in fact the Spirit of God dwells in you. Any one who does not have the Spirit of Christ does not belong to him.
060810 But if Christ is in you, although your bodies are dead because of sin, your spirits are alive because of righteousness.
060811 If the Spirit of him who raised Jesus from the dead dwells in you, he who raised Christ Jesus from the dead will give life to your mortal bodies also through his Spirit which dwells in you.
060812 So then, brethren, we are debtors, not to the flesh, to live according to the flesh --
060813 for if you live according to the flesh you will die, but if by the Spirit you put to death the deeds of the body you will live.
060814 For all who are led by the Spirit of God are sons of God.
060815 For you did not receive the spirit of slavery to fall back into fear, but you have received the spirit of sonship. When we cry, "Abba! Father!"
060816 it is the Spirit himself bearing witness with our spirit that we are children of God,
060817 and if children, then heirs, heirs of God and fellow heirs with Christ, provided we suffer with him in order that we may also be glorified with him.
060818 I consider that the sufferings of this present time are not worth comparing with the glory that is to be revealed to us.
060819 For the creation waits with eager longing for the revealing of the sons of God;
060820 for the creation was subjected to futility, not of its own will but by the will of him who subjected it in hope;
060821 because the creation itself will be set free from its bondage to decay and obtain the glorious liberty of the children of God.
060822 We know that the whole creation has been groaning in travail together until now;
060823 and not only the creation, but we ourselves, who have the first fruits of the Spirit, groan inwardly as we wait for adoption as sons, the redemption of our bodies.
060824 For in this hope we were saved. Now hope that is seen is not hope. For who hopes for what he sees?
060825 But if we hope for what we do not see, we wait for it with patience.
060826 Likewise the Spirit helps us in our weakness; for we do not know how to pray as we ought, but the Spirit himself intercedes for us with sighs too deep for words.
060827 And he who searches the hearts of men knows what is the mind of the Spirit, because the Spirit intercedes for the saints according to the will of God.
060828 We know that in everything God works for good with those who love him, who are called according to his purpose.
060829 For those whom he foreknew he also predestined to be conformed to the image of his Son, in order that he might be the first-born among many brethren.
060830 And those whom he predestined he also called; and those whom he called he also justified; and those whom he justified he also glorified.
060831 What then shall we say to this? If God is for us, who is against us?
060832 He who did not spare his own Son but gave him up for us all, will he not also give us all things with him?
060833 Who shall bring any charge against God's elect? It is God who justifies;
060834 who is to condemn? Is it Christ Jesus, who died, yes, who was raised from the dead, who is at the right hand of God, who indeed intercedes for us?
060835 Who shall separate us from the love of Christ? Shall tribulation, or distress, or persecution, or famine, or nakedness, or peril, or sword?
060836 As it is written, "For thy sake we are being killed all the day long; we are regarded as sheep to be slaughtered."
060837 No, in all these things we are more than conquerors through him who loved us.
060838 For I am sure that neither death, nor life, nor angels, nor principalities, nor things present, nor things to come, nor powers,
060839 nor height, nor depth, nor anything else in all creation, will be able to separate us from the love of God in Christ Jesus our Lord.
060901 I am speaking the truth in Christ, I am not lying; my conscience bears me witness in the Holy Spirit,
060902 that I have great sorrow and unceasing anguish in my heart.
060903 For I could wish that I myself were accursed and cut off from Christ for the sake of my brethren, my kinsmen by race.
060904 They are Israelites, and to them belong the sonship, the glory, the covenants, the giving of the law, the worship, and the promises;
060905 to them belong the patriarchs, and of their race, according to the flesh, is the Christ. God who is over all be blessed for ever. Amen.
060906 But it is not as though the word of God had failed. For not all who are descended from Israel belong to Israel,
060907 and not all are children of Abraham because they are his descendants; but "Through Isaac shall your descendants be named."
060908 This means that it is not the children of the flesh who are the children of God, but the children of the promise are reckoned as descendants.
060909 For this is what the promise said, "About this time I will return and Sarah shall have a son."
060910 And not only so, but also when Rebecca had conceived children by one man, our forefather Isaac,
060911 though they were not yet born and had done nothing either good or bad, in order that God's purpose of election might continue, not because of works but because of his call,
060912 she was told, "The elder will serve the younger."
060913 As it is written, "Jacob I loved, but Esau I hated."
060914 What shall we say then? Is there injustice on God's part? By no means!
060915 For he says to Moses, "I will have mercy on whom I have mercy, and I will have compassion on whom I have compassion."
060916 So it depends not upon man's will or exertion, but upon God's mercy.
060917 For the scripture says to Pharaoh, "I have raised you up for the very purpose of showing my power in you, so that my name may be proclaimed in all the earth."
060918 So then he has mercy upon whomever he wills, and he hardens the heart of whomever he wills.
060919 You will say to me then, "Why does he still find fault? For who can resist his will?"
060920 But who are you, a man, to answer back to God? Will what is molded say to its molder, "Why have you made me thus?"
060921 Has the potter no right over the clay, to make out of the same lump one vessel for beauty and another for menial use?
060922 What if God, desiring to show his wrath and to make known his power, has endured with much patience the vessels of wrath made for destruction,
060923 in order to make known the riches of his glory for the vessels of mercy, which he has prepared beforehand for glory,
060924 even us whom he has called, not from the Jews only but also from the Gentiles?
060925 As indeed he says in Hose'a, "Those who were not my people I will call 'my people,' and her who was not beloved I will call 'my beloved.'"
060926 "And in the very place where it was said to them, 'You are not my people,' they will be called 'sons of the living God.'"
060927 And Isaiah cries out concerning Israel: "Though the number of the sons of Israel be as the sand of the sea, only a remnant of them will be saved;
060928 for the Lord will execute his sentence upon the earth with rigor and dispatch."
060929 And as Isaiah predicted, "If the Lord of hosts had not left us children, we would have fared like Sodom and been made like Gomor'rah."
060930 What shall we say, then? That Gentiles who did not pursue righteousness have attained it, that is, righteousness through faith;
060931 but that Israel who pursued the righteousness which is based on law did not succeed in fulfilling that law.
060932 Why? Because they did not pursue it through faith, but as if it were based on works. They have stumbled over the stumbling stone,
060933 as it is written, "Behold, I am laying in Zion a stone that will make men stumble, a rock that will make them fall; and he who believes in him will not be put to shame."
061001 Brethren, my heart's desire and prayer to God for them is that they may be saved.
061002 I bear them witness that they have a zeal for God, but it is not enlightened.
061003 For, being ignorant of the righteousness that comes from God, and seeking to establish their own, they did not submit to God's righteousness.
061004 For Christ is the end of the law, that every one who has faith may be justified.
061005 Moses writes that the man who practices the righteousness which is based on the law shall live by it.
061006 But the righteousness based on faith says, Do not say in your heart, "Who will ascend into heaven?" (that is, to bring Christ down)
061007 or "Who will descend into the abyss?" (that is, to bring Christ up from the dead).
061008 But what does it say? The word is near you, on your lips and in your heart (that is, the word of faith which we preach);
061009 because, if you confess with your lips that Jesus is Lord and believe in your heart that God raised him from the dead, you will be saved.
061010 For man believes with his heart and so is justified, and he confesses with his lips and so is saved.
061011 The scripture says, "No one who believes in him will be put to shame."
061012 For there is no distinction between Jew and Greek; the same Lord is Lord of all and bestows his riches upon all who call upon him.
061013 For, "every one who calls upon the name of the Lord will be saved."
061014 But how are men to call upon him in whom they have not believed? And how are they to believe in him of whom they have never heard? And how are they to hear without a preacher?
061015 And how can men preach unless they are sent? As it is written, "How beautiful are the feet of those who preach good news!"
061016 But they have not all obeyed the gospel; for Isaiah says, "Lord, who has believed what he has heard from us?"
061017 So faith comes from what is heard, and what is heard comes by the preaching of Christ.
061018 But I ask, have they not heard? Indeed they have; for "Their voice has gone out to all the earth, and their words to the ends of the world."
061019 Again I ask, did Israel not understand? First Moses says, "I will make you jealous of those who are not a nation; with a foolish nation I will make you angry."
061020 Then Isaiah is so bold as to say, "I have been found by those who did not seek me; I have shown myself to those who did not ask for me."
061021 But of Israel he says, "All day long I have held out my hands to a disobedient and contrary people."
061101 I ask, then, has God rejected his people? By no means! I myself am an Israelite, a descendant of Abraham, a member of the tribe of Benjamin.
061102 God has not rejected his people whom he foreknew. Do you not know what the scripture says of Eli'jah, how he pleads with God against Israel?
061103 "Lord, they have killed thy prophets, they have demolished thy altars, and I alone am left, and they seek my life."
061104 But what is God's reply to him? "I have kept for myself seven thousand men who have not bowed the knee to Ba'al."
061105 So too at the present time there is a remnant, chosen by grace.
061106 But if it is by grace, it is no longer on the basis of works; otherwise grace would no longer be grace.
061107 What then? Israel failed to obtain what it sought. The elect obtained it, but the rest were hardened,
061108 as it is written, "God gave them a spirit of stupor, eyes that should not see and ears that should not hear, down to this very day."
061109 And David says, "Let their table become a snare and a trap, a pitfall and a retribution for them;
061110 let their eyes be darkened so that they cannot see, and bend their backs for ever."
061111 So I ask, have they stumbled so as to fall? By no means! But through their trespass salvation has come to the Gentiles, so as to make Israel jealous.
061112 Now if their trespass means riches for the world, and if their failure means riches for the Gentiles, how much more will their full inclusion mean!
061113 Now I am speaking to you Gentiles. Inasmuch then as I am an apostle to the Gentiles, I magnify my ministry
061114 in order to make my fellow Jews jealous, and thus save some of them.
061115 For if their rejection means the reconciliation of the world, what will their acceptance mean but life from the dead?
061116 If the dough offered as first fruits is holy, so is the whole lump; and if the root is holy, so are the branches.
061117 But if some of the branches were broken off, and you, a wild olive shoot, were grafted in their place to share the richness of the olive tree,
061118 do not boast over the branches. If you do boast, remember it is not you that support the root, but the root that supports you.
061119 You will say, "Branches were broken off so that I might be grafted in."
061120 That is true. They were broken off because of their unbelief, but you stand fast only through faith. So do not become proud, but stand in awe.
061121 For if God did not spare the natural branches, neither will he spare you.
061122 Note then the kindness and the severity of God: severity toward those who have fallen, but God's kindness to you, provided you continue in his kindness; otherwise you too will be cut off.
061123 And even the others, if they do not persist in their unbelief, will be grafted in, for God has the power to graft them in again.
061124 For if you have been cut from what is by nature a wild olive tree, and grafted, contrary to nature, into a cultivated olive tree, how much more will these natural branches be grafted back into their own olive tree.
061125 Lest you be wise in your own conceits, I want you to understand this mystery, brethren: a hardening has come upon part of Israel, until the full number of the Gentiles come in,
061126 and so all Israel will be saved; as it is written, "The Deliverer will come from Zion, he will banish ungodliness from Jacob";
061127 "and this will be my covenant with them when I take away their sins."
061128 As regards the gospel they are enemies of God, for your sake; but as regards election they are beloved for the sake of their forefathers.
061129 For the gifts and the call of God are irrevocable.
061130 Just as you were once disobedient to God but now have received mercy because of their disobedience,
061131 so they have now been disobedient in order that by the mercy shown to you they also may receive mercy.
061132 For God has consigned all men to disobedience, that he may have mercy upon all.
061133 O the depth of the riches and wisdom and knowledge of God! How unsearchable are his judgments and how inscrutable his ways!
061134 "For who has known the mind of the Lord, or who has been his counselor?"
061135 "Or who has given a gift to him that he might be repaid?"
061136 For from him and through him and to him are all things. To him be glory for ever. Amen.
061201 I appeal to you therefore, brethren, by the mercies of God, to present your bodies as a living sacrifice, holy and acceptable to God, which is your spiritual worship.
061202 Do not be conformed to this world but be transformed by the renewal of your mind, that you may prove what is the will of God, what is good and acceptable and perfect.
061203 For by the grace given to me I bid every one among you not to think of himself more highly than he ought to think, but to think with sober judgment, each according to the measure of faith which God has assigned him.
061204 For as in one body we have many members, and all the members do not have the same function,
061205 so we, though many, are one body in Christ, and individually members one of another.
061206 Having gifts that differ according to the grace given to us, let us use them: if prophecy, in proportion to our faith;
061207 if service, in our serving; he who teaches, in his teaching;
061208 he who exhorts, in his exhortation; he who contributes, in liberality; he who gives aid, with zeal; he who does acts of mercy, with cheerfulness.
061209 Let love be genuine; hate what is evil, hold fast to what is good;
061210 love one another with brotherly affection; outdo one another in showing honor.
061211 Never flag in zeal, be aglow with the Spirit, serve the Lord.
061212 Rejoice in your hope, be patient in tribulation, be constant in prayer.
061213 Contribute to the needs of the saints, practice hospitality.
061214 Bless those who persecute you; bless and do not curse them.
061215 Rejoice with those who rejoice, weep with those who weep.
061216 Live in harmony with one another; do not be haughty, but associate with the lowly; never be conceited.
061217 Repay no one evil for evil, but take thought for what is noble in the sight of all.
061218 If possible, so far as it depends upon you, live peaceably with all.
061219 Beloved, never avenge yourselves, but leave it to the wrath of God; for it is written, "Vengeance is mine, I will repay, says the Lord."
061220 No, "if your enemy is hungry, feed him; if he is thirsty, give him drink; for by so doing you will heap burning coals upon his head."
061221 Do not be overcome by evil, but overcome evil with good.
061301 Let every person be subject to the governing authorities. For there is no authority except from God, and those that exist have been instituted by God.
061302 Therefore he who resists the authorities resists what God has appointed, and those who resist will incur judgment.
061303 For rulers are not a terror to good conduct, but to bad. Would you have no fear of him who is in authority? Then do what is good, and you will receive his approval,
061304 for he is God's servant for your good. But if you do wrong, be afraid, for he does not bear the sword in vain; he is the servant of God to execute his wrath on the wrongdoer.
061305 Therefore one must be subject, not only to avoid God's wrath but also for the sake of conscience.
061306 For the same reason you also pay taxes, for the authorities are ministers of God, attending to this very thing.
061307 Pay all of them their dues, taxes to whom taxes are due, revenue to whom revenue is due, respect to whom respect is due, honor to whom honor is due.
061308 Owe no one anything, except to love one another; for he who loves his neighbor has fulfilled the law.
061309 The commandments, "You shall not commit adultery, You shall not kill, You shall not steal, You shall not covet," and any other commandment, are summed up in this sentence, "You shall love your neighbor as yourself."
061310 Love does no wrong to a neighbor; therefore love is the fulfilling of the law.
061311 Besides this you know what hour it is, how it is full time now for you to wake from sleep. For salvation is nearer to us now than when we first believed;
061312 the night is far gone, the day is at hand. Let us then cast off the works of darkness and put on the armor of light;
061313 let us conduct ourselves becomingly as in the day, not in reveling and drunkenness, not in debauchery and licentiousness, not in quarreling and jealousy.
061314 But put on the Lord Jesus Christ, and make no provision for the flesh, to gratify its desires.
061401 As for the man who is weak in faith, welcome him, but not for disputes over opinions.
061402 One believes he may eat anything, while the weak man eats only vegetables.
061403 Let not him who eats despise him who abstains, and let not him who abstains pass judgment on him who eats; for God has welcomed him.
061404 Who are you to pass judgment on the servant of another? It is before his own master that he stands or falls. And he will be upheld, for the Master is able to make him stand.
061405 One man esteems one day as better than another, while another man esteems all days alike. Let every one be fully convinced in his own mind.
061406 He who observes the day, observes it in honor of the Lord. He also who eats, eats in honor of the Lord, since he gives thanks to God; while he who abstains, abstains in honor of the Lord and gives thanks to God.
061407 None of us lives to himself, and none of us dies to himself.
061408 If we live, we live to the Lord, and if we die, we die to the Lord; so then, whether we live or whether we die, we are the Lord's.
061409 For to this end Christ died and lived again, that he might be Lord both of the dead and of the living.
061410 Why do you pass judgment on your brother? Or you, why do you despise your brother? For we shall all stand before the judgment seat of God;
061411 for it is written, "As I live, says the Lord, every knee shall bow to me, and every tongue shall give praise to God."
061412 So each of us shall give account of himself to God.
061413 Then let us no more pass judgment on one another, but rather decide never to put a stumbling block or hindrance in the way of a brother.
061414 I know and am persuaded in the Lord Jesus that nothing is unclean in itself; but it is unclean for any one who thinks it unclean.
061415 If your brother is being injured by what you eat, you are no longer walking in love. Do not let what you eat cause the ruin of one for whom Christ died.
061416 So do not let your good be spoken of as evil.
061417 For the kingdom of God is not food and drink but righteousness and peace and joy in the Holy Spirit;
061418 he who thus serves Christ is acceptable to God and approved by men.
061419 Let us then pursue what makes for peace and for mutual upbuilding.
061420 Do not, for the sake of food, destroy the work of God. Everything is indeed clean, but it is wrong for any one to make others fall by what he eats;
061421 it is right not to eat meat or drink wine or do anything that makes your brother stumble.
061422 The faith that you have, keep between yourself and God; happy is he who has no reason to judge himself for what he approves.
061423 But he who has doubts is condemned, if he eats, because he does not act from faith; for whatever does not proceed from faith is sin.
061501 We who are strong ought to bear with the failings of the weak, and not to please ourselves;
061502 let each of us please his neighbor for his good, to edify him.
061503 For Christ did not please himself; but, as it is written, "The reproaches of those who reproached thee fell on me."
061504 For whatever was written in former days was written for our instruction, that by steadfastness and by the encouragement of the scriptures we might have hope.
061505 May the God of steadfastness and encouragement grant you to live in such harmony with one another, in accord with Christ Jesus,
061506 that together you may with one voice glorify the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ.
061507 Welcome one another, therefore, as Christ has welcomed you, for the glory of God.
061508 For I tell you that Christ became a servant to the circumcised to show God's truthfulness, in order to confirm the promises given to the patriarchs,
061509 and in order that the Gentiles might glorify God for his mercy. As it is written, "Therefore I will praise thee among the Gentiles, and sing to thy name";
061510 and again it is said, "Rejoice, O Gentiles, with his people";
061511 and again, "Praise the Lord, all Gentiles, and let all the peoples praise him";
061512 and further Isaiah says, "The root of Jesse shall come, he who rises to rule the Gentiles; in him shall the Gentiles hope."
061513 May the God of hope fill you with all joy and peace in believing, so that by the power of the Holy Spirit you may abound in hope.
061514 I myself am satisfied about you, my brethren, that you yourselves are full of goodness, filled with all knowledge, and able to instruct one another.
061515 But on some points I have written to you very boldly by way of reminder, because of the grace given me by God
061516 to be a minister of Christ Jesus to the Gentiles in the priestly service of the gospel of God, so that the offering of the Gentiles may be acceptable, sanctified by the Holy Spirit.
061517 In Christ Jesus, then, I have reason to be proud of my work for God.
061518 For I will not venture to speak of anything except what Christ has wrought through me to win obedience from the Gentiles, by word and deed,
061519 by the power of signs and wonders, by the power of the Holy Spirit, so that from Jerusalem and as far round as Illyr'icum I have fully preached the gospel of Christ,
061520 thus making it my ambition to preach the gospel, not where Christ has already been named, lest I build on another man's foundation,
061521 but as it is written, "They shall see who have never been told of him, and they shall understand who have never heard of him."
061522 This is the reason why I have so often been hindered from coming to you.
061523 But now, since I no longer have any room for work in these regions, and since I have longed for many years to come to you,
061524 I hope to see you in passing as I go to Spain, and to be sped on my journey there by you, once I have enjoyed your company for a little.
061525 At present, however, I am going to Jerusalem with aid for the saints.
061526 For Macedo'nia and Acha'ia have been pleased to make some contribution for the poor among the saints at Jerusalem;
061527 they were pleased to do it, and indeed they are in debt to them, for if the Gentiles have come to share in their spiritual blessings, they ought also to be of service to them in material blessings.
061528 When therefore I have completed this, and have delivered to them what has been raised, I shall go on by way of you to Spain;
061529 and I know that when I come to you I shall come in the fulness of the blessing of Christ.
061530 I appeal to you, brethren, by our Lord Jesus Christ and by the love of the Spirit, to strive together with me in your prayers to God on my behalf,
061531 that I may be delivered from the unbelievers in Judea, and that my service for Jerusalem may be acceptable to the saints,
061532 so that by God's will I may come to you with joy and be refreshed in your company.
061533 The God of peace be with you all. Amen.
061601 I commend to you our sister Phoebe, a deaconess of the church at Cen'chre-ae,
061602 that you may receive her in the Lord as befits the saints, and help her in whatever she may require from you, for she has been a helper of many and of myself as well.
061603 Greet Prisca and Aq'uila, my fellow workers in Christ Jesus,
061604 who risked their necks for my life, to whom not only I but also all the churches of the Gentiles give thanks;
061605 greet also the church in their house. Greet my beloved Epae'netus, who was the first convert in Asia for Christ.
061606 Greet Mary, who has worked hard among you.
061607 Greet Androni'cus and Ju'nias, my kinsmen and my fellow prisoners; they are men of note among the apostles, and they were in Christ before me.
061608 Greet Amplia'tus, my beloved in the Lord.
061609 Greet Urba'nus, our fellow worker in Christ, and my beloved Stachys.
061610 Greet Apel'les, who is approved in Christ. Greet those who belong to the family of Aristobu'lus.
061611 Greet my kinsman Hero'dion. Greet those in the Lord who belong to the family of Narcis'sus.
061612 Greet those workers in the Lord, Tryphae'na and Trypho'sa. Greet the beloved Persis, who has worked hard in the Lord.
061613 Greet Rufus, eminent in the Lord, also his mother and mine.
061614 Greet Asyn'critus, Phlegon, Hermes, Pat'robas, Hermas, and the brethren who are with them.
061615 Greet Philol'ogus, Julia, Nereus and his sister, and Olym'pas, and all the saints who are with them.
061616 Greet one another with a holy kiss. All the churches of Christ greet you.
061617 I appeal to you, brethren, to take note of those who create dissensions and difficulties, in opposition to the doctrine which you have been taught; avoid them.
061618 For such persons do not serve our Lord Christ, but their own appetites, and by fair and flattering words they deceive the hearts of the simple-minded.
061619 For while your obedience is known to all, so that I rejoice over you, I would have you wise as to what is good and guileless as to what is evil;
061620 then the God of peace will soon crush Satan under your feet. The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with you.
061621 Timothy, my fellow worker, greets you; so do Lucius and Jason and Sosip'ater, my kinsmen.
061622 I Tertius, the writer of this letter, greet you in the Lord.
061623 Ga'ius, who is host to me and to the whole church, greets you. Eras'tus, the city treasurer, and our brother Quartus, greet you.
061624
061625 Now to him who is able to strengthen you according to my gospel and the preaching of Jesus Christ, according to the revelation of the mystery which was kept secret for long ages
061626 but is now disclosed and through the prophetic writings is made known to all nations, according to the command of the eternal God, to bring about the obedience of faith --
061627 to the only wise God be glory for evermore through Jesus Christ! Amen.
070101 Paul, called by the will of God to be an apostle of Christ Jesus, and our brother Sos'thenes,
070102 To the church of God which is at Corinth, to those sanctified in Christ Jesus, called to be saints together with all those who in every place call on the name of our Lord Jesus Christ, both their Lord and ours:
070103 Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ.
070104 I give thanks to God always for you because of the grace of God which was given you in Christ Jesus,
070105 that in every way you were enriched in him with all speech and all knowledge --
070106 even as the testimony to Christ was confirmed among you --
070107 so that you are not lacking in any spiritual gift, as you wait for the revealing of our Lord Jesus Christ;
070108 who will sustain you to the end, guiltless in the day of our Lord Jesus Christ.
070109 God is faithful, by whom you were called into the fellowship of his Son, Jesus Christ our Lord.
070110 I appeal to you, brethren, by the name of our Lord Jesus Christ, that all of you agree and that there be no dissensions among you, but that you be united in the same mind and the same judgment.
070111 For it has been reported to me by Chlo'e's people that there is quarreling among you, my brethren.
070112 What I mean is that each one of you says, "I belong to Paul," or "I belong to Apol'los," or "I belong to Cephas," or "I belong to Christ."
070113 Is Christ divided? Was Paul crucified for you? Or were you baptized in the name of Paul?
070114 I am thankful that I baptized none of you except Crispus and Ga'ius;
070115 lest any one should say that you were baptized in my name.
070116 (I did baptize also the household of Steph'anas. Beyond that, I do not know whether I baptized any one else.)
070117 For Christ did not send me to baptize but to preach the gospel, and not with eloquent wisdom, lest the cross of Christ be emptied of its power.
070118 For the word of the cross is folly to those who are perishing, but to us who are being saved it is the power of God.
070119 For it is written, "I will destroy the wisdom of the wise, and the cleverness of the clever I will thwart."
070120 Where is the wise man? Where is the scribe? Where is the debater of this age? Has not God made foolish the wisdom of the world?
070121 For since, in the wisdom of God, the world did not know God through wisdom, it pleased God through the folly of what we preach to save those who believe.
070122 For Jews demand signs and Greeks seek wisdom,
070123 but we preach Christ crucified, a stumbling block to Jews and folly to Gentiles,
070124 but to those who are called, both Jews and Greeks, Christ the power of God and the wisdom of God.
070125 For the foolishness of God is wiser than men, and the weakness of God is stronger than men.
070126 For consider your call, brethren; not many of you were wise according to worldly standards, not many were powerful, not many were of noble birth;
070127 but God chose what is foolish in the world to shame the wise, God chose what is weak in the world to shame the strong,
070128 God chose what is low and despised in the world, even things that are not, to bring to nothing things that are,
070129 so that no human being might boast in the presence of God.
070130 He is the source of your life in Christ Jesus, whom God made our wisdom, our righteousness and sanctification and redemption;
070131 therefore, as it is written, "Let him who boasts, boast of the Lord."
070201 When I came to you, brethren, I did not come proclaiming to you the testimony of God in lofty words or wisdom.
070202 For I decided to know nothing among you except Jesus Christ and him crucified.
070203 And I was with you in weakness and in much fear and trembling;
070204 and my speech and my message were not in plausible words of wisdom, but in demonstration of the Spirit and of power,
070205 that your faith might not rest in the wisdom of men but in the power of God.
070206 Yet among the mature we do impart wisdom, although it is not a wisdom of this age or of the rulers of this age, who are doomed to pass away.
070207 But we impart a secret and hidden wisdom of God, which God decreed before the ages for our glorification.
070208 None of the rulers of this age understood this; for if they had, they would not have crucified the Lord of glory.
070209 But, as it is written, "What no eye has seen, nor ear heard, nor the heart of man conceived, what God has prepared for those who love him,"
070210 God has revealed to us through the Spirit. For the Spirit searches everything, even the depths of God.
070211 For what person knows a man's thoughts except the spirit of the man which is in him? So also no one comprehends the thoughts of God except the Spirit of God.
070212 Now we have received not the spirit of the world, but the Spirit which is from God, that we might understand the gifts bestowed on us by God.
070213 And we impart this in words not taught by human wisdom but taught by the Spirit, interpreting spiritual truths to those who possess the Spirit.
070214 The unspiritual man does not receive the gifts of the Spirit of God, for they are folly to him, and he is not able to understand them because they are spiritually discerned.
070215 The spiritual man judges all things, but is himself to be judged by no one.
070216 "For who has known the mind of the Lord so as to instruct him?" But we have the mind of Christ.
070301 But I, brethren, could not address you as spiritual men, but as men of the flesh, as babes in Christ.
070302 I fed you with milk, not solid food; for you were not ready for it; and even yet you are not ready,
070303 for you are still of the flesh. For while there is jealousy and strife among you, are you not of the flesh, and behaving like ordinary men?
070304 For when one says, "I belong to Paul," and another, "I belong to Apol'los," are you not merely men?
070305 What then is Apol'los? What is Paul? Servants through whom you believed, as the Lord assigned to each.
070306 I planted, Apol'los watered, but God gave the growth.
070307 So neither he who plants nor he who waters is anything, but only God who gives the growth.
070308 He who plants and he who waters are equal, and each shall receive his wages according to his labor.
070309 For we are God's fellow workers; you are God's field, God's building.
070310 According to the grace of God given to me, like a skilled master builder I laid a foundation, and another man is building upon it. Let each man take care how he builds upon it.
070311 For no other foundation can any one lay than that which is laid, which is Jesus Christ.
070312 Now if any one builds on the foundation with gold, silver, precious stones, wood, hay, straw --
070313 each man's work will become manifest; for the Day will disclose it, because it will be revealed with fire, and the fire will test what sort of work each one has done.
070314 If the work which any man has built on the foundation survives, he will receive a reward.
070315 If any man's work is burned up, he will suffer loss, though he himself will be saved, but only as through fire.
070316 Do you not know that you are God's temple and that God's Spirit dwells in you?
070317 If any one destroys God's temple, God will destroy him. For God's temple is holy, and that temple you are.
070318 Let no one deceive himself. If any one among you thinks that he is wise in this age, let him become a fool that he may become wise.
070319 For the wisdom of this world is folly with God. For it is written, "He catches the wise in their craftiness,"
070320 and again, "The Lord knows that the thoughts of the wise are futile."
070321 So let no one boast of men. For all things are yours,
070322 whether Paul or Apol'los or Cephas or the world or life or death or the present or the future, all are yours;
070323 and you are Christ's; and Christ is God's.
070401 This is how one should regard us, as servants of Christ and stewards of the mysteries of God.
070402 Moreover it is required of stewards that they be found trustworthy.
070403 But with me it is a very small thing that I should be judged by you or by any human court. I do not even judge myself.
070404 I am not aware of anything against myself, but I am not thereby acquitted. It is the Lord who judges me.
070405 Therefore do not pronounce judgment before the time, before the Lord comes, who will bring to light the things now hidden in darkness and will disclose the purposes of the heart. Then every man will receive his commendation from God.
070406 I have applied all this to myself and Apol'los for your benefit, brethren, that you may learn by us not to go beyond what is written, that none of you may be puffed up in favor of one against another.
070407 For who sees anything different in you? What have you that you did not receive? If then you received it, why do you boast as if it were not a gift?
070408 Already you are filled! Already you have become rich! Without us you have become kings! And would that you did reign, so that we might share the rule with you!
070409 For I think that God has exhibited us apostles as last of all, like men sentenced to death; because we have become a spectacle to the world, to angels and to men.
070410 We are fools for Christ's sake, but you are wise in Christ. We are weak, but you are strong. You are held in honor, but we in disrepute.
070411 To the present hour we hunger and thirst, we are ill-clad and buffeted and homeless,
070412 and we labor, working with our own hands. When reviled, we bless; when persecuted, we endure;
070413 when slandered, we try to conciliate; we have become, and are now, as the refuse of the world, the offscouring of all things.
070414 I do not write this to make you ashamed, but to admonish you as my beloved children.
070415 For though you have countless guides in Christ, you do not have many fathers. For I became your father in Christ Jesus through the gospel.
070416 I urge you, then, be imitators of me.
070417 Therefore I sent to you Timothy, my beloved and faithful child in the Lord, to remind you of my ways in Christ, as I teach them everywhere in every church.
070418 Some are arrogant, as though I were not coming to you.
070419 But I will come to you soon, if the Lord wills, and I will find out not the talk of these arrogant people but their power.
070420 For the kingdom of God does not consist in talk but in power.
070421 What do you wish? Shall I come to you with a rod, or with love in a spirit of gentleness?
070501 It is actually reported that there is immorality among you, and of a kind that is not found even among pagans; for a man is living with his father's wife.
070502 And you are arrogant! Ought you not rather to mourn? Let him who has done this be removed from among you.
070503 For though absent in body I am present in spirit, and as if present, I have already pronounced judgment
070504 in the name of the Lord Jesus on the man who has done such a thing. When you are assembled, and my spirit is present, with the power of our Lord Jesus,
070505 you are to deliver this man to Satan for the destruction of the flesh, that his spirit may be saved in the day of the Lord Jesus.
070506 Your boasting is not good. Do you not know that a little leaven leavens the whole lump?
070507 Cleanse out the old leaven that you may be a new lump, as you really are unleavened. For Christ, our paschal lamb, has been sacrificed.
070508 Let us, therefore, celebrate the festival, not with the old leaven, the leaven of malice and evil, but with the unleavened bread of sincerity and truth.
070509 I wrote to you in my letter not to associate with immoral men;
070510 not at all meaning the immoral of this world, or the greedy and robbers, or idolaters, since then you would need to go out of the world.
070511 But rather I wrote to you not to associate with any one who bears the name of brother if he is guilty of immorality or greed, or is an idolater, reviler, drunkard, or robber -- not even to eat with such a one.
070512 For what have I to do with judging outsiders? Is it not those inside the church whom you are to judge?
070513 God judges those outside. "Drive out the wicked person from among you."
070601 When one of you has a grievance against a brother, does he dare go to law before the unrighteous instead of the saints?
070602 Do you not know that the saints will judge the world? And if the world is to be judged by you, are you incompetent to try trivial cases?
070603 Do you not know that we are to judge angels? How much more, matters pertaining to this life!
070604 If then you have such cases, why do you lay them before those who are least esteemed by the church?
070605 I say this to your shame. Can it be that there is no man among you wise enough to decide between members of the brotherhood,
070606 but brother goes to law against brother, and that before unbelievers?
070607 To have lawsuits at all with one another is defeat for you. Why not rather suffer wrong? Why not rather be defrauded?
070608 But you yourselves wrong and defraud, and that even your own brethren.
070609 Do you not know that the unrighteous will not inherit the kingdom of God? Do not be deceived; neither the immoral, nor idolaters, nor adulterers, nor sexual perverts,
070610 nor thieves, nor the greedy, nor drunkards, nor revilers, nor robbers will inherit the kingdom of God.
070611 And such were some of you. But you were washed, you were sanctified, you were justified in the name of the Lord Jesus Christ and in the Spirit of our God.
070612 "All things are lawful for me," but not all things are helpful. "All things are lawful for me," but I will not be enslaved by anything.
070613 "Food is meant for the stomach and the stomach for food" -- and God will destroy both one and the other. The body is not meant for immorality, but for the Lord, and the Lord for the body.
070614 And God raised the Lord and will also raise us up by his power.
070615 Do you not know that your bodies are members of Christ? Shall I therefore take the members of Christ and make them members of a prostitute? Never!
070616 Do you not know that he who joins himself to a prostitute becomes one body with her? For, as it is written, "The two shall become one flesh."
070617 But he who is united to the Lord becomes one spirit with him.
070618 Shun immorality. Every other sin which a man commits is outside the body; but the immoral man sins against his own body.
070619 Do you not know that your body is a temple of the Holy Spirit within you, which you have from God? You are not your own;
070620 you were bought with a price. So glorify God in your body.
070701 Now concerning the matters about which you wrote. It is well for a man not to touch a woman.
070702 But because of the temptation to immorality, each man should have his own wife and each woman her own husband.
070703 The husband should give to his wife her conjugal rights, and likewise the wife to her husband.
070704 For the wife does not rule over her own body, but the husband does; likewise the husband does not rule over his own body, but the wife does.
070705 Do not refuse one another except perhaps by agreement for a season, that you may devote yourselves to prayer; but then come together again, lest Satan tempt you through lack of self-control.
070706 I say this by way of concession, not of command.
070707 I wish that all were as I myself am. But each has his own special gift from God, one of one kind and one of another.
070708 To the unmarried and the widows I say that it is well for them to remain single as I do.
070709 But if they cannot exercise self-control, they should marry. For it is better to marry than to be aflame with passion.
070710 To the married I give charge, not I but the Lord, that the wife should not separate from her husband
070711 (but if she does, let her remain single or else be reconciled to her husband) -- and that the husband should not divorce his wife.
070712 To the rest I say, not the Lord, that if any brother has a wife who is an unbeliever, and she consents to live with him, he should not divorce her.
070713 If any woman has a husband who is an unbeliever, and he consents to live with her, she should not divorce him.
070714 For the unbelieving husband is consecrated through his wife, and the unbelieving wife is consecrated through her husband. Otherwise, your children would be unclean, but as it is they are holy.
070715 But if the unbelieving partner desires to separate, let it be so; in such a case the brother or sister is not bound. For God has called us to peace.
070716 Wife, how do you know whether you will save your husband? Husband, how do you know whether you will save your wife?
070717 Only, let every one lead the life which the Lord has assigned to him, and in which God has called him. This is my rule in all the churches.
070718 Was any one at the time of his call already circumcised? Let him not seek to remove the marks of circumcision. Was any one at the time of his call uncircumcised? Let him not seek circumcision.
070719 For neither circumcision counts for anything nor uncircumcision, but keeping the commandments of God.
070720 Every one should remain in the state in which he was called.
070721 Were you a slave when called? Never mind. But if you can gain your freedom, avail yourself of the opportunity.
070722 For he who was called in the Lord as a slave is a freedman of the Lord. Likewise he who was free when called is a slave of Christ.
070723 You were bought with a price; do not become slaves of men.
070724 So, brethren, in whatever state each was called, there let him remain with God.
070725 Now concerning the unmarried, I have no command of the Lord, but I give my opinion as one who by the Lord's mercy is trustworthy.
070726 I think that in view of the present distress it is well for a person to remain as he is.
070727 Are you bound to a wife? Do not seek to be free. Are you free from a wife? Do not seek marriage.
070728 But if you marry, you do not sin, and if a girl marries she does not sin. Yet those who marry will have worldly troubles, and I would spare you that.
070729 I mean, brethren, the appointed time has grown very short; from now on, let those who have wives live as though they had none,
070730 and those who mourn as though they were not mourning, and those who rejoice as though they were not rejoicing, and those who buy as though they had no goods,
070731 and those who deal with the world as though they had no dealings with it. For the form of this world is passing away.
070732 I want you to be free from anxieties. The unmarried man is anxious about the affairs of the Lord, how to please the Lord;
070733 but the married man is anxious about worldly affairs, how to please his wife,
070734 and his interests are divided. And the unmarried woman or girl is anxious about the affairs of the Lord, how to be holy in body and spirit; but the married woman is anxious about worldly affairs, how to please her husband.
070735 I say this for your own benefit, not to lay any restraint upon you, but to promote good order and to secure your undivided devotion to the Lord.
070736 If any one thinks that he is not behaving properly toward his betrothed, if his passions are strong, and it has to be, let him do as he wishes: let them marry -- it is no sin.
070737 But whoever is firmly established in his heart, being under no necessity but having his desire under control, and has determined this in his heart, to keep her as his betrothed, he will do well.
070738 So that he who marries his betrothed does well; and he who refrains from marriage will do better.
070739 A wife is bound to her husband as long as he lives. If the husband dies, she is free to be married to whom she wishes, only in the Lord.
070740 But in my judgment she is happier if she remains as she is. And I think that I have the Spirit of God.
070801 Now concerning food offered to idols: we know that "all of us possess knowledge." "Knowledge" puffs up, but love builds up.
070802 If any one imagines that he knows something, he does not yet know as he ought to know.
070803 But if one loves God, one is known by him.
070804 Hence, as to the eating of food offered to idols, we know that "an idol has no real existence," and that "there is no God but one."
070805 For although there may be so-called gods in heaven or on earth -- as indeed there are many "gods" and many "lords" --
070806 yet for us there is one God, the Father, from whom are all things and for whom we exist, and one Lord, Jesus Christ, through whom are all things and through whom we exist.
070807 However, not all possess this knowledge. But some, through being hitherto accustomed to idols, eat food as really offered to an idol; and their conscience, being weak, is defiled.
070808 Food will not commend us to God. We are no worse off if we do not eat, and no better off if we do.
070809 Only take care lest this liberty of yours somehow become a stumbling block to the weak.
070810 For if any one sees you, a man of knowledge, at table in an idol's temple, might he not be encouraged, if his conscience is weak, to eat food offered to idols?
070811 And so by your knowledge this weak man is destroyed, the brother for whom Christ died.
070812 Thus, sinning against your brethren and wounding their conscience when it is weak, you sin against Christ.
070813 Therefore, if food is a cause of my brother's falling, I will never eat meat, lest I cause my brother to fall.
070901 Am I not free? Am I not an apostle? Have I not seen Jesus our Lord? Are not you my workmanship in the Lord?
070902 If to others I am not an apostle, at least I am to you; for you are the seal of my apostleship in the Lord.
070903 This is my defense to those who would examine me.
070904 Do we not have the right to our food and drink?
070905 Do we not have the right to be accompanied by a wife, as the other apostles and the brothers of the Lord and Cephas?
070906 Or is it only Barnabas and I who have no right to refrain from working for a living?
070907 Who serves as a soldier at his own expense? Who plants a vineyard without eating any of its fruit? Who tends a flock without getting some of the milk?
070908 Do I say this on human authority? Does not the law say the same?
070909 For it is written in the law of Moses, "You shall not muzzle an ox when it is treading out the grain." Is it for oxen that God is concerned?
070910 Does he not speak entirely for our sake? It was written for our sake, because the plowman should plow in hope and the thresher thresh in hope of a share in the crop.
070911 If we have sown spiritual good among you, is it too much if we reap your material benefits?
070912 If others share this rightful claim upon you, do not we still more? Nevertheless, we have not made use of this right, but we endure anything rather than put an obstacle in the way of the gospel of Christ.
070913 Do you not know that those who are employed in the temple service get their food from the temple, and those who serve at the altar share in the sacrificial offerings?
070914 In the same way, the Lord commanded that those who proclaim the gospel should get their living by the gospel.
070915 But I have made no use of any of these rights, nor am I writing this to secure any such provision. For I would rather die than have any one deprive me of my ground for boasting.
070916 For if I preach the gospel, that gives me no ground for boasting. For necessity is laid upon me. Woe to me if I do not preach the gospel!
070917 For if I do this of my own will, I have a reward; but if not of my own will, I am entrusted with a commission.
070918 What then is my reward? Just this: that in my preaching I may make the gospel free of charge, not making full use of my right in the gospel.
070919 For though I am free from all men, I have made myself a slave to all, that I might win the more.
070920 To the Jews I became as a Jew, in order to win Jews; to those under the law I became as one under the law -- though not being myself under the law -- that I might win those under the law.
