070921 To those outside the law I became as one outside the law -- not being without law toward God but under the law of Christ -- that I might win those outside the law.
070922 To the weak I became weak, that I might win the weak. I have become all things to all men, that I might by all means save some.
070923 I do it all for the sake of the gospel, that I may share in its blessings.
070924 Do you not know that in a race all the runners compete, but only one receives the prize? So run that you may obtain it.
070925 Every athlete exercises self-control in all things. They do it to receive a perishable wreath, but we an imperishable.
070926 Well, I do not run aimlessly, I do not box as one beating the air;
070927 but I pommel my body and subdue it, lest after preaching to others I myself should be disqualified.
071001 I want you to know, brethren, that our fathers were all under the cloud, and all passed through the sea,
071002 and all were baptized into Moses in the cloud and in the sea,
071003 and all ate the same supernatural food
071004 and all drank the same supernatural drink. For they drank from the supernatural Rock which followed them, and the Rock was Christ.
071005 Nevertheless with most of them God was not pleased; for they were overthrown in the wilderness.
071006 Now these things are warnings for us, not to desire evil as they did.
071007 Do not be idolaters as some of them were; as it is written, "The people sat down to eat and drink and rose up to dance."
071008 We must not indulge in immorality as some of them did, and twenty-three thousand fell in a single day.
071009 We must not put the Lord to the test, as some of them did and were destroyed by serpents;
071010 nor grumble, as some of them did and were destroyed by the Destroyer.
071011 Now these things happened to them as a warning, but they were written down for our instruction, upon whom the end of the ages has come.
071012 Therefore let any one who thinks that he stands take heed lest he fall.
071013 No temptation has overtaken you that is not common to man. God is faithful, and he will not let you be tempted beyond your strength, but with the temptation will also provide the way of escape, that you may be able to endure it.
071014 Therefore, my beloved, shun the worship of idols.
071015 I speak as to sensible men; judge for yourselves what I say.
071016 The cup of blessing which we bless, is it not a participation in the blood of Christ? The bread which we break, is it not a participation in the body of Christ?
071017 Because there is one bread, we who are many are one body, for we all partake of the one bread.
071018 Consider the people of Israel; are not those who eat the sacrifices partners in the altar?
071019 What do I imply then? That food offered to idols is anything, or that an idol is anything?
071020 No, I imply that what pagans sacrifice they offer to demons and not to God. I do not want you to be partners with demons.
071021 You cannot drink the cup of the Lord and the cup of demons. You cannot partake of the table of the Lord and the table of demons.
071022 Shall we provoke the Lord to jealousy? Are we stronger than he?
071023 "All things are lawful," but not all things are helpful. "All things are lawful," but not all things build up.
071024 Let no one seek his own good, but the good of his neighbor.
071025 Eat whatever is sold in the meat market without raising any question on the ground of conscience.
071026 For "the earth is the Lord's, and everything in it."
071027 If one of the unbelievers invites you to dinner and you are disposed to go, eat whatever is set before you without raising any question on the ground of conscience.
071028 (But if some one says to you, "This has been offered in sacrifice," then out of consideration for the man who informed you, and for conscience' sake --
071029 I mean his conscience, not yours -- do not eat it.) For why should my liberty be determined by another man's scruples?
071030 If I partake with thankfulness, why am I denounced because of that for which I give thanks?
071031 So, whether you eat or drink, or whatever you do, do all to the glory of God.
071032 Give no offense to Jews or to Greeks or to the church of God,
071033 just as I try to please all men in everything I do, not seeking my own advantage, but that of many, that they may be saved.
071101 Be imitators of me, as I am of Christ.
071102 I commend you because you remember me in everything and maintain the traditions even as I have delivered them to you.
071103 But I want you to understand that the head of every man is Christ, the head of a woman is her husband, and the head of Christ is God.
071104 Any man who prays or prophesies with his head covered dishonors his head,
071105 but any woman who prays or prophesies with her head unveiled dishonors her head -- it is the same as if her head were shaven.
071106 For if a woman will not veil herself, then she should cut off her hair; but if it is disgraceful for a woman to be shorn or shaven, let her wear a veil.
071107 For a man ought not to cover his head, since he is the image and glory of God; but woman is the glory of man.
071108 (For man was not made from woman, but woman from man.
071109 Neither was man created for woman, but woman for man.)
071110 That is why a woman ought to have a veil on her head, because of the angels.
071111 (Nevertheless, in the Lord woman is not independent of man nor man of woman;
071112 for as woman was made from man, so man is now born of woman. And all things are from God.)
071113 Judge for yourselves; is it proper for a woman to pray to God with her head uncovered?
071114 Does not nature itself teach you that for a man to wear long hair is degrading to him,
071115 but if a woman has long hair, it is her pride? For her hair is given to her for a covering.
071116 If any one is disposed to be contentious, we recognize no other practice, nor do the churches of God.
071117 But in the following instructions I do not commend you, because when you come together it is not for the better but for the worse.
071118 For, in the first place, when you assemble as a church, I hear that there are divisions among you; and I partly believe it,
071119 for there must be factions among you in order that those who are genuine among you may be recognized.
071120 When you meet together, it is not the Lord's supper that you eat.
071121 For in eating, each one goes ahead with his own meal, and one is hungry and another is drunk.
071122 What! Do you not have houses to eat and drink in? Or do you despise the church of God and humiliate those who have nothing? What shall I say to you? Shall I commend you in this? No, I will not.
071123 For I received from the Lord what I also delivered to you, that the Lord Jesus on the night when he was betrayed took bread,
071124 and when he had given thanks, he broke it, and said, "This is my body which is for you. Do this in remembrance of me."
071125 In the same way also the cup, after supper, saying, "This cup is the new covenant in my blood. Do this, as often as you drink it, in remembrance of me."
071126 For as often as you eat this bread and drink the cup, you proclaim the Lord's death until he comes.
071127 Whoever, therefore, eats the bread or drinks the cup of the Lord in an unworthy manner will be guilty of profaning the body and blood of the Lord.
071128 Let a man examine himself, and so eat of the bread and drink of the cup.
071129 For any one who eats and drinks without discerning the body eats and drinks judgment upon himself.
071130 That is why many of you are weak and ill, and some have died.
071131 But if we judged ourselves truly, we should not be judged.
071132 But when we are judged by the Lord, we are chastened so that we may not be condemned along with the world.
071133 So then, my brethren, when you come together to eat, wait for one another --
071134 if any one is hungry, let him eat at home -- lest you come together to be condemned. About the other things I will give directions when I come.
071201 Now concerning spiritual gifts, brethren, I do not want you to be uninformed.
071202 You know that when you were heathen, you were led astray to dumb idols, however you may have been moved.
071203 Therefore I want you to understand that no one speaking by the Spirit of God ever says "Jesus be cursed!" and no one can say "Jesus is Lord" except by the Holy Spirit.
071204 Now there are varieties of gifts, but the same Spirit;
071205 and there are varieties of service, but the same Lord;
071206 and there are varieties of working, but it is the same God who inspires them all in every one.
071207 To each is given the manifestation of the Spirit for the common good.
071208 To one is given through the Spirit the utterance of wisdom, and to another the utterance of knowledge according to the same Spirit,
071209 to another faith by the same Spirit, to another gifts of healing by the one Spirit,
071210 to another the working of miracles, to another prophecy, to another the ability to distinguish between spirits, to another various kinds of tongues, to another the interpretation of tongues.
071211 All these are inspired by one and the same Spirit, who apportions to each one individually as he wills.
071212 For just as the body is one and has many members, and all the members of the body, though many, are one body, so it is with Christ.
071213 For by one Spirit we were all baptized into one body -- Jews or Greeks, slaves or free -- and all were made to drink of one Spirit.
071214 For the body does not consist of one member but of many.
071215 If the foot should say, "Because I am not a hand, I do not belong to the body," that would not make it any less a part of the body.
071216 And if the ear should say, "Because I am not an eye, I do not belong to the body," that would not make it any less a part of the body.
071217 If the whole body were an eye, where would be the hearing? If the whole body were an ear, where would be the sense of smell?
071218 But as it is, God arranged the organs in the body, each one of them, as he chose.
071219 If all were a single organ, where would the body be?
071220 As it is, there are many parts, yet one body.
071221 The eye cannot say to the hand, "I have no need of you," nor again the head to the feet, "I have no need of you."
071222 On the contrary, the parts of the body which seem to be weaker are indispensable,
071223 and those parts of the body which we think less honorable we invest with the greater honor, and our unpresentable parts are treated with greater modesty,
071224 which our more presentable parts do not require. But God has so composed the body, giving the greater honor to the inferior part,
071225 that there may be no discord in the body, but that the members may have the same care for one another.
071226 If one member suffers, all suffer together; if one member is honored, all rejoice together.
071227 Now you are the body of Christ and individually members of it.
071228 And God has appointed in the church first apostles, second prophets, third teachers, then workers of miracles, then healers, helpers, administrators, speakers in various kinds of tongues.
071229 Are all apostles? Are all prophets? Are all teachers? Do all work miracles?
071230 Do all possess gifts of healing? Do all speak with tongues? Do all interpret?
071231 But earnestly desire the higher gifts. And I will show you a still more excellent way.
071301 If I speak in the tongues of men and of angels, but have not love, I am a noisy gong or a clanging cymbal.
071302 And if I have prophetic powers, and understand all mysteries and all knowledge, and if I have all faith, so as to remove mountains, but have not love, I am nothing.
071303 If I give away all I have, and if I deliver my body to be burned, but have not love, I gain nothing.
071304 Love is patient and kind; love is not jealous or boastful;
071305 it is not arrogant or rude. Love does not insist on its own way; it is not irritable or resentful;
071306 it does not rejoice at wrong, but rejoices in the right.
071307 Love bears all things, believes all things, hopes all things, endures all things.
071308 Love never ends; as for prophecies, they will pass away; as for tongues, they will cease; as for knowledge, it will pass away.
071309 For our knowledge is imperfect and our prophecy is imperfect;
071310 but when the perfect comes, the imperfect will pass away.
071311 When I was a child, I spoke like a child, I thought like a child, I reasoned like a child; when I became a man, I gave up childish ways.
071312 For now we see in a mirror dimly, but then face to face. Now I know in part; then I shall understand fully, even as I have been fully understood.
071313 So faith, hope, love abide, these three; but the greatest of these is love.
071401 Make love your aim, and earnestly desire the spiritual gifts, especially that you may prophesy.
071402 For one who speaks in a tongue speaks not to men but to God; for no one understands him, but he utters mysteries in the Spirit.
071403 On the other hand, he who prophesies speaks to men for their upbuilding and encouragement and consolation.
071404 He who speaks in a tongue edifies himself, but he who prophesies edifies the church.
071405 Now I want you all to speak in tongues, but even more to prophesy. He who prophesies is greater than he who speaks in tongues, unless some one interprets, so that the church may be edified.
071406 Now, brethren, if I come to you speaking in tongues, how shall I benefit you unless I bring you some revelation or knowledge or prophecy or teaching?
071407 If even lifeless instruments, such as the flute or the harp, do not give distinct notes, how will any one know what is played?
071408 And if the bugle gives an indistinct sound, who will get ready for battle?
071409 So with yourselves; if you in a tongue utter speech that is not intelligible, how will any one know what is said? For you will be speaking into the air.
071410 There are doubtless many different languages in the world, and none is without meaning;
071411 but if I do not know the meaning of the language, I shall be a foreigner to the speaker and the speaker a foreigner to me.
071412 So with yourselves; since you are eager for manifestations of the Spirit, strive to excel in building up the church.
071413 Therefore, he who speaks in a tongue should pray for the power to interpret.
071414 For if I pray in a tongue, my spirit prays but my mind is unfruitful.
071415 What am I to do? I will pray with the spirit and I will pray with the mind also; I will sing with the spirit and I will sing with the mind also.
071416 Otherwise, if you bless with the spirit, how can any one in the position of an outsider say the "Amen" to your thanksgiving when he does not know what you are saying?
071417 For you may give thanks well enough, but the other man is not edified.
071418 I thank God that I speak in tongues more than you all;
071419 nevertheless, in church I would rather speak five words with my mind, in order to instruct others, than ten thousand words in a tongue.
071420 Brethren, do not be children in your thinking; be babes in evil, but in thinking be mature.
071421 In the law it is written, "By men of strange tongues and by the lips of foreigners will I speak to this people, and even then they will not listen to me, says the Lord."
071422 Thus, tongues are a sign not for believers but for unbelievers, while prophecy is not for unbelievers but for believers.
071423 If, therefore, the whole church assembles and all speak in tongues, and outsiders or unbelievers enter, will they not say that you are mad?
071424 But if all prophesy, and an unbeliever or outsider enters, he is convicted by all, he is called to account by all,
071425 the secrets of his heart are disclosed; and so, falling on his face, he will worship God and declare that God is really among you.
071426 What then, brethren? When you come together, each one has a hymn, a lesson, a revelation, a tongue, or an interpretation. Let all things be done for edification.
071427 If any speak in a tongue, let there be only two or at most three, and each in turn; and let one interpret.
071428 But if there is no one to interpret, let each of them keep silence in church and speak to himself and to God.
071429 Let two or three prophets speak, and let the others weigh what is said.
071430 If a revelation is made to another sitting by, let the first be silent.
071431 For you can all prophesy one by one, so that all may learn and all be encouraged;
071432 and the spirits of prophets are subject to prophets.
071433 For God is not a God of confusion but of peace. As in all the churches of the saints,
071434 the women should keep silence in the churches. For they are not permitted to speak, but should be subordinate, as even the law says.
071435 If there is anything they desire to know, let them ask their husbands at home. For it is shameful for a woman to speak in church.
071436 What! Did the word of God originate with you, or are you the only ones it has reached?
071437 If any one thinks that he is a prophet, or spiritual, he should acknowledge that what I am writing to you is a command of the Lord.
071438 If any one does not recognize this, he is not recognized.
071439 So, my brethren, earnestly desire to prophesy, and do not forbid speaking in tongues;
071440 but all things should be done decently and in order.
071501 Now I would remind you, brethren, in what terms I preached to you the gospel, which you received, in which you stand,
071502 by which you are saved, if you hold it fast -- unless you believed in vain.
071503 For I delivered to you as of first importance what I also received, that Christ died for our sins in accordance with the scriptures,
071504 that he was buried, that he was raised on the third day in accordance with the scriptures,
071505 and that he appeared to Cephas, then to the twelve.
071506 Then he appeared to more than five hundred brethren at one time, most of whom are still alive, though some have fallen asleep.
071507 Then he appeared to James, then to all the apostles.
071508 Last of all, as to one untimely born, he appeared also to me.
071509 For I am the least of the apostles, unfit to be called an apostle, because I persecuted the church of God.
071510 But by the grace of God I am what I am, and his grace toward me was not in vain. On the contrary, I worked harder than any of them, though it was not I, but the grace of God which is with me.
071511 Whether then it was I or they, so we preach and so you believed.
071512 Now if Christ is preached as raised from the dead, how can some of you say that there is no resurrection of the dead?
071513 But if there is no resurrection of the dead, then Christ has not been raised;
071514 if Christ has not been raised, then our preaching is in vain and your faith is in vain.
071515 We are even found to be misrepresenting God, because we testified of God that he raised Christ, whom he did not raise if it is true that the dead are not raised.
071516 For if the dead are not raised, then Christ has not been raised.
071517 If Christ has not been raised, your faith is futile and you are still in your sins.
071518 Then those also who have fallen asleep in Christ have perished.
071519 If for this life only we have hoped in Christ, we are of all men most to be pitied.
071520 But in fact Christ has been raised from the dead, the first fruits of those who have fallen asleep.
071521 For as by a man came death, by a man has come also the resurrection of the dead.
071522 For as in Adam all die, so also in Christ shall all be made alive.
071523 But each in his own order: Christ the first fruits, then at his coming those who belong to Christ.
071524 Then comes the end, when he delivers the kingdom to God the Father after destroying every rule and every authority and power.
071525 For he must reign until he has put all his enemies under his feet.
071526 The last enemy to be destroyed is death.
071527 "For God has put all things in subjection under his feet." But when it says, "All things are put in subjection under him," it is plain that he is excepted who put all things under him.
071528 When all things are subjected to him, then the Son himself will also be subjected to him who put all things under him, that God may be everything to every one.
071529 Otherwise, what do people mean by being baptized on behalf of the dead? If the dead are not raised at all, why are people baptized on their behalf?
071530 Why am I in peril every hour?
071531 I protest, brethren, by my pride in you which I have in Christ Jesus our Lord, I die every day!
071532 What do I gain if, humanly speaking, I fought with beasts at Ephesus? If the dead are not raised, "Let us eat and drink, for tomorrow we die."
071533 Do not be deceived: "Bad company ruins good morals."
071534 Come to your right mind, and sin no more. For some have no knowledge of God. I say this to your shame.
071535 But some one will ask, "How are the dead raised? With what kind of body do they come?"
071536 You foolish man! What you sow does not come to life unless it dies.
071537 And what you sow is not the body which is to be, but a bare kernel, perhaps of wheat or of some other grain.
071538 But God gives it a body as he has chosen, and to each kind of seed its own body.
071539 For not all flesh is alike, but there is one kind for men, another for animals, another for birds, and another for fish.
071540 There are celestial bodies and there are terrestrial bodies; but the glory of the celestial is one, and the glory of the terrestrial is another.
071541 There is one glory of the sun, and another glory of the moon, and another glory of the stars; for star differs from star in glory.
071542 So is it with the resurrection of the dead. What is sown is perishable, what is raised is imperishable.
071543 It is sown in dishonor, it is raised in glory. It is sown in weakness, it is raised in power.
071544 It is sown a physical body, it is raised a spiritual body. If there is a physical body, there is also a spiritual body.
071545 Thus it is written, "The first man Adam became a living being"; the last Adam became a life-giving spirit.
071546 But it is not the spiritual which is first but the physical, and then the spiritual.
071547 The first man was from the earth, a man of dust; the second man is from heaven.
071548 As was the man of dust, so are those who are of the dust; and as is the man of heaven, so are those who are of heaven.
071549 Just as we have borne the image of the man of dust, we shall also bear the image of the man of heaven.
071550 I tell you this, brethren: flesh and blood cannot inherit the kingdom of God, nor does the perishable inherit the imperishable.
071551 Lo! I tell you a mystery. We shall not all sleep, but we shall all be changed,
071552 in a moment, in the twinkling of an eye, at the last trumpet. For the trumpet will sound, and the dead will be raised imperishable, and we shall be changed.
071553 For this perishable nature must put on the imperishable, and this mortal nature must put on immortality.
071554 When the perishable puts on the imperishable, and the mortal puts on immortality, then shall come to pass the saying that is written: "Death is swallowed up in victory."
071555 "O death, where is thy victory? O death, where is thy sting?"
071556 The sting of death is sin, and the power of sin is the law.
071557 But thanks be to God, who gives us the victory through our Lord Jesus Christ.
071558 Therefore, my beloved brethren, be steadfast, immovable, always abounding in the work of the Lord, knowing that in the Lord your labor is not in vain.
071601 Now concerning the contribution for the saints: as I directed the churches of Galatia, so you also are to do.
071602 On the first day of every week, each of you is to put something aside and store it up, as he may prosper, so that contributions need not be made when I come.
071603 And when I arrive, I will send those whom you accredit by letter to carry your gift to Jerusalem.
071604 If it seems advisable that I should go also, they will accompany me.
071605 I will visit you after passing through Macedo'nia, for I intend to pass through Macedo'nia,
071606 and perhaps I will stay with you or even spend the winter, so that you may speed me on my journey, wherever I go.
071607 For I do not want to see you now just in passing; I hope to spend some time with you, if the Lord permits.
071608 But I will stay in Ephesus until Pentecost,
071609 for a wide door for effective work has opened to me, and there are many adversaries.
071610 When Timothy comes, see that you put him at ease among you, for he is doing the work of the Lord, as I am.
071611 So let no one despise him. Speed him on his way in peace, that he may return to me; for I am expecting him with the brethren.
071612 As for our brother Apol'los, I strongly urged him to visit you with the other brethren, but it was not at all his will to come now. He will come when he has opportunity.
071613 Be watchful, stand firm in your faith, be courageous, be strong.
071614 Let all that you do be done in love.
071615 Now, brethren, you know that the household of Steph'anas were the first converts in Acha'ia, and they have devoted themselves to the service of the saints;
071616 I urge you to be subject to such men and to every fellow worker and laborer.
071617 I rejoice at the coming of Steph'anas and Fortuna'tus and Acha'icus, because they have made up for your absence;
071618 for they refreshed my spirit as well as yours. Give recognition to such men.
071619 The churches of Asia send greetings. Aq'uila and Prisca, together with the church in their house, send you hearty greetings in the Lord.
071620 All the brethren send greetings. Greet one another with a holy kiss.
071621 I, Paul, write this greeting with my own hand.
071622 If any one has no love for the Lord, let him be accursed. Our Lord, come!
071623 The grace of the Lord Jesus be with you.
071624 My love be with you all in Christ Jesus. Amen.
080101 Paul, an apostle of Christ Jesus by the will of God, and Timothy our brother. To the church of God which is at Corinth, with all the saints who are in the whole of Acha'ia:
080102 Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ.
080103 Blessed be the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ, the Father of mercies and God of all comfort,
080104 who comforts us in all our affliction, so that we may be able to comfort those who are in any affliction, with the comfort with which we ourselves are comforted by God.
080105 For as we share abundantly in Christ's sufferings, so through Christ we share abundantly in comfort too.
080106 If we are afflicted, it is for your comfort and salvation; and if we are comforted, it is for your comfort, which you experience when you patiently endure the same sufferings that we suffer.
080107 Our hope for you is unshaken; for we know that as you share in our sufferings, you will also share in our comfort.
080108 For we do not want you to be ignorant, brethren, of the affliction we experienced in Asia; for we were so utterly, unbearably crushed that we despaired of life itself.
080109 Why, we felt that we had received the sentence of death; but that was to make us rely not on ourselves but on God who raises the dead;
080110 he delivered us from so deadly a peril, and he will deliver us; on him we have set our hope that he will deliver us again.
080111 You also must help us by prayer, so that many will give thanks on our behalf for the blessing granted us in answer to many prayers.
080112 For our boast is this, the testimony of our conscience that we have behaved in the world, and still more toward you, with holiness and godly sincerity, not by earthly wisdom but by the grace of God.
080113 For we write you nothing but what you can read and understand; I hope you will understand fully,
080114 as you have understood in part, that you can be proud of us as we can be of you, on the day of the Lord Jesus.
080115 Because I was sure of this, I wanted to come to you first, so that you might have a double pleasure;
080116 I wanted to visit you on my way to Macedo'nia, and to come back to you from Macedo'nia and have you send me on my way to Judea.
080117 Was I vacillating when I wanted to do this? Do I make my plans like a worldly man, ready to say Yes and No at once?
080118 As surely as God is faithful, our word to you has not been Yes and No.
080119 For the Son of God, Jesus Christ, whom we preached among you, Silva'nus and Timothy and I, was not Yes and No; but in him it is always Yes.
080120 For all the promises of God find their Yes in him. That is why we utter the Amen through him, to the glory of God.
080121 But it is God who establishes us with you in Christ, and has commissioned us;
080122 he has put his seal upon us and given us his Spirit in our hearts as a guarantee.
080123 But I call God to witness against me -- it was to spare you that I refrained from coming to Corinth.
080124 Not that we lord it over your faith; we work with you for your joy, for you stand firm in your faith.
080201 For I made up my mind not to make you another painful visit.
080202 For if I cause you pain, who is there to make me glad but the one whom I have pained?
080203 And I wrote as I did, so that when I came I might not suffer pain from those who should have made me rejoice, for I felt sure of all of you, that my joy would be the joy of you all.
080204 For I wrote you out of much affliction and anguish of heart and with many tears, not to cause you pain but to let you know the abundant love that I have for you.
080205 But if any one has caused pain, he has caused it not to me, but in some measure -- not to put it too severely -- to you all.
080206 For such a one this punishment by the majority is enough;
080207 so you should rather turn to forgive and comfort him, or he may be overwhelmed by excessive sorrow.
080208 So I beg you to reaffirm your love for him.
080209 For this is why I wrote, that I might test you and know whether you are obedient in everything.
080210 Any one whom you forgive, I also forgive. What I have forgiven, if I have forgiven anything, has been for your sake in the presence of Christ,
080211 to keep Satan from gaining the advantage over us; for we are not ignorant of his designs.
080212 When I came to Tro'as to preach the gospel of Christ, a door was opened for me in the Lord;
080213 but my mind could not rest because I did not find my brother Titus there. So I took leave of them and went on to Macedo'nia.
080214 But thanks be to God, who in Christ always leads us in triumph, and through us spreads the fragrance of the knowledge of him everywhere.
080215 For we are the aroma of Christ to God among those who are being saved and among those who are perishing,
080216 to one a fragrance from death to death, to the other a fragrance from life to life. Who is sufficient for these things?
080217 For we are not, like so many, peddlers of God's word; but as men of sincerity, as commissioned by God, in the sight of God we speak in Christ.
080301 Are we beginning to commend ourselves again? Or do we need, as some do, letters of recommendation to you, or from you?
080302 You yourselves are our letter of recommendation, written on your hearts, to be known and read by all men;
080303 and you show that you are a letter from Christ delivered by us, written not with ink but with the Spirit of the living God, not on tablets of stone but on tablets of human hearts.
080304 Such is the confidence that we have through Christ toward God.
080305 Not that we are competent of ourselves to claim anything as coming from us; our competence is from God,
080306 who has made us competent to be ministers of a new covenant, not in a written code but in the Spirit; for the written code kills, but the Spirit gives life.
080307 Now if the dispensation of death, carved in letters on stone, came with such splendor that the Israelites could not look at Moses' face because of its brightness, fading as this was,
080308 will not the dispensation of the Spirit be attended with greater splendor?
080309 For if there was splendor in the dispensation of condemnation, the dispensation of righteousness must far exceed it in splendor.
080310 Indeed, in this case, what once had splendor has come to have no splendor at all, because of the splendor that surpasses it.
080311 For if what faded away came with splendor, what is permanent must have much more splendor.
080312 Since we have such a hope, we are very bold,
080313 not like Moses, who put a veil over his face so that the Israelites might not see the end of the fading splendor.
080314 But their minds were hardened; for to this day, when they read the old covenant, that same veil remains unlifted, because only through Christ is it taken away.
080315 Yes, to this day whenever Moses is read a veil lies over their minds;
080316 but when a man turns to the Lord the veil is removed.
080317 Now the Lord is the Spirit, and where the Spirit of the Lord is, there is freedom.
080318 And we all, with unveiled face, beholding the glory of the Lord, are being changed into his likeness from one degree of glory to another; for this comes from the Lord who is the Spirit.
080401 Therefore, having this ministry by the mercy of God, we do not lose heart.
080402 We have renounced disgraceful, underhanded ways; we refuse to practice cunning or to tamper with God's word, but by the open statement of the truth we would commend ourselves to every man's conscience in the sight of God.
080403 And even if our gospel is veiled, it is veiled only to those who are perishing.
080404 In their case the god of this world has blinded the minds of the unbelievers, to keep them from seeing the light of the gospel of the glory of Christ, who is the likeness of God.
080405 For what we preach is not ourselves, but Jesus Christ as Lord, with ourselves as your servants for Jesus' sake.
080406 For it is the God who said, "Let light shine out of darkness," who has shone in our hearts to give the light of the knowledge of the glory of God in the face of Christ.
080407 But we have this treasure in earthen vessels, to show that the transcendent power belongs to God and not to us.
080408 We are afflicted in every way, but not crushed; perplexed, but not driven to despair;
080409 persecuted, but not forsaken; struck down, but not destroyed;
080410 always carrying in the body the death of Jesus, so that the life of Jesus may also be manifested in our bodies.
080411 For while we live we are always being given up to death for Jesus' sake, so that the life of Jesus may be manifested in our mortal flesh.
080412 So death is at work in us, but life in you.
080413 Since we have the same spirit of faith as he had who wrote, "I believed, and so I spoke," we too believe, and so we speak,
080414 knowing that he who raised the Lord Jesus will raise us also with Jesus and bring us with you into his presence.
080415 For it is all for your sake, so that as grace extends to more and more people it may increase thanksgiving, to the glory of God.
080416 So we do not lose heart. Though our outer nature is wasting away, our inner nature is being renewed every day.
080417 For this slight momentary affliction is preparing for us an eternal weight of glory beyond all comparison,
080418 because we look not to the things that are seen but to the things that are unseen; for the things that are seen are transient, but the things that are unseen are eternal.
080501 For we know that if the earthly tent we live in is destroyed, we have a building from God, a house not made with hands, eternal in the heavens.
080502 Here indeed we groan, and long to put on our heavenly dwelling,
080503 so that by putting it on we may not be found naked.
080504 For while we are still in this tent, we sigh with anxiety; not that we would be unclothed, but that we would be further clothed, so that what is mortal may be swallowed up by life.
080505 He who has prepared us for this very thing is God, who has given us the Spirit as a guarantee.
080506 So we are always of good courage; we know that while we are at home in the body we are away from the Lord,
080507 for we walk by faith, not by sight.
080508 We are of good courage, and we would rather be away from the body and at home with the Lord.
080509 So whether we are at home or away, we make it our aim to please him.
080510 For we must all appear before the judgment seat of Christ, so that each one may receive good or evil, according to what he has done in the body.
080511 Therefore, knowing the fear of the Lord, we persuade men; but what we are is known to God, and I hope it is known also to your conscience.
080512 We are not commending ourselves to you again but giving you cause to be proud of us, so that you may be able to answer those who pride themselves on a man's position and not on his heart.
080513 For if we are beside ourselves, it is for God; if we are in our right mind, it is for you.
080514 For the love of Christ controls us, because we are convinced that one has died for all; therefore all have died.
080515 And he died for all, that those who live might live no longer for themselves but for him who for their sake died and was raised.
080516 From now on, therefore, we regard no one from a human point of view; even though we once regarded Christ from a human point of view, we regard him thus no longer.
080517 Therefore, if any one is in Christ, he is a new creation; the old has passed away, behold, the new has come.
080518 All this is from God, who through Christ reconciled us to himself and gave us the ministry of reconciliation;
080519 that is, in Christ God was reconciling the world to himself, not counting their trespasses against them, and entrusting to us the message of reconciliation.
080520 So we are ambassadors for Christ, God making his appeal through us. We beseech you on behalf of Christ, be reconciled to God.
080521 For our sake he made him to be sin who knew no sin, so that in him we might become the righteousness of God.
080601 Working together with him, then, we entreat you not to accept the grace of God in vain.
080602 For he says, "At the acceptable time I have listened to you, and helped you on the day of salvation." Behold, now is the acceptable time; behold, now is the day of salvation.
080603 We put no obstacle in any one's way, so that no fault may be found with our ministry,
080604 but as servants of God we commend ourselves in every way: through great endurance, in afflictions, hardships, calamities,
080605 beatings, imprisonments, tumults, labors, watching, hunger;
080606 by purity, knowledge, forbearance, kindness, the Holy Spirit, genuine love,
080607 truthful speech, and the power of God; with the weapons of righteousness for the right hand and for the left;
080608 in honor and dishonor, in ill repute and good repute. We are treated as impostors, and yet are true;
080609 as unknown, and yet well known; as dying, and behold we live; as punished, and yet not killed;
080610 as sorrowful, yet always rejoicing; as poor, yet making many rich; as having nothing, and yet possessing everything.
080611 Our mouth is open to you, Corinthians; our heart is wide.
080612 You are not restricted by us, but you are restricted in your own affections.
080613 In return -- I speak as to children -- widen your hearts also.
080614 Do not be mismated with unbelievers. For what partnership have righteousness and iniquity? Or what fellowship has light with darkness?
080615 What accord has Christ with Be'lial? Or what has a believer in common with an unbeliever?
080616 What agreement has the temple of God with idols? For we are the temple of the living God; as God said, "I will live in them and move among them, and I will be their God, and they shall be my people.
080617 Therefore come out from them, and be separate from them, says the Lord, and touch nothing unclean; then I will welcome you,
080618 and I will be a father to you, and you shall be my sons and daughters, says the Lord Almighty."
080701 Since we have these promises, beloved, let us cleanse ourselves from every defilement of body and spirit, and make holiness perfect in the fear of God.
080702 Open your hearts to us; we have wronged no one, we have corrupted no one, we have taken advantage of no one.
080703 I do not say this to condemn you, for I said before that you are in our hearts, to die together and to live together.
080704 I have great confidence in you; I have great pride in you; I am filled with comfort. With all our affliction, I am overjoyed.
080705 For even when we came into Macedo'nia, our bodies had no rest but we were afflicted at every turn -- fighting without and fear within.
080706 But God, who comforts the downcast, comforted us by the coming of Titus,
080707 and not only by his coming but also by the comfort with which he was comforted in you, as he told us of your longing, your mourning, your zeal for me, so that I rejoiced still more.
080708 For even if I made you sorry with my letter, I do not regret it (though I did regret it), for I see that that letter grieved you, though only for a while.
080709 As it is, I rejoice, not because you were grieved, but because you were grieved into repenting; for you felt a godly grief, so that you suffered no loss through us.
080710 For godly grief produces a repentance that leads to salvation and brings no regret, but worldly grief produces death.
080711 For see what earnestness this godly grief has produced in you, what eagerness to clear yourselves, what indignation, what alarm, what longing, what zeal, what punishment! At every point you have proved yourselves guiltless in the matter.
080712 So although I wrote to you, it was not on account of the one who did the wrong, nor on account of the one who suffered the wrong, but in order that your zeal for us might be revealed to you in the sight of God.
080713 Therefore we are comforted. And besides our own comfort we rejoiced still more at the joy of Titus, because his mind has been set at rest by you all.
080714 For if I have expressed to him some pride in you, I was not put to shame; but just as everything we said to you was true, so our boasting before Titus has proved true.
080715 And his heart goes out all the more to you, as he remembers the obedience of you all, and the fear and trembling with which you received him.
080716 I rejoice, because I have perfect confidence in you.
080801 We want you to know, brethren, about the grace of God which has been shown in the churches of Macedo'nia,
080802 for in a severe test of affliction, their abundance of joy and their extreme poverty have overflowed in a wealth of liberality on their part.
080803 For they gave according to their means, as I can testify, and beyond their means, of their own free will,
080804 begging us earnestly for the favor of taking part in the relief of the saints --
080805 and this, not as we expected, but first they gave themselves to the Lord and to us by the will of God.
080806 Accordingly we have urged Titus that as he had already made a beginning, he should also complete among you this gracious work.
080807 Now as you excel in everything -- in faith, in utterance, in knowledge, in all earnestness, and in your love for us -- see that you excel in this gracious work also.
080808 I say this not as a command, but to prove by the earnestness of others that your love also is genuine.
080809 For you know the grace of our Lord Jesus Christ, that though he was rich, yet for your sake he became poor, so that by his poverty you might become rich.
080810 And in this matter I give my advice: it is best for you now to complete what a year ago you began not only to do but to desire,
080811 so that your readiness in desiring it may be matched by your completing it out of what you have.
080812 For if the readiness is there, it is acceptable according to what a man has, not according to what he has not.
080813 I do not mean that others should be eased and you burdened,
080814 but that as a matter of equality your abundance at the present time should supply their want, so that their abundance may supply your want, that there may be equality.
080815 As it is written, "He who gathered much had nothing over, and he who gathered little had no lack."
080816 But thanks be to God who puts the same earnest care for you into the heart of Titus.
080817 For he not only accepted our appeal, but being himself very earnest he is going to you of his own accord.
080818 With him we are sending the brother who is famous among all the churches for his preaching of the gospel;
080819 and not only that, but he has been appointed by the churches to travel with us in this gracious work which we are carrying on, for the glory of the Lord and to show our good will.
080820 We intend that no one should blame us about this liberal gift which we are administering,
080821 for we aim at what is honorable not only in the Lord's sight but also in the sight of men.
080822 And with them we are sending our brother whom we have often tested and found earnest in many matters, but who is now more earnest than ever because of his great confidence in you.
080823 As for Titus, he is my partner and fellow worker in your service; and as for our brethren, they are messengers of the churches, the glory of Christ.
080824 So give proof, before the churches, of your love and of our boasting about you to these men.
080901 Now it is superfluous for me to write to you about the offering for the saints,
080902 for I know your readiness, of which I boast about you to the people of Macedo'nia, saying that Acha'ia has been ready since last year; and your zeal has stirred up most of them.
080903 But I am sending the brethren so that our boasting about you may not prove vain in this case, so that you may be ready, as I said you would be;
080904 lest if some Macedo'nians come with me and find that you are not ready, we be humiliated -- to say nothing of you -- for being so confident.
080905 So I thought it necessary to urge the brethren to go on to you before me, and arrange in advance for this gift you have promised, so that it may be ready not as an exaction but as a willing gift.
080906 The point is this: he who sows sparingly will also reap sparingly, and he who sows bountifully will also reap bountifully.
080907 Each one must do as he has made up his mind, not reluctantly or under compulsion, for God loves a cheerful giver.
080908 And God is able to provide you with every blessing in abundance, so that you may always have enough of everything and may provide in abundance for every good work.
080909 As it is written, "He scatters abroad, he gives to the poor; his righteousness endures for ever."
080910 He who supplies seed to the sower and bread for food will supply and multiply your resources and increase the harvest of your righteousness.
080911 You will be enriched in every way for great generosity, which through us will produce thanksgiving to God;
080912 for the rendering of this service not only supplies the wants of the saints but also overflows in many thanksgivings to God.
080913 Under the test of this service, you will glorify God by your obedience in acknowledging the gospel of Christ, and by the generosity of your contribution for them and for all others;
080914 while they long for you and pray for you, because of the surpassing grace of God in you.
080915 Thanks be to God for his inexpressible gift!
081001 I, Paul, myself entreat you, by the meekness and gentleness of Christ -- I who am humble when face to face with you, but bold to you when I am away! --
081002 I beg of you that when I am present I may not have to show boldness with such confidence as I count on showing against some who suspect us of acting in worldly fashion.
081003 For though we live in the world we are not carrying on a worldly war,
081004 for the weapons of our warfare are not worldly but have divine power to destroy strongholds.
081005 We destroy arguments and every proud obstacle to the knowledge of God, and take every thought captive to obey Christ,
081006 being ready to punish every disobedience, when your obedience is complete.
081007 Look at what is before your eyes. If any one is confident that he is Christ's, let him remind himself that as he is Christ's, so are we.
081008 For even if I boast a little too much of our authority, which the Lord gave for building you up and not for destroying you, I shall not be put to shame.
081009 I would not seem to be frightening you with letters.
081010 For they say, "His letters are weighty and strong, but his bodily presence is weak, and his speech of no account."
081011 Let such people understand that what we say by letter when absent, we do when present.
081012 Not that we venture to class or compare ourselves with some of those who commend themselves. But when they measure themselves by one another, and compare themselves with one another, they are without understanding.
081013 But we will not boast beyond limit, but will keep to the limits God has apportioned us, to reach even to you.
081014 For we are not overextending ourselves, as though we did not reach you; we were the first to come all the way to you with the gospel of Christ.
081015 We do not boast beyond limit, in other men's labors; but our hope is that as your faith increases, our field among you may be greatly enlarged,
081016 so that we may preach the gospel in lands beyond you, without boasting of work already done in another's field.
081017 "Let him who boasts, boast of the Lord."
081018 For it is not the man who commends himself that is accepted, but the man whom the Lord commends.
081101 I wish you would bear with me in a little foolishness. Do bear with me!
081102 I feel a divine jealousy for you, for I betrothed you to Christ to present you as a pure bride to her one husband.
081103 But I am afraid that as the serpent deceived Eve by his cunning, your thoughts will be led astray from a sincere and pure devotion to Christ.
081104 For if some one comes and preaches another Jesus than the one we preached, or if you receive a different spirit from the one you received, or if you accept a different gospel from the one you accepted, you submit to it readily enough.
081105 I think that I am not in the least inferior to these superlative apostles.
081106 Even if I am unskilled in speaking, I am not in knowledge; in every way we have made this plain to you in all things.
081107 Did I commit a sin in abasing myself so that you might be exalted, because I preached God's gospel without cost to you?
081108 I robbed other churches by accepting support from them in order to serve you.
081109 And when I was with you and was in want, I did not burden any one, for my needs were supplied by the brethren who came from Macedo'nia. So I refrained and will refrain from burdening you in any way.
081110 As the truth of Christ is in me, this boast of mine shall not be silenced in the regions of Acha'ia.
081111 And why? Because I do not love you? God knows I do!
081112 And what I do I will continue to do, in order to undermine the claim of those who would like to claim that in their boasted mission they work on the same terms as we do.
081113 For such men are false apostles, deceitful workmen, disguising themselves as apostles of Christ.
081114 And no wonder, for even Satan disguises himself as an angel of light.
081115 So it is not strange if his servants also disguise themselves as servants of righteousness. Their end will correspond to their deeds.
081116 I repeat, let no one think me foolish; but even if you do, accept me as a fool, so that I too may boast a little.
081117 (What I am saying I say not with the Lord's authority but as a fool, in this boastful confidence;
081118 since many boast of worldly things, I too will boast.)
081119 For you gladly bear with fools, being wise yourselves!
081120 For you bear it if a man makes slaves of you, or preys upon you, or takes advantage of you, or puts on airs, or strikes you in the face.
081121 To my shame, I must say, we were too weak for that! But whatever any one dares to boast of -- I am speaking as a fool -- I also dare to boast of that.
081122 Are they Hebrews? So am I. Are they Israelites? So am I. Are they descendants of Abraham? So am I.
081123 Are they servants of Christ? I am a better one -- I am talking like a madman -- with far greater labors, far more imprisonments, with countless beatings, and often near death.
081124 Five times I have received at the hands of the Jews the forty lashes less one.
081125 Three times I have been beaten with rods; once I was stoned. Three times I have been shipwrecked; a night and a day I have been adrift at sea;
081126 on frequent journeys, in danger from rivers, danger from robbers, danger from my own people, danger from Gentiles, danger in the city, danger in the wilderness, danger at sea, danger from false brethren;
081127 in toil and hardship, through many a sleepless night, in hunger and thirst, often without food, in cold and exposure.
081128 And, apart from other things, there is the daily pressure upon me of my anxiety for all the churches.
081129 Who is weak, and I am not weak? Who is made to fall, and I am not indignant?
081130 If I must boast, I will boast of the things that show my weakness.
081131 The God and Father of the Lord Jesus, he who is blessed for ever, knows that I do not lie.
081132 At Damascus, the governor under King Ar'etas guarded the city of Damascus in order to seize me,
081133 but I was let down in a basket through a window in the wall, and escaped his hands.
081201 I must boast; there is nothing to be gained by it, but I will go on to visions and revelations of the Lord.
081202 I know a man in Christ who fourteen years ago was caught up to the third heaven -- whether in the body or out of the body I do not know, God knows.
081203 And I know that this man was caught up into Paradise -- whether in the body or out of the body I do not know, God knows --
081204 and he heard things that cannot be told, which man may not utter.
081205 On behalf of this man I will boast, but on my own behalf I will not boast, except of my weaknesses.
081206 Though if I wish to boast, I shall not be a fool, for I shall be speaking the truth. But I refrain from it, so that no one may think more of me than he sees in me or hears from me.
081207 And to keep me from being too elated by the abundance of revelations, a thorn was given me in the flesh, a messenger of Satan, to harass me, to keep me from being too elated.
081208 Three times I besought the Lord about this, that it should leave me;
081209 but he said to me, "My grace is sufficient for you, for my power is made perfect in weakness." I will all the more gladly boast of my weaknesses, that the power of Christ may rest upon me.
081210 For the sake of Christ, then, I am content with weaknesses, insults, hardships, persecutions, and calamities; for when I am weak, then I am strong.
081211 I have been a fool! You forced me to it, for I ought to have been commended by you. For I was not at all inferior to these superlative apostles, even though I am nothing.
081212 The signs of a true apostle were performed among you in all patience, with signs and wonders and mighty works.
081213 For in what were you less favored than the rest of the churches, except that I myself did not burden you? Forgive me this wrong!
081214 Here for the third time I am ready to come to you. And I will not be a burden, for I seek not what is yours but you; for children ought not to lay up for their parents, but parents for their children.
081215 I will most gladly spend and be spent for your souls. If I love you the more, am I to be loved the less?
081216 But granting that I myself did not burden you, I was crafty, you say, and got the better of you by guile.
081217 Did I take advantage of you through any of those whom I sent to you?
081218 I urged Titus to go, and sent the brother with him. Did Titus take advantage of you? Did we not act in the same spirit? Did we not take the same steps?
081219 Have you been thinking all along that we have been defending ourselves before you? It is in the sight of God that we have been speaking in Christ, and all for your upbuilding, beloved.
081220 For I fear that perhaps I may come and find you not what I wish, and that you may find me not what you wish; that perhaps there may be quarreling, jealousy, anger, selfishness, slander, gossip, conceit, and disorder.
081221 I fear that when I come again my God may humble me before you, and I may have to mourn over many of those who sinned before and have not repented of the impurity, immorality, and licentiousness which they have practiced.
081301 This is the third time I am coming to you. Any charge must be sustained by the evidence of two or three witnesses.
081302 I warned those who sinned before and all the others, and I warn them now while absent, as I did when present on my second visit, that if I come again I will not spare them --
081303 since you desire proof that Christ is speaking in me. He is not weak in dealing with you, but is powerful in you.
081304 For he was crucified in weakness, but lives by the power of God. For we are weak in him, but in dealing with you we shall live with him by the power of God.
081305 Examine yourselves, to see whether you are holding to your faith. Test yourselves. Do you not realize that Jesus Christ is in you? -- unless indeed you fail to meet the test!
081306 I hope you will find out that we have not failed.
081307 But we pray God that you may not do wrong -- not that we may appear to have met the test, but that you may do what is right, though we may seem to have failed.
081308 For we cannot do anything against the truth, but only for the truth.
081309 For we are glad when we are weak and you are strong. What we pray for is your improvement.
081310 I write this while I am away from you, in order that when I come I may not have to be severe in my use of the authority which the Lord has given me for building up and not for tearing down.
081311 Finally, brethren, farewell. Mend your ways, heed my appeal, agree with one another, live in peace, and the God of love and peace will be with you.
081312 Greet one another with a holy kiss.
081313 All the saints greet you.
081314 The grace of the Lord Jesus Christ and the love of God and the fellowship of the Holy Spirit be with you all.
090101 Paul an apostle -- not from men nor through man, but through Jesus Christ and God the Father, who raised him from the dead --
090102 and all the brethren who are with me, To the churches of Galatia:
090103 Grace to you and peace from God the Father and our Lord Jesus Christ,
090104 who gave himself for our sins to deliver us from the present evil age, according to the will of our God and Father;
090105 to whom be the glory for ever and ever. Amen.
090106 I am astonished that you are so quickly deserting him who called you in the grace of Christ and turning to a different gospel --
090107 not that there is another gospel, but there are some who trouble you and want to pervert the gospel of Christ.
090108 But even if we, or an angel from heaven, should preach to you a gospel contrary to that which we preached to you, let him be accursed.
090109 As we have said before, so now I say again, If any one is preaching to you a gospel contrary to that which you received, let him be accursed.
090110 Am I now seeking the favor of men, or of God? Or am I trying to please men? If I were still pleasing men, I should not be a servant of Christ.
090111 For I would have you know, brethren, that the gospel which was preached by me is not man's gospel.
090112 For I did not receive it from man, nor was I taught it, but it came through a revelation of Jesus Christ.
090113 For you have heard of my former life in Judaism, how I persecuted the church of God violently and tried to destroy it;
090114 and I advanced in Judaism beyond many of my own age among my people, so extremely zealous was I for the traditions of my fathers.
090115 But when he who had set me apart before I was born, and had called me through his grace,
090116 was pleased to reveal his Son to me, in order that I might preach him among the Gentiles, I did not confer with flesh and blood,
090117 nor did I go up to Jerusalem to those who were apostles before me, but I went away into Arabia; and again I returned to Damascus.
090118 Then after three years I went up to Jerusalem to visit Cephas, and remained with him fifteen days.
090119 But I saw none of the other apostles except James the Lord's brother.
090120 (In what I am writing to you, before God, I do not lie!)
090121 Then I went into the regions of Syria and Cili'cia.
090122 And I was still not known by sight to the churches of Christ in Judea;
090123 they only heard it said, "He who once persecuted us is now preaching the faith he once tried to destroy."
090124 And they glorified God because of me.
090201 Then after fourteen years I went up again to Jerusalem with Barnabas, taking Titus along with me.
090202 I went up by revelation; and I laid before them (but privately before those who were of repute) the gospel which I preach among the Gentiles, lest somehow I should be running or had run in vain.
090203 But even Titus, who was with me, was not compelled to be circumcised, though he was a Greek.
090204 But because of false brethren secretly brought in, who slipped in to spy out our freedom which we have in Christ Jesus, that they might bring us into bondage --
090205 to them we did not yield submission even for a moment, that the truth of the gospel might be preserved for you.
090206 And from those who were reputed to be something (what they were makes no difference to me; God shows no partiality) -- those, I say, who were of repute added nothing to me;
090207 but on the contrary, when they saw that I had been entrusted with the gospel to the uncircumcised, just as Peter had been entrusted with the gospel to the circumcised
090208 (for he who worked through Peter for the mission to the circumcised worked through me also for the Gentiles),
090209 and when they perceived the grace that was given to me, James and Cephas and John, who were reputed to be pillars, gave to me and Barnabas the right hand of fellowship, that we should go to the Gentiles and they to the circumcised;
090210 only they would have us remember the poor, which very thing I was eager to do.
090211 But when Cephas came to Antioch I opposed him to his face, because he stood condemned.
090212 For before certain men came from James, he ate with the Gentiles; but when they came he drew back and separated himself, fearing the circumcision party.
090213 And with him the rest of the Jews acted insincerely, so that even Barnabas was carried away by their insincerity.
090214 But when I saw that they were not straightforward about the truth of the gospel, I said to Cephas before them all, "If you, though a Jew, live like a Gentile and not like a Jew, how can you compel the Gentiles to live like Jews?"
090215 We ourselves, who are Jews by birth and not Gentile sinners,
090216 yet who know that a man is not justified by works of the law but through faith in Jesus Christ, even we have believed in Christ Jesus, in order to be justified by faith in Christ, and not by works of the law, because by works of the law shall no one be justified.
090217 But if, in our endeavor to be justified in Christ, we ourselves were found to be sinners, is Christ then an agent of sin? Certainly not!
090218 But if I build up again those things which I tore down, then I prove myself a transgressor.
090219 For I through the law died to the law, that I might live to God.
090220 I have been crucified with Christ; it is no longer I who live, but Christ who lives in me; and the life I now live in the flesh I live by faith in the Son of God, who loved me and gave himself for me.
090221 I do not nullify the grace of God; for if justification were through the law, then Christ died to no purpose.
090301 O foolish Galatians! Who has bewitched you, before whose eyes Jesus Christ was publicly portrayed as crucified?
090302 Let me ask you only this: Did you receive the Spirit by works of the law, or by hearing with faith?
090303 Are you so foolish? Having begun with the Spirit, are you now ending with the flesh?
090304 Did you experience so many things in vain? -- if it really is in vain.
090305 Does he who supplies the Spirit to you and works miracles among you do so by works of the law, or by hearing with faith?
090306 Thus Abraham "believed God, and it was reckoned to him as righteousness."
090307 So you see that it is men of faith who are the sons of Abraham.
090308 And the scripture, foreseeing that God would justify the Gentiles by faith, preached the gospel beforehand to Abraham, saying, "In you shall all the nations be blessed."
090309 So then, those who are men of faith are blessed with Abraham who had faith.
090310 For all who rely on works of the law are under a curse; for it is written, "Cursed be every one who does not abide by all things written in the book of the law, and do them."
090311 Now it is evident that no man is justified before God by the law; for "He who through faith is righteous shall live";
090312 but the law does not rest on faith, for "He who does them shall live by them."
090313 Christ redeemed us from the curse of the law, having become a curse for us -- for it is written, "Cursed be every one who hangs on a tree" --
090314 that in Christ Jesus the blessing of Abraham might come upon the Gentiles, that we might receive the promise of the Spirit through faith.
090315 To give a human example, brethren: no one annuls even a man's will, or adds to it, once it has been ratified.
090316 Now the promises were made to Abraham and to his offspring. It does not say, "And to offsprings," referring to many; but, referring to one, "And to your offspring," which is Christ.
090317 This is what I mean: the law, which came four hundred and thirty years afterward, does not annul a covenant previously ratified by God, so as to make the promise void.
090318 For if the inheritance is by the law, it is no longer by promise; but God gave it to Abraham by a promise.
090319 Why then the law? It was added because of transgressions, till the offspring should come to whom the promise had been made; and it was ordained by angels through an intermediary.
090320 Now an intermediary implies more than one; but God is one.
090321 Is the law then against the promises of God? Certainly not; for if a law had been given which could make alive, then righteousness would indeed be by the law.
090322 But the scripture consigned all things to sin, that what was promised to faith in Jesus Christ might be given to those who believe.
090323 Now before faith came, we were confined under the law, kept under restraint until faith should be revealed.
090324 So that the law was our custodian until Christ came, that we might be justified by faith.
090325 But now that faith has come, we are no longer under a custodian;
090326 for in Christ Jesus you are all sons of God, through faith.
090327 For as many of you as were baptized into Christ have put on Christ.
090328 There is neither Jew nor Greek, there is neither slave nor free, there is neither male nor female; for you are all one in Christ Jesus.
090329 And if you are Christ's, then you are Abraham's offspring, heirs according to promise.
090401 I mean that the heir, as long as he is a child, is no better than a slave, though he is the owner of all the estate;
090402 but he is under guardians and trustees until the date set by the father.
090403 So with us; when we were children, we were slaves to the elemental spirits of the universe.
090404 But when the time had fully come, God sent forth his Son, born of woman, born under the law,
090405 to redeem those who were under the law, so that we might receive adoption as sons.
090406 And because you are sons, God has sent the Spirit of his Son into our hearts, crying, "Abba! Father!"
090407 So through God you are no longer a slave but a son, and if a son then an heir.
090408 Formerly, when you did not know God, you were in bondage to beings that by nature are no gods;
090409 but now that you have come to know God, or rather to be known by God, how can you turn back again to the weak and beggarly elemental spirits, whose slaves you want to be once more?
090410 You observe days, and months, and seasons, and years!
090411 I am afraid I have labored over you in vain.
090412 Brethren, I beseech you, become as I am, for I also have become as you are. You did me no wrong;
090413 you know it was because of a bodily ailment that I preached the gospel to you at first;
090414 and though my condition was a trial to you, you did not scorn or despise me, but received me as an angel of God, as Christ Jesus.
090415 What has become of the satisfaction you felt? For I bear you witness that, if possible, you would have plucked out your eyes and given them to me.
090416 Have I then become your enemy by telling you the truth?
090417 They make much of you, but for no good purpose; they want to shut you out, that you may make much of them.
090418 For a good purpose it is always good to be made much of, and not only when I am present with you.
090419 My little children, with whom I am again in travail until Christ be formed in you!
090420 I could wish to be present with you now and to change my tone, for I am perplexed about you.
090421 Tell me, you who desire to be under law, do you not hear the law?
090422 For it is written that Abraham had two sons, one by a slave and one by a free woman.
090423 But the son of the slave was born according to the flesh, the son of the free woman through promise.
090424 Now this is an allegory: these women are two covenants. One is from Mount Sinai, bearing children for slavery; she is Hagar.
090425 Now Hagar is Mount Sinai in Arabia; she corresponds to the present Jerusalem, for she is in slavery with her children.
090426 But the Jerusalem above is free, and she is our mother.
090427 For it is written, "Rejoice, O barren one who does not bear; break forth and shout, you who are not in travail; for the children of the desolate one are many more than the children of her that is married."
090428 Now we, brethren, like Isaac, are children of promise.
090429 But as at that time he who was born according to the flesh persecuted him who was born according to the Spirit, so it is now.
090430 But what does the scripture say? "Cast out the slave and her son; for the son of the slave shall not inherit with the son of the free woman."
090431 So, brethren, we are not children of the slave but of the free woman.
090501 For freedom Christ has set us free; stand fast therefore, and do not submit again to a yoke of slavery.
090502 Now I, Paul, say to you that if you receive circumcision, Christ will be of no advantage to you.
090503 I testify again to every man who receives circumcision that he is bound to keep the whole law.
090504 You are severed from Christ, you who would be justified by the law; you have fallen away from grace.
090505 For through the Spirit, by faith, we wait for the hope of righteousness.
090506 For in Christ Jesus neither circumcision nor uncircumcision is of any avail, but faith working through love.
090507 You were running well; who hindered you from obeying the truth?
090508 This persuasion is not from him who calls you.
090509 A little leaven leavens the whole lump.
090510 I have confidence in the Lord that you will take no other view than mine; and he who is troubling you will bear his judgment, whoever he is.
090511 But if I, brethren, still preach circumcision, why am I still persecuted? In that case the stumbling block of the cross has been removed.
090512 I wish those who unsettle you would mutilate themselves!
090513 For you were called to freedom, brethren; only do not use your freedom as an opportunity for the flesh, but through love be servants of one another.
090514 For the whole law is fulfilled in one word, "You shall love your neighbor as yourself."
090515 But if you bite and devour one another take heed that you are not consumed by one another.
090516 But I say, walk by the Spirit, and do not gratify the desires of the flesh.
090517 For the desires of the flesh are against the Spirit, and the desires of the Spirit are against the flesh; for these are opposed to each other, to prevent you from doing what you would.
090518 But if you are led by the Spirit you are not under the law.
090519 Now the works of the flesh are plain: fornication, impurity, licentiousness,
090520 idolatry, sorcery, enmity, strife, jealousy, anger, selfishness, dissension, party spirit,
090521 envy, drunkenness, carousing, and the like. I warn you, as I warned you before, that those who do such things shall not inherit the kingdom of God.
090522 But the fruit of the Spirit is love, joy, peace, patience, kindness, goodness, faithfulness,
090523 gentleness, self-control; against such there is no law.
090524 And those who belong to Christ Jesus have crucified the flesh with its passions and desires.
090525 If we live by the Spirit, let us also walk by the Spirit.
090526 Let us have no self-conceit, no provoking of one another, no envy of one another.
090601 Brethren, if a man is overtaken in any trespass, you who are spiritual should restore him in a spirit of gentleness. Look to yourself, lest you too be tempted.
090602 Bear one another's burdens, and so fulfil the law of Christ.
090603 For if any one thinks he is something, when he is nothing, he deceives himself.
090604 But let each one test his own work, and then his reason to boast will be in himself alone and not in his neighbor.
090605 For each man will have to bear his own load.
090606 Let him who is taught the word share all good things with him who teaches.
090607 Do not be deceived; God is not mocked, for whatever a man sows, that he will also reap.
090608 For he who sows to his own flesh will from the flesh reap corruption; but he who sows to the Spirit will from the Spirit reap eternal life.
090609 And let us not grow weary in well-doing, for in due season we shall reap, if we do not lose heart.
090610 So then, as we have opportunity, let us do good to all men, and especially to those who are of the household of faith.
090611 See with what large letters I am writing to you with my own hand.
090612 It is those who want to make a good showing in the flesh that would compel you to be circumcised, and only in order that they may not be persecuted for the cross of Christ.
090613 For even those who receive circumcision do not themselves keep the law, but they desire to have you circumcised that they may glory in your flesh.
090614 But far be it from me to glory except in the cross of our Lord Jesus Christ, by which the world has been crucified to me, and I to the world.
090615 For neither circumcision counts for anything, nor uncircumcision, but a new creation.
090616 Peace and mercy be upon all who walk by this rule, upon the Israel of God.
090617 Henceforth let no man trouble me; for I bear on my body the marks of Jesus.
090618 The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with your spirit, brethren. Amen.
100101 Paul, an apostle of Christ Jesus by the will of God, To the saints who are also faithful in Christ Jesus:
100102 Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ.
100103 Blessed be the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ, who has blessed us in Christ with every spiritual blessing in the heavenly places,
100104 even as he chose us in him before the foundation of the world, that we should be holy and blameless before him.
100105 He destined us in love to be his sons through Jesus Christ, according to the purpose of his will,
100106 to the praise of his glorious grace which he freely bestowed on us in the Beloved.
100107 In him we have redemption through his blood, the forgiveness of our trespasses, according to the riches of his grace
100108 which he lavished upon us.
100109 For he has made known to us in all wisdom and insight the mystery of his will, according to his purpose which he set forth in Christ
100110 as a plan for the fulness of time, to unite all things in him, things in heaven and things on earth.
100111 In him, according to the purpose of him who accomplishes all things according to the counsel of his will,
100112 we who first hoped in Christ have been destined and appointed to live for the praise of his glory.
100113 In him you also, who have heard the word of truth, the gospel of your salvation, and have believed in him, were sealed with the promised Holy Spirit,
100114 which is the guarantee of our inheritance until we acquire possession of it, to the praise of his glory.
100115 For this reason, because I have heard of your faith in the Lord Jesus and your love toward all the saints,
100116 I do not cease to give thanks for you, remembering you in my prayers,
100117 that the God of our Lord Jesus Christ, the Father of glory, may give you a spirit of wisdom and of revelation in the knowledge of him,
100118 having the eyes of your hearts enlightened, that you may know what is the hope to which he has called you, what are the riches of his glorious inheritance in the saints,
100119 and what is the immeasurable greatness of his power in us who believe, according to the working of his great might
100120 which he accomplished in Christ when he raised him from the dead and made him sit at his right hand in the heavenly places,
100121 far above all rule and authority and power and dominion, and above every name that is named, not only in this age but also in that which is to come;
100122 and he has put all things under his feet and has made him the head over all things for the church,
100123 which is his body, the fulness of him who fills all in all.
100201 And you he made alive, when you were dead through the trespasses and sins
100202 in which you once walked, following the course of this world, following the prince of the power of the air, the spirit that is now at work in the sons of disobedience.
100203 Among these we all once lived in the passions of our flesh, following the desires of body and mind, and so we were by nature children of wrath, like the rest of mankind.
100204 But God, who is rich in mercy, out of the great love with which he loved us,
100205 even when we were dead through our trespasses, made us alive together with Christ (by grace you have been saved),
100206 and raised us up with him, and made us sit with him in the heavenly places in Christ Jesus,
100207 that in the coming ages he might show the immeasurable riches of his grace in kindness toward us in Christ Jesus.
100208 For by grace you have been saved through faith; and this is not your own doing, it is the gift of God --
100209 not because of works, lest any man should boast.
100210 For we are his workmanship, created in Christ Jesus for good works, which God prepared beforehand, that we should walk in them.
100211 Therefore remember that at one time you Gentiles in the flesh, called the uncircumcision by what is called the circumcision, which is made in the flesh by hands --
100212 remember that you were at that time separated from Christ, alienated from the commonwealth of Israel, and strangers to the covenants of promise, having no hope and without God in the world.
100213 But now in Christ Jesus you who once were far off have been brought near in the blood of Christ.
100214 For he is our peace, who has made us both one, and has broken down the dividing wall of hostility,
