100215 by abolishing in his flesh the law of commandments and ordinances, that he might create in himself one new man in place of the two, so making peace,
100216 and might reconcile us both to God in one body through the cross, thereby bringing the hostility to an end.
100217 And he came and preached peace to you who were far off and peace to those who were near;
100218 for through him we both have access in one Spirit to the Father.
100219 So then you are no longer strangers and sojourners, but you are fellow citizens with the saints and members of the household of God,
100220 built upon the foundation of the apostles and prophets, Christ Jesus himself being the cornerstone,
100221 in whom the whole structure is joined together and grows into a holy temple in the Lord;
100222 in whom you also are built into it for a dwelling place of God in the Spirit.
100301 For this reason I, Paul, a prisoner for Christ Jesus on behalf of you Gentiles --
100302 assuming that you have heard of the stewardship of God's grace that was given to me for you,
100303 how the mystery was made known to me by revelation, as I have written briefly.
100304 When you read this you can perceive my insight into the mystery of Christ,
100305 which was not made known to the sons of men in other generations as it has now been revealed to his holy apostles and prophets by the Spirit;
100306 that is, how the Gentiles are fellow heirs, members of the same body, and partakers of the promise in Christ Jesus through the gospel.
100307 Of this gospel I was made a minister according to the gift of God's grace which was given me by the working of his power.
100308 To me, though I am the very least of all the saints, this grace was given, to preach to the Gentiles the unsearchable riches of Christ,
100309 and to make all men see what is the plan of the mystery hidden for ages in God who created all things;
100310 that through the church the manifold wisdom of God might now be made known to the principalities and powers in the heavenly places.
100311 This was according to the eternal purpose which he has realized in Christ Jesus our Lord,
100312 in whom we have boldness and confidence of access through our faith in him.
100313 So I ask you not to lose heart over what I am suffering for you, which is your glory.
100314 For this reason I bow my knees before the Father,
100315 from whom every family in heaven and on earth is named,
100316 that according to the riches of his glory he may grant you to be strengthened with might through his Spirit in the inner man,
100317 and that Christ may dwell in your hearts through faith; that you, being rooted and grounded in love,
100318 may have power to comprehend with all the saints what is the breadth and length and height and depth,
100319 and to know the love of Christ which surpasses knowledge, that you may be filled with all the fulness of God.
100320 Now to him who by the power at work within us is able to do far more abundantly than all that we ask or think,
100321 to him be glory in the church and in Christ Jesus to all generations, for ever and ever. Amen.
100401 I therefore, a prisoner for the Lord, beg you to lead a life worthy of the calling to which you have been called,
100402 with all lowliness and meekness, with patience, forbearing one another in love,
100403 eager to maintain the unity of the Spirit in the bond of peace.
100404 There is one body and one Spirit, just as you were called to the one hope that belongs to your call,
100405 one Lord, one faith, one baptism,
100406 one God and Father of us all, who is above all and through all and in all.
100407 But grace was given to each of us according to the measure of Christ's gift.
100408 Therefore it is said, "When he ascended on high he led a host of captives, and he gave gifts to men."
100409 (In saying, "He ascended," what does it mean but that he had also descended into the lower parts of the earth?
100410 He who descended is he who also ascended far above all the heavens, that he might fill all things.)
100411 And his gifts were that some should be apostles, some prophets, some evangelists, some pastors and teachers,
100412 to equip the saints for the work of ministry, for building up the body of Christ,
100413 until we all attain to the unity of the faith and of the knowledge of the Son of God, to mature manhood, to the measure of the stature of the fulness of Christ;
100414 so that we may no longer be children, tossed to and fro and carried about with every wind of doctrine, by the cunning of men, by their craftiness in deceitful wiles.
100415 Rather, speaking the truth in love, we are to grow up in every way into him who is the head, into Christ,
100416 from whom the whole body, joined and knit together by every joint with which it is supplied, when each part is working properly, makes bodily growth and upbuilds itself in love.
100417 Now this I affirm and testify in the Lord, that you must no longer live as the Gentiles do, in the futility of their minds;
100418 they are darkened in their understanding, alienated from the life of God because of the ignorance that is in them, due to their hardness of heart;
100419 they have become callous and have given themselves up to licentiousness, greedy to practice every kind of uncleanness.
100420 You did not so learn Christ! --
100421 assuming that you have heard about him and were taught in him, as the truth is in Jesus.
100422 Put off your old nature which belongs to your former manner of life and is corrupt through deceitful lusts,
100423 and be renewed in the spirit of your minds,
100424 and put on the new nature, created after the likeness of God in true righteousness and holiness.
100425 Therefore, putting away falsehood, let every one speak the truth with his neighbor, for we are members one of another.
100426 Be angry but do not sin; do not let the sun go down on your anger,
100427 and give no opportunity to the devil.
100428 Let the thief no longer steal, but rather let him labor, doing honest work with his hands, so that he may be able to give to those in need.
100429 Let no evil talk come out of your mouths, but only such as is good for edifying, as fits the occasion, that it may impart grace to those who hear.
100430 And do not grieve the Holy Spirit of God, in whom you were sealed for the day of redemption.
100431 Let all bitterness and wrath and anger and clamor and slander be put away from you, with all malice,
100432 and be kind to one another, tenderhearted, forgiving one another, as God in Christ forgave you.
100501 Therefore be imitators of God, as beloved children.
100502 And walk in love, as Christ loved us and gave himself up for us, a fragrant offering and sacrifice to God.
100503 But fornication and all impurity or covetousness must not even be named among you, as is fitting among saints.
100504 Let there be no filthiness, nor silly talk, nor levity, which are not fitting; but instead let there be thanksgiving.
100505 Be sure of this, that no fornicator or impure man, or one who is covetous (that is, an idolater), has any inheritance in the kingdom of Christ and of God.
100506 Let no one deceive you with empty words, for it is because of these things that the wrath of God comes upon the sons of disobedience.
100507 Therefore do not associate with them,
100508 for once you were darkness, but now you are light in the Lord; walk as children of light
100509 (for the fruit of light is found in all that is good and right and true),
100510 and try to learn what is pleasing to the Lord.
100511 Take no part in the unfruitful works of darkness, but instead expose them.
100512 For it is a shame even to speak of the things that they do in secret;
100513 but when anything is exposed by the light it becomes visible, for anything that becomes visible is light.
100514 Therefore it is said, "Awake, O sleeper, and arise from the dead, and Christ shall give you light."
100515 Look carefully then how you walk, not as unwise men but as wise,
100516 making the most of the time, because the days are evil.
100517 Therefore do not be foolish, but understand what the will of the Lord is.
100518 And do not get drunk with wine, for that is debauchery; but be filled with the Spirit,
100519 addressing one another in psalms and hymns and spiritual songs, singing and making melody to the Lord with all your heart,
100520 always and for everything giving thanks in the name of our Lord Jesus Christ to God the Father.
100521 Be subject to one another out of reverence for Christ.
100522 Wives, be subject to your husbands, as to the Lord.
100523 For the husband is the head of the wife as Christ is the head of the church, his body, and is himself its Savior.
100524 As the church is subject to Christ, so let wives also be subject in everything to their husbands.
100525 Husbands, love your wives, as Christ loved the church and gave himself up for her,
100526 that he might sanctify her, having cleansed her by the washing of water with the word,
100527 that he might present the church to himself in splendor, without spot or wrinkle or any such thing, that she might be holy and without blemish.
100528 Even so husbands should love their wives as their own bodies. He who loves his wife loves himself.
100529 For no man ever hates his own flesh, but nourishes and cherishes it, as Christ does the church,
100530 because we are members of his body.
100531 "For this reason a man shall leave his father and mother and be joined to his wife, and the two shall become one flesh."
100532 This mystery is a profound one, and I am saying that it refers to Christ and the church;
100533 however, let each one of you love his wife as himself, and let the wife see that she respects her husband.
100601 Children, obey your parents in the Lord, for this is right.
100602 "Honor your father and mother" (this is the first commandment with a promise),
100603 "that it may be well with you and that you may live long on the earth."
100604 Fathers, do not provoke your children to anger, but bring them up in the discipline and instruction of the Lord.
100605 Slaves, be obedient to those who are your earthly masters, with fear and trembling, in singleness of heart, as to Christ;
100606 not in the way of eye-service, as men-pleasers, but as servants of Christ, doing the will of God from the heart,
100607 rendering service with a good will as to the Lord and not to men,
100608 knowing that whatever good any one does, he will receive the same again from the Lord, whether he is a slave or free.
100609 Masters, do the same to them, and forbear threatening, knowing that he who is both their Master and yours is in heaven, and that there is no partiality with him.
100610 Finally, be strong in the Lord and in the strength of his might.
100611 Put on the whole armor of God, that you may be able to stand against the wiles of the devil.
100612 For we are not contending against flesh and blood, but against the principalities, against the powers, against the world rulers of this present darkness, against the spiritual hosts of wickedness in the heavenly places.
100613 Therefore take the whole armor of God, that you may be able to withstand in the evil day, and having done all, to stand.
100614 Stand therefore, having girded your loins with truth, and having put on the breastplate of righteousness,
100615 and having shod your feet with the equipment of the gospel of peace;
100616 besides all these, taking the shield of faith, with which you can quench all the flaming darts of the evil one.
100617 And take the helmet of salvation, and the sword of the Spirit, which is the word of God.
100618 Pray at all times in the Spirit, with all prayer and supplication. To that end keep alert with all perseverance, making supplication for all the saints,
100619 and also for me, that utterance may be given me in opening my mouth boldly to proclaim the mystery of the gospel,
100620 for which I am an ambassador in chains; that I may declare it boldly, as I ought to speak.
100621 Now that you also may know how I am and what I am doing, Tych'icus the beloved brother and faithful minister in the Lord will tell you everything.
100622 I have sent him to you for this very purpose, that you may know how we are, and that he may encourage your hearts.
100623 Peace be to the brethren, and love with faith, from God the Father and the Lord Jesus Christ.
100624 Grace be with all who love our Lord Jesus Christ with love undying.
110101 Paul and Timothy, servants of Christ Jesus, To all the saints in Christ Jesus who are at Philip'pi, with the bishops and deacons:
110102 Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ.
110103 I thank my God in all my remembrance of you,
110104 always in every prayer of mine for you all making my prayer with joy,
110105 thankful for your partnership in the gospel from the first day until now.
110106 And I am sure that he who began a good work in you will bring it to completion at the day of Jesus Christ.
110107 It is right for me to feel thus about you all, because I hold you in my heart, for you are all partakers with me of grace, both in my imprisonment and in the defense and confirmation of the gospel.
110108 For God is my witness, how I yearn for you all with the affection of Christ Jesus.
110109 And it is my prayer that your love may abound more and more, with knowledge and all discernment,
110110 so that you may approve what is excellent, and may be pure and blameless for the day of Christ,
110111 filled with the fruits of righteousness which come through Jesus Christ, to the glory and praise of God.
110112 I want you to know, brethren, that what has happened to me has really served to advance the gospel,
110113 so that it has become known throughout the whole praetorian guard and to all the rest that my imprisonment is for Christ;
110114 and most of the brethren have been made confident in the Lord because of my imprisonment, and are much more bold to speak the word of God without fear.
110115 Some indeed preach Christ from envy and rivalry, but others from good will.
110116 The latter do it out of love, knowing that I am put here for the defense of the gospel;
110117 the former proclaim Christ out of partisanship, not sincerely but thinking to afflict me in my imprisonment.
110118 What then? Only that in every way, whether in pretense or in truth, Christ is proclaimed; and in that I rejoice.
110119 Yes, and I shall rejoice. For I know that through your prayers and the help of the Spirit of Jesus Christ this will turn out for my deliverance,
110120 as it is my eager expectation and hope that I shall not be at all ashamed, but that with full courage now as always Christ will be honored in my body, whether by life or by death.
110121 For to me to live is Christ, and to die is gain.
110122 If it is to be life in the flesh, that means fruitful labor for me. Yet which I shall choose I cannot tell.
110123 I am hard pressed between the two. My desire is to depart and be with Christ, for that is far better.
110124 But to remain in the flesh is more necessary on your account.
110125 Convinced of this, I know that I shall remain and continue with you all, for your progress and joy in the faith,
110126 so that in me you may have ample cause to glory in Christ Jesus, because of my coming to you again.
110127 Only let your manner of life be worthy of the gospel of Christ, so that whether I come and see you or am absent, I may hear of you that you stand firm in one spirit, with one mind striving side by side for the faith of the gospel,
110128 and not frightened in anything by your opponents. This is a clear omen to them of their destruction, but of your salvation, and that from God.
110129 For it has been granted to you that for the sake of Christ you should not only believe in him but also suffer for his sake,
110130 engaged in the same conflict which you saw and now hear to be mine.
110201 So if there is any encouragement in Christ, any incentive of love, any participation in the Spirit, any affection and sympathy,
110202 complete my joy by being of the same mind, having the same love, being in full accord and of one mind.
110203 Do nothing from selfishness or conceit, but in humility count others better than yourselves.
110204 Let each of you look not only to his own interests, but also to the interests of others.
110205 Have this mind among yourselves, which is yours in Christ Jesus,
110206 who, though he was in the form of God, did not count equality with God a thing to be grasped,
110207 but emptied himself, taking the form of a servant, being born in the likeness of men.
110208 And being found in human form he humbled himself and became obedient unto death, even death on a cross.
110209 Therefore God has highly exalted him and bestowed on him the name which is above every name,
110210 that at the name of Jesus every knee should bow, in heaven and on earth and under the earth,
110211 and every tongue confess that Jesus Christ is Lord, to the glory of God the Father.
110212 Therefore, my beloved, as you have always obeyed, so now, not only as in my presence but much more in my absence, work out your own salvation with fear and trembling;
110213 for God is at work in you, both to will and to work for his good pleasure.
110214 Do all things without grumbling or questioning,
110215 that you may be blameless and innocent, children of God without blemish in the midst of a crooked and perverse generation, among whom you shine as lights in the world,
110216 holding fast the word of life, so that in the day of Christ I may be proud that I did not run in vain or labor in vain.
110217 Even if I am to be poured as a libation upon the sacrificial offering of your faith, I am glad and rejoice with you all.
110218 Likewise you also should be glad and rejoice with me.
110219 I hope in the Lord Jesus to send Timothy to you soon, so that I may be cheered by news of you.
110220 I have no one like him, who will be genuinely anxious for your welfare.
110221 They all look after their own interests, not those of Jesus Christ.
110222 But Timothy's worth you know, how as a son with a father he has served with me in the gospel.
110223 I hope therefore to send him just as soon as I see how it will go with me;
110224 and I trust in the Lord that shortly I myself shall come also.
110225 I have thought it necessary to send to you Epaphrodi'tus my brother and fellow worker and fellow soldier, and your messenger and minister to my need,
110226 for he has been longing for you all, and has been distressed because you heard that he was ill.
110227 Indeed he was ill, near to death. But God had mercy on him, and not only on him but on me also, lest I should have sorrow upon sorrow.
110228 I am the more eager to send him, therefore, that you may rejoice at seeing him again, and that I may be less anxious.
110229 So receive him in the Lord with all joy; and honor such men,
110230 for he nearly died for the work of Christ, risking his life to complete your service to me.
110301 Finally, my brethren, rejoice in the Lord. To write the same things to you is not irksome to me, and is safe for you.
110302 Look out for the dogs, look out for the evil-workers, look out for those who mutilate the flesh.
110303 For we are the true circumcision, who worship God in spirit, and glory in Christ Jesus, and put no confidence in the flesh.
110304 Though I myself have reason for confidence in the flesh also. If any other man thinks he has reason for confidence in the flesh, I have more:
110305 circumcised on the eighth day, of the people of Israel, of the tribe of Benjamin, a Hebrew born of Hebrews; as to the law a Pharisee,
110306 as to zeal a persecutor of the church, as to righteousness under the law blameless.
110307 But whatever gain I had, I counted as loss for the sake of Christ.
110308 Indeed I count everything as loss because of the surpassing worth of knowing Christ Jesus my Lord. For his sake I have suffered the loss of all things, and count them as refuse, in order that I may gain Christ
110309 and be found in him, not having a righteousness of my own, based on law, but that which is through faith in Christ, the righteousness from God that depends on faith;
110310 that I may know him and the power of his resurrection, and may share his sufferings, becoming like him in his death,
110311 that if possible I may attain the resurrection from the dead.
110312 Not that I have already obtained this or am already perfect; but I press on to make it my own, because Christ Jesus has made me his own.
110313 Brethren, I do not consider that I have made it my own; but one thing I do, forgetting what lies behind and straining forward to what lies ahead,
110314 I press on toward the goal for the prize of the upward call of God in Christ Jesus.
110315 Let those of us who are mature be thus minded; and if in anything you are otherwise minded, God will reveal that also to you.
110316 Only let us hold true to what we have attained.
110317 Brethren, join in imitating me, and mark those who so live as you have an example in us.
110318 For many, of whom I have often told you and now tell you even with tears, live as enemies of the cross of Christ.
110319 Their end is destruction, their god is the belly, and they glory in their shame, with minds set on earthly things.
110320 But our commonwealth is in heaven, and from it we await a Savior, the Lord Jesus Christ,
110321 who will change our lowly body to be like his glorious body, by the power which enables him even to subject all things to himself.
110401 Therefore, my brethren, whom I love and long for, my joy and crown, stand firm thus in the Lord, my beloved.
110402 I entreat Eu-o'dia and I entreat Syn'tyche to agree in the Lord.
110403 And I ask you also, true yokefellow, help these women, for they have labored side by side with me in the gospel together with Clement and the rest of my fellow workers, whose names are in the book of life.
110404 Rejoice in the Lord always; again I will say, Rejoice.
110405 Let all men know your forbearance. The Lord is at hand.
110406 Have no anxiety about anything, but in everything by prayer and supplication with thanksgiving let your requests be made known to God.
110407 And the peace of God, which passes all understanding, will keep your hearts and your minds in Christ Jesus.
110408 Finally, brethren, whatever is true, whatever is honorable, whatever is just, whatever is pure, whatever is lovely, whatever is gracious, if there is any excellence, if there is anything worthy of praise, think about these things.
110409 What you have learned and received and heard and seen in me, do; and the God of peace will be with you.
110410 I rejoice in the Lord greatly that now at length you have revived your concern for me; you were indeed concerned for me, but you had no opportunity.
110411 Not that I complain of want; for I have learned, in whatever state I am, to be content.
110412 I know how to be abased, and I know how to abound; in any and all circumstances I have learned the secret of facing plenty and hunger, abundance and want.
110413 I can do all things in him who strengthens me.
110414 Yet it was kind of you to share my trouble.
110415 And you Philippians yourselves know that in the beginning of the gospel, when I left Macedo'nia, no church entered into partnership with me in giving and receiving except you only;
110416 for even in Thessaloni'ca you sent me help once and again.
110417 Not that I seek the gift; but I seek the fruit which increases to your credit.
110418 I have received full payment, and more; I am filled, having received from Epaphrodi'tus the gifts you sent, a fragrant offering, a sacrifice acceptable and pleasing to God.
110419 And my God will supply every need of yours according to his riches in glory in Christ Jesus.
110420 To our God and Father be glory for ever and ever. Amen.
110421 Greet every saint in Christ Jesus. The brethren who are with me greet you.
110422 All the saints greet you, especially those of Caesar's household.
110423 The grace of the Lord Jesus Christ be with your spirit.
120101 Paul, an apostle of Christ Jesus by the will of God, and Timothy our brother,
120102 To the saints and faithful brethren in Christ at Colos'sae: Grace to you and peace from God our Father.
120103 We always thank God, the Father of our Lord Jesus Christ, when we pray for you,
120104 because we have heard of your faith in Christ Jesus and of the love which you have for all the saints,
120105 because of the hope laid up for you in heaven. Of this you have heard before in the word of the truth, the gospel
120106 which has come to you, as indeed in the whole world it is bearing fruit and growing -- so among yourselves, from the day you heard and understood the grace of God in truth,
120107 as you learned it from Ep'aphras our beloved fellow servant. He is a faithful minister of Christ on our behalf
120108 and has made known to us your love in the Spirit.
120109 And so, from the day we heard of it, we have not ceased to pray for you, asking that you may be filled with the knowledge of his will in all spiritual wisdom and understanding,
120110 to lead a life worthy of the Lord, fully pleasing to him, bearing fruit in every good work and increasing in the knowledge of God.
120111 May you be strengthened with all power, according to his glorious might, for all endurance and patience with joy,
120112 giving thanks to the Father, who has qualified us to share in the inheritance of the saints in light.
120113 He has delivered us from the dominion of darkness and transferred us to the kingdom of his beloved Son,
120114 in whom we have redemption, the forgiveness of sins.
120115 He is the image of the invisible God, the first-born of all creation;
120116 for in him all things were created, in heaven and on earth, visible and invisible, whether thrones or dominions or principalities or authorities -- all things were created through him and for him.
120117 He is before all things, and in him all things hold together.
120118 He is the head of the body, the church; he is the beginning, the first-born from the dead, that in everything he might be pre-eminent.
120119 For in him all the fulness of God was pleased to dwell,
120120 and through him to reconcile to himself all things, whether on earth or in heaven, making peace by the blood of his cross.
120121 And you, who once were estranged and hostile in mind, doing evil deeds,
120122 he has now reconciled in his body of flesh by his death, in order to present you holy and blameless and irreproachable before him,
120123 provided that you continue in the faith, stable and steadfast, not shifting from the hope of the gospel which you heard, which has been preached to every creature under heaven, and of which I, Paul, became a minister.
120124 Now I rejoice in my sufferings for your sake, and in my flesh I complete what is lacking in Christ's afflictions for the sake of his body, that is, the church,
120125 of which I became a minister according to the divine office which was given to me for you, to make the word of God fully known,
120126 the mystery hidden for ages and generations but now made manifest to his saints.
120127 To them God chose to make known how great among the Gentiles are the riches of the glory of this mystery, which is Christ in you, the hope of glory.
120128 Him we proclaim, warning every man and teaching every man in all wisdom, that we may present every man mature in Christ.
120129 For this I toil, striving with all the energy which he mightily inspires within me.
120201 For I want you to know how greatly I strive for you, and for those at La-odice'a, and for all who have not seen my face,
120202 that their hearts may be encouraged as they are knit together in love, to have all the riches of assured understanding and the knowledge of God's mystery, of Christ,
120203 in whom are hid all the treasures of wisdom and knowledge.
120204 I say this in order that no one may delude you with beguiling speech.
120205 For though I am absent in body, yet I am with you in spirit, rejoicing to see your good order and the firmness of your faith in Christ.
120206 As therefore you received Christ Jesus the Lord, so live in him,
120207 rooted and built up in him and established in the faith, just as you were taught, abounding in thanksgiving.
120208 See to it that no one makes a prey of you by philosophy and empty deceit, according to human tradition, according to the elemental spirits of the universe, and not according to Christ.
120209 For in him the whole fulness of deity dwells bodily,
120210 and you have come to fulness of life in him, who is the head of all rule and authority.
120211 In him also you were circumcised with a circumcision made without hands, by putting off the body of flesh in the circumcision of Christ;
120212 and you were buried with him in baptism, in which you were also raised with him through faith in the working of God, who raised him from the dead.
120213 And you, who were dead in trespasses and the uncircumcision of your flesh, God made alive together with him, having forgiven us all our trespasses,
120214 having canceled the bond which stood against us with its legal demands; this he set aside, nailing it to the cross.
120215 He disarmed the principalities and powers and made a public example of them, triumphing over them in him.
120216 Therefore let no one pass judgment on you in questions of food and drink or with regard to a festival or a new moon or a sabbath.
120217 These are only a shadow of what is to come; but the substance belongs to Christ.
120218 Let no one disqualify you, insisting on self-abasement and worship of angels, taking his stand on visions, puffed up without reason by his sensuous mind,
120219 and not holding fast to the Head, from whom the whole body, nourished and knit together through its joints and ligaments, grows with a growth that is from God.
120220 If with Christ you died to the elemental spirits of the universe, why do you live as if you still belonged to the world? Why do you submit to regulations,
120221 "Do not handle, Do not taste, Do not touch"
120222 (referring to things which all perish as they are used), according to human precepts and doctrines?
120223 These have indeed an appearance of wisdom in promoting rigor of devotion and self-abasement and severity to the body, but they are of no value in checking the indulgence of the flesh.
120301 If then you have been raised with Christ, seek the things that are above, where Christ is, seated at the right hand of God.
120302 Set your minds on things that are above, not on things that are on earth.
120303 For you have died, and your life is hid with Christ in God.
120304 When Christ who is our life appears, then you also will appear with him in glory.
120305 Put to death therefore what is earthly in you: fornication, impurity, passion, evil desire, and covetousness, which is idolatry.
120306 On account of these the wrath of God is coming.
120307 In these you once walked, when you lived in them.
120308 But now put them all away: anger, wrath, malice, slander, and foul talk from your mouth.
120309 Do not lie to one another, seeing that you have put off the old nature with its practices
120310 and have put on the new nature, which is being renewed in knowledge after the image of its creator.
120311 Here there cannot be Greek and Jew, circumcised and uncircumcised, barbarian, Scyth'ian, slave, free man, but Christ is all, and in all.
120312 Put on then, as God's chosen ones, holy and beloved, compassion, kindness, lowliness, meekness, and patience,
120313 forbearing one another and, if one has a complaint against another, forgiving each other; as the Lord has forgiven you, so you also must forgive.
120314 And above all these put on love, which binds everything together in perfect harmony.
120315 And let the peace of Christ rule in your hearts, to which indeed you were called in the one body. And be thankful.
120316 Let the word of Christ dwell in you richly, teach and admonish one another in all wisdom, and sing psalms and hymns and spiritual songs with thankfulness in your hearts to God.
120317 And whatever you do, in word or deed, do everything in the name of the Lord Jesus, giving thanks to God the Father through him.
120318 Wives, be subject to your husbands, as is fitting in the Lord.
120319 Husbands, love your wives, and do not be harsh with them.
120320 Children, obey your parents in everything, for this pleases the Lord.
120321 Fathers, do not provoke your children, lest they become discouraged.
120322 Slaves, obey in everything those who are your earthly masters, not with eyeservice, as men-pleasers, but in singleness of heart, fearing the Lord.
120323 Whatever your task, work heartily, as serving the Lord and not men,
120324 knowing that from the Lord you will receive the inheritance as your reward; you are serving the Lord Christ.
120325 For the wrongdoer will be paid back for the wrong he has done, and there is no partiality.
120401 Masters, treat your slaves justly and fairly, knowing that you also have a Master in heaven.
120402 Continue steadfastly in prayer, being watchful in it with thanksgiving;
120403 and pray for us also, that God may open to us a door for the word, to declare the mystery of Christ, on account of which I am in prison,
120404 that I may make it clear, as I ought to speak.
120405 Conduct yourselves wisely toward outsiders, making the most of the time.
120406 Let your speech always be gracious, seasoned with salt, so that you may know how you ought to answer every one.
120407 Tych'icus will tell you all about my affairs; he is a beloved brother and faithful minister and fellow servant in the Lord.
120408 I have sent him to you for this very purpose, that you may know how we are and that he may encourage your hearts,
120409 and with him Ones'imus, the faithful and beloved brother, who is one of yourselves. They will tell you of everything that has taken place here.
120410 Aristar'chus my fellow prisoner greets you, and Mark the cousin of Barnabas (concerning whom you have received instructions -- if he comes to you, receive him),
120411 and Jesus who is called Justus. These are the only men of the circumcision among my fellow workers for the kingdom of God, and they have been a comfort to me.
120412 Ep'aphras, who is one of yourselves, a servant of Christ Jesus, greets you, always remembering you earnestly in his prayers, that you may stand mature and fully assured in all the will of God.
120413 For I bear him witness that he has worked hard for you and for those in La-odice'a and in Hi-erap'olis.
120414 Luke the beloved physician and Demas greet you.
120415 Give my greetings to the brethren at La-odice'a, and to Nympha and the church in her house.
120416 And when this letter has been read among you, have it read also in the church of the La-odice'ans; and see that you read also the letter from La-odice'a.
120417 And say to Archip'pus, "See that you fulfil the ministry which you have received in the Lord."
120418 I, Paul, write this greeting with my own hand. Remember my fetters. Grace be with you.
130101 Paul, Silva'nus, and Timothy, To the church of the Thessalo'nians in God the Father and the Lord Jesus Christ: Grace to you and peace.
130102 We give thanks to God always for you all, constantly mentioning you in our prayers,
130103 remembering before our God and Father your work of faith and labor of love and steadfastness of hope in our Lord Jesus Christ.
130104 For we know, brethren beloved by God, that he has chosen you;
130105 for our gospel came to you not only in word, but also in power and in the Holy Spirit and with full conviction. You know what kind of men we proved to be among you for your sake.
130106 And you became imitators of us and of the Lord, for you received the word in much affliction, with joy inspired by the Holy Spirit;
130107 so that you became an example to all the believers in Macedo'nia and in Acha'ia.
130108 For not only has the word of the Lord sounded forth from you in Macedo'nia and Acha'ia, but your faith in God has gone forth everywhere, so that we need not say anything.
130109 For they themselves report concerning us what a welcome we had among you, and how you turned to God from idols, to serve a living and true God,
130110 and to wait for his Son from heaven, whom he raised from the dead, Jesus who delivers us from the wrath to come.
130201 For you yourselves know, brethren, that our visit to you was not in vain;
130202 but though we had already suffered and been shamefully treated at Philip'pi, as you know, we had courage in our God to declare to you the gospel of God in the face of great opposition.
130203 For our appeal does not spring from error or uncleanness, nor is it made with guile;
130204 but just as we have been approved by God to be entrusted with the gospel, so we speak, not to please men, but to please God who tests our hearts.
130205 For we never used either words of flattery, as you know, or a cloak for greed, as God is witness;
130206 nor did we seek glory from men, whether from you or from others, though we might have made demands as apostles of Christ.
130207 But we were gentle among you, like a nurse taking care of her children.
130208 So, being affectionately desirous of you, we were ready to share with you not only the gospel of God but also our own selves, because you had become very dear to us.
130209 For you remember our labor and toil, brethren; we worked night and day, that we might not burden any of you, while we preached to you the gospel of God.
130210 You are witnesses, and God also, how holy and righteous and blameless was our behavior to you believers;
130211 for you know how, like a father with his children, we exhorted each one of you and encouraged you and charged you
130212 to lead a life worthy of God, who calls you into his own kingdom and glory.
130213 And we also thank God constantly for this, that when you received the word of God which you heard from us, you accepted it not as the word of men but as what it really is, the word of God, which is at work in you believers.
130214 For you, brethren, became imitators of the churches of God in Christ Jesus which are in Judea; for you suffered the same things from your own countrymen as they did from the Jews,
130215 who killed both the Lord Jesus and the prophets, and drove us out, and displease God and oppose all men
130216 by hindering us from speaking to the Gentiles that they may be saved -- so as always to fill up the measure of their sins. But God's wrath has come upon them at last!
130217 But since we were bereft of you, brethren, for a short time, in person not in heart, we endeavored the more eagerly and with great desire to see you face to face;
130218 because we wanted to come to you -- I, Paul, again and again -- but Satan hindered us.
130219 For what is our hope or joy or crown of boasting before our Lord Jesus at his coming? Is it not you?
130220 For you are our glory and joy.
130301 Therefore when we could bear it no longer, we were willing to be left behind at Athens alone,
130302 and we sent Timothy, our brother and God's servant in the gospel of Christ, to establish you in your faith and to exhort you,
130303 that no one be moved by these afflictions. You yourselves know that this is to be our lot.
130304 For when we were with you, we told you beforehand that we were to suffer affliction; just as it has come to pass, and as you know.
130305 For this reason, when I could bear it no longer, I sent that I might know your faith, for fear that somehow the tempter had tempted you and that our labor would be in vain.
130306 But now that Timothy has come to us from you, and has brought us the good news of your faith and love and reported that you always remember us kindly and long to see us, as we long to see you --
130307 for this reason, brethren, in all our distress and affliction we have been comforted about you through your faith;
130308 for now we live, if you stand fast in the Lord.
130309 For what thanksgiving can we render to God for you, for all the joy which we feel for your sake before our God,
130310 praying earnestly night and day that we may see you face to face and supply what is lacking in your faith?
130311 Now may our God and Father himself, and our Lord Jesus, direct our way to you;
130312 and may the Lord make you increase and abound in love to one another and to all men, as we do to you,
130313 so that he may establish your hearts unblamable in holiness before our God and Father, at the coming of our Lord Jesus with all his saints.
130401 Finally, brethren, we beseech and exhort you in the Lord Jesus, that as you learned from us how you ought to live and to please God, just as you are doing, you do so more and more.
130402 For you know what instructions we gave you through the Lord Jesus.
130403 For this is the will of God, your sanctification: that you abstain from unchastity;
130404 that each one of you know how to take a wife for himself in holiness and honor,
130405 not in the passion of lust like heathen who do not know God;
130406 that no man transgress, and wrong his brother in this matter, because the Lord is an avenger in all these things, as we solemnly forewarned you.
130407 For God has not called us for uncleanness, but in holiness.
130408 Therefore whoever disregards this, disregards not man but God, who gives his Holy Spirit to you.
130409 But concerning love of the brethren you have no need to have any one write to you, for you yourselves have been taught by God to love one another;
130410 and indeed you do love all the brethren throughout Macedo'nia. But we exhort you, brethren, to do so more and more,
130411 to aspire to live quietly, to mind your own affairs, and to work with your hands, as we charged you;
130412 so that you may command the respect of outsiders, and be dependent on nobody.
130413 But we would not have you ignorant, brethren, concerning those who are asleep, that you may not grieve as others do who have no hope.
130414 For since we believe that Jesus died and rose again, even so, through Jesus, God will bring with him those who have fallen asleep.
130415 For this we declare to you by the word of the Lord, that we who are alive, who are left until the coming of the Lord, shall not precede those who have fallen asleep.
130416 For the Lord himself will descend from heaven with a cry of command, with the archangel's call, and with the sound of the trumpet of God. And the dead in Christ will rise first;
130417 then we who are alive, who are left, shall be caught up together with them in the clouds to meet the Lord in the air; and so we shall always be with the Lord.
130418 Therefore comfort one another with these words.
130501 But as to the times and the seasons, brethren, you have no need to have anything written to you.
130502 For you yourselves know well that the day of the Lord will come like a thief in the night.
130503 When people say, "There is peace and security," then sudden destruction will come upon them as travail comes upon a woman with child, and there will be no escape.
130504 But you are not in darkness, brethren, for that day to surprise you like a thief.
130505 For you are all sons of light and sons of the day; we are not of the night or of darkness.
130506 So then let us not sleep, as others do, but let us keep awake and be sober.
130507 For those who sleep sleep at night, and those who get drunk are drunk at night.
130508 But, since we belong to the day, let us be sober, and put on the breastplate of faith and love, and for a helmet the hope of salvation.
130509 For God has not destined us for wrath, but to obtain salvation through our Lord Jesus Christ,
130510 who died for us so that whether we wake or sleep we might live with him.
130511 Therefore encourage one another and build one another up, just as you are doing.
130512 But we beseech you, brethren, to respect those who labor among you and are over you in the Lord and admonish you,
130513 and to esteem them very highly in love because of their work. Be at peace among yourselves.
130514 And we exhort you, brethren, admonish the idlers, encourage the fainthearted, help the weak, be patient with them all.
130515 See that none of you repays evil for evil, but always seek to do good to one another and to all.
130516 Rejoice always,
130517 pray constantly,
130518 give thanks in all circumstances; for this is the will of God in Christ Jesus for you.
130519 Do not quench the Spirit,
130520 do not despise prophesying,
130521 but test everything; hold fast what is good,
130522 abstain from every form of evil.
130523 May the God of peace himself sanctify you wholly; and may your spirit and soul and body be kept sound and blameless at the coming of our Lord Jesus Christ.
130524 He who calls you is faithful, and he will do it.
130525 Brethren, pray for us.
130526 Greet all the brethren with a holy kiss.
130527 I adjure you by the Lord that this letter be read to all the brethren.
130528 The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with you.
140101 Paul, Silva'nus, and Timothy, To the church of the Thessalo'nians in God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ:
140102 Grace to you and peace from God the Father and the Lord Jesus Christ.
140103 We are bound to give thanks to God always for you, brethren, as is fitting, because your faith is growing abundantly, and the love of every one of you for one another is increasing.
140104 Therefore we ourselves boast of you in the churches of God for your steadfastness and faith in all your persecutions and in the afflictions which you are enduring.
140105 This is evidence of the righteous judgment of God, that you may be made worthy of the kingdom of God, for which you are suffering --
140106 since indeed God deems it just to repay with affliction those who afflict you,
140107 and to grant rest with us to you who are afflicted, when the Lord Jesus is revealed from heaven with his mighty angels in flaming fire,
140108 inflicting vengeance upon those who do not know God and upon those who do not obey the gospel of our Lord Jesus.
140109 They shall suffer the punishment of eternal destruction and exclusion from the presence of the Lord and from the glory of his might,
140110 when he comes on that day to be glorified in his saints, and to be marveled at in all who have believed, because our testimony to you was believed.
140111 To this end we always pray for you, that our God may make you worthy of his call, and may fulfil every good resolve and work of faith by his power,
140112 so that the name of our Lord Jesus may be glorified in you, and you in him, according to the grace of our God and the Lord Jesus Christ.
140201 Now concerning the coming of our Lord Jesus Christ and our assembling to meet him, we beg you, brethren,
140202 not to be quickly shaken in mind or excited, either by spirit or by word, or by letter purporting to be from us, to the effect that the day of the Lord has come.
140203 Let no one deceive you in any way; for that day will not come, unless the rebellion comes first, and the man of lawlessness is revealed, the son of perdition,
140204 who opposes and exalts himself against every so-called god or object of worship, so that he takes his seat in the temple of God, proclaiming himself to be God.
140205 Do you not remember that when I was still with you I told you this?
140206 And you know what is restraining him now so that he may be revealed in his time.
140207 For the mystery of lawlessness is already at work; only he who now restrains it will do so until he is out of the way.
140208 And then the lawless one will be revealed, and the Lord Jesus will slay him with the breath of his mouth and destroy him by his appearing and his coming.
140209 The coming of the lawless one by the activity of Satan will be with all power and with pretended signs and wonders,
140210 and with all wicked deception for those who are to perish, because they refused to love the truth and so be saved.
140211 Therefore God sends upon them a strong delusion, to make them believe what is false,
140212 so that all may be condemned who did not believe the truth but had pleasure in unrighteousness.
140213 But we are bound to give thanks to God always for you, brethren beloved by the Lord, because God chose you from the beginning to be saved, through sanctification by the Spirit and belief in the truth.
140214 To this he called you through our gospel, so that you may obtain the glory of our Lord Jesus Christ.
140215 So then, brethren, stand firm and hold to the traditions which you were taught by us, either by word of mouth or by letter.
140216 Now may our Lord Jesus Christ himself, and God our Father, who loved us and gave us eternal comfort and good hope through grace,
140217 comfort your hearts and establish them in every good work and word.
140301 Finally, brethren, pray for us, that the word of the Lord may speed on and triumph, as it did among you,
140302 and that we may be delivered from wicked and evil men; for not all have faith.
140303 But the Lord is faithful; he will strengthen you and guard you from evil.
140304 And we have confidence in the Lord about you, that you are doing and will do the things which we command.
140305 May the Lord direct your hearts to the love of God and to the steadfastness of Christ.
140306 Now we command you, brethren, in the name of our Lord Jesus Christ, that you keep away from any brother who is living in idleness and not in accord with the tradition that you received from us.
140307 For you yourselves know how you ought to imitate us; we were not idle when we were with you,
140308 we did not eat any one's bread without paying, but with toil and labor we worked night and day, that we might not burden any of you.
140309 It was not because we have not that right, but to give you in our conduct an example to imitate.
140310 For even when we were with you, we gave you this command: If any one will not work, let him not eat.
140311 For we hear that some of you are living in idleness, mere busybodies, not doing any work.
140312 Now such persons we command and exhort in the Lord Jesus Christ to do their work in quietness and to earn their own living.
140313 Brethren, do not be weary in well-doing.
140314 If any one refuses to obey what we say in this letter, note that man, and have nothing to do with him, that he may be ashamed.
140315 Do not look on him as an enemy, but warn him as a brother.
140316 Now may the Lord of peace himself give you peace at all times in all ways. The Lord be with you all.
140317 I, Paul, write this greeting with my own hand. This is the mark in every letter of mine; it is the way I write.
140318 The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with you all.
150101 Paul, an apostle of Christ Jesus by command of God our Savior and of Christ Jesus our hope,
150102 To Timothy, my true child in the faith: Grace, mercy, and peace from God the Father and Christ Jesus our Lord.
150103 As I urged you when I was going to Macedonia, remain at Ephesus that you may charge certain persons not to teach any different doctrine,
150104 nor to occupy themselves with myths and endless genealogies which promote speculations rather than the divine training that is in faith;
150105 whereas the aim of our charge is love that issues from a pure heart and a good conscience and sincere faith.
150106 Certain persons by swerving from these have wandered away into vain discussion,
150107 desiring to be teachers of the law, without understanding either what they are saying or the things about which they make assertions.
150108 Now we know that the law is good, if any one uses it lawfully,
150109 understanding this, that the law is not laid down for the just but for the lawless and disobedient, for the ungodly and sinners, for the unholy and profane, for murderers of fathers and murderers of mothers, for manslayers,
150110 immoral persons, sodomites, kidnapers, liars, perjurers, and whatever else is contrary to sound doctrine,
150111 in accordance with the glorious gospel of the blessed God with which I have been entrusted.
150112 I thank him who has given me strength for this, Christ Jesus our Lord, because he judged me faithful by appointing me to his service,
150113 though I formerly blasphemed and persecuted and insulted him; but I received mercy because I had acted ignorantly in unbelief,
150114 and the grace of our Lord overflowed for me with the faith and love that are in Christ Jesus.
150115 The saying is sure and worthy of full acceptance, that Christ Jesus came into the world to save sinners. And I am the foremost of sinners;
150116 but I received mercy for this reason, that in me, as the foremost, Jesus Christ might display his perfect patience for an example to those who were to believe in him for eternal life.
150117 To the King of ages, immortal, invisible, the only God, be honor and glory for ever and ever. Amen.
150118 This charge I commit to you, Timothy, my son, in accordance with the prophetic utterances which pointed to you, that inspired by them you may wage the good warfare,
150119 holding faith and a good conscience. By rejecting conscience, certain persons have made shipwreck of their faith,
150120 among them Hymenae'us and Alexander, whom I have delivered to Satan that they may learn not to blaspheme.
150201 First of all, then, I urge that supplications, prayers, intercessions, and thanksgivings be made for all men,
150202 for kings and all who are in high positions, that we may lead a quiet and peaceable life, godly and respectful in every way.
150203 This is good, and it is acceptable in the sight of God our Savior,
150204 who desires all men to be saved and to come to the knowledge of the truth.
150205 For there is one God, and there is one mediator between God and men, the man Christ Jesus,
150206 who gave himself as a ransom for all, the testimony to which was borne at the proper time.
150207 For this I was appointed a preacher and apostle (I am telling the truth, I am not lying), a teacher of the Gentiles in faith and truth.
150208 I desire then that in every place the men should pray, lifting holy hands without anger or quarreling;
150209 also that women should adorn themselves modestly and sensibly in seemly apparel, not with braided hair or gold or pearls or costly attire
150210 but by good deeds, as befits women who profess religion.
150211 Let a woman learn in silence with all submissiveness.
150212 I permit no woman to teach or to have authority over men; she is to keep silent.
150213 For Adam was formed first, then Eve;
150214 and Adam was not deceived, but the woman was deceived and became a transgressor.
150215 Yet woman will be saved through bearing children, if she continues in faith and love and holiness, with modesty.
150301 The saying is sure: If any one aspires to the office of bishop, he desires a noble task.
150302 Now a bishop must be above reproach, the husband of one wife, temperate, sensible, dignified, hospitable, an apt teacher,
150303 no drunkard, not violent but gentle, not quarrelsome, and no lover of money.
150304 He must manage his own household well, keeping his children submissive and respectful in every way;
150305 for if a man does not know how to manage his own household, how can he care for God's church?
150306 He must not be a recent convert, or he may be puffed up with conceit and fall into the condemnation of the devil;
150307 moreover he must be well thought of by outsiders, or he may fall into reproach and the snare of the devil.
150308 Deacons likewise must be serious, not double-tongued, not addicted to much wine, not greedy for gain;
150309 they must hold the mystery of the faith with a clear conscience.
150310 And let them also be tested first; then if they prove themselves blameless let them serve as deacons.
150311 The women likewise must be serious, no slanderers, but temperate, faithful in all things.
150312 Let deacons be the husband of one wife, and let them manage their children and their households well;
150313 for those who serve well as deacons gain a good standing for themselves and also great confidence in the faith which is in Christ Jesus.
150314 I hope to come to you soon, but I am writing these instructions to you so that,
150315 if I am delayed, you may know how one ought to behave in the household of God, which is the church of the living God, the pillar and bulwark of the truth.
150316 Great indeed, we confess, is the mystery of our religion: He was manifested in the flesh, vindicated in the Spirit, seen by angels, preached among the nations, believed on in the world, taken up in glory.
150401 Now the Spirit expressly says that in later times some will depart from the faith by giving heed to deceitful spirits and doctrines of demons,
150402 through the pretensions of liars whose consciences are seared,
150403 who forbid marriage and enjoin abstinence from foods which God created to be received with thanksgiving by those who believe and know the truth.
150404 For everything created by God is good, and nothing is to be rejected if it is received with thanksgiving;
150405 for then it is consecrated by the word of God and prayer.
150406 If you put these instructions before the brethren, you will be a good minister of Christ Jesus, nourished on the words of the faith and of the good doctrine which you have followed.
150407 Have nothing to do with godless and silly myths. Train yourself in godliness;
150408 for while bodily training is of some value, godliness is of value in every way, as it holds promise for the present life and also for the life to come.
150409 The saying is sure and worthy of full acceptance.
150410 For to this end we toil and strive, because we have our hope set on the living God, who is the Savior of all men, especially of those who believe.
150411 Command and teach these things.
150412 Let no one despise your youth, but set the believers an example in speech and conduct, in love, in faith, in purity.
150413 Till I come, attend to the public reading of scripture, to preaching, to teaching.
150414 Do not neglect the gift you have, which was given you by prophetic utterance when the council of elders laid their hands upon you.
150415 Practice these duties, devote yourself to them, so that all may see your progress.
150416 Take heed to yourself and to your teaching; hold to that, for by so doing you will save both yourself and your hearers.
150501 Do not rebuke an older man but exhort him as you would a father; treat younger men like brothers,
150502 older women like mothers, younger women like sisters, in all purity.
150503 Honor widows who are real widows.
150504 If a widow has children or grandchildren, let them first learn their religious duty to their own family and make some return to their parents; for this is acceptable in the sight of God.
150505 She who is a real widow, and is left all alone, has set her hope on God and continues in supplications and prayers night and day;
150506 whereas she who is self-indulgent is dead even while she lives.
150507 Command this, so that they may be without reproach.
150508 If any one does not provide for his relatives, and especially for his own family, he has disowned the faith and is worse than an unbeliever.
150509 Let a widow be enrolled if she is not less than sixty years of age, having been the wife of one husband;
150510 and she must be well attested for her good deeds, as one who has brought up children, shown hospitality, washed the feet of the saints, relieved the afflicted, and devoted herself to doing good in every way.
150511 But refuse to enrol younger widows; for when they grow wanton against Christ they desire to marry,
150512 and so they incur condemnation for having violated their first pledge.
150513 Besides that, they learn to be idlers, gadding about from house to house, and not only idlers but gossips and busybodies, saying what they should not.
150514 So I would have younger widows marry, bear children, rule their households, and give the enemy no occasion to revile us.
150515 For some have already strayed after Satan.
150516 If any believing woman has relatives who are widows, let her assist them; let the church not be burdened, so that it may assist those who are real widows.
150517 Let the elders who rule well be considered worthy of double honor, especially those who labor in preaching and teaching;
150518 for the scripture says, "You shall not muzzle an ox when it is treading out the grain," and, "The laborer deserves his wages."
150519 Never admit any charge against an elder except on the evidence of two or three witnesses.
150520 As for those who persist in sin, rebuke them in the presence of all, so that the rest may stand in fear.
150521 In the presence of God and of Christ Jesus and of the elect angels I charge you to keep these rules without favor, doing nothing from partiality.
150522 Do not be hasty in the laying on of hands, nor participate in another man's sins; keep yourself pure.
150523 No longer drink only water, but use a little wine for the sake of your stomach and your frequent ailments.
150524 The sins of some men are conspicuous, pointing to judgment, but the sins of others appear later.
150525 So also good deeds are conspicuous; and even when they are not, they cannot remain hidden.
150601 Let all who are under the yoke of slavery regard their masters as worthy of all honor, so that the name of God and the teaching may not be defamed.
150602 Those who have believing masters must not be disrespectful on the ground that they are brethren; rather they must serve all the better since those who benefit by their service are believers and beloved. Teach and urge these duties.
150603 If any one teaches otherwise and does not agree with the sound words of our Lord Jesus Christ and the teaching which accords with godliness,
150604 he is puffed up with conceit, he knows nothing; he has a morbid craving for controversy and for disputes about words, which produce envy, dissension, slander, base suspicions,
150605 and wrangling among men who are depraved in mind and bereft of the truth, imagining that godliness is a means of gain.
150606 There is great gain in godliness with contentment;
150607 for we brought nothing into the world, and we cannot take anything out of the world;
150608 but if we have food and clothing, with these we shall be content.
150609 But those who desire to be rich fall into temptation, into a snare, into many senseless and hurtful desires that plunge men into ruin and destruction.
150610 For the love of money is the root of all evils; it is through this craving that some have wandered away from the faith and pierced their hearts with many pangs.
150611 But as for you, man of God, shun all this; aim at righteousness, godliness, faith, love, steadfastness, gentleness.
150612 Fight the good fight of the faith; take hold of the eternal life to which you were called when you made the good confession in the presence of many witnesses.
150613 In the presence of God who gives life to all things, and of Christ Jesus who in his testimony before Pontius Pilate made the good confession,
150614 I charge you to keep the commandment unstained and free from reproach until the appearing of our Lord Jesus Christ;
150615 and this will be made manifest at the proper time by the blessed and only Sovereign, the King of kings and Lord of lords,
150616 who alone has immortality and dwells in unapproachable light, whom no man has ever seen or can see. To him be honor and eternal dominion. Amen.
150617 As for the rich in this world, charge them not to be haughty, nor to set their hopes on uncertain riches but on God who richly furnishes us with everything to enjoy.
150618 They are to do good, to be rich in good deeds, liberal and generous,
150619 thus laying up for themselves a good foundation for the future, so that they may take hold of the life which is life indeed.
150620 O Timothy, guard what has been entrusted to you. Avoid the godless chatter and contradictions of what is falsely called knowledge,
150621 for by professing it some have missed the mark as regards the faith. Grace be with you.
160101 Paul, an apostle of Christ Jesus by the will of God according to the promise of the life which is in Christ Jesus,
160102 To Timothy, my beloved child: Grace, mercy, and peace from God the Father and Christ Jesus our Lord.
160103 I thank God whom I serve with a clear conscience, as did my fathers, when I remember you constantly in my prayers.
160104 As I remember your tears, I long night and day to see you, that I may be filled with joy.
160105 I am reminded of your sincere faith, a faith that dwelt first in your grandmother Lo'is and your mother Eunice and now, I am sure, dwells in you.
160106 Hence I remind you to rekindle the gift of God that is within you through the laying on of my hands;
160107 for God did not give us a spirit of timidity but a spirit of power and love and self-control.
160108 Do not be ashamed then of testifying to our Lord, nor of me his prisoner, but share in suffering for the gospel in the power of God,
160109 who saved us and called us with a holy calling, not in virtue of our works but in virtue of his own purpose and the grace which he gave us in Christ Jesus ages ago,
160110 and now has manifested through the appearing of our Savior Christ Jesus, who abolished death and brought life and immortality to light through the gospel.
160111 For this gospel I was appointed a preacher and apostle and teacher,
160112 and therefore I suffer as I do. But I am not ashamed, for I know whom I have believed, and I am sure that he is able to guard until that Day what has been entrusted to me.
160113 Follow the pattern of the sound words which you have heard from me, in the faith and love which are in Christ Jesus;
160114 guard the truth that has been entrusted to you by the Holy Spirit who dwells within us.
160115 You are aware that all who are in Asia turned away from me, and among them Phy'gelus and Hermog'enes.
160116 May the Lord grant mercy to the household of Onesiph'orus, for he often refreshed me; he was not ashamed of my chains,
160117 but when he arrived in Rome he searched for me eagerly and found me --
160118 may the Lord grant him to find mercy from the Lord on that Day -- and you well know all the service he rendered at Ephesus.
160201 You then, my son, be strong in the grace that is in Christ Jesus,
160202 and what you have heard from me before many witnesses entrust to faithful men who will be able to teach others also.
160203 Share in suffering as a good soldier of Christ Jesus.
160204 No soldier on service gets entangled in civilian pursuits, since his aim is to satisfy the one who enlisted him.
160205 An athlete is not crowned unless he competes according to the rules.
160206 It is the hard-working farmer who ought to have the first share of the crops.
160207 Think over what I say, for the Lord will grant you understanding in everything.
160208 Remember Jesus Christ, risen from the dead, descended from David, as preached in my gospel,
160209 the gospel for which I am suffering and wearing fetters like a criminal. But the word of God is not fettered.
160210 Therefore I endure everything for the sake of the elect, that they also may obtain salvation in Christ Jesus with its eternal glory.
160211 The saying is sure: If we have died with him, we shall also live with him;
160212 if we endure, we shall also reign with him; if we deny him, he also will deny us;
160213 if we are faithless, he remains faithful -- for he cannot deny himself.
160214 Remind them of this, and charge them before the Lord to avoid disputing about words, which does no good, but only ruins the hearers.
160215 Do your best to present yourself to God as one approved, a workman who has no need to be ashamed, rightly handling the word of truth.
160216 Avoid such godless chatter, for it will lead people into more and more ungodliness,
160217 and their talk will eat its way like gangrene. Among them are Hymenae'us and Phile'tus,
160218 who have swerved from the truth by holding that the resurrection is past already. They are upsetting the faith of some.
160219 But God's firm foundation stands, bearing this seal: "The Lord knows those who are his," and, "Let every one who names the name of the Lord depart from iniquity."
160220 In a great house there are not only vessels of gold and silver but also of wood and earthenware, and some for noble use, some for ignoble.
160221 If any one purifies himself from what is ignoble, then he will be a vessel for noble use, consecrated and useful to the master of the house, ready for any good work.
160222 So shun youthful passions and aim at righteousness, faith, love, and peace, along with those who call upon the Lord from a pure heart.
160223 Have nothing to do with stupid, senseless controversies; you know that they breed quarrels.
160224 And the Lord's servant must not be quarrelsome but kindly to every one, an apt teacher, forbearing,
160225 correcting his opponents with gentleness. God may perhaps grant that they will repent and come to know the truth,
160226 and they may escape from the snare of the devil, after being captured by him to do his will.
160301 But understand this, that in the last days there will come times of stress.
160302 For men will be lovers of self, lovers of money, proud, arrogant, abusive, disobedient to their parents, ungrateful, unholy,
160303 inhuman, implacable, slanderers, profligates, fierce, haters of good,
160304 treacherous, reckless, swollen with conceit, lovers of pleasure rather than lovers of God,
160305 holding the form of religion but denying the power of it. Avoid such people.
160306 For among them are those who make their way into households and capture weak women, burdened with sins and swayed by various impulses,
160307 who will listen to anybody and can never arrive at a knowledge of the truth.
160308 As Jannes and Jambres opposed Moses, so these men also oppose the truth, men of corrupt mind and counterfeit faith;
160309 but they will not get very far, for their folly will be plain to all, as was that of those two men.
160310 Now you have observed my teaching, my conduct, my aim in life, my faith, my patience, my love, my steadfastness,
160311 my persecutions, my sufferings, what befell me at Antioch, at Ico'nium, and at Lystra, what persecutions I endured; yet from them all the Lord rescued me.
160312 Indeed all who desire to live a godly life in Christ Jesus will be persecuted,
160313 while evil men and impostors will go on from bad to worse, deceivers and deceived.
160314 But as for you, continue in what you have learned and have firmly believed, knowing from whom you learned it
160315 and how from childhood you have been acquainted with the sacred writings which are able to instruct you for salvation through faith in Christ Jesus.
160316 All scripture is inspired by God and profitable for teaching, for reproof, for correction, and for training in righteousness,
160317 that the man of God may be complete, equipped for every good work.
160401 I charge you in the presence of God and of Christ Jesus who is to judge the living and the dead, and by his appearing and his kingdom:
160402 preach the word, be urgent in season and out of season, convince, rebuke, and exhort, be unfailing in patience and in teaching.
160403 For the time is coming when people will not endure sound teaching, but having itching ears they will accumulate for themselves teachers to suit their own likings,
160404 and will turn away from listening to the truth and wander into myths.
160405 As for you, always be steady, endure suffering, do the work of an evangelist, fulfil your ministry.
160406 For I am already on the point of being sacrificed; the time of my departure has come.
160407 I have fought the good fight, I have finished the race, I have kept the faith.
160408 Henceforth there is laid up for me the crown of righteousness, which the Lord, the righteous judge, will award to me on that Day, and not only to me but also to all who have loved his appearing.
160409 Do your best to come to me soon.
160410 For Demas, in love with this present world, has deserted me and gone to Thessaloni'ca; Crescens has gone to Galatia, Titus to Dalmatia.
160411 Luke alone is with me. Get Mark and bring him with you; for he is very useful in serving me.
160412 Tych'icus I have sent to Ephesus.
160413 When you come, bring the cloak that I left with Carpus at Tro'as, also the books, and above all the parchments.
160414 Alexander the coppersmith did me great harm; the Lord will requite him for his deeds.
160415 Beware of him yourself, for he strongly opposed our message.
160416 At my first defense no one took my part; all deserted me. May it not be charged against them!
160417 But the Lord stood by me and gave me strength to proclaim the message fully, that all the Gentiles might hear it. So I was rescued from the lion's mouth.
160418 The Lord will rescue me from every evil and save me for his heavenly kingdom. To him be the glory for ever and ever. Amen.
160419 Greet Prisca and Aq'uila, and the household of Onesiph'orus.
160420 Eras'tus remained at Corinth; Troph'imus I left ill at Mile'tus.
160421 Do your best to come before winter. Eubu'lus sends greetings to you, as do Pudens and Linus and Claudia and all the brethren.
160422 The Lord be with your spirit. Grace be with you.
170101 Paul, a servant of God and an apostle of Jesus Christ, to further the faith of God's elect and their knowledge of the truth which accords with godliness,
170102 in hope of eternal life which God, who never lies, promised ages ago
170103 and at the proper time manifested in his word through the preaching with which I have been entrusted by command of God our Savior;
170104 To Titus, my true child in a common faith: Grace and peace from God the Father and Christ Jesus our Savior.
170105 This is why I left you in Crete, that you might amend what was defective, and appoint elders in every town as I directed you,
170106 if any man is blameless, the husband of one wife, and his children are believers and not open to the charge of being profligate or insubordinate.
170107 For a bishop, as God's steward, must be blameless; he must not be arrogant or quick-tempered or a drunkard or violent or greedy for gain,
170108 but hospitable, a lover of goodness, master of himself, upright, holy, and self-controlled;
170109 he must hold firm to the sure word as taught, so that he may be able to give instruction in sound doctrine and also to confute those who contradict it.
170110 For there are many insubordinate men, empty talkers and deceivers, especially the circumcision party;
170111 they must be silenced, since they are upsetting whole families by teaching for base gain what they have no right to teach.
170112 One of themselves, a prophet of their own, said, "Cretans are always liars, evil beasts, lazy gluttons."
170113 This testimony is true. Therefore rebuke them sharply, that they may be sound in the faith,
170114 instead of giving heed to Jewish myths or to commands of men who reject the truth.
170115 To the pure all things are pure, but to the corrupt and unbelieving nothing is pure; their very minds and consciences are corrupted.
170116 They profess to know God, but they deny him by their deeds; they are detestable, disobedient, unfit for any good deed.
170201 But as for you, teach what befits sound doctrine.
170202 Bid the older men be temperate, serious, sensible, sound in faith, in love, and in steadfastness.
170203 Bid the older women likewise to be reverent in behavior, not to be slanderers or slaves to drink; they are to teach what is good,
170204 and so train the young women to love their husbands and children,
170205 to be sensible, chaste, domestic, kind, and submissive to their husbands, that the word of God may not be discredited.
170206 Likewise urge the younger men to control themselves.
170207 Show yourself in all respects a model of good deeds, and in your teaching show integrity, gravity,
170208 and sound speech that cannot be censured, so that an opponent may be put to shame, having nothing evil to say of us.
170209 Bid slaves to be submissive to their masters and to give satisfaction in every respect; they are not to be refractory,
170210 nor to pilfer, but to show entire and true fidelity, so that in everything they may adorn the doctrine of God our Savior.
170211 For the grace of God has appeared for the salvation of all men,
170212 training us to renounce irreligion and worldly passions, and to live sober, upright, and godly lives in this world,
170213 awaiting our blessed hope, the appearing of the glory of our great God and Savior Jesus Christ,
170214 who gave himself for us to redeem us from all iniquity and to purify for himself a people of his own who are zealous for good deeds.
170215 Declare these things; exhort and reprove with all authority. Let no one disregard you.
170301 Remind them to be submissive to rulers and authorities, to be obedient, to be ready for any honest work,
170302 to speak evil of no one, to avoid quarreling, to be gentle, and to show perfect courtesy toward all men.
170303 For we ourselves were once foolish, disobedient, led astray, slaves to various passions and pleasures, passing our days in malice and envy, hated by men and hating one another;
170304 but when the goodness and loving kindness of God our Savior appeared,
170305 he saved us, not because of deeds done by us in righteousness, but in virtue of his own mercy, by the washing of regeneration and renewal in the Holy Spirit,
170306 which he poured out upon us richly through Jesus Christ our Savior,
170307 so that we might be justified by his grace and become heirs in hope of eternal life.
170308 The saying is sure. I desire you to insist on these things, so that those who have believed in God may be careful to apply themselves to good deeds; these are excellent and profitable to men.
170309 But avoid stupid controversies, genealogies, dissensions, and quarrels over the law, for they are unprofitable and futile.
170310 As for a man who is factious, after admonishing him once or twice, have nothing more to do with him,
170311 knowing that such a person is perverted and sinful; he is self-condemned.
170312 When I send Artemas or Tych'icus to you, do your best to come to me at Nicop'olis, for I have decided to spend the winter there.
170313 Do your best to speed Zenas the lawyer and Apol'los on their way; see that they lack nothing.
170314 And let our people learn to apply themselves to good deeds, so as to help cases of urgent need, and not to be unfruitful.
170315 All who are with me send greetings to you. Greet those who love us in the faith. Grace be with you all.
180101 Paul, a prisoner of Christ Jesus, and Timothy our brother, to Philemon our beloved and fellow worker,
180102 and Ap'phia our sister and Archip'pus our fellow soldier, and the church in your house:
180103 Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ.
180104 I thank my God always when I remember you in my prayers,
180105 because I hear of your love and of the faith which you have toward the Lord Jesus and all the saints,
180106 and I pray that the sharing of your faith may promote the knowledge of all the good that is ours in Christ.
180107 For I have derived much joy and comfort from your love, my brother, because the hearts of the saints have been refreshed through you.
180108 Accordingly, though I am bold enough in Christ to command you to do what is required,
180109 yet for love's sake I prefer to appeal to you -- I, Paul, an ambassador and now a prisoner also for Christ Jesus --
