180110 I appeal to you for my child, Ones'imus, whose father I have become in my imprisonment.
180111 (Formerly he was useless to you, but now he is indeed useful to you and to me.)
180112 I am sending him back to you, sending my very heart.
180113 I would have been glad to keep him with me, in order that he might serve me on your behalf during my imprisonment for the gospel;
180114 but I preferred to do nothing without your consent in order that your goodness might not be by compulsion but of your own free will.
180115 Perhaps this is why he was parted from you for a while, that you might have him back for ever,
180116 no longer as a slave but more than a slave, as a beloved brother, especially to me but how much more to you, both in the flesh and in the Lord.
180117 So if you consider me your partner, receive him as you would receive me.
180118 If he has wronged you at all, or owes you anything, charge that to my account.
180119 I, Paul, write this with my own hand, I will repay it -- to say nothing of your owing me even your own self.
180120 Yes, brother, I want some benefit from you in the Lord. Refresh my heart in Christ.
180121 Confident of your obedience, I write to you, knowing that you will do even more than I say.
180122 At the same time, prepare a guest room for me, for I am hoping through your prayers to be granted to you.
180123 Ep'aphras, my fellow prisoner in Christ Jesus, sends greetings to you,
180124 and so do Mark, Aristar'chus, Demas, and Luke, my fellow workers.
180125 The grace of the Lord Jesus Christ be with your spirit.
190101 In many and various ways God spoke of old to our fathers by the prophets;
190102 but in these last days he has spoken to us by a Son, whom he appointed the heir of all things, through whom also he created the world.
190103 He reflects the glory of God and bears the very stamp of his nature, upholding the universe by his word of power. When he had made purification for sins, he sat down at the right hand of the Majesty on high,
190104 having become as much superior to angels as the name he has obtained is more excellent than theirs.
190105 For to what angel did God ever say, "Thou art my Son, today I have begotten thee"? Or again, "I will be to him a father, and he shall be to me a son"?
190106 And again, when he brings the first-born into the world, he says, "Let all God's angels worship him."
190107 Of the angels he says, "Who makes his angels winds, and his servants flames of fire."
190108 But of the Son he says, "Thy throne, O God, is for ever and ever, the righteous scepter is the scepter of thy kingdom.
190109 Thou hast loved righteousness and hated lawlessness; therefore God, thy God, has anointed thee with the oil of gladness beyond thy comrades."
190110 And, "Thou, Lord, didst found the earth in the beginning, and the heavens are the work of thy hands;
190111 they will perish, but thou remainest; they will all grow old like a garment,
190112 like a mantle thou wilt roll them up, and they will be changed. But thou art the same, and thy years will never end."
190113 But to what angel has he ever said, "Sit at my right hand, till I make thy enemies a stool for thy feet"?
190114 Are they not all ministering spirits sent forth to serve, for the sake of those who are to obtain salvation?
190201 Therefore we must pay the closer attention to what we have heard, lest we drift away from it.
190202 For if the message declared by angels was valid and every transgression or disobedience received a just retribution,
190203 how shall we escape if we neglect such a great salvation? It was declared at first by the Lord, and it was attested to us by those who heard him,
190204 while God also bore witness by signs and wonders and various miracles and by gifts of the Holy Spirit distributed according to his own will.
190205 For it was not to angels that God subjected the world to come, of which we are speaking.
190206 It has been testified somewhere, "What is man that thou art mindful of him, or the son of man, that thou carest for him?
190207 Thou didst make him for a little while lower than the angels, thou hast crowned him with glory and honor,
190208 putting everything in subjection under his feet." Now in putting everything in subjection to him, he left nothing outside his control. As it is, we do not yet see everything in subjection to him.
190209 But we see Jesus, who for a little while was made lower than the angels, crowned with glory and honor because of the suffering of death, so that by the grace of God he might taste death for every one.
190210 For it was fitting that he, for whom and by whom all things exist, in bringing many sons to glory, should make the pioneer of their salvation perfect through suffering.
190211 For he who sanctifies and those who are sanctified have all one origin. That is why he is not ashamed to call them brethren,
190212 saying, "I will proclaim thy name to my brethren, in the midst of the congregation I will praise thee."
190213 And again, "I will put my trust in him." And again, "Here am I, and the children God has given me."
190214 Since therefore the children share in flesh and blood, he himself likewise partook of the same nature, that through death he might destroy him who has the power of death, that is, the devil,
190215 and deliver all those who through fear of death were subject to lifelong bondage.
190216 For surely it is not with angels that he is concerned but with the descendants of Abraham.
190217 Therefore he had to be made like his brethren in every respect, so that he might become a merciful and faithful high priest in the service of God, to make expiation for the sins of the people.
190218 For because he himself has suffered and been tempted, he is able to help those who are tempted.
190301 Therefore, holy brethren, who share in a heavenly call, consider Jesus, the apostle and high priest of our confession.
190302 He was faithful to him who appointed him, just as Moses also was faithful in God's house.
190303 Yet Jesus has been counted worthy of as much more glory than Moses as the builder of a house has more honor than the house.
190304 (For every house is built by some one, but the builder of all things is God.)
190305 Now Moses was faithful in all God's house as a servant, to testify to the things that were to be spoken later,
190306 but Christ was faithful over God's house as a son. And we are his house if we hold fast our confidence and pride in our hope.
190307 Therefore, as the Holy Spirit says, "Today, when you hear his voice,
190308 do not harden your hearts as in the rebellion, on the day of testing in the wilderness,
190309 where your fathers put me to the test and saw my works for forty years.
190310 Therefore I was provoked with that generation, and said, 'They always go astray in their hearts; they have not known my ways.'
190311 As I swore in my wrath, 'They shall never enter my rest.'"
190312 Take care, brethren, lest there be in any of you an evil, unbelieving heart, leading you to fall away from the living God.
190313 But exhort one another every day, as long as it is called "today," that none of you may be hardened by the deceitfulness of sin.
190314 For we share in Christ, if only we hold our first confidence firm to the end,
190315 while it is said, "Today, when you hear his voice, do not harden your hearts as in the rebellion."
190316 Who were they that heard and yet were rebellious? Was it not all those who left Egypt under the leadership of Moses?
190317 And with whom was he provoked forty years? Was it not with those who sinned, whose bodies fell in the wilderness?
190318 And to whom did he swear that they should never enter his rest, but to those who were disobedient?
190319 So we see that they were unable to enter because of unbelief.
190401 Therefore, while the promise of entering his rest remains, let us fear lest any of you be judged to have failed to reach it.
190402 For good news came to us just as to them; but the message which they heard did not benefit them, because it did not meet with faith in the hearers.
190403 For we who have believed enter that rest, as he has said, "As I swore in my wrath, 'They shall never enter my rest,'" although his works were finished from the foundation of the world.
190404 For he has somewhere spoken of the seventh day in this way, "And God rested on the seventh day from all his works."
190405 And again in this place he said, "They shall never enter my rest."
190406 Since therefore it remains for some to enter it, and those who formerly received the good news failed to enter because of disobedience,
190407 again he sets a certain day, "Today," saying through David so long afterward, in the words already quoted, "Today, when you hear his voice, do not harden your hearts."
190408 For if Joshua had given them rest, God would not speak later of another day.
190409 So then, there remains a sabbath rest for the people of God;
190410 for whoever enters God's rest also ceases from his labors as God did from his.
190411 Let us therefore strive to enter that rest, that no one fall by the same sort of disobedience.
190412 For the word of God is living and active, sharper than any two-edged sword, piercing to the division of soul and spirit, of joints and marrow, and discerning the thoughts and intentions of the heart.
190413 And before him no creature is hidden, but all are open and laid bare to the eyes of him with whom we have to do.
190414 Since then we have a great high priest who has passed through the heavens, Jesus, the Son of God, let us hold fast our confession.
190415 For we have not a high priest who is unable to sympathize with our weaknesses, but one who in every respect has been tempted as we are, yet without sin.
190416 Let us then with confidence draw near to the throne of grace, that we may receive mercy and find grace to help in time of need.
190501 For every high priest chosen from among men is appointed to act on behalf of men in relation to God, to offer gifts and sacrifices for sins.
190502 He can deal gently with the ignorant and wayward, since he himself is beset with weakness.
190503 Because of this he is bound to offer sacrifice for his own sins as well as for those of the people.
190504 And one does not take the honor upon himself, but he is called by God, just as Aaron was.
190505 So also Christ did not exalt himself to be made a high priest, but was appointed by him who said to him, "Thou art my Son, today I have begotten thee";
190506 as he says also in another place, "Thou art a priest for ever, after the order of Melchiz'edek."
190507 In the days of his flesh, Jesus offered up prayers and supplications, with loud cries and tears, to him who was able to save him from death, and he was heard for his godly fear.
190508 Although he was a Son, he learned obedience through what he suffered;
190509 and being made perfect he became the source of eternal salvation to all who obey him,
190510 being designated by God a high priest after the order of Melchiz'edek.
190511 About this we have much to say which is hard to explain, since you have become dull of hearing.
190512 For though by this time you ought to be teachers, you need some one to teach you again the first principles of God's word. You need milk, not solid food;
190513 for every one who lives on milk is unskilled in the word of righteousness, for he is a child.
190514 But solid food is for the mature, for those who have their faculties trained by practice to distinguish good from evil.
190601 Therefore let us leave the elementary doctrine of Christ and go on to maturity, not laying again a foundation of repentance from dead works and of faith toward God,
190602 with instruction about ablutions, the laying on of hands, the resurrection of the dead, and eternal judgment.
190603 And this we will do if God permits.
190604 For it is impossible to restore again to repentance those who have once been enlightened, who have tasted the heavenly gift, and have become partakers of the Holy Spirit,
190605 and have tasted the goodness of the word of God and the powers of the age to come,
190606 if they then commit apostasy, since they crucify the Son of God on their own account and hold him up to contempt.
190607 For land which has drunk the rain that often falls upon it, and brings forth vegetation useful to those for whose sake it is cultivated, receives a blessing from God.
190608 But if it bears thorns and thistles, it is worthless and near to being cursed; its end is to be burned.
190609 Though we speak thus, yet in your case, beloved, we feel sure of better things that belong to salvation.
190610 For God is not so unjust as to overlook your work and the love which you showed for his sake in serving the saints, as you still do.
190611 And we desire each one of you to show the same earnestness in realizing the full assurance of hope until the end,
190612 so that you may not be sluggish, but imitators of those who through faith and patience inherit the promises.
190613 For when God made a promise to Abraham, since he had no one greater by whom to swear, he swore by himself,
190614 saying, "Surely I will bless you and multiply you."
190615 And thus Abraham, having patiently endured, obtained the promise.
190616 Men indeed swear by a greater than themselves, and in all their disputes an oath is final for confirmation.
190617 So when God desired to show more convincingly to the heirs of the promise the unchangeable character of his purpose, he interposed with an oath,
190618 so that through two unchangeable things, in which it is impossible that God should prove false, we who have fled for refuge might have strong encouragement to seize the hope set before us.
190619 We have this as a sure and steadfast anchor of the soul, a hope that enters into the inner shrine behind the curtain,
190620 where Jesus has gone as a forerunner on our behalf, having become a high priest for ever after the order of Melchiz'edek.
190701 For this Melchiz'edek, king of Salem, priest of the Most High God, met Abraham returning from the slaughter of the kings and blessed him;
190702 and to him Abraham apportioned a tenth part of everything. He is first, by translation of his name, king of righteousness, and then he is also king of Salem, that is, king of peace.
190703 He is without father or mother or genealogy, and has neither beginning of days nor end of life, but resembling the Son of God he continues a priest for ever.
190704 See how great he is! Abraham the patriarch gave him a tithe of the spoils.
190705 And those descendants of Levi who receive the priestly office have a commandment in the law to take tithes from the people, that is, from their brethren, though these also are descended from Abraham.
190706 But this man who has not their genealogy received tithes from Abraham and blessed him who had the promises.
190707 It is beyond dispute that the inferior is blessed by the superior.
190708 Here tithes are received by mortal men; there, by one of whom it is testified that he lives.
190709 One might even say that Levi himself, who receives tithes, paid tithes through Abraham,
190710 for he was still in the loins of his ancestor when Melchiz'edek met him.
190711 Now if perfection had been attainable through the Levit'ical priesthood (for under it the people received the law), what further need would there have been for another priest to arise after the order of Melchiz'edek, rather than one named after the order of Aaron?
190712 For when there is a change in the priesthood, there is necessarily a change in the law as well.
190713 For the one of whom these things are spoken belonged to another tribe, from which no one has ever served at the altar.
190714 For it is evident that our Lord was descended from Judah, and in connection with that tribe Moses said nothing about priests.
190715 This becomes even more evident when another priest arises in the likeness of Melchiz'edek,
190716 who has become a priest, not according to a legal requirement concerning bodily descent but by the power of an indestructible life.
190717 For it is witnessed of him, "Thou art a priest for ever, after the order of Melchiz'edek."
190718 On the one hand, a former commandment is set aside because of its weakness and uselessness
190719 (for the law made nothing perfect); on the other hand, a better hope is introduced, through which we draw near to God.
190720 And it was not without an oath.
190721 Those who formerly became priests took their office without an oath, but this one was addressed with an oath, "The Lord has sworn and will not change his mind, 'Thou art a priest for ever.'"
190722 This makes Jesus the surety of a better covenant.
190723 The former priests were many in number, because they were prevented by death from continuing in office;
190724 but he holds his priesthood permanently, because he continues for ever.
190725 Consequently he is able for all time to save those who draw near to God through him, since he always lives to make intercession for them.
190726 For it was fitting that we should have such a high priest, holy, blameless, unstained, separated from sinners, exalted above the heavens.
190727 He has no need, like those high priests, to offer sacrifices daily, first for his own sins and then for those of the people; he did this once for all when he offered up himself.
190728 Indeed, the law appoints men in their weakness as high priests, but the word of the oath, which came later than the law, appoints a Son who has been made perfect for ever.
190801 Now the point in what we are saying is this: we have such a high priest, one who is seated at the right hand of the throne of the Majesty in heaven,
190802 a minister in the sanctuary and the true tent which is set up not by man but by the Lord.
190803 For every high priest is appointed to offer gifts and sacrifices; hence it is necessary for this priest also to have something to offer.
190804 Now if he were on earth, he would not be a priest at all, since there are priests who offer gifts according to the law.
190805 They serve a copy and shadow of the heavenly sanctuary; for when Moses was about to erect the tent, he was instructed by God, saying, "See that you make everything according to the pattern which was shown you on the mountain."
190806 But as it is, Christ has obtained a ministry which is as much more excellent than the old as the covenant he mediates is better, since it is enacted on better promises.
190807 For if that first covenant had been faultless, there would have been no occasion for a second.
190808 For he finds fault with them when he says: "The days will come, says the Lord, when I will establish a new covenant with the house of Israel and with the house of Judah;
190809 not like the covenant that I made with their fathers on the day when I took them by the hand to lead them out of the land of Egypt; for they did not continue in my covenant, and so I paid no heed to them, says the Lord.
190810 This is the covenant that I will make with the house of Israel after those days, says the Lord: I will put my laws into their minds, and write them on their hearts, and I will be their God, and they shall be my people.
190811 And they shall not teach every one his fellow or every one his brother, saying, 'Know the Lord,' for all shall know me, from the least of them to the greatest.
190812 For I will be merciful toward their iniquities, and I will remember their sins no more."
190813 In speaking of a new covenant he treats the first as obsolete. And what is becoming obsolete and growing old is ready to vanish away.
190901 Now even the first covenant had regulations for worship and an earthly sanctuary.
190902 For a tent was prepared, the outer one, in which were the lampstand and the table and the bread of the Presence; it is called the Holy Place.
190903 Behind the second curtain stood a tent called the Holy of Holies,
190904 having the golden altar of incense and the ark of the covenant covered on all sides with gold, which contained a golden urn holding the manna, and Aaron's rod that budded, and the tables of the covenant;
190905 above it were the cherubim of glory overshadowing the mercy seat. Of these things we cannot now speak in detail.
190906 These preparations having thus been made, the priests go continually into the outer tent, performing their ritual duties;
190907 but into the second only the high priest goes, and he but once a year, and not without taking blood which he offers for himself and for the errors of the people.
190908 By this the Holy Spirit indicates that the way into the sanctuary is not yet opened as long as the outer tent is still standing
190909 (which is symbolic for the present age). According to this arrangement, gifts and sacrifices are offered which cannot perfect the conscience of the worshiper,
190910 but deal only with food and drink and various ablutions, regulations for the body imposed until the time of reformation.
190911 But when Christ appeared as a high priest of the good things that have come, then through the greater and more perfect tent (not made with hands, that is, not of this creation)
190912 he entered once for all into the Holy Place, taking not the blood of goats and calves but his own blood, thus securing an eternal redemption.
190913 For if the sprinkling of defiled persons with the blood of goats and bulls and with the ashes of a heifer sanctifies for the purification of the flesh,
190914 how much more shall the blood of Christ, who through the eternal Spirit offered himself without blemish to God, purify your conscience from dead works to serve the living God.
190915 Therefore he is the mediator of a new covenant, so that those who are called may receive the promised eternal inheritance, since a death has occurred which redeems them from the transgressions under the first covenant.
190916 For where a will is involved, the death of the one who made it must be established.
190917 For a will takes effect only at death, since it is not in force as long as the one who made it is alive.
190918 Hence even the first covenant was not ratified without blood.
190919 For when every commandment of the law had been declared by Moses to all the people, he took the blood of calves and goats, with water and scarlet wool and hyssop, and sprinkled both the book itself and all the people,
190920 saying, "This is the blood of the covenant which God commanded you."
190921 And in the same way he sprinkled with the blood both the tent and all the vessels used in worship.
190922 Indeed, under the law almost everything is purified with blood, and without the shedding of blood there is no forgiveness of sins.
190923 Thus it was necessary for the copies of the heavenly things to be purified with these rites, but the heavenly things themselves with better sacrifices than these.
190924 For Christ has entered, not into a sanctuary made with hands, a copy of the true one, but into heaven itself, now to appear in the presence of God on our behalf.
190925 Nor was it to offer himself repeatedly, as the high priest enters the Holy Place yearly with blood not his own;
190926 for then he would have had to suffer repeatedly since the foundation of the world. But as it is, he has appeared once for all at the end of the age to put away sin by the sacrifice of himself.
190927 And just as it is appointed for men to die once, and after that comes judgment,
190928 so Christ, having been offered once to bear the sins of many, will appear a second time, not to deal with sin but to save those who are eagerly waiting for him.
191001 For since the law has but a shadow of the good things to come instead of the true form of these realities, it can never, by the same sacrifices which are continually offered year after year, make perfect those who draw near.
191002 Otherwise, would they not have ceased to be offered? If the worshipers had once been cleansed, they would no longer have any consciousness of sin.
191003 But in these sacrifices there is a reminder of sin year after year.
191004 For it is impossible that the blood of bulls and goats should take away sins.
191005 Consequently, when Christ came into the world, he said, "Sacrifices and offerings thou hast not desired, but a body hast thou prepared for me;
191006 in burnt offerings and sin offerings thou hast taken no pleasure.
191007 Then I said, 'Lo, I have come to do thy will, O God,' as it is written of me in the roll of the book."
191008 When he said above, "Thou hast neither desired nor taken pleasure in sacrifices and offerings and burnt offerings and sin offerings" (these are offered according to the law),
191009 then he added, "Lo, I have come to do thy will." He abolishes the first in order to establish the second.
191010 And by that will we have been sanctified through the offering of the body of Jesus Christ once for all.
191011 And every priest stands daily at his service, offering repeatedly the same sacrifices, which can never take away sins.
191012 But when Christ had offered for all time a single sacrifice for sins, he sat down at the right hand of God,
191013 then to wait until his enemies should be made a stool for his feet.
191014 For by a single offering he has perfected for all time those who are sanctified.
191015 And the Holy Spirit also bears witness to us; for after saying,
191016 "This is the covenant that I will make with them after those days, says the Lord: I will put my laws on their hearts, and write them on their minds,"
191017 then he adds, "I will remember their sins and their misdeeds no more."
191018 Where there is forgiveness of these, there is no longer any offering for sin.
191019 Therefore, brethren, since we have confidence to enter the sanctuary by the blood of Jesus,
191020 by the new and living way which he opened for us through the curtain, that is, through his flesh,
191021 and since we have a great priest over the house of God,
191022 let us draw near with a true heart in full assurance of faith, with our hearts sprinkled clean from an evil conscience and our bodies washed with pure water.
191023 Let us hold fast the confession of our hope without wavering, for he who promised is faithful;
191024 and let us consider how to stir up one another to love and good works,
191025 not neglecting to meet together, as is the habit of some, but encouraging one another, and all the more as you see the Day drawing near.
191026 For if we sin deliberately after receiving the knowledge of the truth, there no longer remains a sacrifice for sins,
191027 but a fearful prospect of judgment, and a fury of fire which will consume the adversaries.
191028 A man who has violated the law of Moses dies without mercy at the testimony of two or three witnesses.
191029 How much worse punishment do you think will be deserved by the man who has spurned the Son of God, and profaned the blood of the covenant by which he was sanctified, and outraged the Spirit of grace?
191030 For we know him who said, "Vengeance is mine, I will repay." And again, "The Lord will judge his people."
191031 It is a fearful thing to fall into the hands of the living God.
191032 But recall the former days when, after you were enlightened, you endured a hard struggle with sufferings,
191033 sometimes being publicly exposed to abuse and affliction, and sometimes being partners with those so treated.
191034 For you had compassion on the prisoners, and you joyfully accepted the plundering of your property, since you knew that you yourselves had a better possession and an abiding one.
191035 Therefore do not throw away your confidence, which has a great reward.
191036 For you have need of endurance, so that you may do the will of God and receive what is promised.
191037 "For yet a little while, and the coming one shall come and shall not tarry;
191038 but my righteous one shall live by faith, and if he shrinks back, my soul has no pleasure in him."
191039 But we are not of those who shrink back and are destroyed, but of those who have faith and keep their souls.
191101 Now faith is the assurance of things hoped for, the conviction of things not seen.
191102 For by it the men of old received divine approval.
191103 By faith we understand that the world was created by the word of God, so that what is seen was made out of things which do not appear.
191104 By faith Abel offered to God a more acceptable sacrifice than Cain, through which he received approval as righteous, God bearing witness by accepting his gifts; he died, but through his faith he is still speaking.
191105 By faith Enoch was taken up so that he should not see death; and he was not found, because God had taken him. Now before he was taken he was attested as having pleased God.
191106 And without faith it is impossible to please him. For whoever would draw near to God must believe that he exists and that he rewards those who seek him.
191107 By faith Noah, being warned by God concerning events as yet unseen, took heed and constructed an ark for the saving of his household; by this he condemned the world and became an heir of the righteousness which comes by faith.
191108 By faith Abraham obeyed when he was called to go out to a place which he was to receive as an inheritance; and he went out, not knowing where he was to go.
191109 By faith he sojourned in the land of promise, as in a foreign land, living in tents with Isaac and Jacob, heirs with him of the same promise.
191110 For he looked forward to the city which has foundations, whose builder and maker is God.
191111 By faith Sarah herself received power to conceive, even when she was past the age, since she considered him faithful who had promised.
191112 Therefore from one man, and him as good as dead, were born descendants as many as the stars of heaven and as the innumerable grains of sand by the seashore.
191113 These all died in faith, not having received what was promised, but having seen it and greeted it from afar, and having acknowledged that they were strangers and exiles on the earth.
191114 For people who speak thus make it clear that they are seeking a homeland.
191115 If they had been thinking of that land from which they had gone out, they would have had opportunity to return.
191116 But as it is, they desire a better country, that is, a heavenly one. Therefore God is not ashamed to be called their God, for he has prepared for them a city.
191117 By faith Abraham, when he was tested, offered up Isaac, and he who had received the promises was ready to offer up his only son,
191118 of whom it was said, "Through Isaac shall your descendants be named."
191119 He considered that God was able to raise men even from the dead; hence, figuratively speaking, he did receive him back.
191120 By faith Isaac invoked future blessings on Jacob and Esau.
191121 By faith Jacob, when dying, blessed each of the sons of Joseph, bowing in worship over the head of his staff.
191122 By faith Joseph, at the end of his life, made mention of the exodus of the Israelites and gave directions concerning his burial.
191123 By faith Moses, when he was born, was hid for three months by his parents, because they saw that the child was beautiful; and they were not afraid of the king's edict.
191124 By faith Moses, when he was grown up, refused to be called the son of Pharaoh's daughter,
191125 choosing rather to share ill-treatment with the people of God than to enjoy the fleeting pleasures of sin.
191126 He considered abuse suffered for the Christ greater wealth than the treasures of Egypt, for he looked to the reward.
191127 By faith he left Egypt, not being afraid of the anger of the king; for he endured as seeing him who is invisible.
191128 By faith he kept the Passover and sprinkled the blood, so that the Destroyer of the first-born might not touch them.
191129 By faith the people crossed the Red Sea as if on dry land; but the Egyptians, when they attempted to do the same, were drowned.
191130 By faith the walls of Jericho fell down after they had been encircled for seven days.
191131 By faith Rahab the harlot did not perish with those who were disobedient, because she had given friendly welcome to the spies.
191132 And what more shall I say? For time would fail me to tell of Gideon, Barak, Samson, Jephthah, of David and Samuel and the prophets --
191133 who through faith conquered kingdoms, enforced justice, received promises, stopped the mouths of lions,
191134 quenched raging fire, escaped the edge of the sword, won strength out of weakness, became mighty in war, put foreign armies to flight.
191135 Women received their dead by resurrection. Some were tortured, refusing to accept release, that they might rise again to a better life.
191136 Others suffered mocking and scourging, and even chains and imprisonment.
191137 They were stoned, they were sawn in two, they were killed with the sword; they went about in skins of sheep and goats, destitute, afflicted, ill-treated --
191138 of whom the world was not worthy -- wandering over deserts and mountains, and in dens and caves of the earth.
191139 And all these, though well attested by their faith, did not receive what was promised,
191140 since God had foreseen something better for us, that apart from us they should not be made perfect.
191201 Therefore, since we are surrounded by so great a cloud of witnesses, let us also lay aside every weight, and sin which clings so closely, and let us run with perseverance the race that is set before us,
191202 looking to Jesus the pioneer and perfecter of our faith, who for the joy that was set before him endured the cross, despising the shame, and is seated at the right hand of the throne of God.
191203 Consider him who endured from sinners such hostility against himself, so that you may not grow weary or fainthearted.
191204 In your struggle against sin you have not yet resisted to the point of shedding your blood.
191205 And have you forgotten the exhortation which addresses you as sons? -- "My son, do not regard lightly the discipline of the Lord, nor lose courage when you are punished by him.
191206 For the Lord disciplines him whom he loves, and chastises every son whom he receives."
191207 It is for discipline that you have to endure. God is treating you as sons; for what son is there whom his father does not discipline?
191208 If you are left without discipline, in which all have participated, then you are illegitimate children and not sons.
191209 Besides this, we have had earthly fathers to discipline us and we respected them. Shall we not much more be subject to the Father of spirits and live?
191210 For they disciplined us for a short time at their pleasure, but he disciplines us for our good, that we may share his holiness.
191211 For the moment all discipline seems painful rather than pleasant; later it yields the peaceful fruit of righteousness to those who have been trained by it.
191212 Therefore lift your drooping hands and strengthen your weak knees,
191213 and make straight paths for your feet, so that what is lame may not be put out of joint but rather be healed.
191214 Strive for peace with all men, and for the holiness without which no one will see the Lord.
191215 See to it that no one fail to obtain the grace of God; that no "root of bitterness" spring up and cause trouble, and by it the many become defiled;
191216 that no one be immoral or irreligious like Esau, who sold his birthright for a single meal.
191217 For you know that afterward, when he desired to inherit the blessing, he was rejected, for he found no chance to repent, though he sought it with tears.
191218 For you have not come to what may be touched, a blazing fire, and darkness, and gloom, and a tempest,
191219 and the sound of a trumpet, and a voice whose words made the hearers entreat that no further messages be spoken to them.
191220 For they could not endure the order that was given, "If even a beast touches the mountain, it shall be stoned."
191221 Indeed, so terrifying was the sight that Moses said, "I tremble with fear."
191222 But you have come to Mount Zion and to the city of the living God, the heavenly Jerusalem, and to innumerable angels in festal gathering,
191223 and to the assembly of the first-born who are enrolled in heaven, and to a judge who is God of all, and to the spirits of just men made perfect,
191224 and to Jesus, the mediator of a new covenant, and to the sprinkled blood that speaks more graciously than the blood of Abel.
191225 See that you do not refuse him who is speaking. For if they did not escape when they refused him who warned them on earth, much less shall we escape if we reject him who warns from heaven.
191226 His voice then shook the earth; but now he has promised, "Yet once more I will shake not only the earth but also the heaven."
191227 This phrase, "Yet once more," indicates the removal of what is shaken, as of what has been made, in order that what cannot be shaken may remain.
191228 Therefore let us be grateful for receiving a kingdom that cannot be shaken, and thus let us offer to God acceptable worship, with reverence and awe;
191229 for our God is a consuming fire.
191301 Let brotherly love continue.
191302 Do not neglect to show hospitality to strangers, for thereby some have entertained angels unawares.
191303 Remember those who are in prison, as though in prison with them; and those who are ill-treated, since you also are in the body.
191304 Let marriage be held in honor among all, and let the marriage bed be undefiled; for God will judge the immoral and adulterous.
191305 Keep your life free from love of money, and be content with what you have; for he has said, "I will never fail you nor forsake you."
191306 Hence we can confidently say, "The Lord is my helper, I will not be afraid; what can man do to me?"
191307 Remember your leaders, those who spoke to you the word of God; consider the outcome of their life, and imitate their faith.
191308 Jesus Christ is the same yesterday and today and for ever.
191309 Do not be led away by diverse and strange teachings; for it is well that the heart be strengthened by grace, not by foods, which have not benefited their adherents.
191310 We have an altar from which those who serve the tent have no right to eat.
191311 For the bodies of those animals whose blood is brought into the sanctuary by the high priest as a sacrifice for sin are burned outside the camp.
191312 So Jesus also suffered outside the gate in order to sanctify the people through his own blood.
191313 Therefore let us go forth to him outside the camp and bear the abuse he endured.
191314 For here we have no lasting city, but we seek the city which is to come.
191315 Through him then let us continually offer up a sacrifice of praise to God, that is, the fruit of lips that acknowledge his name.
191316 Do not neglect to do good and to share what you have, for such sacrifices are pleasing to God.
191317 Obey your leaders and submit to them; for they are keeping watch over your souls, as men who will have to give account. Let them do this joyfully, and not sadly, for that would be of no advantage to you.
191318 Pray for us, for we are sure that we have a clear conscience, desiring to act honorably in all things.
191319 I urge you the more earnestly to do this in order that I may be restored to you the sooner.
191320 Now may the God of peace who brought again from the dead our Lord Jesus, the great shepherd of the sheep, by the blood of the eternal covenant,
191321 equip you with everything good that you may do his will, working in you that which is pleasing in his sight, through Jesus Christ; to whom be glory for ever and ever. Amen.
191322 I appeal to you, brethren, bear with my word of exhortation, for I have written to you briefly.
191323 You should understand that our brother Timothy has been released, with whom I shall see you if he comes soon.
191324 Greet all your leaders and all the saints. Those who come from Italy send you greetings.
191325 Grace be with all of you. Amen.
200101 James, a servant of God and of the Lord Jesus Christ, To the twelve tribes in the Dispersion: Greeting.
200102 Count it all joy, my brethren, when you meet various trials,
200103 for you know that the testing of your faith produces steadfastness.
200104 And let steadfastness have its full effect, that you may be perfect and complete, lacking in nothing.
200105 If any of you lacks wisdom, let him ask God, who gives to all men generously and without reproaching, and it will be given him.
200106 But let him ask in faith, with no doubting, for he who doubts is like a wave of the sea that is driven and tossed by the wind.
200107 For that person must not suppose that a double-minded man,
200108 unstable in all his ways, will receive anything from the Lord.
200109 Let the lowly brother boast in his exaltation,
200110 and the rich in his humiliation, because like the flower of the grass he will pass away.
200111 For the sun rises with its scorching heat and withers the grass; its flower falls, and its beauty perishes. So will the rich man fade away in the midst of his pursuits.
200112 Blessed is the man who endures trial, for when he has stood the test he will receive the crown of life which God has promised to those who love him.
200113 Let no one say when he is tempted, "I am tempted by God"; for God cannot be tempted with evil and he himself tempts no one;
200114 but each person is tempted when he is lured and enticed by his own desire.
200115 Then desire when it has conceived gives birth to sin; and sin when it is full-grown brings forth death.
200116 Do not be deceived, my beloved brethren.
200117 Every good endowment and every perfect gift is from above, coming down from the Father of lights with whom there is no variation or shadow due to change.
200118 Of his own will he brought us forth by the word of truth that we should be a kind of first fruits of his creatures.
200119 Know this, my beloved brethren. Let every man be quick to hear, slow to speak, slow to anger,
200120 for the anger of man does not work the righteousness of God.
200121 Therefore put away all filthiness and rank growth of wickedness and receive with meekness the implanted word, which is able to save your souls.
200122 But be doers of the word, and not hearers only, deceiving yourselves.
200123 For if any one is a hearer of the word and not a doer, he is like a man who observes his natural face in a mirror;
200124 for he observes himself and goes away and at once forgets what he was like.
200125 But he who looks into the perfect law, the law of liberty, and perseveres, being no hearer that forgets but a doer that acts, he shall be blessed in his doing.
200126 If any one thinks he is religious, and does not bridle his tongue but deceives his heart, this man's religion is vain.
200127 Religion that is pure and undefiled before God and the Father is this: to visit orphans and widows in their affliction, and to keep oneself unstained from the world.
200201 My brethren, show no partiality as you hold the faith of our Lord Jesus Christ, the Lord of glory.
200202 For if a man with gold rings and in fine clothing comes into your assembly, and a poor man in shabby clothing also comes in,
200203 and you pay attention to the one who wears the fine clothing and say, "Have a seat here, please," while you say to the poor man, "Stand there," or, "Sit at my feet,"
200204 have you not made distinctions among yourselves, and become judges with evil thoughts?
200205 Listen, my beloved brethren. Has not God chosen those who are poor in the world to be rich in faith and heirs of the kingdom which he has promised to those who love him?
200206 But you have dishonored the poor man. Is it not the rich who oppress you, is it not they who drag you into court?
200207 Is it not they who blaspheme that honorable name which was invoked over you?
200208 If you really fulfil the royal law, according to the scripture, "You shall love your neighbor as yourself," you do well.
200209 But if you show partiality, you commit sin, and are convicted by the law as transgressors.
200210 For whoever keeps the whole law but fails in one point has become guilty of all of it.
200211 For he who said, "Do not commit adultery," said also, "Do not kill." If you do not commit adultery but do kill, you have become a transgressor of the law.
200212 So speak and so act as those who are to be judged under the law of liberty.
200213 For judgment is without mercy to one who has shown no mercy; yet mercy triumphs over judgment.
200214 What does it profit, my brethren, if a man says he has faith but has not works? Can his faith save him?
200215 If a brother or sister is ill-clad and in lack of daily food,
200216 and one of you says to them, "Go in peace, be warmed and filled," without giving them the things needed for the body, what does it profit?
200217 So faith by itself, if it has no works, is dead.
200218 But some one will say, "You have faith and I have works." Show me your faith apart from your works, and I by my works will show you my faith.
200219 You believe that God is one; you do well. Even the demons believe -- and shudder.
200220 Do you want to be shown, you shallow man, that faith apart from works is barren?
200221 Was not Abraham our father justified by works, when he offered his son Isaac upon the altar?
200222 You see that faith was active along with his works, and faith was completed by works,
200223 and the scripture was fulfilled which says, "Abraham believed God, and it was reckoned to him as righteousness"; and he was called the friend of God.
200224 You see that a man is justified by works and not by faith alone.
200225 And in the same way was not also Rahab the harlot justified by works when she received the messengers and sent them out another way?
200226 For as the body apart from the spirit is dead, so faith apart from works is dead.
200301 Let not many of you become teachers, my brethren, for you know that we who teach shall be judged with greater strictness.
200302 For we all make many mistakes, and if any one makes no mistakes in what he says he is a perfect man, able to bridle the whole body also.
200303 If we put bits into the mouths of horses that they may obey us, we guide their whole bodies.
200304 Look at the ships also; though they are so great and are driven by strong winds, they are guided by a very small rudder wherever the will of the pilot directs.
200305 So the tongue is a little member and boasts of great things. How great a forest is set ablaze by a small fire!
200306 And the tongue is a fire. The tongue is an unrighteous world among our members, staining the whole body, setting on fire the cycle of nature, and set on fire by hell.
200307 For every kind of beast and bird, of reptile and sea creature, can be tamed and has been tamed by humankind,
200308 but no human being can tame the tongue -- a restless evil, full of deadly poison.
200309 With it we bless the Lord and Father, and with it we curse men, who are made in the likeness of God.
200310 From the same mouth come blessing and cursing. My brethren, this ought not to be so.
200311 Does a spring pour forth from the same opening fresh water and brackish?
200312 Can a fig tree, my brethren, yield olives, or a grapevine figs? No more can salt water yield fresh.
200313 Who is wise and understanding among you? By his good life let him show his works in the meekness of wisdom.
200314 But if you have bitter jealousy and selfish ambition in your hearts, do not boast and be false to the truth.
200315 This wisdom is not such as comes down from above, but is earthly, unspiritual, devilish.
200316 For where jealousy and selfish ambition exist, there will be disorder and every vile practice.
200317 But the wisdom from above is first pure, then peaceable, gentle, open to reason, full of mercy and good fruits, without uncertainty or insincerity.
200318 And the harvest of righteousness is sown in peace by those who make peace.
200401 What causes wars, and what causes fightings among you? Is it not your passions that are at war in your members?
200402 You desire and do not have; so you kill. And you covet and cannot obtain; so you fight and wage war. You do not have, because you do not ask.
200403 You ask and do not receive, because you ask wrongly, to spend it on your passions.
200404 Unfaithful creatures! Do you not know that friendship with the world is enmity with God? Therefore whoever wishes to be a friend of the world makes himself an enemy of God.
200405 Or do you suppose it is in vain that the scripture says, "He yearns jealously over the spirit which he has made to dwell in us"?
200406 But he gives more grace; therefore it says, "God opposes the proud, but gives grace to the humble."
200407 Submit yourselves therefore to God. Resist the devil and he will flee from you.
200408 Draw near to God and he will draw near to you. Cleanse your hands, you sinners, and purify your hearts, you men of double mind.
200409 Be wretched and mourn and weep. Let your laughter be turned to mourning and your joy to dejection.
200410 Humble yourselves before the Lord and he will exalt you.
200411 Do not speak evil against one another, brethren. He that speaks evil against a brother or judges his brother, speaks evil against the law and judges the law. But if you judge the law, you are not a doer of the law but a judge.
200412 There is one lawgiver and judge, he who is able to save and to destroy. But who are you that you judge your neighbor?
200413 Come now, you who say, "Today or tomorrow we will go into such and such a town and spend a year there and trade and get gain";
200414 whereas you do not know about tomorrow. What is your life? For you are a mist that appears for a little time and then vanishes.
200415 Instead you ought to say, "If the Lord wills, we shall live and we shall do this or that."
200416 As it is, you boast in your arrogance. All such boasting is evil.
200417 Whoever knows what is right to do and fails to do it, for him it is sin.
200501 Come now, you rich, weep and howl for the miseries that are coming upon you.
200502 Your riches have rotted and your garments are moth-eaten.
200503 Your gold and silver have rusted, and their rust will be evidence against you and will eat your flesh like fire. You have laid up treasure for the last days.
200504 Behold, the wages of the laborers who mowed your fields, which you kept back by fraud, cry out; and the cries of the harvesters have reached the ears of the Lord of hosts.
200505 You have lived on the earth in luxury and in pleasure; you have fattened your hearts in a day of slaughter.
200506 You have condemned, you have killed the righteous man; he does not resist you.
200507 Be patient, therefore, brethren, until the coming of the Lord. Behold, the farmer waits for the precious fruit of the earth, being patient over it until it receives the early and the late rain.
200508 You also be patient. Establish your hearts, for the coming of the Lord is at hand.
200509 Do not grumble, brethren, against one another, that you may not be judged; behold, the Judge is standing at the doors.
200510 As an example of suffering and patience, brethren, take the prophets who spoke in the name of the Lord.
200511 Behold, we call those happy who were steadfast. You have heard of the steadfastness of Job, and you have seen the purpose of the Lord, how the Lord is compassionate and merciful.
200512 But above all, my brethren, do not swear, either by heaven or by earth or with any other oath, but let your yes be yes and your no be no, that you may not fall under condemnation.
200513 Is any one among you suffering? Let him pray. Is any cheerful? Let him sing praise.
200514 Is any among you sick? Let him call for the elders of the church, and let them pray over him, anointing him with oil in the name of the Lord;
200515 and the prayer of faith will save the sick man, and the Lord will raise him up; and if he has committed sins, he will be forgiven.
200516 Therefore confess your sins to one another, and pray for one another, that you may be healed. The prayer of a righteous man has great power in its effects.
200517 Eli'jah was a man of like nature with ourselves and he prayed fervently that it might not rain, and for three years and six months it did not rain on the earth.
200518 Then he prayed again and the heaven gave rain, and the earth brought forth its fruit.
200519 My brethren, if any one among you wanders from the truth and some one brings him back,
200520 let him know that whoever brings back a sinner from the error of his way will save his soul from death and will cover a multitude of sins.
210101 Peter, an apostle of Jesus Christ, To the exiles of the Dispersion in Pontus, Galatia, Cappado'cia, Asia, and Bithyn'ia,
210102 chosen and destined by God the Father and sanctified by the Spirit for obedience to Jesus Christ and for sprinkling with his blood: May grace and peace be multiplied to you.
210103 Blessed be the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ! By his great mercy we have been born anew to a living hope through the resurrection of Jesus Christ from the dead,
210104 and to an inheritance which is imperishable, undefiled, and unfading, kept in heaven for you,
210105 who by God's power are guarded through faith for a salvation ready to be revealed in the last time.
210106 In this you rejoice, though now for a little while you may have to suffer various trials,
210107 so that the genuineness of your faith, more precious than gold which though perishable is tested by fire, may redound to praise and glory and honor at the revelation of Jesus Christ.
210108 Without having seen him you love him; though you do not now see him you believe in him and rejoice with unutterable and exalted joy.
210109 As the outcome of your faith you obtain the salvation of your souls.
210110 The prophets who prophesied of the grace that was to be yours searched and inquired about this salvation;
210111 they inquired what person or time was indicated by the Spirit of Christ within them when predicting the sufferings of Christ and the subsequent glory.
210112 It was revealed to them that they were serving not themselves but you, in the things which have now been announced to you by those who preached the good news to you through the Holy Spirit sent from heaven, things into which angels long to look.
210113 Therefore gird up your minds, be sober, set your hope fully upon the grace that is coming to you at the revelation of Jesus Christ.
210114 As obedient children, do not be conformed to the passions of your former ignorance,
210115 but as he who called you is holy, be holy yourselves in all your conduct;
210116 since it is written, "You shall be holy, for I am holy."
210117 And if you invoke as Father him who judges each one impartially according to his deeds, conduct yourselves with fear throughout the time of your exile.
210118 You know that you were ransomed from the futile ways inherited from your fathers, not with perishable things such as silver or gold,
210119 but with the precious blood of Christ, like that of a lamb without blemish or spot.
210120 He was destined before the foundation of the world but was made manifest at the end of the times for your sake.
210121 Through him you have confidence in God, who raised him from the dead and gave him glory, so that your faith and hope are in God.
210122 Having purified your souls by your obedience to the truth for a sincere love of the brethren, love one another earnestly from the heart.
210123 You have been born anew, not of perishable seed but of imperishable, through the living and abiding word of God;
210124 for "All flesh is like grass and all its glory like the flower of grass. The grass withers, and the flower falls,
210125 but the word of the Lord abides for ever." That word is the good news which was preached to you.
210201 So put away all malice and all guile and insincerity and envy and all slander.
210202 Like newborn babes, long for the pure spiritual milk, that by it you may grow up to salvation;
210203 for you have tasted the kindness of the Lord.
210204 Come to him, to that living stone, rejected by men but in God's sight chosen and precious;
210205 and like living stones be yourselves built into a spiritual house, to be a holy priesthood, to offer spiritual sacrifices acceptable to God through Jesus Christ.
210206 For it stands in scripture: "Behold, I am laying in Zion a stone, a cornerstone chosen and precious, and he who believes in him will not be put to shame."
210207 To you therefore who believe, he is precious, but for those who do not believe, "The very stone which the builders rejected has become the head of the corner,"
210208 and "A stone that will make men stumble, a rock that will make them fall"; for they stumble because they disobey the word, as they were destined to do.
210209 But you are a chosen race, a royal priesthood, a holy nation, God's own people, that you may declare the wonderful deeds of him who called you out of darkness into his marvelous light.
210210 Once you were no people but now you are God's people; once you had not received mercy but now you have received mercy.
210211 Beloved, I beseech you as aliens and exiles to abstain from the passions of the flesh that wage war against your soul.
210212 Maintain good conduct among the Gentiles, so that in case they speak against you as wrongdoers, they may see your good deeds and glorify God on the day of visitation.
210213 Be subject for the Lord's sake to every human institution, whether it be to the emperor as supreme,
210214 or to governors as sent by him to punish those who do wrong and to praise those who do right.
210215 For it is God's will that by doing right you should put to silence the ignorance of foolish men.
210216 Live as free men, yet without using your freedom as a pretext for evil; but live as servants of God.
210217 Honor all men. Love the brotherhood. Fear God. Honor the emperor.
210218 Servants, be submissive to your masters with all respect, not only to the kind and gentle but also to the overbearing.
210219 For one is approved if, mindful of God, he endures pain while suffering unjustly.
210220 For what credit is it, if when you do wrong and are beaten for it you take it patiently? But if when you do right and suffer for it you take it patiently, you have God's approval.
210221 For to this you have been called, because Christ also suffered for you, leaving you an example, that you should follow in his steps.
210222 He committed no sin; no guile was found on his lips.
210223 When he was reviled, he did not revile in return; when he suffered, he did not threaten; but he trusted to him who judges justly.
210224 He himself bore our sins in his body on the tree, that we might die to sin and live to righteousness. By his wounds you have been healed.
210225 For you were straying like sheep, but have now returned to the Shepherd and Guardian of your souls.
210301 Likewise you wives, be submissive to your husbands, so that some, though they do not obey the word, may be won without a word by the behavior of their wives,
210302 when they see your reverent and chaste behavior.
210303 Let not yours be the outward adorning with braiding of hair, decoration of gold, and wearing of fine clothing,
210304 but let it be the hidden person of the heart with the imperishable jewel of a gentle and quiet spirit, which in God's sight is very precious.
210305 So once the holy women who hoped in God used to adorn themselves and were submissive to their husbands,
210306 as Sarah obeyed Abraham, calling him lord. And you are now her children if you do right and let nothing terrify you.
210307 Likewise you husbands, live considerately with your wives, bestowing honor on the woman as the weaker sex, since you are joint heirs of the grace of life, in order that your prayers may not be hindered.
210308 Finally, all of you, have unity of spirit, sympathy, love of the brethren, a tender heart and a humble mind.
210309 Do not return evil for evil or reviling for reviling; but on the contrary bless, for to this you have been called, that you may obtain a blessing.
210310 For "He that would love life and see good days, let him keep his tongue from evil and his lips from speaking guile;
210311 let him turn away from evil and do right; let him seek peace and pursue it.
210312 For the eyes of the Lord are upon the righteous, and his ears are open to their prayer. But the face of the Lord is against those that do evil."
210313 Now who is there to harm you if you are zealous for what is right?
210314 But even if you do suffer for righteousness' sake, you will be blessed. Have no fear of them, nor be troubled,
210315 but in your hearts reverence Christ as Lord. Always be prepared to make a defense to any one who calls you to account for the hope that is in you, yet do it with gentleness and reverence;
210316 and keep your conscience clear, so that, when you are abused, those who revile your good behavior in Christ may be put to shame.
210317 For it is better to suffer for doing right, if that should be God's will, than for doing wrong.
210318 For Christ also died for sins once for all, the righteous for the unrighteous, that he might bring us to God, being put to death in the flesh but made alive in the spirit;
210319 in which he went and preached to the spirits in prison,
210320 who formerly did not obey, when God's patience waited in the days of Noah, during the building of the ark, in which a few, that is, eight persons, were saved through water.
210321 Baptism, which corresponds to this, now saves you, not as a removal of dirt from the body but as an appeal to God for a clear conscience, through the resurrection of Jesus Christ,
210322 who has gone into heaven and is at the right hand of God, with angels, authorities, and powers subject to him.
210401 Since therefore Christ suffered in the flesh, arm yourselves with the same thought, for whoever has suffered in the flesh has ceased from sin,
210402 so as to live for the rest of the time in the flesh no longer by human passions but by the will of God.
210403 Let the time that is past suffice for doing what the Gentiles like to do, living in licentiousness, passions, drunkenness, revels, carousing, and lawless idolatry.
210404 They are surprised that you do not now join them in the same wild profligacy, and they abuse you;
210405 but they will give account to him who is ready to judge the living and the dead.
210406 For this is why the gospel was preached even to the dead, that though judged in the flesh like men, they might live in the spirit like God.
210407 The end of all things is at hand; therefore keep sane and sober for your prayers.
210408 Above all hold unfailing your love for one another, since love covers a multitude of sins.
210409 Practice hospitality ungrudgingly to one another.
210410 As each has received a gift, employ it for one another, as good stewards of God's varied grace:
210411 whoever speaks, as one who utters oracles of God; whoever renders service, as one who renders it by the strength which God supplies; in order that in everything God may be glorified through Jesus Christ. To him belong glory and dominion for ever and ever. Amen.
210412 Beloved, do not be surprised at the fiery ordeal which comes upon you to prove you, as though something strange were happening to you.
210413 But rejoice in so far as you share Christ's sufferings, that you may also rejoice and be glad when his glory is revealed.
210414 If you are reproached for the name of Christ, you are blessed, because the spirit of glory and of God rests upon you.
210415 But let none of you suffer as a murderer, or a thief, or a wrongdoer, or a mischief-maker;
210416 yet if one suffers as a Christian, let him not be ashamed, but under that name let him glorify God.
210417 For the time has come for judgment to begin with the household of God; and if it begins with us, what will be the end of those who do not obey the gospel of God?
210418 And "If the righteous man is scarcely saved, where will the impious and sinner appear?"
210419 Therefore let those who suffer according to God's will do right and entrust their souls to a faithful Creator.
210501 So I exhort the elders among you, as a fellow elder and a witness of the sufferings of Christ as well as a partaker in the glory that is to be revealed.
210502 Tend the flock of God that is your charge, not by constraint but willingly, not for shameful gain but eagerly,
210503 not as domineering over those in your charge but being examples to the flock.
210504 And when the chief Shepherd is manifested you will obtain the unfading crown of glory.
210505 Likewise you that are younger be subject to the elders. Clothe yourselves, all of you, with humility toward one another, for "God opposes the proud, but gives grace to the humble."
210506 Humble yourselves therefore under the mighty hand of God, that in due time he may exalt you.
210507 Cast all your anxieties on him, for he cares about you.
210508 Be sober, be watchful. Your adversary the devil prowls around like a roaring lion, seeking some one to devour.
210509 Resist him, firm in your faith, knowing that the same experience of suffering is required of your brotherhood throughout the world.
210510 And after you have suffered a little while, the God of all grace, who has called you to his eternal glory in Christ, will himself restore, establish, and strengthen you.
210511 To him be the dominion for ever and ever. Amen.
210512 By Silva'nus, a faithful brother as I regard him, I have written briefly to you, exhorting and declaring that this is the true grace of God; stand fast in it.
210513 She who is at Babylon, who is likewise chosen, sends you greetings; and so does my son Mark.
210514 Greet one another with the kiss of love. Peace to all of you that are in Christ.
220101 Simeon Peter, a servant and apostle of Jesus Christ, To those who have obtained a faith of equal standing with ours in the righteousness of our God and Savior Jesus Christ:
220102 May grace and peace be multiplied to you in the knowledge of God and of Jesus our Lord.
220103 His divine power has granted to us all things that pertain to life and godliness, through the knowledge of him who called us to his own glory and excellence,
220104 by which he has granted to us his precious and very great promises, that through these you may escape from the corruption that is in the world because of passion, and become partakers of the divine nature.
220105 For this very reason make every effort to supplement your faith with virtue, and virtue with knowledge,
220106 and knowledge with self-control, and self-control with steadfastness, and steadfastness with godliness,
220107 and godliness with brotherly affection, and brotherly affection with love.
220108 For if these things are yours and abound, they keep you from being ineffective or unfruitful in the knowledge of our Lord Jesus Christ.
220109 For whoever lacks these things is blind and shortsighted and has forgotten that he was cleansed from his old sins.
220110 Therefore, brethren, be the more zealous to confirm your call and election, for if you do this you will never fall;
220111 so there will be richly provided for you an entrance into the eternal kingdom of our Lord and Savior Jesus Christ.
220112 Therefore I intend always to remind you of these things, though you know them and are established in the truth that you have.
220113 I think it right, as long as I am in this body, to arouse you by way of reminder,
220114 since I know that the putting off of my body will be soon, as our Lord Jesus Christ showed me.
220115 And I will see to it that after my departure you may be able at any time to recall these things.
220116 For we did not follow cleverly devised myths when we made known to you the power and coming of our Lord Jesus Christ, but we were eyewitnesses of his majesty.
220117 For when he received honor and glory from God the Father and the voice was borne to him by the Majestic Glory, "This is my beloved Son, with whom I am well pleased,"
220118 we heard this voice borne from heaven, for we were with him on the holy mountain.
220119 And we have the prophetic word made more sure. You will do well to pay attention to this as to a lamp shining in a dark place, until the day dawns and the morning star rises in your hearts.
220120 First of all you must understand this, that no prophecy of scripture is a matter of one's own interpretation,
220121 because no prophecy ever came by the impulse of man, but men moved by the Holy Spirit spoke from God.
220201 But false prophets also arose among the people, just as there will be false teachers among you, who will secretly bring in destructive heresies, even denying the Master who bought them, bringing upon themselves swift destruction.
220202 And many will follow their licentiousness, and because of them the way of truth will be reviled.
220203 And in their greed they will exploit you with false words; from of old their condemnation has not been idle, and their destruction has not been asleep.
220204 For if God did not spare the angels when they sinned, but cast them into hell and committed them to pits of nether gloom to be kept until the judgment;
220205 if he did not spare the ancient world, but preserved Noah, a herald of righteousness, with seven other persons, when he brought a flood upon the world of the ungodly;
220206 if by turning the cities of Sodom and Gomor'rah to ashes he condemned them to extinction and made them an example to those who were to be ungodly;
220207 and if he rescued righteous Lot, greatly distressed by the licentiousness of the wicked
220208 (for by what that righteous man saw and heard as he lived among them, he was vexed in his righteous soul day after day with their lawless deeds),
220209 then the Lord knows how to rescue the godly from trial, and to keep the unrighteous under punishment until the day of judgment,
220210 and especially those who indulge in the lust of defiling passion and despise authority. Bold and wilful, they are not afraid to revile the glorious ones,
220211 whereas angels, though greater in might and power, do not pronounce a reviling judgment upon them before the Lord.
220212 But these, like irrational animals, creatures of instinct, born to be caught and killed, reviling in matters of which they are ignorant, will be destroyed in the same destruction with them,
220213 suffering wrong for their wrongdoing. They count it pleasure to revel in the daytime. They are blots and blemishes, reveling in their dissipation, carousing with you.
220214 They have eyes full of adultery, insatiable for sin. They entice unsteady souls. They have hearts trained in greed. Accursed children!
220215 Forsaking the right way they have gone astray; they have followed the way of Balaam, the son of Be'or, who loved gain from wrongdoing,
220216 but was rebuked for his own transgression; a dumb ass spoke with human voice and restrained the prophet's madness.
220217 These are waterless springs and mists driven by a storm; for them the nether gloom of darkness has been reserved.
220218 For, uttering loud boasts of folly, they entice with licentious passions of the flesh men who have barely escaped from those who live in error.
220219 They promise them freedom, but they themselves are slaves of corruption; for whatever overcomes a man, to that he is enslaved.
220220 For if, after they have escaped the defilements of the world through the knowledge of our Lord and Savior Jesus Christ, they are again entangled in them and overpowered, the last state has become worse for them than the first.
220221 For it would have been better for them never to have known the way of righteousness than after knowing it to turn back from the holy commandment delivered to them.
220222 It has happened to them according to the true proverb, The dog turns back to his own vomit, and the sow is washed only to wallow in the mire.
220301 This is now the second letter that I have written to you, beloved, and in both of them I have aroused your sincere mind by way of reminder;
220302 that you should remember the predictions of the holy prophets and the commandment of the Lord and Savior through your apostles.
220303 First of all you must understand this, that scoffers will come in the last days with scoffing, following their own passions
220304 and saying, "Where is the promise of his coming? For ever since the fathers fell asleep, all things have continued as they were from the beginning of creation."
220305 They deliberately ignore this fact, that by the word of God heavens existed long ago, and an earth formed out of water and by means of water,
220306 through which the world that then existed was deluged with water and perished.
220307 But by the same word the heavens and earth that now exist have been stored up for fire, being kept until the day of judgment and destruction of ungodly men.
220308 But do not ignore this one fact, beloved, that with the Lord one day is as a thousand years, and a thousand years as one day.
220309 The Lord is not slow about his promise as some count slowness, but is forbearing toward you, not wishing that any should perish, but that all should reach repentance.
220310 But the day of the Lord will come like a thief, and then the heavens will pass away with a loud noise, and the elements will be dissolved with fire, and the earth and the works that are upon it will be burned up.
220311 Since all these things are thus to be dissolved, what sort of persons ought you to be in lives of holiness and godliness,
220312 waiting for and hastening the coming of the day of God, because of which the heavens will be kindled and dissolved, and the elements will melt with fire!
220313 But according to his promise we wait for new heavens and a new earth in which righteousness dwells.
220314 Therefore, beloved, since you wait for these, be zealous to be found by him without spot or blemish, and at peace.
220315 And count the forbearance of our Lord as salvation. So also our beloved brother Paul wrote to you according to the wisdom given him,
220316 speaking of this as he does in all his letters. There are some things in them hard to understand, which the ignorant and unstable twist to their own destruction, as they do the other scriptures.
220317 You therefore, beloved, knowing this beforehand, beware lest you be carried away with the error of lawless men and lose your own stability.
220318 But grow in the grace and knowledge of our Lord and Savior Jesus Christ. To him be the glory both now and to the day of eternity. Amen.
230101 That which was from the beginning, which we have heard, which we have seen with our eyes, which we have looked upon and touched with our hands, concerning the word of life --
230102 the life was made manifest, and we saw it, and testify to it, and proclaim to you the eternal life which was with the Father and was made manifest to us --
230103 that which we have seen and heard we proclaim also to you, so that you may have fellowship with us; and our fellowship is with the Father and with his Son Jesus Christ.
230104 And we are writing this that our joy may be complete.
230105 This is the message we have heard from him and proclaim to you, that God is light and in him is no darkness at all.
230106 If we say we have fellowship with him while we walk in darkness, we lie and do not live according to the truth;
230107 but if we walk in the light, as he is in the light, we have fellowship with one another, and the blood of Jesus his Son cleanses us from all sin.
230108 If we say we have no sin, we deceive ourselves, and the truth is not in us.
230109 If we confess our sins, he is faithful and just, and will forgive our sins and cleanse us from all unrighteousness.
230110 If we say we have not sinned, we make him a liar, and his word is not in us.
230201 My little children, I am writing this to you so that you may not sin; but if any one does sin, we have an advocate with the Father, Jesus Christ the righteous;
230202 and he is the expiation for our sins, and not for ours only but also for the sins of the whole world.
230203 And by this we may be sure that we know him, if we keep his commandments.
230204 He who says "I know him" but disobeys his commandments is a liar, and the truth is not in him;
230205 but whoever keeps his word, in him truly love for God is perfected. By this we may be sure that we are in him:
230206 he who says he abides in him ought to walk in the same way in which he walked.
230207 Beloved, I am writing you no new commandment, but an old commandment which you had from the beginning; the old commandment is the word which you have heard.
230208 Yet I am writing you a new commandment, which is true in him and in you, because the darkness is passing away and the true light is already shining.
230209 He who says he is in the light and hates his brother is in the darkness still.
230210 He who loves his brother abides in the light, and in it there is no cause for stumbling.
230211 But he who hates his brother is in the darkness and walks in the darkness, and does not know where he is going, because the darkness has blinded his eyes.
230212 I am writing to you, little children, because your sins are forgiven for his sake.
230213 I am writing to you, fathers, because you know him who is from the beginning. I am writing to you, young men, because you have overcome the evil one. I write to you, children, because you know the Father.
230214 I write to you, fathers, because you know him who is from the beginning. I write to you, young men, because you are strong, and the word of God abides in you, and you have overcome the evil one.
230215 Do not love the world or the things in the world. If any one loves the world, love for the Father is not in him.
230216 For all that is in the world, the lust of the flesh and the lust of the eyes and the pride of life, is not of the Father but is of the world.
230217 And the world passes away, and the lust of it; but he who does the will of God abides for ever.
230218 Children, it is the last hour; and as you have heard that antichrist is coming, so now many antichrists have come; therefore we know that it is the last hour.
230219 They went out from us, but they were not of us; for if they had been of us, they would have continued with us; but they went out, that it might be plain that they all are not of us.
230220 But you have been anointed by the Holy One, and you all know.
230221 I write to you, not because you do not know the truth, but because you know it, and know that no lie is of the truth.
230222 Who is the liar but he who denies that Jesus is the Christ? This is the antichrist, he who denies the Father and the Son.
230223 No one who denies the Son has the Father. He who confesses the Son has the Father also.
230224 Let what you heard from the beginning abide in you. If what you heard from the beginning abides in you, then you will abide in the Son and in the Father.
230225 And this is what he has promised us, eternal life.
230226 I write this to you about those who would deceive you;
230227 but the anointing which you received from him abides in you, and you have no need that any one should teach you; as his anointing teaches you about everything, and is true, and is no lie, just as it has taught you, abide in him.
230228 And now, little children, abide in him, so that when he appears we may have confidence and not shrink from him in shame at his coming.
230229 If you know that he is righteous, you may be sure that every one who does right is born of him.
230301 See what love the Father has given us, that we should be called children of God; and so we are. The reason why the world does not know us is that it did not know him.
